### [1] [Unifying spacetime approaches to quantum mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12539)
*N. L. Diaz,M. Cerezo,Paolo Braccia*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了“时空量子力学”（spacetime quantum mechanics）框架中的核心对象——时空态（spacetime states），证明路径积分、时间上的量子态、伪密度矩阵、Page-Wootters机制等主要文献提案均为同一底层对象的不同表现，并通过这一统一框架揭示了各形式体系之间的数学关系及所捕获的时空信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，为将时间和空间置于更平等地位以重新表述量子力学（quantum mechanics），涌现了大量面向时空（spacetime-oriented）的理论方法，但这些方法彼此之间的关系尚未得到系统澄清。

Method: 对时空态这一核心对象进行详细数学研究，通过特定求值（evaluations）、信息约化（reduced information）、线性映射（linear maps）或量子信道（quantum channels）等操作，将路径积分（path integrals）、时间上的量子态、伪密度矩阵、Page-Wootters机制、超密度算符及类时纠缠提案等统一表示为时空态的不同呈现形式。

Result: 时空态是上述多种形式的统一底层对象；该统一框架提供了各形式体系的显式数学表示，揭示了它们之间的内在关联，并阐明了每种形式所捕获的时空信息内容。

Conclusion: 该统一视角对Leggett-Garg不等式、离序时间关联函数（OTOCs）、时间张量网络、费米子系统、相对论性量子场论（relativistic QFTs）、量子参考系（quantum reference frames）及经典物理等领域具有广泛的启示意义。

Abstract: Recent efforts to formulate quantum mechanics in a way that treats space and time on a more equal footing have led to a large variety of spacetime-oriented approaches. In this work we present a detailed study of spacetime states, the objects that play the role of quantum states in the recently introduced framework of spacetime quantum mechanics, and show that the main proposals in the literature are different manifestations of the same underlying object. Path integrals, quantum states over time, pseudo-density matrices, the Page and Wootters mechanism, superdensity operators, and timelike-entanglement proposals all arise from spacetime states through particular evaluations, reduced information, linear maps, or quantum channels. This unification provides explicit mathematical representations of these formalisms, reveals relations among them, and clarifies the spacetime information each one captures. We also study the broader relevance of the spacetime-state point of view for Leggett-Garg inequalities, OTOCs, temporal tensor networks, fermionic systems, relativistic QFTs, quantum reference frames, and classical physics, together with additional insights and perspectives revealed by the common unifying framework.

</details>


### [2] [Supersymmetry of dissipative Bose-Fermi systems with application to Jaynes-Cummings and Dicke models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12682)
*Colin V. Coane,Francesco Iachello*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了如何利用耦合玻色-费米系统的超对称性（supersymmetry）将Jaynes-Cummings模型和Dicke模型在旋转波近似下的哈密顿量置于矩阵形式，并给出本征值的显式解析解；进而将该超对称性扩展至马尔可夫开放系统的刘维尔算符（Liouvillian），同样给出本征值的显式解。这些结果源于Jaynes-Cummings模型的哈密顿量与超代数$u(1|1)$的线性卡西米尔不变量对易，而Dicke模型的哈密顿量则与$\sum_{i} u_{i}(1|1)$的线性不变量以及一个额外的$su(2)$代数的不变量同时对易。该方法适用于多种具有$u(1|1)$乃至$u(n|m)$动力学超代数的耦合玻色-费米系统，有望为更复杂系统的研究提供高效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为耦合玻色-费米系统（coupled Bose-Fermi systems）中的Jaynes-Cummings模型和Dicke模型在旋转波近似（rotating wave approximation）下，提供一种基于超对称性的统一矩阵化方法，从而得到本征值的显式解析解，并进一步推广至开放系统的刘维尔算符。

Method: 利用哈密顿量与超代数$u(1|1)$的线性卡西米尔不变量（linear Casimir invariant）之间的对易关系，以及Dicke模型中与$\sum_{i} u_{i}(1|1)$和附加$su(2)$代数不变量的同时对易性质，将哈密顿量和刘维尔算符置于矩阵形式，并求解本征值。

Result: 成功将Jaynes-Cummings模型和Dicke模型在旋转波近似下的哈密顿量以及对应马尔可夫开放系统（Markovian open systems）的刘维尔算符矩阵化，并给出了各自本征值的显式解析解。

Conclusion: 该超对称性方法不仅适用于$u(1|1)$动力学超代数（dynamical superalgebras）描述的耦合玻色-费米系统，还可推广至更一般的$u(n|m)$情形，为复杂系统的研究提供了高效分析工具。

Abstract: We demonstrate how supersymmetries of Hamiltonians for coupled Bose-Fermi systems can be used to place the Hamiltonians of the Jaynes-Cummings model and Dicke model under the rotating wave approximation in matrix form and provide explicit analytic solutions for their eigenvalues. We then use this supersymmetry to place the Liouvillians of the associated Markovian open systems in matrix form and provide explicit solutions for their eigenvalues. These results are a consequence of the fact that the Hamiltonian of the Jaynes-Cummings model commutes with the linear Casimir invariant of the superalgebra $u(1|1)$ and that the Hamiltonian of the Dicke model commutes both with the linear invariant of $\sum_{i} u_{i}(1|1)$ and with the invariant of an additional $su(2)$ algebra. Our methods apply to various coupled Bose-Fermi systems with $u(1|1)$ and more generally with $u(n|m)$ dynamical superalgebras, and may provide efficient tools for studying more complicated examples.

</details>


### [3] [Measurement Geometry for Quantum Random Access Codes: Beyond Nayak Bound and Toward Optimality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12700)
*Seiseki Akibue,Rudy Raymond,Suguru Tamaki,Kosei Teramoto*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将量子随机存取码设计重新表述为一种非交换测量谱问题，给出了Nayak界的初等证明，并得到了在整个有限尺寸范围内优于Nayak界的上界；在此基础上引入互无偏投影算子测量（MUPVMs），证明了两量子比特QRAC达到猜想界时其解码测量必须形成MUPVM，并提出了基于MUPVM的(M+2,M)-QRAC构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子随机存取码（QRAC）研究将N个经典比特编码到M个量子比特中并能恢复任意单个比特的最优性能。虽然Nayak界是解码概率的标准通用上界，但数值证据表明在小量子比特（qubit）区域存在更强的上界，现有证明缺乏对这一有限尺寸改进的刻画。

Method: 将最优解码概率表述为解码测量问题，从而将QRAC设计转化为非交换测量（noncommuting measurements）的谱问题；通过简化Chernoff界（Chernoff-bound）论证给出Nayak界的初等证明，并进一步精炼该论证以获得改进的上界。

Result: 得到了在整个有限尺寸（finite-size）区域内优于Nayak界的上界；证明了达到猜想界的两个量子比特QRAC的解码测量必须形成互无偏投影算子测量（mutually unbiased projector-valued measurements, MUPVMs）；证明了任何MUPVM在辅助一个附加量子比特（ancillary qubit）后，即可实现具有最优N缩放解码概率的QRAC；提出了一个基于MUPVM的(M+2,M)-QRAC族构造，该构造达到猜想界。

Conclusion: 通过非交换测量的谱方法，不仅给出了Nayak界的初等证明，还获得了有限尺寸下的改进上界；MUPVM作为互无偏基（mutually unbiased bases）的推广，在QRAC最优性刻画中起核心作用，并提供了达到猜想界的构造性方案。

Abstract: Quantum random access codes (QRACs) ask how well N classical bits can be encoded into M qubits while allowing any single bit to be recovered. Although the Nayak bound remains the standard general upper bound on the decoding probability, numerical evidence suggests a stronger upper bound in the small-qubit regime.
  In this work, we formulate the optimal decoding probability in terms of decoding measurements, reformulating QRAC design as a spectral problem for noncommuting measurements. Using this formulation, we give an elementary proof of the Nayak bound by simplifying the Chernoff-bound argument. Moreover, we refine the argument to obtain upper bounds that improve over Nayak's bound in the entire finite-size regime.
  The equality conditions of our bounds justify defining mutually unbiased projector-valued measurements (MUPVMs), a generalization of mutually unbiased bases. We show that decoding measurement of any two-qubit QRAC attaining the conjectured bound must form MUPVMs. We also show that any MUPVM, assisted by one ancillary qubit, yields a QRAC with optimal N-scaling decoding probability. Finally, we propose a new MUPVM-based construction for the (M+2,M)-QRAC family attaining the conjectured bound.

</details>


### [4] [Accidental Symmetry in the Tavis-Cummings Model via the Schwinger Boson Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12813)
*Plato Deliyannis,Iman Marvian*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Tavis-Cummings (TC)哈密顿量中发现了一个此前未被注意到的新对称性，给出了对应的守恒可观测量，并证明了该对称性对 n>2 量子比特体系的可实现酉变换施加了强约束；这些约束可通过添加 J_z² 项被解除，且该对称性的起源可利用Schwinger玻色子表示加以解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TC模型（Tavis-Cummings模型）是多量子比特与单玻色子模式耦合的经典体系，其结构通常由置换不变性和U(1)对称性描述。然而，是否存在其他独立对称性仍未明确，这限制了人们对TC系统可控性及其量子计算应用的深入理解。

Method: 通过理论分析识别TC哈密顿量中新增的“偶然对称性（accidental symmetry）”，构造对应的守恒可观测量；利用Schwinger玻色子表示（Schwinger's boson representation of angular momentum）解释该对称性的起源，并检验在添加全局 J_z 或 J_z² 哈密顿量时对称性约束的存续与消除条件。

Result: 对于 n>2 量子比特，新发现的对称性对可实现酉变换（unitary transformations）施加了强约束；这些约束在添加全局 J_z 哈密顿量时仍然存在，但加入 J_z² 项后被消除，尽管 J_z² 同时保留了置换不变性和U(1)对称性。

Conclusion: 该对称性对TC系统的可控性及其在量子计算中的应用具有重要影响，后续在姊妹论文中进一步探讨。

Abstract: The Jaynes-Cummings (JC) Hamiltonian is a paradigmatic model of light-matter interaction and, more generally, qubit-boson interactions, widely used across atomic, optical, and superconducting qubit platforms. In the multi-qubit setting, where n qubits are identically coupled to a single boson mode, this interaction is known as the Tavis-Cummings (TC) Hamiltonian. The structure of the TC model is usually understood in terms of two standard symmetries: permutation invariance of the qubits and a U(1) symmetry associated with conservation of the total excitation number. Here we identify an additional, independent "accidental" symmetry of the TC Hamiltonian and construct the corresponding conserved observable. We show that, for n>2 qubits, this symmetry imposes strong constraints on the realizable unitary transformations. These constraints persist in the presence of the global $J_z$ Hamiltonian, but are removed by adding $J_z^2$, even though $J_z^2$ preserves both permutation invariance and the U(1) symmetry. Finally, we explain the origin of this previously unnoticed symmetry using Schwinger's boson representation of angular momentum. These restrictions have important implications for controllability of the TC system and for its applications to quantum computing, which are investigated further in a companion paper.

</details>


### [5] [Global Control with the Tavis-Cummings Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12906)
*Plato Deliyannis,Iman Marvian*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究在全局控制下量子比特系统的可控性，分析了基于Tavis-Cummings（TC）相互作用的量子比特-玻色子联合系统，发现对于n>2个量子比特，可实现酉算符受到一种“偶然对称性”（accidental symmetry）的限制，而引入J_z^2哈密顿量可打破该对称性，从而实现半通用性（semi-universality）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索全局控制条件下多量子比特系统的可控性边界，尤其是存在一个共同玻色模式耦合时的量子操控能力。

Method: 通过分析Tavis-Cummings（TC）相互作用与全局z场J_z联合生成的酉算符群，刻画可实现酉算符的代数结构，并识别出TC哈密顿量中存在的一种“偶然对称性”（accidental symmetry）。

Result: 对于n>2个量子比特，可实现酉算符受到该偶然对称性的限制；引入J_z^2哈密顿量可打破该对称性，与TC相互作用和J_z联合实现半通用性（semi-universality），即允许实现所有满足置换对称性和U(1)对称性的任意酉算符（中心部分存在约束）。

Conclusion: 全局控制下量子比特-玻色子系统的可控性受偶然对称性约束；通过额外控制项J_z^2可提升操控能力至半通用水平；该偶然对称性可通过Schwinger玻色子角动量模型进一步理解。

Abstract: We study the controllability of a system of qubits under global control, where control pulses act identically on all qubits. Specifically, we consider a collection of qubits identically coupled to a single bosonic mode, or harmonic oscillator, via the Jaynes-Cummings interaction. This collective coupling, known as the Tavis-Cummings (TC) interaction, has been realized in several quantum computing platforms, including superconducting and atomic qubit systems. Although the qubits do not interact directly with one another, they can become entangled through their common coupling to the bosonic mode. We characterize the group of unitaries that can be implemented on the joint Hilbert space of the qubits and bosonic mode using the TC interaction together with a global $z$ field $J_z$, corresponding to identical z rotations on all qubits. We show that for n>2 qubits the set of realizable unitaries is restricted by an "accidental" symmetry of the TC Hamiltonian, distinct from its "standard" U(1) and permutational symmetries. On the other hand, we find that the Hamiltonian $J_z^2$ breaks this accidental symmetry and, together with the TC interaction and $J_z$, achieves semi-universality: it allows the implementation of arbitrary unitaries that respect permutational and U(1) symmetry, up to certain constraints on the center of the group. In a companion paper, we further analyze this remarkable accidental symmetry and show that it can be understood through Schwinger's bosonic model of angular momentum.

</details>


### [6] [Kubo-Martin-Schwinger conditions for non-Hermitian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13251)
*Chen Lan,Luyao Ma,Hao Yang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过三条互补路径将Kubo-Martin-Schwinger (KMS)热平衡条件推广至具有实谱和双正交本征系统的非厄米哈密顿量，核心结果是给出准厄米性（quasi-Hermiticity）的热力学刻画：双正交Gibbs泛函对所有算符满足非负性当且仅当哈密顿量是准厄米的。进一步证明在准厄米条件下，η-Gibbs态满足全部三条解析KMS条件，并分析了在例外点（exceptional points）和复谱情形下的失效模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将KMS热平衡条件从标准厄米量子系统拓展至非厄米哈密顿量系统，探索在实谱和双正交本征系统框架下热力学平衡的严格刻画，并厘清准厄米性在其中的核心角色。

Method: 采用三条互补分析路径：(1) 利用Riesz表示定理直接从双正交Gibbs泛函的本征投影构造度规η，提供不依赖先验度规的准厄米性判据；(2) 运用Hadamard三线定理和Bari定理（Riesz基理论）证明η-Gibbs态满足KMS条件；(3) 通过相似变换与等谱厄米伙伴（isospectral Hermitian partner）的对比分析，揭示KMS性质不能简单从厄米理论导出。

Result: 建立了双正交Gibbs泛函的非负性（对任意算符A满足ω_bi(A†A)≥0）与哈密顿量准厄米性之间的等价关系；证明了在准厄米假设下η-Gibbs态满足全部三条解析KMS条件；发现当度规η与等谱厄米伙伴h不对易时，传输态与标准Gibbs态不同，因此KMS性质无法通过相似变换从厄米理论继承。

Conclusion: 给出了非厄米系统中热平衡态的结构性刻画，明确了准厄米性在KMS条件成立中的充分必要性，同时指出了与完整Haag-Hugenholtz-Winnink C*-代数框架之间的差距，并分析了例外点和复谱情形下的失效机制以及与Fagnola-Umanità量子细致平衡条件的关联。

Abstract: We investigate the extension of the Kubo--Martin--Schwinger (KMS) thermal equilibrium condition to non-Hermitian Hamiltonians with real spectra and biorthogonal eigensystems, providing a systematic analysis through three complementary routes. Our central result is a thermodynamic characterisation of quasi-Hermiticity: for $H \in M_d(\mathbb{C})$ diagonalisable with real spectrum, the biorthogonal Gibbs functional $ω_{\rm{bi}}(A) = Z_{\rm{bi}}^{-1} \sum_n e^{-βE_n}\langleφ_n|A|ψ_n\rangle$ satisfies $ω_{\rm{bi}}(A^†A) \geq 0$ for all $A$ if and only if $H$ is quasi-Hermitian. The proof constructs the metric $η$ directly from the eigenprojectors of $ω_{\rm{bi}}$ via the Riesz representation theorem, with no prior choice of $η$, providing a metric-free certificate of quasi-Hermiticity outside the Mostafazadeh--Scholtz framework. Under the full quasi-Hermitian hypothesis, we prove that the $η$-Gibbs state $ω_η(A) = Z_η^{-1}\, \rm{Tr}[ηe^{-βH}A]$ satisfies all three analytic KMS conditions, using the Hadamard three-line theorem and Bari's theorem on Riesz bases. The result is non-trivial: the transported state $\hatω(X) = \rm{Tr}[e^{-βh}Xη]/Z_η$ differs from the Gibbs state of the isospectral Hermitian partner $h = η^{1/2}Hη^{-1/2}$ whenever $[η,h]\neq 0$, so the KMS property cannot be deduced from the Hermitian theory by similarity. The gap between this result and the full Haag--Hugenholtz--Winnink $C^*$-algebraic framework is identified. Failure modes at exceptional points and for complex spectra are analysed, and the relation to the Fagnola--Umanità quantum detailed balance condition for open systems is discussed.

</details>


### [7] [Effective Geometry and Position-Dependent Mass in Dual-$q$ Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12444)
*A. Boumali,A. Makhlouf*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 研究表明，Borges 变形导数形式体系（deformed-derivative formalism）中引入非线性对偶导数会导致非线性薛定谔方程，但通过坐标和波函数的同步变换可将其转化为普通线性薛定谔方程，等价于一个厄米的位置依赖质量（position-dependent-mass, PDM）哈密顿量。变形参数 q 决定了有效质量分布和关联度规，q<1 时有效约束长度减小、能谱升高并增强隧穿；q>1 时反之。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示 Borges 变形导数形式体系中线性算子 D_(q) 与其非线性对偶算子 D^(q) 之间的关系，并解决将对偶导数直接引入动能项时出现的非线性薛定谔方程问题，恢复叠加原理与概率解释的常规理解。

Method: 通过同步变换坐标和波函数，消除由对偶导数引入的非线性，将问题转化为变形坐标系下的普通线性薛定谔方程，进而等价于一个厄米的位置依赖质量哈密顿量（Hermitian PDM Hamiltonian）。

Result: 得了自由粒子、无限深方势阱、矩形势垒和谐振子在弱变形区域下的解；并与 Costa Filho 等人的非可加平移方法（nonadditive-translation approach）进行了对比，表明两种途径导向相同的有效几何结构。q<1 时有效约束长度缩短，导致束缚态能谱升高、隧穿增强；q>1 时有效长度增长，能谱降低、隧穿减弱。

Conclusion: Borges 对偶-q 框架（Borges dual-q framework）为描述有效几何结构提供了一条替代路径，变形参数 q 同时调控有效质量分布和关联度规，从而系统地影响能谱与隧穿行为。

Abstract: This work investigates the deformed-derivative formalism introduced by Borges, with emphasis on the relation between the linear operator $D_{(q)}$ and its nonlinear dual counterpart $D^{(q)}$. Directly inserting the dual derivative into the kinetic term leads to a nonlinear Schrödinger equation and obscures the usual interpretation of superposition and probability. We show that this nonlinearity can be removed by a simultaneous transformation of the coordinate and of the wave function. The transformed problem is an ordinary linear Schrödinger equation in a deformed coordinate, and its representation in the physical coordinate is equivalent to a Hermitian position-dependent-mass (PDM) Hamiltonian. In this formulation, the deformation parameter $q$ determines both the effective mass profile and the associated metric. The formalism is applied to the free particle, the infinite square well, the rectangular barrier, and the harmonic oscillator in the weak-deformation regime. Comparison with the nonadditive-translation approach of Costa Filho \emph{et al.} shows that the Borges dual-$q$ framework provides an alternative route to the same effective geometric structure. For $q<1$, the effective confinement length is reduced, which raises the bound-state spectrum and enhances tunneling; for $q>1$, the effective length is increased, which lowers the spectrum and suppresses tunneling relative to the undeformed limit $q=1$.

</details>


### [8] [Quantum Logic Codes: Complete Transversal Logical Clifford Instruction Sets for High-Rate Stabilizer Quantum Error Correcting Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13521)
*Adam Holmes*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了稳定子量子纠错码的结构与横向逻辑门能力，揭示了生成完整逻辑Clifford代数所需的电路深度普适下界，提出了旋转表面码中深度为1的横向相位门$\mathrm{\overline{S}}$与2D环面码中深度为1的块内$\mathrm{\overline{CZ}}$门等新构造，并构建了一个高速率非LDPC CSS码族（参数$[[n,\sqrt{n},Θ({n^β})]]$，$β\approx 0.2823$），该码族具备常数深度的完整2-局域横向逻辑Clifford基指令集架构（ISA），并可通过平铺（tiling）与级联（concatenation）扩展至实用规模。作者将这些码称为量子逻辑码（Quantum Logic Codes）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索稳定子量子纠错码（stabilizer quantum error correcting codes）的结构与横向逻辑能力（transversal logical capabilities），旨在识别生成完整逻辑Clifford代数（logical Clifford algebra）所需的电路深度通用下界，并构造具备恒定深度或深度为1的完整横向Clifford基指令集架构（ISA）的新型码族，以提升量子计算的容错效率与可扩展性。

Method: 通过理论分析建立生成完整逻辑Clifford代数的电路深度普适下界；针对旋转表面码（rotated surface code）构造深度为1的横向$\mathrm{\overline{S}}$门，针对2D环面码（2D-toric code）构造深度为1的块内$\mathrm{\overline{CZ}}$门，并推广至所有奇数距离与所有长度$L\ge3$；基于参数为$[[n_0, 2, d_0]]$的小码，通过平铺与级联构建高速率非LDPC CSS码族，证明该构造在组合操作下保持深度为1的完整横向Clifford基ISA。

Result: 识别了生成完整逻辑Clifford代数的电路深度普适下界；实现了旋转表面码中深度为1的横向$\mathrm{\overline{S}}$门；实现了2D环面码中深度为1的块内$\mathrm{\overline{CZ}}$门（适用于所有奇数距离及所有$L\ge3$）；构建了参数为$[[n,\sqrt{n},Θ({n^β})]]$（$β\approx 0.2823$）的高速非LDPC CSS码族，该码族具备常数深度的完整2-局域横向逻辑Clifford基ISA（包含全部可单独定址的$\mathrm{\overline{S}}$、$\mathrm{\overline{SHS}} = \sqrt{X}$和$\mathrm{\overline{CZ}}$门），特定子族可实现深度为1，且在平铺与级联扩展后仍保持深度为1至深度为2的可定址操作。

Conclusion: 本文提出的量子逻辑码（Quantum Logic Codes）通过结合小码平铺与级联的策略，实现了在实用规模下保持恒定深度乃至深度为1的完整横向逻辑Clifford基指令集架构，为容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computing）提供了一种兼具高码率与低深度逻辑门实现的可扩展编码方案。

Abstract: We study the structure and transversal logical capabilities of stabilizer quantum error correcting codes. Among our results, we identify universal lower bounds on circuit depth to generate a full logical Clifford algebra, and develop novel constructions of logical transversal gates including a new depth-one transversal phase $\mathrm{\overline{S}}$ gate in the rotated surface code and a depth-one intra-block $\mathrm{\overline{CZ}}$ gate in the 2D-toric code that generalizes to all odd distances and all lengths $L\ge3$, respectively. Finally, we construct a high-rate non-LDPC CSS code family with parameters $[[n,\sqrt{n},Θ({n^β})]]$ where $β\approx 0.2823$ in one demonstrated case, that provably possesses a constant-depth complete 2-local transversal logical Clifford basis instruction set architecture (ISA) composed of all individually targeted $\mathrm{\overline{S}}$, $\mathrm{\overline{SHS}} = \sqrt{X}$, and $\mathrm{\overline{CZ}}$ gates. This ISA is depth-one for certain subfamilies that we design and generally constant-depth under certain conditions. The code family is built from a small code with parameters $[[n_0, 2, d_0]]$, and is tunable in the standard way: it tiles out to form utility-scale logical qubit counts, and it scales up through concatenation to achieve higher distances and error suppression. We show that this construction preserves the depth-one complete transversal logical Clifford basis ISA when composed with these commuting construction actions, inheriting structure from the core codes so that at scale the complete logical Clifford basis ISA remains depth-one up to depth-two addressable operations between tiled cores. We call these Quantum Logic Codes.

### [9] [Statistical Mechanics and Symmetries of Non-Abelian Anyon Proliferation: From Deformation to Decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12527)
*Avi Vadali,Robijn Vanhove,Ruben Verresen,Jason Alicea,Pablo Sala*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过统计力学模型和蒙特卡洛模拟，研究了非阿贝尔拓扑序在波函数形变和退相干下的稳定性，发现两种非阿贝尔任意子的共同增殖会导致阿贝尔任意子寄生凝聚，从而破坏拓扑序，且最终平庸相会“记住”是哪些任意子发生了凝聚。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑量子计算依赖非阿贝尔任意子（non-Abelian anyon）的编织操作，但前提是底层拓扑序（topological order）能抵御不完美的态制备和环境噪声。然而，拓扑序在波函数形变和退相干下的不稳定性机制尚未被充分理解，因此需要发展一套统一的框架来刻画这些破坏效应。

Method: 提出一种通用框架，将拓扑序的不稳定性转化为统计力学（stat-mech）模型，利用其对称性自然地揭示导致破坏的任意子激发。以 $D_4$ 拓扑序为例，结合该框架与蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte-Carlo simulations），研究在多个非阿贝尔任意子物种增殖（proliferation）下的稳定性。

Result: 发现存在有限阈值：当两种非阿贝尔任意子物种共同增殖超过该阈值时，会寄生凝聚（parasitically condense）一个共享的阿贝尔任意子融合产物，从而破坏拓扑序。由对称性方法得到的平庸相与凝聚所有阿贝尔荷（Abelian charges）所得的平庸相不同，即该相“记住”了哪些任意子发生了凝聚。

Conclusion: 该对称性基础框架为基于症候测量（syndrome measurements）识别非阿贝尔拓扑序最优解码器所需的相关对称性提供了第一步，有助于推进拓扑量子计算的容错实现。

Abstract: Topological quantum computation relies on braiding non-Abelian anyons, but requires the underlying topological order to survive imperfect state preparation and environmental noise. We show that the instability of topological order to wavefunction deformations and to decoherence, with the latter probed by syndrome distributions, are generically captured by stat-mech models whose symmetries naturally expose the corrupting anyonic excitations. As an example, we combine this framework with Monte-Carlo simulations to resolve the stability of $D_4$ topological order under deformations and quantum channels that proliferate multiple non-Abelian anyon species that individually are unable to condense. We show that beyond a finite threshold, proliferation of two non-Abelian anyon species parasitically condenses a shared Abelian-anyon fusion outcome, destroying the topological order. Our symmetry-based approach sharply differentiates the resulting trivial phase from that obtained by condensing all Abelian charges; in other words, the trivial phase "remembers" which anyons condensed. This framework provides a first step into identifying the relevant symmetry for optimal decoders, conditioned on syndrome measurements, of non-Abelian topological order.

### [10] [Spectral analysis of equilibration: information leakage in isolated quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12545)

Main category: quant-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为孤立量子系统提供一种不依赖系综假设（ensemble assumption）或微扰论证（perturbative argument）的统一动力学-谱框架，以刻画信息流失（information flow）与记忆丧失（memory loss）的机制。

Method: 基于子空间粗粒化（subspace coarse-graining）方法；定义泄漏保真度函数（Leakage Fidelity Function, LFF）作为单位演化态离开初始子空间支撑的概率；引入谱功率分布（spectral power distribution）和关联的熵度量（entropic measures）；结合量子速度极限（quantum speed limits）分析热化时间尺度。

Result: 推导出LFF时间涨落的普适界限，该界限依赖于谱间隙结构（spectral gap structure）和有效维数平方（square of the effective dimension）；表明大谱离域性（large spectral delocalization）抑制涨落并保证平均意义上的热化；建立了相位混合（phase mixing）、间隙参与度（gap participation）与动力学稳定性之间的定量联系；揭示了热化所需的平均时间。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种依赖于初始态且几何透明的视角，阐明谱复杂性（spectral complexity）与子空间信息泄漏（subspace information leakage）如何共同支配封闭量子多体系统的不可逆性（irreversibility）。

Abstract: We develop a unified dynamical-spectral framework for equilibration in isolated quantum systems based on a subspace coarse-graining approach. Central to our formulation is the Leakage Fidelity Function (LFF), defined as the probability that a unitarily evolving state escapes the support of its initial subspace. This quantity provides a direct, operational measure of information flow and memory loss without invoking ensemble assumptions or perturbative arguments. We derive universal bounds on temporal fluctuations of the LFF, in terms of the spectral gap structure and the square of the effective dimension, evincing that large spectral delocalization suppresses fluctuations and guarantees equilibration on average. By introducing spectral power distributions and associated entropic measures, we establish a quantitative link between phase mixing, gap participation, and dynamical stability. We further investigate the equilibration timescale by connecting the LFF to quantum speed limits, thereby revealing the average time required for equilibration. Our results provide a state-dependent, geometrically transparent perspective on how spectral complexity and subspace information leakage jointly govern irreversibility in closed quantum many-body systems.

### [11] [Multiple Topological Haldane Phases for Symmetry-Protected Quantum Information Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12685)

Method: 将一个自旋-1/2梯子系统划分为多个独立的 Haldane 相（Haldane phase）子系统，利用对称保护拓扑序作为架构基础。量子比特编码在每个子系统 $S^z=0$ 扇区的两个拓扑态中。通过可控的有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）产生能级分裂，使用局域磁场实现单量子比特旋转；利用相邻子系统边缘之间的 Ising 型相互作用（Ising-type interaction）生成纠缠门。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种利用对称保护拓扑相实现可扩展、基于门的量子计算的具体方案，表明拓扑保护的边缘态和有限尺寸效应可以在真实系统中直接服务于通用量子计算。

Abstract: Symmetry-protected topological phases have attracted significant interest at the fundamental level and as a potential platform for quantum information processing, owing to their protected edge states and resilience to perturbations. Applying these features for practical and efficient quantum computation is highly desirable, but remains an open challenge. Here, we demonstrate the partitioning into multiple independent Haldane phase subsystems of a single spin-1/2 ladder system and propose this as a scalable architecture for gate-based quantum computation, which takes advantage of the symmetry-protected topological order. We encode qubits in the two topological states of the $S^{z}=0$ sector of each subsystem. Finite-size effects, typically viewed as detrimental, instead provide a controllable energy splitting that enables single-qubit rotations using only local magnetic fields. An Ising-type interaction between neighboring subsystem edges generates entangling gates, enabling universal quantum computation driven by two control parameters that are easily accessible experimentally. Our results demonstrate how symmetry-protected topological phases can be directly harnessed for circuit-model quantum computation in realistic systems.

Abstract: Ground-state preparation is a critical task in quantum simulation and quantum computing, as it enables the study of correlated phases and the generation of entangled resource states. While measurement--feedback control has emerged as a promising route to state preparation, existing schemes either rely on handcrafted, task-specific policies or are designed using full quantum-state information that is unavailable in real experiments and becomes impractical for large many-body systems. Here we develop an adaptive measurement--feedback protocol based on reinforcement learning under partial observability. The controller uses only the history of experimentally accessible measurement outcomes to choose both the measurement operator and the feedback action in real time. To make training compatible with experiments, we introduce a stochastic terminal reward built from one-shot measurements of randomly sampled Hamiltonian components, avoiding unphysical full-state reconstruction while remaining an unbiased estimator of the target energy. We demonstrate the method by preparing ground states of the Bose--Hubbard model and by generating GHZ states, establishing a scalable and hardware-compatible route to quantum state preparation.

Abstract: Ultracold atoms in multimode optical cavities provide a rich testbed for many-body phenomena enabled by light-mediated interactions. Recent experiments include realizations of spin glasses and associative memories, as described by multimode Dicke models with disordered couplings. However, the properties of multimode Dicke models with ordered coupling geometries remain largely unexplored. In this work, we investigate the stable steady-states of the multimode Dicke model with an ordered nearest-neighbor coupling geometry, where $n_c$ atomic clusters are coupled via $n_c-1$ cavity modes. ### [14] [Interference of critical dynamics associated with zero modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13200)
*Zhi-Han Zhang,Han-Chuan Kou,Peng Li*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用闭合淬火路径（closed quench paths）依次穿越两个临界点，通过读取最终零模转移概率（zero-mode transfer probability）来研究ICDZM干涉图样；运用WKB分析（WKB analysis）框架阐明干涉相位（interference phase）的积累机制；利用边界粒子数（boundary particle number）相对于初始分数值的偏差来探测零模转移概率。

Result: 发现了依赖于淬火路径的丰富ICDZM干涉图样。当闭合路径连接两个拓扑非平凡相时，ICDZM图样可能消失或出现周期加倍（period doubling）。零模转移概率既能捕获ICDZM振荡，也能捕获非闭合淬火路径中已知的反常缺陷产生（anomalous defect production）。

Abstract: We study the interference of critical dynamics associated with zero modes (ICDZM) in the generalized Creutz ladders using closed quench paths that pass through two critical points successively. By reading out the final zero-mode transfer probability, we find rich ICDZM interference patterns dependent on the quench path. In particular, when the closed path links two topologically nontrivial phases, the ICDZM pattern may either vanish or exhibit period doubling. Within the framework of WKB analysis, this phenomenon is well clarified by the interference phase accumulated in the quench procedure. We also demonstrate that the zero-mode transfer probability can be detected by the deviation of the boundary particle number from its initial fractional value, which arises from the blending of bulk modes in the critical dynamics. As an edge defect, the zero-mode transfer probability captures both the ICDZM oscillation and the known anomalous defect production in a non-closed quench path. These results identify ICDZM and the corresponding edge defect as probes for critical dynamics associated with topological zero modes.

### [15] [Steady-State Noise Signatures of Lindbladian Exceptional Points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13377)
*Shihang Pan,Gianmichele Blasi,Géraldine Haack*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在开放量子系统中，林德布拉德算符（Lindbladian）的奇异点（exceptional points, EPs）可以通过稳态下的电流噪声（current noise）被探测到，而非仅局限于瞬态可观测量。作者推导了林德布拉德主方程框架下的电流关联函数（current correlation functions）的一般表达式，并以两个相互作用量子比特与两个热库耦合的范例展示了过阻尼、欠阻尼与临界三种动力学区的噪声特征，从而将电流关联函数确立为探测林德布拉德奇异点的稳态探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异点（exceptional points, EPs）是开放量子系统中非厄米简并（non-Hermitian degeneracies）的重要特征，其此前主要在有限时间可观测量中被识别，而稳态平均电流一般无法直接反映奇异点结构。因此，需要新的稳态观测手段来揭示林德布拉德算符（Lindbladian）的奇异点特征。

Method: 基于林德布拉德主方程（Lindblad master-equation）框架，推导电流关联函数（current correlation functions）关于时间延迟的通用表达式，阐明奇异点如何影响其行为。以两个相互作用量子比特耦合到两个热库的范例模型进行数值验证。

Result: 稳态电流噪声（steady-state current noise）作为时间延迟的函数，可以清晰地区分出过阻尼（overdamped）、欠阻尼（underdamped）与临界（critical）三种动力学区域，从而揭示林德布拉德奇异点的存在。

Conclusion: 电流关联函数可以作为开放量子系统中林德布拉德奇异点（Lindbladian EPs）的稳态探针（steady-state probe），为在稳态条件下探测非厄米简并特征提供了新途径。

Abstract: Exceptional points (EPs) are non-Hermitian degeneracies at which two or more eigenvalues and their corresponding eigenvectors coalesce. In open quantum systems, exceptional points can arise in the Lindbladian governing the dissipative dynamics. Their signatures have so far been mainly identified in finite-time observables, such as transient currents, while steady-state average currents generally provide no direct evidence of the underlying exceptional-point structure. In this work, we demonstrate that signatures of Lindbladian EPs can nevertheless be accessed in the steady-state regime through current noise. We derive general expressions for current correlation functions within a Lindblad master-equation framework and show, in particular, how exceptional points affect their behaviour as a function of the time delay. We illustrate these results with the paradigmatic example of two interacting qubits coupled to two reservoirs, where the steady-state noise clearly distinguishes overdamped, underdamped, and critical regimes. Our results establish current correlation functions as a steady-state probe of Lindbladian EPs in open quantum systems.

</details>


### [16] [A refined thermodynamic analysis of nonsecular master equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13504)
*Mohamed Boubakour,Talia Szikman,Cyril Elouard*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文对非对易主方程（nonsecular master equations）进行了系统的热力学分析，构建了统一的热力学框架。研究表明，尽管系统稳态不是其裸哈密顿量的吉布斯态（Gibbs state），但通过基于系统-环境关联的微观第二定律表述和微扰理论，可以保持第二定律的正定性。系统-浴相互作用能和兰姆移位（Lamb-shift）参与能量平衡并产生功，且非对易主方程的熵产生率与基于Spohn不等式的定义存在差异，但该差异在单热浴情形下是纯粹的瞬态效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于部分对易近似（partial secular approximation）和几何-算术近似（geometric-arithmetic approximation）导出的非对易主方程，其稳态不是系统裸哈密顿量的吉布斯态，因此需要建立统一且自洽的热力学框架来处理这类非马尔可夫动力学过程的热力学一致性。

Method: 基于系统-环境关联的微观第二定律表达式，采用系统微扰理论（systematic perturbation theory）对动力学近似进行修正，以保持第二定律的正定性。同时，对比基于约化系统动力学压缩性（contractivity）的Spohn不等式定义的熵产生。

Result: 结果表明，在弱系统-浴耦合下，系统-浴相互作用能及兰姆移位参与了能量平衡，产生系统对浴的做功。与对易主方程不同，非对易主方程的两种熵产生率因稳态能量本征基下的非零相干性而存在差异；但单热浴情形下该差异是纯瞬态的，无法从非吉布斯稳态中循环提取功。

Conclusion: 本文为非对易主方程提供了统一的热力学解释，通过简单算例阐明并完善了量子马尔可夫动力学（Markovian dynamics）的热力学图像。

Abstract: We present a systematic thermodynamic analysis of nonsecular master equations. We consider master equations resulting either from the partial secular and the geometric-arithmetic approximations, two approximations ensuring the positivity of the system's dynamics when some of its transition frequencies are too small to enable the full secular approximation. Both cause the system to relax towards a steady state which is not the Gibbs state of its bare Hamiltonian. Nonetheless, we build a unified, consistent thermodynamic framework for those dynamics. Starting from a microscopic expression of the second law based on system-environment correlations, we employ a systematic perturbation theory to preserve the positivity of the second law despite the approximations done on the dynamics. We show that, in spite of the weak system-bath coupling, the system-bath interaction energy participates to the energy balance, as well as the Lamb-shift. Those extra contributions give rise to work performed by the system on the bath when the former is out of equilibrium. We compare this microscopic entropy production with the definition based on the contractivity of the reduced system dynamics (Spohn inequality). We show that, unlike for secular master equations, the two entropy production rates differ because of the presence of non-vanishing stationary coherences in the energy eigenbasis. However, in the case of a single thermal bath, the difference is purely transient, and no work can be cyclically extracted from the steady-state despite its non-Gibbs form. Finally, we illustrate our results with a simple example, clarifying and completing the thermodynamic picture of Markovian dynamics in the quantum regime.

</details>


### [17] [Diffusive Dynamics of Nonstabilizerness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13606)
*Zhenyu Xiao,Shinsei Ryu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了U(1)对称一维随机电路中非稳定化子性（nonstabilizerness）的动力学，通过稳定子Rényi熵（stabilizer Rényi entropy）测量，发现其晚期趋近随机态值的间隙以1/t的扩散普适类闭合，并在能量守恒的非可积伊辛链中验证了相同标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称性对多体系统量子信息动力学的影响已被广泛研究，但对称性如何影响非稳定化子性——一种与纠缠互补的量子资源——尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示U(1)对称性下非稳定化子性的标度行为与普适类。

Method: 计算U(1)对称一维随机电路中稳定子Rényi熵；采用四副本张量网络（four-replica tensor network）描述无序平均动力学，并通过S₄适配的无限时间演化块消减（$S_4$-adapted infinite time-evolving block decimation, iTEBD）直接在热力学极限下求解；辅以流体动力学论证（hydrodynamic argument）分析晚期行为。

Result: 非稳定化子性在晚期趋近随机态值时，稳定子Rényi熵的间隙以1/t的速率闭合，对应扩散普适类（diffusive universality class）。该标度同样在能量守恒的非可积伊辛链中得到验证。

Conclusion: 本文为理解非稳定化子性的产生提供了流体动力学视角，并对哈密顿动力学中近似Haar随机态的设计提供了理论洞见。

Abstract: Symmetries shape the quantum-information dynamics of many-body systems, but their effect on nonstabilizerness, the resource complementary to entanglement, is less understood. We compute the stabilizer Rényi entropy, a measure of nonstabilizerness, in $\mathrm{U}(1)$-symmetric one-dimensional random circuits. The disorder-averaged dynamics is captured by a four-replica tensor network, which we evaluate by $S_4$-adapted infinite time-evolving block decimation (iTEBD) directly in the thermodynamic limit. Together with a hydrodynamic argument, our results identify a diffusive universality class for the late-time approach of nonstabilizerness to its random-state value, with the stabilizer Rényi entropy gap closing as $1/t$. The same scaling is verified in an energy-conserving nonintegrable Ising chain. More broadly, our framework provides a hydrodynamic perspective on nonstabilizerness generation and offers insight into the design of approximate Haar-random states in Hamiltonian dynamics.

</details>

### [18] [Rank recursion for $q$-Whittaker and Macdonald operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12796)
*Philippe Di Francesco,Hieu Trung Vu*

Result: 成功证明了 $q$-Whittaker 和 Macdonald 算子的秩递推关系，获得了 $q$-Whittaker 算子 $k$ 次幂的显式表达式，以及 Macdonald 算子秩递推关系的柯西行列式形式。

Conclusion: 本文建立的秩递推关系及其显式表达式，为 $q$-Whittaker 和 Macdonald 算子的进一步研究提供了新的代数工具。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce and prove a set of rank recurrence relations for $q$-Whittaker and Macdonald operators. ### [19] [Adjusted Cup-Product Neural Layer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13568)
*Snigdha Chandan Khilar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种调整杯积神经层（adjusted cup product neural layer），将杯积（cup product）与高阶规范理论（higher gauge theory）中的调整项硬编码为神经原语（neural primitive），实现了设计上的规范不变性（gauge invariance）。主要理论结果表明，在闭合循环（closed cycle）上，输出完全取决于调整系数，该系数是规范不变信号的唯一来源，且该可观测量为非零二次型（nonzero quadratic form），在单重和双重规范变换下严格不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理学和几何学中的许多重要可观测物理量（observables）都是上链的杯积（cup products of cochains），因此需要一种能够直接嵌入杯积运算并确保规范不变性（gauge invariance）的神经网络结构。

Method: 引入调整杯积神经层（adjusted cup product neural layer），将杯积与来自高阶规范理论（higher gauge theory）的调整项（adjustment term）硬编码为神经原语（neural primitive），使输出天然具备规范不变性。

Result: 在闭合循环（closed cycle）上，输出完全取决于调整系数（adjustment coefficient）；调整系数为零时，输出完全消失，表明调整是规范不变信号（gauge invariant signal）的唯一来源。该可观测量是一个非零二次型（nonzero quadratic form）。

Conclusion: 该可观测量的非零二次型在单重和双重规范变换（one and two gauge transformations）下严格不变，证明了调整杯积神经层在理论上的规范不变性保证。

Abstract: Many important observables in physics and geometry are cup products of cochains. The adjusted cup product neural layer has been introduced in this paper. It is a neural primitive that hard wires the cup product with an adjustment term from higher gauge theory. This creates a readout that is gauge invariant by design. Their main theoretical result shows that on a closed cycle the output relies entirely on the adjustment coefficient. Setting this coefficient to zero removes the output completely regardless of other parameters. Thus the adjustment is the only source of gauge invariant signal. They prove this observable is a nonzero quadratic form and is exactly invariant under one and two gauge transformations.

</details>


### [20] [Boltzmann Attention: Learnable Ising Couplings for Cooperative Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12478)
*Gilhan Kim,Daniel K. Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出玻尔兹曼注意力（Boltzmann attention），将注意力机制推广为基于相互作用的伊辛模型（Ising model），通过学习可调配对耦合（pairwise couplings）来显式建模注意力决策之间的协同或拮抗关系，在字符级语言建模和括号匹配任务上优于标准 softmax 注意力，并展示了量子退火（quantum annealing）作为可行训练策略的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准注意力机制仅通过逐查询-键相似度（query-key similarity）和 softmax 归一化引入位置间的间接竞争，未能显式参数化注意力决策之间可学习的相互作用，限制了模型直接建模协同或拮抗式共注意力结构（co-attention structure）的能力。

Method: 提出玻尔兹曼注意力（Boltzmann attention），将注意力模式建模为能量基模型（energy-based model），具体采用相互作用的伊辛模型（Ising model）。该方法在通常的数据依赖局部场（data-dependent local fields）基础上增加可学习的配对耦合项，从而显式捕获位置间的相关性，超越 softmax 或 sigmoid 注意力的表达能力。

Result: 在字符级语言建模和合成括号匹配任务中，采用标准 Transformer 架构时，玻尔兹曼注意力始终优于标准 softmax 注意力，且优势随序列长度增加而更加显著。四路消融实验（four-way ablation）确认改进主要来源于可学习的配对耦合。

Conclusion: 显式的位置间相互作用为基于注意力的序列建模提供了一种有理论依据的增强方案。伊辛模型公式化为基于量子计算的采样策略开辟了自然路径：非绝热量子退火（diabatic quantum annealing）可作为实用的训练方法，在保持与精确玻尔兹曼计算相当的性能的同时提供替代实现。

Abstract: Attention mechanisms are central to modern sequence models, yet standard attention computes relevance primarily through individual query--key similarities. Although softmax normalization introduces competition among positions, a standard attention layer does not explicitly parameterize learnable interactions between attention decisions. This limits its ability to directly model cooperative or antagonistic co-attention structure within the attention mechanism itself. We propose Boltzmann attention, an energy-based generalization in which attention patterns are governed by an interacting Ising model. The method augments the usual data-dependent local fields with learnable pairwise couplings, allowing the model to represent inter-position correlations beyond those captured by softmax or sigmoid attention. Experiments on character-level language modeling and synthetic bracket matching show that Boltzmann attention consistently improves over standard softmax attention within a standard Transformer architecture, with the advantage becoming more pronounced as sequence length increases. A four-way ablation confirms that the improvement arises from the learnable pairwise couplings. These results suggest that explicit inter-position interactions provide a principled enhancement for attention-based sequence modeling. Moreover, the Ising formulation opens a natural path toward quantum-computing-based sampling strategies: we demonstrate that diabatic quantum annealing provides a practical training method while maintaining competitive performance with exact Boltzmann computation.

</details>

### [22] [Optical Implementation of Equilibrium Propagation Using Spatial Photonic Ising Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13454)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用混合光-数字架构实现平衡传播（Equilibrium Propagation, EP），其中核心硬件为空间光子伊辛机（SPIM）。该方法利用规范变换（gauge transformation）技术，通过空间光调制器（spatial light modulator）以相位调制方式光学编码连续的神经元状态（continuous neuron states）和秩1二值可训练模式（rank-1 binary trainable patterns）；推理过程采用有限差分格式（finite difference scheme）完成。

Abstract: Equilibrium Propagation offers a compelling alternative to traditional machine learning for training energy-based networks. Here we demonstrate a hybrid optical-digital implementation of EP using a Spatial Photonic Ising Machine (SPIM). The SPIM exploits the gauge transformation method to optically encode both continuous neuron states and rank-1 binary trainable patterns as phase modulations via a spatial light modulator, with inference realized using a finite difference scheme. The experimental system is evaluated on the Wine classification dataset. The potential of this approach, including the use of continuous couplings and structured coupling matrices, is evaluated numerically on the more complex MNIST dataset. ### [23] [Temporal glide symmetry enforces a parity sideband selection rule in scalar bulk media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13609)
*Miguel Camacho*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文发现时间滑移对称性（temporal glide symmetry）在时空调制波导中施加了一种精确的选择规则，将频率转换与横模奇偶性（transverse parity）联系起来，实现了模式与频率之间的受控能量转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间滑移对称性（temporal glide symmetry）——一种结合反射与半周期时间平移的时空对称性——在光子模式耦合与频率转换中的新物理机制，以补充已有的空间滑移对称性（spatial glide symmetry）研究。

Method: 采用标量时间调制三层波导（scalar time-modulated trilayer waveguide）模型，通过Floquet本征态分析和有限截面时域仿真，检验时间滑移对称性对模式奇偶性与边带（sideband）指数之间的选择规则。

Result: 时间滑移对称性施加了严格选择规则：每个Floquet本征态的宇称含量（parity content）随边带指数交替变化；散射中，定宇称模式在奇边带只能发射到相反横宇称模式，在偶边带则只能发射到相同横宇称模式。仿真验证了该规则，奇数波导模式转换为偶数频率边带，所有对称性禁止的输出通道数值上可忽略。

Conclusion: 时间滑移对称性并非空间滑移能带粘附（band sticking）的时间类比，而是一种独特的对称原理，用于在选定模式与频率之间转换电磁能量。

Abstract: Symmetry is a powerful way to control coupling between photonic mode families. In spatially periodic structures, glide symmetry can protect band contacts and suppress stop bands. Here we show a different role for temporal glide, a spatiotemporal counterpart combining reflection with a half-period time translation. In a scalar time-modulated trilayer waveguide, temporal glide imposes an exact selection rule linking frequency conversion to transverse-mode symmetry: the parity content of every Floquet eigenstate alternates with sideband index, up to a state-dependent sign. In scattering, this means that a mode of definite parity can emit only into the opposite transverse parity at odd sidebands and into the same parity at even sidebands. We verify the rule directly in bulk Floquet eigenstates and in finite-section time-domain simulations. An incident odd waveguide mode is converted into an even frequency sideband, while all symmetry-forbidden output channels at the analysed sidebands are suppressed to numerically negligible values. Rather than acting as a temporal copy of spatial-glide band sticking, temporal glide provides a distinct symmetry principle for converting electromagnetic energy between selected modes and frequencies.

</details>


### [24] [Electric-Field Mapping of Optically Perturbed CdTe Radiation Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13622)
*Adriano Cola,Lorenzo Dominici,Antonio Valletta*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文利用Pockels效应在Schottky CdTe探测器中实现了二维电场分布的实验测量，并结合数值模拟验证了一个基于单一深能级的二能级模型，该模型能够完整解释辐射诱导下的电场时空动力学及其导致的极化效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 辐射探测器中电场（electric field）的空间分布对其正常运行至关重要，而入射辐射引发的内部空间电荷（space charge）积累等扰动效应会严重破坏探测器性能。因此，获取电场分布并理解其受辐射扰动后的动态变化机制，具有重要的战略意义。

Method: 采用基于Pockels效应（Pockels effect）的电光成像装置，结合自定义数据处理流程，对Schottky CdTe探测器在施加偏压-光暴露序列过程中的二维电场矢量图（electric-field vector maps）及其动力学进行提取。

Result: 实验测量的电场分布与数值模拟（numerical simulations）结果一致，验证了一个基于单一深能级的二能级模型（two-level model）。该模型能够完全解释受扰动电场的时空动力学特征。

Conclusion: 该实验与建模方法深化了对CdTe Schottky探测器中非平衡电场分布主要机制（如极化polarization）的理解，未来可用于预测和优化平面或电极分段探测器的性能。

Abstract: In radiation detectors, the spatial distribution of the electric field plays a fundamental role in their operation. Access to this field distribution is of strategic importance, especially when investigating the perturbing effects induced by incident radiation. For example, one dangerous effect that prevents their proper operation is the accumulation of internal space charge. Here, we probe the two-dimensional electric field in a Schottky CdTe detector using the Pockels effect and report on its local perturbation after exposure to an optical beam at the anode electrode. Our electro-optical imaging setup, together with a custom processing routine, allows the extraction of the electric-field vector maps and their dynamics during a voltage bias-optical exposure sequence. The results are in agreement with numerical simulations, allowing us to confirm a two-level model based on a dominant deep level. Such a simple model is indeed able to fully account for both the temporal and spatial dynamics of the perturbed electric field. This approach thus allows a deeper understanding of the main mechanisms affecting the non-equilibrium electric-field distribution in CdTe Schottky detectors, such as those leading to polarization. In the future, it could also be used to predict and improve the performance of planar or electrode-segmented detectors.

</details>

### [25] [Spontaneous symmetry breaking under Bose--Einstein condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12606)

Method: 本文以简要综述（brief survey）的形式，聚焦于玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚条件、博戈留波夫准平均方法（Bogolubov method of quasiaverages）、自发规范对称性破缺、遍历分解、非热力学粒子涨落与巨正则灾难之间的关系，以及系统稳定性要求等核心要点进行辨析。

Result: 文章澄清了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚条件与自发规范对称性破缺、遍历分解之间的逻辑关联，否定了导致所谓“巨正则灾难”的非热力学粒子涨落的存在，并明确了系统稳定性所必须满足的条件。

Conclusion: 该综述旨在厘清玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚相关理论中的主要混淆点，为准确理解自发对称性破缺、遍历分解及粒子涨落等概念提供清晰的逻辑框架。

Abstract: Due to high current interest to Bose-Einstein condensation, the related topics, such as spontaneous gauge symmetry breaking, ergodic decomposition, and particle fluctuations, are intensively discussed in literature. These discussions, unfortunately, involve quite a number of controversies and confusions. The goal of the present brief survey is to clarify some of these confusions, concentrating on the principal points, such as the relationship between the conditions of Bose-Einstein condensation, the Bogolubov method of quasiaverages, spontaneous gauge symmetry breaking, ergodic decomposition, the presumed existence of nonthermodynamic particle fluctuations leading to the so-called ``grand canonical catastrophe", and the requirements for system stability.

### [26] [Continuum Neural Momentum Eigenstate for Variationally Solving Quasiparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12928)
*David D. Dai,Marin Soljačić*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文设计了首个用于连续粒子的神经量子态架构EVE，使其对任意允许动量k都能精确成为总动量本征态（本征值k），从而支持使用现成变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）方法求解不同动量扇区的基态。在二维1/r相互作用玻色子系统上的测试表明，单一统一ansatz能描述超流、旋子（roton）、晶体和声子四种不同物态，并可通过色散形状和密度-密度关联函数识别物相及激发结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经量子态方法主要关注总动量零扇区的基态，缺乏能够系统研究整个动量空间中激发态和物相结构的方法。本文致力于设计一种架构，使其输出态天然是总动量算符的本征态，从而允许变分蒙特卡洛直接对有确定动量k的扇区进行求解。

Method: 论文提出了名为EVE（未在摘要中展开全称）的神经网络架构，该架构通过对任意选择的允许动量k构造使得输出态精确成为总动量本征值为k的本征态。结合现成的变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）方法，对二维具有互作用1/r的玻色子系统进行数值模拟。

Result: 在二维1/r相互作用玻色子系统中，单一统一ansatz同时描述了超流、旋子、晶体和声子四种物态。在r_s=20.0时观测到有限k处的旋子极小值（roton minimum），指示超流相；在r_s=100.0时观察到显著的能带折叠（zone folding）现象，周期间距极小值形成浮晶（floating crystals），其间由声子弧（phonon arcs）连接。通过密度-密度关联函数确认了物相诊断并探测了激发关联结构。进一步分析旋子的相位纹理时，发现多个涡旋偶极子合并形成的多粒子相位弦（multi-particle phase strings）。

Conclusion: EVE架构成功将神经量子态方法拓展到连续粒子系统的有限动量激发，为利用变分蒙特卡洛系统研究动量扇区物理提供了有效工具。其在不同密度下准确捕捉超流、旋子、晶体和声子等多种物相的能力，以及揭示的旋子相位弦等新结构，展示了神经量子态在强关联连续系统研究中的潜力。

Abstract: We design the first neural quantum state for continuum particles that, for any chosen allowed momentum $\mathbf{k}$, is by construction an exact eigenstate of total momentum with eigenvalue $\mathbf{k}$. Our architecture, EVE, enables off-the-shelf VMC to solve for momentum-sector ground states. We test EVE on 2D bosons with mutual $1/r$ interactions, finding that a single unified ansatz is capable of describing four qualitatively different states: superfluid, roton, crystal, and phonon. At different densities, we extract the underlying phase of matter from the dispersion's shape. At $r_s = 20.0$, we see the roton minimum at finite $k$ expected of a superfluid. At $r_s = 100.0$, we see striking zone folding indicative of crystalline order, with periodically spaced minima representing floating crystals connected by phonon arcs in between. Using density-density correlation functions, we confirm the phase diagnoses and probe the excitations' correlation structures. Finally, we analyze the roton's phase texture and find unexpected multi-particle phase strings, formed when several vortex dipoles merge, leaving two vortices connected by a phase slip.

</details>


### [27] [Quasi-2D trapped tilted dipoles at zero and finite temperatures in the strongly dipolar regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13502)
*Juan Sánchez-Baena*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文基于Bogoliubov理论，系统研究了强轴向约束下全极化偶极子（dipolar）体系的零温和有限温物理特性，包括偶极子倾斜角、粒子数、散射长度和盒状陷阱纵横比的影响，发现特定构型下温度升高会显著促进空间调制（spatial modulation），与先前三维蒙特卡洛结果定性一致，并对准二维强偶极区域的零温物理解释和温度计应用具有参考价值。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在保持总粒子数不变的特定构型下，温度升高会显著促进空间调制(spatial modulation)的出现；盒状陷阱的纵横比影响体系的液体特性及其结构；该结果与先前三维几何中的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）结果定性一致。

Conclusion: 研究有助于理解准二维极限和强偶极区被困偶极系统的零温物理，同时可在实验相关条件下评估温度对平衡态性质的影响，为温度计(thermometry)应用提供参考。

Abstract: Motivated by the recent experimental observation of dipolar supersolid stripes in a quasi two-dimensional geometry [arXiv:2512.13280 (2025)], we study a trapped system of fully polarized dipoles in a strongly axially confined geometry, both at zero and finite temperatures, by means of Bogoliubov theory. The dipoles are strongly harmonically trapped along the z axis and subjected to a box trap in the x-y plane. We characterize the physics of the trapped system at zero and finite temperatures as a function of the tilting angle of the dipoles, the number of particles and the scattering length, restricting ourselves to the experimentally relevant regime of large condensate fractions. We also illustrate the influence of the aspect ratio of the box trap in the liquid character of the system and its structure. We observe a remarkable promotion of spatial modulations when temperature is increased while keeping the total particle number constant for specific configurations, in qualitative agreement with previous Monte Carlo results in a 3D geometry. Our results are useful to understand the zero temperature physics of the trapped dipolar system in the quasi-2D limit and in the strongly dipolar regime. In addition, they allow to assess the effect of temperature in its equilibrium properties in experimentally relevant conditions, which may be useful for thermometry applications.

### [28] [Driven dynamics of an attractive Bose polaron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13645)
*Saptarshi Majumdar,Aleksandra Petković*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维均匀弱相互作用玻色子体系中，受恒定外力驱动的杂质在无晶格条件下呈现漂移布洛赫振荡（drifted Bloch oscillations）的非平衡动力学，并重点分析了吸引性杂质-玻色子相互作用下的漂移速度、振荡振幅与周期等关键行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在无晶格（lattice）背景的一维玻色系统中，杂质受恒定外力驱动时的非平衡动力学（out-of-equilibrium dynamics），特别是布洛赫振荡（Bloch oscillations）是否能在无周期势条件下出现，以及吸引性杂质-玻色子相互作用（attractive impurity-boson interaction）如何影响系统的输运响应。

Method: 通过分析一维均匀弱相互作用玻色子（homogeneous weakly-interacting bosons）体系中的杂质动力学，研究杂质在恒定外力驱动下的运动；表征宿主玻色子（host bosons）的动态响应，并揭示布洛赫振荡（Bloch oscillations）产生的微观机制。

Result: 在无晶格条件下，杂质在宽泛的外力范围内表现出漂移布洛赫振荡。与排斥性杂质-玻色子相互作用不同，吸引性相互作用下漂移速度（drift velocity）对小外力呈现亚线性依赖关系 $V_d \sim F^\alpha$，其中指数 $\alpha<1$。漂移速度随外力单调增加，但标度行为在不同力区间差异显著。振荡振幅先随外力衰减，达到最小值后回升，呈现复活（revival）现象。

Conclusion: 杂质在无晶格的一维玻色系统中仍可出现布洛赫振荡，且吸引性杂质-玻色子相互作用下的输运行为与排斥情形存在本质区别，这为理解周期性驱动和非平衡多体系统的动力学提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study the out-of-equilibrium dynamics of an impurity driven by a constant external force through a system of homogeneous weakly-interacting bosons in one spatial dimension. The impurity-boson interaction is assumed to be attractive. We show that the impurity exhibits drifted Bloch oscillations in a wide range of forces in the absence of a lattice. We characterize the dynamical response of the host bosons and explain the mechanism underlying the Bloch oscillations. We analyse the behavior of the drift velocity, the Bloch amplitude and the time period of oscillations in a wide range of forces and other system parameters. In contrast to the case of repulsive impurity-boson interaction, the drift velocity exhibits a sub-linear dependence on a weak applied force, $V_d\sim {F}^α$ with a positive exponent $α$ smaller than unity. The drift velocity monotonically increases with force, though the scaling behavior varies considerably across different regimes of $F$. Moreover, the amplitude of the velocity oscillations displays rich behavior: it first undergoes a decay with force, reaches a minimum, and then presents a revival, increasing with force.

### [29] [Influence-solvability: a systematic theory of $(1+1)D$ solvability and its application to brickwork circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12538)
*Friedrich Hübner,Sun Woo P. Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“影响可解电路”（influence-solvable circuits）的概念，发展了一套系统理论来分类和理解经典与量子系统中可解电路（solvable circuits）的一般性质，该理论将影响矩阵表示为具有有限键维数（bond-dimension）的均匀矩阵乘积态（MPS），并给出了局部充要条件；通过系统分类，发现了未被已有可解性条件捕捉的新可解电路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管诸如对偶酉门（dual unitaries）及其推广等“可解电路”已成为经典与量子系统中可处理的混沌非平衡动力学（tractable chaotic non-equilibrium dynamics）的范例，但学界缺乏一套能够系统分类和理解可解电路一般特征的理论。

Method: 本文提出了影响可解电路的概念，利用开放边界条件下矩阵乘积态基本定理（fundamental theorem of MPS）的版本，推导出了一组局部的充要条件（necessary and sufficient local conditions）。

Result: 将理论应用于砖墙电路（brickwork circuits），完成了影响可解性为χ=1时经典砖墙电路（局域维度d≤3）与量子砖墙电路（d=2）的系统分类，发现了未被已知可解性条件涵盖的新可解电路。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个统一的系统框架来分类可解电路，其蕴含了所有已知的可解电路例子，并通过分类发现了新的可解电路。

Abstract: `Solvable' circuits, such as dual unitaries and its generalisations, have arisen as paradigmatic examples of tractable chaotic non-equilibrium dynamics, both in classical and quantum systems. However, while increasingly more complicated sufficient conditions have been proposed, a systematic theory classifying and understanding general features of solvable circuits is missing. We develop such a theory by introducing influence-solvable circuits, a class of $(1+1)D$ circuits whose influence matrix, which represents the `bath' generated by its own evolution, is given by a uniform MPS with finite bond-dimension $χ$. This property allows for efficient computation of subsystem dynamics and essentially contains all known examples of solvable circuits. We derive a set of necessary and sufficient local conditions by using a version of the fundamental theorem of MPS for open boundary conditions. Next we apply our theory to brickwork circuits with $χ=1$ influence-solvability and perform a systematic classification of classical brickwork circuits with local dimension up to $d=3$ and quantum brickwork circuits with $d=2$. Our search reveals new solvable circuits that are not captured by known solvability conditions.

### [30] [The formation of magnetic reentrancy in the Ising model on a decorated square lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12572)
*A. V. Zarubin,F. A. Kassan-Ogly*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于具有任意数量自旋修饰的装饰正方晶格（decorated square lattice）上 Ising 模型的精确解，证明了在竞争交换相互作用（competing exchange interactions）区域中描述多重磁相变（磁重入现象）的基本可行性，并给出了产生一重、三重乃至五重磁相变的参数条件。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在竞争交换相互作用条件下，Ising 模型是否能够描述多重磁相变（magnetic phase transitions）及磁重入现象（magnetic reentrancy），并建立其发生的条件。

Method: 采用装饰正方晶格上具有任意数量装饰自旋（decorating spins）的 Ising 模型的精确解（exact solution）进行分析，并提出了用于确定临界温度（critical temperatures）的独特方法。

Result: 确定了模型参数关系，证实该系统可产生一重、三重甚至五重磁相变；通过复杂的磁相图（magnetic phase diagram）验证了该结论；所提出的临界温度方法能够精确确定相变次数及温度值，包括极低温度下的情形。

Conclusion: 在竞争交换相互作用框架下，该装饰 Ising 模型能从根本上描述多重磁相变现象，且所提出的临界温度方法具有高精度与广泛适用性。

Abstract: In our work, based on an exact solution of the Ising model on a decorated square lattice with an arbitrary number of decorating spins, we have demonstrated the fundamental possibility of describing the phenomenon of multiple magnetic phase transitions (magnetic reentrancy) in the regime of competing exchange interactions. We analyzed the magnetic behavior of the system and established the conditions for the occurrence of magnetic reentrancy. We have determined the relationships of the model parameter under which the formation of one, three, and even five magnetic phase transitions is possible, which is confirmed by a complicated magnetic phase diagram. We have also proposed a unique method for finding critical temperatures that allows for the precise determination of their number and values, including those at extremely low temperatures.

### [31] [When proofreading improves both speed and accuracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12795)
*Arup Biswas,L. Mahadevan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过非马尔可夫更新框架（non-Markovian renewal framework）证明，在存在长寿命停滞态（long-lived stalled states）的随机过程中，校对（proofreading）可以同时提升速度与准确性，从而逆转传统的速度-精度权衡。研究给出了任意停滞时间分布下错误率与完成时间的精确表达式，并指出停滞时间涨落（而非均值）决定了这一反转是否发生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为校对通过牺牲速度换取精度。本文试图探索在具有长寿命停滞态的随机过程中，这一权衡是否可以被逆转，即校对能否同时提升速度与准确性。

Method: 采用非马尔可夫更新框架（non-Markovian renewal framework），推导了校对机制下任意停滞时间分布（stall-time distributions）的错误率与完成时间的精确解析表达式。

Result: 发现停滞持续时间（stall durations）的涨落（而非均值）决定了校对能否同时提升速度与精度。在强停滞极限下，当停滞时间的变异系数（coefficient of variation）超过由内在错误率（intrinsic error rate）设定的阈值时，该反转机制出现。

Conclusion: 本研究为自组装、聚合物复制、免疫识别及其他非平衡信息处理系统中的校对机制提供了通用的判定准则。

Abstract: Proofreading is generally thought to improve accuracy at the expense of speed. We show that this trade-off can be reversed in stochastic processes with long-lived stalled states. Using a non-Markovian renewal framework, we derive exact expressions for the error rate and completion time under proofreading for arbitrary stall-time distributions. Our analysis reveals that fluctuations in stall durations, rather than their mean alone, determine whether proofreading can simultaneously increase speed and accuracy. In the limit of strong stalling, this regime emerges when the coefficient of variation of the stall time exceeds a threshold set by the intrinsic error rate. These results provide a general criterion for proofreading in systems ranging from self-assembly and polymer replication to immune recognition and other nonequilibrium information-processing systems.

</details>


### [32] [Population dynamics of surface-mediated autocatalytic processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13498)
*Denis S. Grebenkov,Yilin Ye*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了表面介导的自催化过程（surface-mediated autocatalytic processes）中粒子在复杂环境里扩散、被表面区域杀死或复制所导致的种群随机演化，通过生成函数（generating function）系统分析了种群大小的分布、均值、方差和高阶矩，利用非线性积分方程（nonlinear integral equations）和具有非线性边界条件的偏微分方程（partial differential equations）描述了这些量，并在种群均值消失、达到稳态或指数增长三种情形下考察了长期行为，数值求解和蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）验证了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解表面介导的自催化过程中扩散、杀死和复制等相反机制相互竞争所导致的种群随机演化行为，为这类复杂环境下的种群动力学提供系统的理论分析框架。

Method: 通过生成函数（generating function）对种群大小进行系统分析，推导其分布、均值、方差和高阶矩；采用非线性积分方程（nonlinear integral equations）和具有非线性边界条件的偏微分方程（partial differential equations with nonlinear boundary conditions）对这些量进行等价描述；数值求解相关积分方程，并辅以独立的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）验证理论结果。

Result: 识别出种群动力学的三种长期行为模式：平均种群大小消失、达到稳态水平或呈指数增长。数值求解和蒙特卡洛模拟的结果支持了理论预测。

Conclusion: 所提供的生成函数分析及非线性积分/偏微分方程描述框架能够有效刻画表面介导自催化过程的种群随机演化，且理论预测与数值模拟一致。

Abstract: We investigate the population dynamics of surface-mediated autocatalytic processes, in which particles diffuse in a complex environment towards surface regions where they can be either killed or replicated. These opposite mechanisms compete with each other and lead to a sophisticated stochastic evolution of the population size. We provide a systematic analysis of the generating function of the population size. We also deduce its distribution, mean, variance and higher-order moments. For this purpose, we employ several equivalent descriptions of these quantities in terms of nonlinear integral equations and partial differential equations with nonlinear boundary conditions. We inspect the long-time behavior of the population dynamics in three regimes when the mean population size vanishes, reaches a steady-state level, or grows exponentially. A numerical solution of the underlying integral equations and independent Monte Carlo simulations support our theoretical predictions.

</details>

### [33] [Lattice chiral non-Abelian gauge symmetry via bosonization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12358)
*Soma Onoda*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文基于非阿贝尔玻色化（non-Abelian bosonization），提出了一种二维非阿贝尔手征规范理论（chiral gauge theory）的格点（lattice）正则化方案。该方案通过在有限格距（finite lattice spacing）下构造带有三维体扩展（three-dimensional bulk extension）的规范华氏-祖米诺-维滕模型（gauged Wess–Zumino–Witten model），实现了反常自由条件（anomaly-free condition）下左右体贡献的指数相消，从而在格点上再现了连续理论中反常消除（anomaly cancellation）的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征规范理论的格点正则化面临一个核心困难：如何使连续理论中的反常消除机制（anomaly cancellation mechanism）在有限格距下得以实现。本文旨在基于非阿贝尔玻色化描述，为二维非阿贝尔手征规范理论构建一种格点表述，使得反常消除能够在晶格尺度上发生。

Method: 利用非阿贝尔玻色化，将手征费米子（chiral fermions）的规范反常（gauge anomaly）映射为连续理论中规范华氏-祖米诺-维滕模型内来自三维陈-西蒙斯型体贡献（three-dimensional Chern–Simons-type bulk contribution）的反常流入（anomaly inflow）。基于此结构引入规范中性旁观费米子（gauge-neutral spectator fermions），得到玻色化描述。进一步在适当光滑性条件下，构造带有三维体扩展的格点华氏-祖米诺-维滕模型。

Result: 该格点构造的一个显著特征是指数化作用量（exponentiated action）中左右体贡献的相消。当满足反常自由条件，即左右表示具有相同的二次指标（identical quadratic indices）时，这一相消在取连续极限之前即可发生。

Conclusion: 该构造通过二维反常自由手征规范理论的玻色化描述，在有限格距下实现了反常消除机制。然而，建立所需的连续极限（continuum limit）仍然是一个重要的未解决问题。

Abstract: A central issue in lattice formulations of chiral gauge theories is how the anomaly cancellation mechanism of the continuum theory can be realized at finite lattice spacing. In the present paper, based on non-Abelian bosonization, we propose a lattice formulation of the bosonic theory corresponding to a two-dimensional non-Abelian chiral gauge theory. In the continuum theory, the gauge anomaly of chiral fermions is represented, in the bosonized description, as anomaly inflow from a three-dimensional Chern--Simons-type bulk contribution contained in a gauged Wess--Zumino--Witten model. Motivated by this structure, we introduce gauge-neutral spectator fermions and use the resulting bosonized description. We then construct a lattice counterpart of the gauged Wess--Zumino--Witten model with a three-dimensional bulk extension under appropriate smoothness conditions. A salient feature of this lattice formulation is the cancellation of the left and right bulk contributions in the exponentiated action. This cancellation occurs even before taking the continuum limit when the anomaly-free condition is satisfied, namely when the left and right representations have identical quadratic indices. Thus, the present construction realizes the anomaly-cancellation mechanism at finite lattice spacing via the bosonized description of two-dimensional anomaly-free chiral gauge theories. Establishing the desired continuum limit remains an important open problem.

</details>


### [34] [Numerical Hints for Dyon Condensation at $θ=2π$ via Wilson-'t Hooft Loops in $SU(2)$ Yang-Mills Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13428)
*Hiromasa Watanabe,Issaku Kanamori,Okuto Morikawa,Yuki Nagai,Yuya Tanizaki,Akio Tomiya*

TL;DR: 通过测量SU(2) Wilson格点规范作用下的Wilson-'t Hooft环算符，在θ=2π处获得与理论预测一致的dyon凝聚数值证据，而非磁单极凝聚。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验Yang-Mills理论中2π周期性的非平凡实现：理论预期θ=0和θ=2π处的禁闭真空属于不同的对称性保护拓扑态（symmetry-protected topological state, SPT state），且θ=2π处应为dyon凝聚而非磁单极凝聚，需通过数值模拟进行验证。

Method: 在SU(2) Wilson格点规范作用框架下，测量θ=2π处的Wilson-'t Hooft环算符。为在存在缺陷情况下正确识别规范拓扑荷，采用1-形式协变DBW2梯度流（1-form covariant DBW2 gradient flow）对格点规范场进行涂抹处理。

Result: 数值结果与dyon凝聚（dyon condensation）在θ=2π处发生的理论预言一致，而非磁单极凝聚（monopole condensation）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为Yang-Mills理论中2π周期性在广义全局对称性框架下的非平凡实现提供了数值支持，证实了θ=0和θ=2π处禁闭真空属于不同1-形式中心对称性（1-form center symmetry）保护的SPT态的理论预测。

Abstract: Yang-Mills theories at $θ$ and $θ+2π$ are unitarily equivalent, but their $2π$ periodicity has a nontrivial realization. Recent developments in generalized global symmetries show that confinement vacua at $θ=0$ and $2π$ should belong to different symmetry-protected topological (SPT) states with the $1$-form center symmetry. For its examination, we measure the Wilson-'t Hooft loop operators at $θ=2π$ for the $SU(2)$ Wilson lattice gauge action and discuss their long-distance behaviors. This requires us to identify the gauge topological charge in the presence of defects, and we employ the $1$-form covariant DBW2 gradient flow to smear lattice gauge fields. We then obtain numerical evidence consistent with dyon condensation at $θ=2π$, rather than monopole condensation, as theoretically predicted.

### [35] [Mixed-dimensional quantum Monte Carlo studies of M-point moiré materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12508)
*Dumitru Călugăru,Konstantinos Vasiliou,Haoyu Hu,B. Andrei Bernevig,Werner Krauth,S. A. Parameswaran*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文针对一种基于扭转二维三角格子单层形成的M点莫尔材料（twisted AA-stacked SnSe₂），通过开发新的无符号问题随机级数展开量子蒙特卡洛算法（SSE QMC），系统研究了其混合维度Hubbard模型的相图，发现了依赖于扭转角的关联绝缘体和Wigner-Mott绝缘体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近提出的基于二维三角格子单层扭转形成的M点莫尔材料平台，其连续模型表明SnSe₂扭转AA堆叠结构中的导带电子可实现三轨道Hubbard模型，具有轨道选择的准一维（quasi-1D）跳跃。该混合维度（mixed-dimensional）极限——各谷内跳跃为准一维，而谷间通过相互作用耦合为全二维网络——为研究强关联物理提供了新平台，但其相图尚未被系统探索。

Method: 本文开发了一种高效的随机级数展开量子蒙特卡洛（SSE QMC）算法，该算法结合了自定义全局更新（global updates）和平行回火（parallel tempering），以克服混合维度设定下的平衡化挑战。该算法在任意填充下均无符号问题（sign problem）。

Result: 在广泛且实际的扭转角和相互作用强度范围内，整数量填充时系统支持关联绝缘体（correlated insulators），其性质和强度对扭转角高度敏感。在特定的公度分数填充下，进一步发现了Wigner-Mott绝缘体（Wigner-Mott insulators）的证据。

Conclusion: 数值结果的主要特征可通过强耦合描述（strong-coupling description）进行解析解释。文章还讨论了偏离混合维度极限的微扰，以及将该方法推广到其他混合维度Hubbard模型实现的可能性。

Abstract: A new moiré-material platform has recently been proposed based on twisting two-dimensional triangular-lattice monolayers whose low-energy states lie at the three M points of the Brillouin zone. Continuum models derived from extensive ab initio simulations suggest that electrons in the conduction bands of one such M-point moiré material, twisted AA-stacked SnSe$_2$, realize a three-orbital Hubbard model with orbitally-selective, quasi-one-dimensional (quasi-1D) hopping, protected by a projective mirror symmetry. Here, we show that the resulting "mixed-dimensional" limit -- in which the hopping is exactly quasi-1D in each valley, while the valleys are coupled by interactions into a fully two-dimensional network -- can be sampled with Stochastic Series Expansion (SSE) quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) without a sign problem at any filling. We develop an efficient new SSE QMC algorithm that combines custom global updates with parallel tempering to overcome the equilibration challenges posed by the mixed-dimensional setting. We then use this algorithm to explore the phase diagram of M-point twisted AA-stacked SnSe$_2$. Over extended and realistic ranges of twist angles and interaction strengths, we find that at integer fillings the system supports correlated insulators whose nature and strength depend strongly on angle. At certain commensurate fractional fillings, we further find evidence for Wigner-Mott insulators. We analytically account for the main features observed numerically using a strong-coupling description. Finally, we discuss perturbations away from the mixed-dimensional limit and the possibility of applying our method to other realizations of mixed-dimensional Hubbard models.

</details>


### [36] [Spin correlations, low-energy scales, and anisotropy scaling in kagome frustrated magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12512)
*Phillip Popp,Stephan Rosenkranz,Arthur P. Ramirez,Sergey Syzranov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于XXZ海森堡模型在几何阻挫（GF）晶格上的绝热连续性新方法，用于区分量子自旋液体候选材料中自旋子激发与磁振子激发的中子散射谱特征。以kagome晶格为例，识别出与隐藏能量尺度T*相关的两个动量无关低能谱峰（ω₁≈3.4T*，ω₂≈6.3T*），并证明低能区域（ω≲T*）的谱特征来源于单磁振子散射，为解释kagome及其他GF量子磁体的中子散射提供了明确的光谱判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子散射（neutron scattering）是识别磁性材料量子态的核心手段。在量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid）的搜寻中，非弹性散射谱的宽谱特征常被视为自旋子（spinon）激发的证据，但这些特征也可能源于淬灭无序（quenched disorder）和强磁振子相互作用下的磁振子（magnon）激发。现有方法难以区分这两种机制，亟需建立一种新的判别标准。

Method: 基于几何阻挫（geometrically frustrating, GF）晶格上XXZ海森堡模型（XXZ Heisenberg model）的绝热连续性（adiabatic continuity），以模型各向异性（anisotropy）为变量，识别有限温度自旋关联函数（finite-temperature spin correlator）的普适特征与能量。

Result: 以kagome晶格为例，低能自旋谱函数（spin spectral function）中存在两个鲁棒（robust）、动量无关的峰，频率分别为ω₁≈3.4T*和ω₂≈6.3T*，其中T*为隐藏能量尺度（hidden energy scale），对应热容低温峰的特征尺度，许多GF磁体在该温度下也会表现出自旋玻璃冻结（spin-glass freezing）。低能区域（ω≲T*）的谱特征源于单磁振子散射（single-magnon scattering）。

Conclusion: 该研究为解释kagome及其他GF量子磁体的中子散射提供了尖锐的光谱判据（spectroscopic criterion）。谱特征随温度的演化及向其他GF晶格的推广也进行了讨论。

Abstract: Neutron scattering is central to identifying quantum states of magnetic materials. In the search for quantum spin liquids, broad spectral features of inelastic spectra have been cited as evidence for spinon excitations, but can also arise from magnon excitations excitations in the presence of quenched disorder and strong magnon interactions. We develop a new approach to this problem, based on the adiabatic continuity in the $XXZ$ Heisenberg model on geometrically frustrating (GF) lattices as a function of the model's anisotropy. Using this approach, we identify universal features and energies of finite-temperature spin correlators. Focusing on the kagome lattice, we show that the low-energy spin spectral function contains robust, momentum-independent peaks with frequencies: $ω_1 \approx 3.4 T^*$ and $ω_2 \approx 6.3 T^*$, where the ``hidden energy scale'' $T^*$ is the characteristic scale of a low-temperature peak in the heat capacity, at which many GF magnets also display spin-glass freezing. We show that the spectral features at low energies $ω\lesssim T^*$ arise from single-magnon scattering and identify the magnetizations of the respective excitations. We explore the evolution of the spectral features with temperature and discuss extensions to other GF lattices. Our results provide a sharp spectroscopic criterion for interpreting neutron scattering in kagome and other GF quantum magnets.

</details>


### [37] [Cyclotron mass-selective de Haas-van Alphen measurements using temperature modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12514)
*Michelle Hollricher,Andreas Bauer,Leo Maximov,Louw Feenstra,Christian Pfleiderer,Marc A. Wilde*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 提出一种温度调制的 dHvA 测量技术，利用 Lifshitz-Kosevich 因子的温度导数实现按有效质量选择性提取量子振荡信号，并在拓扑半金属 MoSi₂ 中实验验证了从 1m* 到 13m* 的质量分辨能力，成功分离了传统频谱中重叠的重轨道弱信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的 de Haas-van Alphen（dHvA）频谱中，重有效质量轨道的弱频率峰往往与轻轨道的强频率峰重叠，难以被可靠分离和识别，因此需要一种能按有效质量选择性提取量子振荡信号的新技术。

Method: 该技术通过对样品温度施加谐波调制（harmonic modulation），并利用锁相检测（phase-sensitive detection）拾取线圈中感应的电压信号；信号的振幅演化由 Lifshitz-Kosevich 因子的温度导数（temperature derivative of the Lifshitz-Kosevich factor）决定，从而实现对不同有效质量 m* 的量子振荡的非单调幅值调控。

Result: 在补偿型拓扑半金属（compensated topological semimetal）MoSi₂ 中，利用强塞曼驱动谐波（Zeeman-driven harmonic）产生的一组自然线性质量梳（natural linear mass comb），覆盖从 1m* 到 13m* 的质量范围，实验证实了质量依赖的量子振荡振幅的可调性，并成功分离了传统 dHvA 频谱中无法分辨的重轨道弱信号。

Conclusion: 该温度调制 dHvA 技术能够可靠地分离和提取难以直接观测的重有效质量轨道振荡信号，为量子振荡测量中轨道质量分辨提供了一种有效的实验途径。

Abstract: We present a temperature-modulated de Haas-van Alphen measurement technique that allows selective addressing of quantum oscillations with different effective masses $m^{\ast}$ using a non-monotonic amplitude evolution with temperature and magnetic field, governed by the temperature derivative of the Lifshitz-Kosevich factor. The technique relies on harmonic modulation of the sample temperature and phase-sensitive detection of quantum oscillations in the voltage induced in a pick-up coil. We use a set of frequencies with strong Zeeman-driven harmonic content in the compensated topological semimetal MoSi$_{2}$ as a natural linear mass comb ranging from 1$m^{\ast}$ to 13$m^{\ast}$ to demonstrate the tunability of the mass-dependent quantum oscillation amplitudes experimentally. The technique allows to reliably isolate weak contributions of heavy orbits that are inaccessible in conventional de Haas-van Alphen frequency spectra because their frequency peaks overlap with much stronger frequency peaks of lighter orbits.

</details>


### [38] [Hidden antiferromagnetism, persistent valley fluctuations, and $U(6)$ crossovers in triangular-lattice M-point moiré materials via determinantal quantum Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12530)
*Konstantinos Vasiliou,Dumitru Călugăru,Johannes S. Hofmann,S. A. Parameswaran*

TL;DR: 本文基于扭转二维原子单层构建的新型莫尔材料平台，提出一种无符号问题的行列式量子蒙特卡洛模拟方法，研究了三电子填充下体系的相图，揭示了近各向同性相互作用下局域矩与巡游性竞争的中间耦合区间及其与U(6)对称性的关联。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该工作为这类新型莫尔材料平台提供了可控的数值模拟手段，揭示了U(6)对称性在决定体系中间耦合行为中的关键作用，并指出这些物理特征具有一定的鲁棒性。

Abstract: A new moiré material platform was recently proposed based on twisting two-dimensional atomic monolayers whose low-energy states lie at the three M-points of the Brillouin Zone. Continuum and ab initio modeling suggest that electrons in the conduction bands of these materials realize three-valley Hubbard models with valley-selective, quasi-one-dimensional hopping. Remarkably, the onsite Hubbard repulsion is almost $U(6)$-symmetric without fine-tuning. Here, we show that this class of systems naturally admits sign-free determinantal Quantum Monte Carlo simulations at a filling of three electrons per moiré unit cell. We use these to explore the phase diagram for interactions of various strengths and $U(6)$-breaking anisotropies. We show that for near-isotropic interactions as relevant to, e.g., AA-stacked twisted SnSe$_2$, the system exhibits an extended intermediate-coupling regime in which local-moment formation and itinerancy compete, and the crossover to a putative low-temperature ordered state can be understood in terms of fluctuating $U(6)$ local moments. We argue that many of these features persist beyond the idealized sign-problem-free limit.

### [39] [Hall conductivity reveals the nature of quantum coherence in strongly correlated metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12665)
*Emily Z. Zhang,Thomas P. Devereaux*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用确定性量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）模拟掺杂Hubbard模型，发现尽管纵向电阻率（resistivity）在不同参数下均呈现稳健的线性温度依赖（T-linear），但霍尔响应（Hall response）对粒子-空穴不对称性、费米面拓扑和多体关联效应高度敏感，揭示出从半经典到量子相干输运（quantum-coherent transport）的交叉转变，这一信息在纵向通道中被掩盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反常金属（strange metal）中线性温度依赖的电阻率是强关联电子体系的普遍特征，但以往研究过度集中于纵向输运通道，忽略了横向响应（transverse response）中蕴含的微观信息。本文旨在通过霍尔效应揭示被纵向电阻掩盖的物理机制。

Method: 采用数值精确的确定性量子蒙特卡洛方法，对磁场下的掺杂Hubbard模型进行模拟，计算纵向和横向输运系数。

Result: 电阻率在不同参数集下均呈现稳健的T-linear行为；霍尔响应则对粒子-空穴不对称性、费米面拓扑及多体关联效应高度敏感；这些因素的共同作用决定了系统进入量子相干态的交叉标度（crossover scale），并反映在霍尔电导率（Hall conductivity）中。

Conclusion: 纵向电阻率的T-linear行为具有普遍性，而霍尔响应揭示了从半经典输运（semi-classical transport）到量子相干输运的交叉，这一信息在纵向通道中不可见。

Abstract: Linear-in-temperature resistivity is a hallmark for strange metallic transport, and appears universally in many strongly correlated electron systems. However, the focus on the longitudinal channel often overshadows the profound microscopic insights contained within the transverse response. Here, we utilize numerically exact determinantal quantum Monte Carlo simulations of the doped Hubbard model in a magnetic field to calculate longitudinal and transverse transport. We demonstrate that while the resistivity is robustly $T$-linear across parameter sets, the Hall response is highly sensitive to particle-hole asymmetry, Fermi surface topology, and many-body correlation effects. Specifically, the combination of these effects determine a crossover scale in which the system becomes quantum-coherent, and is reflected in the Hall conductivity. Our results demonstrate that while the $T$-linearity in resistivity appears universal, the Hall response reveals a crossover from semi-classical to quantum-coherent transport otherwise masked in the longitudinal channel.

</details>


### [40] [Selective stabilization of antiferromagnetic orders in FeTe films via local strain engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13257)
*Hao Xu,Jing Jiang,Xuesong Gai,Haicheng Lin,Kai Liu,Zhong-Yi Lu,Kai Chang,Chong Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过结合高分辨率扫描隧道显微镜（STM）和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，在少层FeTe薄膜中利用局域单轴应变工程实现了双共线（bicollinear）和二聚体（dimer）反铁磁（AFM）序的选择性稳定化，并首次实验证实了长程二聚体反铁磁序的存在，揭示了各向异性应变可有效解除竞争磁态间的简并性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高分辨率扫描隧道显微镜（STM）与密度泛函理论（DFT）计算相结合的方法，在FeTe薄膜及FeTe/FeSe异质结的位错区域附近对应变场进行映射，建立特定应变分量与磁基态之间的直接对应关系。

Result: 沿Fe-Fe次近邻方向施加单轴压缩可稳定双共线反铁磁序，条带方向平行于压缩轴；沿Fe-Fe最近邻方向的各向异性应变可诱导长程二聚体反铁磁序，该相表现为独特的√2 × √2电子重构，且与双共线相具有相同的奈尔温度（Neel temperature）。

Conclusion: 各向异性应变可有效解除竞争磁态间的简并性，为操控难以实现的磁序提供了稳健策略，并揭示了铁基超导体中晶格、自旋与电子自由度之间的相互关联。

Abstract: The parent compound FeTe hosts a complex magnetic landscape that is highly susceptible to lattice distortions. Although theoretical models have predicted a bicollinear to dimer antiferromagnetic (AFM) phase transition under tensile strain, its experimental realization and deterministic control has remained elusive owing to severe magnetic frustration. Here, combining high-resolution scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) and density functional theory (DFT) calculations, we demonstrate the selective stabilization of bicollinear and dimer AFM orders in few-layer FeTe films via local uniaxial strain engineering. By mapping the strain fields near dislocation areas in FeTe films and FeTe/FeSe heterostructures, we establish a direct correspondence between specific strain components and the resulting magnetic ground states. We find that uniaxial compression along the Fe-Fe next-nearest-neighbor direction stabilizes the bicollinear AFM order, with the stripe orientation aligning parallel to the compression axis. Crucially, we report the experimental realization of the long-range dimer AFM order, which emerges under anisotropic strain along the Fe-Fe nearest-neighbor direction. This phase manifests as a distinct $\sqrt{2} \times \sqrt{2}$ electronic reconstruction and shares a common Neel temperature with the bicollinear phase. Our findings reveal that anisotropic strain effectively lifts the magnetic degeneracy among competing states. This work provides a robust strategy for the manipulation of elusive magnetic orders and offers insights into the interplay between lattice, spin, and electronic degrees of freedom in iron-based superconductors.
