### [41] [Phase diagram of the Kitaev-Heisenberg-$Γ$ model: Classical and quantum magnetism, frustration, and subdominant interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13263)
*Kiyu Fukui,Yukitoshi Motome*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用先进数值技术，从经典和量子两个角度重新审视了 Kitaev-Heisenberg-Γ 模型的基态相图。经典情形下揭示了丰富的非共线多-Q 磁序，而量子涨落则抑制了多数竞争序，仅保留少数主导的非公度序。研究还识别出高度阻挫区域，其中螺旋自旋液体态（spiral spin liquid states）及新型磁有序态可能被其他磁相互作用稳定。结果为 Kitaev 自旋液体候选材料的设计与实验解释提供了综合指导。

Method: 采用最先进的数值技术（state-of-the-art numerical techniques），从经典和量子两个视角重新审视 Kitaev-Heisenberg-Γ 模型的基态相图（ground-state phase diagram）。

Result: 经典情形下发现了一系列非共线磁序（noncollinear orders），包括多种带和不带非公度调制的非共线多-Q 磁序。量子情形下，量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）抑制了经典情形的多数竞争序，仅保留少数主导的非公度序。进一步识别出高度阻挫区域（highly frustrated regions），其中螺旋自旋液体态及新的磁有序态可能被其他额外磁相互作用稳定。

Conclusion: 研究为经典和量子自旋下的 Kitaev-Heisenberg-Γ 模型提供了全面的视角，不仅有助于解释候选材料的实验结果，还为新材料的搜索与设计以实现 Kitaev 自旋液体提供了有价值的指导。

Abstract: The Kitaev spin liquid provides a rare example of exactly solvable quantum spin liquid states. Intensive research over the past two decades has identified a variety of its candidate materials. In real materials, however, the Kitaev interaction is inevitably accompanied by additional magnetic interactions such as the Heisenberg and $Γ$ interactions. These interactions often induce magnetic ordering at low temperatures, making it essential to clarify their effects in the search for and design of Kitaev spin liquid candidate materials. In this study, we revisit the ground-state phase diagram of the Kitaev-Heisenberg-$Γ$ model from both classical and quantum perspectives, using state-of-the-art numerical techniques. In the classical case, we reveal a $zoo$ $of$ $noncollinear$ $orders$, where a variety of noncollinear multiple-$Q$ magnetic orders with and without incommensurate modulations emerge. In the quantum case, we unravel that quantum fluctuations suppress many of the competing orders found in the classical case, resulting in a reduced number of dominant incommensurate orders. We further identify $highly$ $frustrated$ regions, where spiral spin liquid states as well as new magnetically ordered states are potentially stabilized by other additional magnetic interactions. Our results provide a comprehensive perspective on the Kitaev-Heisenberg-$Γ$ model for both classical and quantum spins and offer a valuable guide not only for interpreting experimental results on candidate materials, but also for searching and designing new materials to realize the Kitaev spin liquid.

### [42] [Frustration effects on the magnetization plateau physics in a trimerized quantum spin-1/2 chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13265)
*L. M. Ramos,M. Schmidt,F. M. Zimmer*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文通过团簇平均场（cluster mean-field）结合Lanczos精确对角化的方法，研究了三聚化量子自旋链中由阻挫（frustration）引发的不稳定性，揭示了弱阻挫区域中1/3磁化平台（magnetization plateau）的微观机制及其与复合激发（composite excitations）的关联，并通过有限尺寸标度分析表征了零场临界性（zero-field criticality）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用团簇平均场方法结合Lanczos精确对角化（Lanczos exact diagonalization），分析了具有竞争相互作用（competing interactions）的Heisenberg模型在外加磁场下的基态与量子信息性质；通过有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）分析能隙、von Neumann纠缠熵（von Neumann entanglement entropy）和保真度磁化率（fidelity susceptibility）。

Result: 弱阻挫区域系统表现出稳健的1/3磁化平台，对应集体铁磁-亚铁磁三聚体态（collective ferrimagnetic-like trimer state）；增强次近邻三聚体内耦合（next-nearest-neighbor intratrimer coupling）导致自旋关联发生重组，出现向双子关联区域（doublon-like correlation regime）的交叉；低能行为可用弱相互作用的自旋有效描述解释磁化平台的扩展稳定性；有限尺寸标度分析揭示了模型的零场临界性质。

Conclusion: 阻挫在三聚化自旋链中可产生性质上截然不同的量子态，并为理解分数化激发的涌现提供了微观框架。

Abstract: We investigate frustration-induced instabilities in a trimerized quantum spin chain motivated by recent experimental findings for the compound Na$_2$Cu$_3$Ge$_4$O$_{12}$. Employing a cluster mean-field approach combined with Lanczos exact diagonalization, we analyze the ground-state and quantum-information properties of a Heisenberg model with competing interactions in a magnetic field. In the weakly frustrated regime, the system exhibits a robust $1/3$ magnetization plateau associated with a collective ferrimagnetic-like trimer state. Increasing the next-nearest-neighbor intratrimer coupling drives a pronounced reorganization of spin correlations, leading to a crossover toward a doublon-like correlation regime and providing a static ground-state picture consistent with the composite excitations observed dynamically in trimerized chains. The resulting low-energy behavior can be interpreted in terms of weakly interacting emergent spins, offering a microscopic explanation for the extended stability of the magnetization plateau. Furthermore, through finite-size scaling analyses of the energy gap, von Neumann entanglement entropy, and fidelity susceptibility, we characterize the zero-field criticality of the model. Ultimately, our results suggest that frustration gives rise to qualitatively distinct quantum states and provide a microscopic framework for understanding the emergence of fractionalized excitations in trimerized quantum spin systems.

### [43] [Modeling strained Cd$_3$As$_2$ thin films and their behavior in magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13293)
*M. Smith,A. A. Burkov,P. P. Orth,I. Martin,Victor L. Quito*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了Cd₃As₂薄膜在不同应变轮廓（双轴/单轴应变）及磁场下的行为，通过对称性约化构建有效k·p模型，识别了最低朗道能级打开带隙的两种微观机制，并提出了区分二者的新方法，同时发现二维狄拉克半金属相可由大面内磁场诱导且对应变高度敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Cd₃As₂薄膜在应变和磁场下的电子结构行为，解释Ahadi等人（2025）实验中观测到的结果，并区分可能的微观机制。

Method: 基于对称性约化（symmetry reduction）构建有效k·p模型，分别考虑保留C₄对称性但破缺反演的双轴应变（4mm点群），以及两种单轴应变情形：保留反演（mmm群）与破缺反演（2mm群）。通过分析沿限制方向的多子带效应以及朗道能级（Landau level）行为来研究磁场影响。

Result: 最低朗道能级打开带隙需要将对称性降至2mm（同时破缺反演和C₄旋转），或通过应变诱导的能带重整化（band renormalization）发生拓扑相变；大面内磁场可诱导二维狄拉克半金属相（two-dimensional Dirac semimetal phase），该相对应变轮廓高度敏感，当磁场垂直于保留的镜面时出现能带接触。

Conclusion: 所提方法可有效区分两种微观机制，且应变敏感的二维狄拉克半金属相可作为一种探测材料应变轮廓（strain profile）的有力工具。

Abstract: We present a systematic analysis of the behavior of thin films of Cd$_3$As$_2$ under different strain profiles and in magnetic fields. In each case, we construct effective $k \cdot p$ models by considering the reduction of symmetry and all constraints imposed by the remaining symmetries. Our analysis naturally describes both in-plane biaxial and uniaxial strain. Biaxial strain is expected to preserve in-plane $C_4$ rotational symmetry while breaking inversion, allowing for a description in terms of the $4mm$ point group. Uniaxial strain, on the other hand, breaks $C_4$ symmetry. For this case, we consider two scenarios: one preserving inversion, described by the $mmm$ group, and one breaking it, leading to $2mm$ symmetry. After deriving the models, we examine the effects of out-of-plane magnetic fields, identifying two possible microscopic mechanisms that can account for the experimental results reported in Ahadi et al. (2025). Importantly, our analysis proposes a new method for differentiating between them. By incorporating the effects of multiple subbands along the confinement direction, we show that the opening of a gap in the lowest Landau level requires either reducing the symmetry down to $2mm$, breaking both inversion and $C_4$ rotations, or a topological transition of the band structure due to strain-induced band renormalization. Furthermore, we demonstrate that a two-dimensional Dirac semimetal phase can be induced by sufficiently large in-plane magnetic fields. This phase is highly sensitive to different strain profiles, with band touchings occurring when the field is applied perpendicular to preserved mirror planes, serving as a powerful probe of the material's strain profile.

</details>

Abstract: We study a two-orbital Hubbard-Kanamori model, which has been originally proposed for iron-based superconductors, using variational Monte Carlo. We span the nonmagnetic sector at both hole-doping and electron-doping, with respect to the half-filled case $n=2$. We report the presence of a superconductive region with a $s^{\pm}$ symmetry only when the half-filled system is in a Mott state, while orbital selectivity is absent. These results are qualitatively different from what was reported in the three-orbital Hubbard-Kanamori model, where a more extended superconductive region was observed with a concomitant development of orbital selectivity, and they are to some extent more reminiscent of the single-band Hubbard model.

This overview presents the underlying ideas and the resulting equations in a form accessible to nonexperts. We compare theoretical results with all available resistivity data for single-layer High-T$_{c}$ systems, and with some spectral data. The highlighted results include a density dependent quasilinear T-dependence in resistivity, an unusually small quasiparticle weight, and distinct low-temperature emergent scales that dominate transport, thermodynamics and spectral properties of single-layer High T$_c$ systems. Suggestions are made for further experiments to probe the physics of these challenging quantum many-body systems.

### [46] [A solvable model for unsupervised federated learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13045)
*Giovanni Catania,Aurélien Decelle,Gianluca Manzan,Beatriz Seoane,Daniele Tantari*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一个理论框架，通过教师-多学生交互场景分析联邦学习在生成式环境中的表现。利用平衡态无序系统理论，证明学生之间的交互能系统性提升学习性能，推导出教师恢复的贝叶斯最优条件，并将其映射到受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machine, RBM）的平衡采样过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习在分布式生成建模场景下的理论理解尚不充分，缺乏对多个客户端（学生）之间交互如何影响学习效果的严格分析。

Method: 采用教师-多学生（teacher-multiple interacting students）场景，每个学生接收不同噪声或不同子集的数据。运用平衡态无序系统（equilibrium disordered system）理论工具进行解析推导，并通过数值模拟验证。

Result: 交互显著提升学习性能：高噪声学生需要更少样本恢复底层模式，低噪声学生与真实信号（ground-truth signal）的重叠增大。推导出教师恢复的贝叶斯最优条件，该条件与样本复杂度（sample complexity）、噪声水平和交互强度相关。

Conclusion: 学生间的交互动力学可映射为具有结构化隐层的受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machine with structured hidden layer）的平衡采样，为交互如何改进分布式生成建模提供了原则性的理论理解。

Abstract: We introduce a theoretical framework for analyzing federated learning in a generative setting through a teacher-multiple interacting students scenario, in which each student receives a distinct realization of the data, either through a different noise corruption or by accessing a different subset, possibly of varying size. Using theoretical tools in equilibrium disordered system, we analytically show that interactions among students systematically enhance learning performance: highly noisy students require fewer samples to recover the underlying pattern, while low-noise students achieve a larger overlap with the ground-truth signal. We derive the optimal Bayesian conditions for teacher recovery as functions of the sample complexity, noise level, and interaction strength, and validate these predictions through numerical simulations. The resulting dynamics can be mapped onto equilibrium sampling in a Restricted Boltzmann Machine with a structured hidden layer, providing a principled theoretical understanding of how interactions improve distributed generative modeling.

</details>

### [47] [Charting the emergent low-dimensional manifold of quantum materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12520)
*Jason Z. Kim,Omri Lesser,Debanjan Chowdhury*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过无监督非线性降维技术揭示了晶体材料隐藏的几何结构，仅用少量微观描述符即可捕获材料性质的大部分方差。该低维嵌入不仅能自动区分超导体与普通材料，还能超越化学相似性对超导家族进行区分，并直接控制临界温度（$T_c$），实现无需配对机制知识的准确$T_c$预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 元素周期表成功揭示了原子行为的简单组织原理，但晶体材料因其微观复杂性和巨大的构型空间（configurational space），至今缺乏类似的基础性组织框架。尽管已有数千种合成材料的数据库，从中提取可预测且可解释的模型仍是一个巨大挑战。

Method: 应用无监督非线性降维（unsupervised nonlinear dimensionality reduction）和微分几何（differential geometry）技术，对无机晶体结构数据库（Inorganic Crystal Structure Database, ICSD）中的材料数据进行分析，揭示材料景观（materials landscape）中隐藏的几何组织。

Result: 仅用少数微观描述符（microscopic descriptors）的组合即可捕获材料性质的大部分方差。低维嵌入能自主地将超导体与普通材料分离，并以超越化学相似性的方式区分不同的超导家族。该几何组织直接支配多种超导家族的临界温度（$T_c$），可实现无需配对机制知识的准确$T_c$预测。

Conclusion: 该方法揭示了控制宏观量子行为的涌现组织原理（emergent organizing principles），提供了一种直接从实验数据构建复杂量子材料模型的新范式（new paradigm）。

Abstract: The periodic table of elements transformed chemistry by revealing simple organizing principles underlying atomic behavior. Despite decades of effort, no analogous framework has emerged for crystalline materials -- their microscopic complexity and vast configurational space have defied reduction to fundamental organizing principles. Current databases catalog thousands of synthesized materials, but extracting predictive, interpretable models from this wealth of data remains a formidable challenge. Here we demonstrate that the materials landscape possesses a hidden geometric organization that can be unveiled through unsupervised nonlinear dimensionality reduction. Applying differential geometry techniques to the Inorganic Crystal Structure Database (ICSD), we reveal that just a few combinations of microscopic descriptors capture the vast majority of variance in material properties. This low-dimensional embedding autonomously segregates superconductors from ordinary materials and further distinguishes superconducting families in ways that transcend chemical similarity alone. Remarkably, the discovered geometric organization directly governs critical temperatures ($T_c$) across diverse superconducting families, enabling accurate $T_c$ predictions without any knowledge of the pairing mechanism. Our approach uncovers emergent organizing principles that control macroscopic quantum behavior, offering a new paradigm in how we build models of complex quantum materials directly from experimental data.

</details>


### [48] [Dynamical Control of Superconductivity in Superconductor-Ferromagnet Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12544)
*Dimitri Pimenov,Nicholas R. Poniatowski,Charlotte G. L. Bøttcher,Amir Yacoby,Debanjan Chowdhury*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了由铁磁金属、全能隙s波超导体和微波谐振腔组成的混合系统，证明当磁振子与光子频率相近并受外部驱动时，混合驱动的磁振子-极化激元会诱导从预期近邻化节p波超导体到全能隙(p_x+ip_y)超导体的非平衡交叉，且交叉温度与磁振子-光子失谐量成反比，为通过腔光子操控电子集体模以设计新奇物态提供了理论路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在由铁磁金属、全能隙s波超导体与微波谐振腔构成的混合系统中，外部驱动下磁振子与光子的耦合如何诱导超导序的非平衡转变，并解释近期电路量子电动力学（cQED）实验中观察到的低温腔响应对磁振子-光子失谐量的非平凡依赖关系。

Method: 建立简化理论模型，描述铁磁金属、全能隙s波超导体与微波谐振腔的复合系统，其中低能激发包括铁磁磁振子（ferromagnetic magnons）、超导体的Bogoliubov激发以及腔光子（cavity photons）。当磁振子与光子频率接近且施加外部驱动时，分析混合驱动的磁振子-极化激元（magnon-polaritons）对超导序的影响，并计算随温度演化的腔光子频率重整化（renormalization），进而修正谐振器的动感电感（kinetic inductance）。

Result: 发现当磁振子与光子频率相近并受外部驱动时，系统从预期的近邻化节p波超导体（nodal p-wave superconductor）转变为全能隙(p_x+ip_y)超导体；该交叉的特征温度与磁振子-光子失谐量（magnon-photon detuning）成反比；跨该转变过程的腔光子频率重整化呈现出多个与驱动非平衡性质相关的非平凡特征。

Conclusion: 研究结果为通过将腔光子耦合到二维关联材料与界面中的电子集体模来工程化设计新奇物态提供了系统性的理论探索路径，并成功解释了基于坡莫合金-铌双层的cQED实验中观察到的低温腔响应对磁振子-光子失谐量的非平凡依赖。

Abstract: We study a simplified model of a ferromagnetic metal proximitized by a fully-gapped $s-$wave superconductor and integrated with a microwave resonator. The low-energy excitations in the combined system consist of ferromagnetic magnons, Bogoliubov excitations of the superconductor, and cavity photons. We show here that when the magnons and photons have comparable frequencies and are subject to an external drive, the hybridized driven magnon-polaritons induce a non-equilibrium crossover from the expected proximitized nodal $p-$wave superconductor to a fully gapped $(p_x+ip_y)-$superconductor. Moreover, the characteristic crossover temperature is inversely related to the magnon-photon detuning. We compute the temperature-dependent renormalization of the cavity photon frequencies across this nodal to nodeless evolution, which modifies the kinetic inductance of the resonator, and find a number of non-trivial features tied to the non-equilibrium (i.e., driven) nature of the problem. We compare and contrast these results with a recent circuit quantum electrodynamics (cQED) based experiment studying a permalloy-niobium bilayer, where a non-trivial dependence of the low-temperature cavity response on the magnon-photon detuning was observed. Our results pave the way for a principled exploration of engineering novel states of matter by coupling cavity photons to electronic collective modes in correlated two-dimensional materials and interfaces.

### [49] [Multiband Superconductivity and Charge Density Wave in HfxZr1-xTe3 single crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12598)
*F. F. G. Nogueira,M. S. da Luz,M. S. Torikachvili,L. M. Ishikura,Ebrahim Dib,A. J. S. Machado*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道了HfxZr1-xTe3单晶中的体态多带超导电性和电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）。少量Hf掺杂（x=0.02）将CDW转变温度降低至约53 K，并诱导出转变温度约3.3 K的稳健体态超导态，同时上临界磁场Hc2(T)的温度依赖性与双带模型高度吻合，表明体系存在多带超导电性。压力实验显示，静水压会提升TCDW并抑制Tc。研究表明Hf掺杂可通过化学压力效应精细调控CDW与超导电性之间的竞争，并稳定多带超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索准一维层状材料ZrTe3中电荷密度波（CDW）与超导电性之间的竞争关系，并研究通过Hf掺杂（Hf substitution）引入的化学压力效应是否能够稳定体态超导电性及多带超导态。

Method: 制备HfxZr1-xTe3单晶样品，综合采用电阻率（electrical resistivity）、磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）、霍尔效应（Hall effect）、塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）和比热（specific heat）等输运及热力学测量；同时开展高达约2 GPa的静水压（hydrostatic pressure）下的电阻率测量。

Result: 少量Hf掺杂（x=0.02）使CDW转变温度从约63 K降至约53 K，同时体态超导电性在约3.3 K出现；上临界磁场Hc2(T)偏离单带行为，可由双带模型（two-band model）拟合，证实多带超导性；霍尔效应和热电行为显示显著的电子各向异性及增强的有效载流子质量；静水压实验表明压力会提升TCDW并抑制Tc。

Conclusion: Hf掺杂能够通过化学压力效应（chemical pressure effects）精细调控准一维体系中CDW序与超导电性之间的平衡，从而稳定多带超导态；这一发现为理解低维体系中竞争序的调控机制提供了新的实验依据。

Abstract: We report on the bulk multiband superconductivity and charge density wave (CDW) in HfxZr1-xTe3 single crystals. The parent compound ZrTe3 is a layered van der Waals material that undergoes a CDW transition near 63 K and exhibits only filamentary superconductivity below 2.0 K. Upon the introduction of a small amount of Hf (x = 0.02), the CDW transition temperature is reduced to TCDW ~ 53 K, while a robust bulk superconducting state emerges at Tc ~ 3.3 K, underscoring a subtle competition between CDW order and superconductivity in this quasi-one-dimensional system. Electrical resistivity, magnetic susceptibility, Hall effect, Seebeck coefficient, and specific heat measurements consistently confirm the bulk nature of the superconducting phase. The temperature dependence of the upper critical field Hc2(T) deviates markedly from single-band behavior, and it is well described by a two-band model, consistent with multiband superconductivity. Analysis of the Hall effect, and thermoelectric behavior reveal pronounced electronic anisotropy, with enhanced effective carrier masses, indicating that the subtle structural modification introduced by Hf substitutions affects the Fermi surface topology, as well as electronic correlations. Measurements of electrical resistivity in hydrostatic pressures up to ~ 2 GPa reveal that pressure drives TCDW to higher temperatures while suppressing Tc. These findings show that Hf doping can be used to fine-tune the balance between the CDW instability and superconductivity, possibly by means of chemical pressure effects, stabilizing a multiband superconducting state in Hf-doped ZrTe3.

### [50] [Revealing nonvolatile behaviors in magneto-thermal switching using microstructure-controlled superconducting composites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12778)
*Keigo Ito,Yui Sakamoto,Hossein Sepehri-Amin,Yuto Watanabe,Poonam Rani,Kumpei Imamura,Takamasa Hirai,Keisuke Hirata,Shunsuke Mori,Yusuke Nakanishi,Kenichiro Hashimoto,Takasada Shibauchi,Yoshikazu Mizuguchi,Ken-ichi Uchida,Fuyuki Ando*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过累积轧制键合法制备Sn/Pb多层复合材料，系统调控微观结构尺度，发现当Sn畴尺寸达到与超导基体中磁涡旋（magnetic vortex）相当或更小时，形成的磁通钉扎（magnetic flux trapping）可实现持久磁热开关效应（nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching），并确认剩余磁化强度（remanent magnetization）与开关非易失性的相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Arima等人近期观察到超导焊料中磁热开关具有非易失特性，并确定磁通钉扎是产生该效应的必要条件，但此类材料的设计规则尚不明确。

Method: 采用累积轧制键合法（accumulative roll bonding method）制备Sn/Pb多层复合材料；通过改变轧制键合的重复次数来系统调控各层厚度（即微观结构尺度），同时保持样品整体尺寸与平均成分不变。

Result: 随着重复次数增加，微米级Sn畴逐渐形成，磁热导率的非易失性逐渐出现，并与剩余磁化强度相关。

Conclusion: 直接证实了在超导基体中，尺寸与磁涡旋相当或更小的夹杂物（inclusions）是实现磁通钉扎的关键，从而在超导复合材料中实现非易失性磁热开关效应。

Abstract: Thermal conductivity in a conductor changes by the application of an external magnetic field, which functions as a magneto-thermal switch. For superconductors, a large magneto-thermal switching can occur through a superconducting-to-normal conducting phase transition due to the change in the electron contribution in thermal conductivity. Arima et al. recently reported a nonvolatile nature of the magneto-thermal switching for superconducting solders, which consist of phase-separated Sn and Pb domains. Although they clarified that magnetic flux trapping is required to induce the nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching, a rule for such material design is still unclear. Here, we investigate the microstructure dependence of magneto-thermal switching in superconducting Sn/Pb multilayered composites, which are created by an accumulative roll bonding method. The thickness of each layer, that is the scale of microstructure, can be systematically controlled by the repetition number of roll bonding while the whole sample size and average composition are unchanged. We find that, as the formation of micro-scaled Sn domains proceeds by increasing the repetition number, a nonvolatility in the magneto-thermal conductivity gradually appears in correlation with the remanent magnetization. This study directly confirms that the inclusions with a size comparable to or less than the magnetic vortex in superconducting matrix is essential for magnetic flux trapping, enabling the nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching in superconducting composites.

TL;DR: 本文利用机械点接触谱学（MPCS）结合超导Nb针尖，在CrSb单晶的三个主晶向上探测了Andreev反射，提取出动量依赖的自旋极化率（约61.9%-73.4%），并观察到尺寸为250-500 nm的交变磁（altermagnetic）畴结构，证实了CrSb中动量依赖的自旋极化，并建立了Andreev反射作为探测k依赖自旋织构的新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）因其k依赖的自旋分裂能带与零净磁化特性，在下一代自旋电子学应用中具有潜力。其中CrSb因其g波自旋分裂和高奈尔温度（Néel temperature）而受到关注，但对其动量依赖自旋极化的直接实验探测仍待开展。

Method: 采用机械点接触谱学（mechanical point-contact spectroscopy, MPCS）技术，使用超导Nb针尖在CrSb单晶的三个主晶向上进行Andreev反射测量，并结合样品表面空间线扫描（line-scan）分析交变磁畴结构。

Result: 沿(0001)、(-1-120)和(10-10)晶面提取的动量依赖自旋极化率分别约为73.4%、67.9%和61.9%，显著区别于传统反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）。空间线扫描谱显示存在尺寸为250-500 nm的交变磁畴，畴壁宽度约为250 nm。

Conclusion: 实验结果有力支持了交变磁体CrSb中动量依赖的自旋极化特性，并确立了Andreev反射作为探测k依赖自旋织构（k-dependent spin texture）的新方法。

Abstract: Altermagnetic materials have recently emerged as promising candidates for next-generation spintronic applications, characterized by the k-dependent spin-splitted band structure and a simultaneous zero-net-magnetization. Among them, altermagnetic candidate CrSb has attracted considerable attention, owing to its g-wave spin splitting and high Néel temperature. In this article, we employed mechanical point-contact spectroscopy (MPCS) with superconducting Nb tips to probe the Andreev reflection on CrSb single crystals along three principal crystallographic orientations. The extracted momentum-dependent spin polarizations are approximately 73.4% for the (0001) plane, 67.9% for the (-1-120) plane, and 61.9% for the (10-10) plane, respectively, distinct from conventional antiferromagnets. Furthermore, conductance spectra from spatial line-scans on the sample surface support the existence of altermagnetic domains with a characteristic size of 250-500 nm separated by domain-walls with width about 250 nm. These results strongly support the momentum-dependent spin polarization in altermagnetic CrSb and establish Andreev reflection as a new paradigm to probe k-dependent spin textures.

### [52] [Current patterns and loss contributions in CORT cables carrying AC current](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13512)
*Benoît Vanderheyden,Julien Dular,Louis Denis,Steffen Elschner,Christophe Geuzaine,Mariusz Wozniak,Francesco Grilli*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过一种有效的二维模型，研究了单层CORT电缆中涂层导体（CC）内的三维电流分布及其对交流损耗（AC losses）的影响，特别聚焦于Garber电流模式对表面损耗和边缘损耗的贡献，并分析了电缆几何参数（导体厚度、螺距角、相邻CC间隙）的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CORT电缆是小型化截面下传输交流电的潜在方案，但现有数值模型采用直导体或无限薄CC的简化假设，忽略了Garber电流模式（Garber current pattern），导致对CC内部电流分布和三维场分布的误判。因此需要对CC中详细的三维电流分布及其对交流损耗的影响进行系统研究。

Method: 采用一种有效的二维模型（effective 2D model），该模型使用与电缆螺旋结构共形的坐标系，研究单层CORT电缆中CC内的三维电流分布，并分析电缆几何参数（导体厚度、螺距角、相邻CC间隙）对Garber电流模式及交流损耗的影响。

Result: 揭示了CC中详细的电流分布，建立了其与不同交流损耗机制之间的关系；明确了Garber电流模式对两种主要交流损耗分量——表面损耗（surface losses，与平行于超导层宽面的磁场分量穿透相关）和边缘损耗（edge losses，与CC间隙附近垂直磁场分量的穿透相关）——的贡献。

Conclusion: 本文提出的有效二维模型能够更准确地描述CORT电缆中的电流分布和交流损耗，弥补了传统简化模型的不足，为CORT电缆的优化设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Conductor-on-round-tube (CORT) cables are a potential solution for carrying AC power in a small cross-section. Due to the geometry of the cable and the helical arrangement of the coated conductors (CC), the current follows a non-trivial pattern inside each CC. For instance, for the case of a single-layer cable, the current flow is mostly axial along the outer face of the CCs and mostly azimuthal along their inner face. Such a current distribution, known as the Garber current pattern, affects the transport AC losses. In numerical models, commonly adopted simplifications are either based on straight conductors or infinitely thin CCs. Such approaches neglect the Garber current pattern and thus misrepresent both the detailed current flow within the CC and the resulting 3D distribution of the fields. In this work, the detailed 3D current distribution in the CCs is investigated in a one-layer CORT cable, as a function of the cable geometrical parameters such as the conductor thickness, the pitch angle, and the gap between adjacent CCs. In particular, the impact of the Garber current pattern is studied on the two largest contributions to the AC losses, namely the surface losses (associated with the penetration of the component of the magnetic field parallel to the wide faces of the superconducting layer) and the edge losses (associated with the penetration of the perpendicular component of the magnetic field occurring in the vicinity of the gaps between the CCs). The detailed distribution of the currents in the CCs is examined and its relationship with the different AC loss mechanisms is established. This study is carried out by means of an effective 2D model that uses a system of coordinates conforming with the helical structure of the cable.

### [53] [Quantum geometric anomalous Hall response in orbitally nonunitary superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13526)
*Viktor Frilen,Annica M. Black-Schaffer,Ankita Bhattacharya*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过蜂窝晶格紧束缚模型与Kane-Mele自旋-轨道耦合，研究了多带超导体在光学频率下的反常霍尔响应（AHR）。结果表明，仅考虑带内配对时，手性d波自旋单态超导态即使破坏时间反演对称性，AHR仍为零；而手性p波等自旋三重态（即使自旋公正）却可产生有限AHR，其根源在于轨道非公正性（orbital nonunitarity）与量子几何效应（quantum geometry）诱导的带间速度矩阵元。该发现修正了超导体中产生Kerr信号的传统判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究多带超导体中光学频段反常霍尔响应（anomalous Hall response, AHR）的条件，特别是澄清在纯带内配对（intraband pairing）下有限AHR是否可能产生，以及量子几何效应在其中扮演的角色，从而为时间反演对称性破缺超导体的Kerr效应（polar Kerr effect）探测提供更精确的理论判据。

Method: 采用蜂窝晶格（honeycomb lattice）上的紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），引入Kane-Mele自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），分别构建破坏时间反演对称性的手性d波自旋单态（chiral d-wave spin-singlet）和手性p波等自旋三重态（chiral p-wave equal-spin-triplet）配对态，仅考虑带内配对。通过解析推导与数值计算相结合的方式分析AHR。

Result: 自旋单态配对即使破坏时间反演对称性，AHR仍为零；而等自旋三重态（即使自旋公正，spin-unitary）却可产生有限AHR。后者由轨道非公正性（orbital nonunitarity）引起，在自旋-轨道耦合存在下生成自旋极化的Bogoliubov准粒子态，并通过受量子几何（quantum geometry）调控的带间速度矩阵元（interband velocity matrix elements）实现响应。

Conclusion: 确立了自旋公正但轨道非公正（orbitally nonunitary）的超导配对可以在无需带间配对（interband pairing）或无序的条件下产生有限AHR，从而修正了超导体中Kerr信号产生的传统判别标准。

Abstract: We investigate the anomalous Hall response (AHR) in a multiband superconductor at optical frequencies, a phenomenon intimately related to the polar Kerr effect, a key probe of time-reversal symmetry breaking in superconductors. In translationally invariant multiband systems with purely intraband pairing, Galilean invariance decouples center-of-mass and relative motion of Cooper pairs, leading to the widespread expectation that a finite AHR requires either disorder or finite interband pairing amplitudes. However, this restriction can be lifted by the quantum geometric effects inherent to multiband Bloch states. Using a honeycomb lattice tight-binding model with Kane-Mele spin-orbit coupling, we analyze the AHR for the time-reversal symmetry broken chiral $d$-wave spin-singlet and chiral $p$-wave equal-spin-triplet pairing states with intraband pairing only. We demonstrate, through both analytical and numerical calculations, that the spin-singlet state yields a vanishing AHR, even with its broken time-reversal symmetry, whereas the equal-spin triplet state exhibits a finite AHR, even when it is spin-unitary. We attribute the latter to orbital nonunitarity, which, in the presence of spin-orbit coupling, generates the spin-polarized Bogoliubov quasiparticle states required for a finite AHR. The response is mediated by interband velocity matrix elements governed by the quantum geometry. This finding establishes that spin-unitary, but orbitally nonunitary pairing, can generate a finite AHR even without interband pairing and thereby revises the criteria for Kerr signals in superconductors.

</details>


### [54] [Band-Selective Tunneling and Anisotropic Multiband Superconductivity in V$_2$Ga$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13534)
*Jozef Haniš,Jozef Kačmarčík,Filip Košuth,Levente Faber,Pavol Szabo,Szymon Królak,Michał J. Winiarski,Tomasz Klimczuk,Peter Samuely,Martin Gmitra*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过结合第一性原理计算、高灵敏度交流量热法和定向低温扫描隧道谱，对四方晶系多带超导体V₂Ga₅进行了全面研究，揭示了方向依赖的带选择性隧穿效应如何塑造多带量子凝聚体的可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有结构各向异性的多带超导体（multiband superconductor）是探索非传统量子态的重要平台，但解析其方向性配对特征（directional pairing characteristics）一直是一个重大挑战。

Method: 采用第一性原理电子结构计算（first-principles electronic structure calculation）、高灵敏度交流量热法（AC calorimetry）和定向低温扫描隧道谱（directional low-temperature scanning tunneling spectroscopy）；构建了全对称A₁g表示下的自洽各向异性多带单重态s波配对模型（self-consistent anisotropic multiband singlet s-wave pairing model）。

Result: 成功调和了实验比热（specific heat）和上临界场（upper critical field）异常；揭示了定向隧穿实验中体带隙层级（bulk gap hierarchy）的明显反转是带选择性隧穿（band-selective tunneling）的直接结果，该效应由局域费米速度“热点”（Fermi velocity hot spots）与特定费米面拓扑结构（Fermi surface topology）之间的相互作用主导，而非单纯的热力学能隙大小。

Conclusion: 为高度单轴各向异性超导体中方向依赖的带选择性隧穿提供了清晰的微观图像，展示了方向依赖的输运约束如何塑造多带量子凝聚体（multiband quantum condensate）的可观测特征。

Abstract: Multiband superconductors with structural anisotropy offer a fertile ground for exploring unconventional quantum states, yet disentangling their directional pairing characteristics remains a formidable challenge. Here, we present a comprehensive thermodynamic and spectroscopic study of the tetragonal intermetallic superconductor $\text{V}_2\text{Ga}_5$ ($T_{\rm c} \approx 3.5$~K), combining first-principles electronic structure calculations with highly sensitive AC calorimetry and directional low-temperature scanning tunneling spectroscopy. By constructing a self-consistent, anisotropic multiband singlet $s$-wave pairing model within the fully symmetric $A_{1g}$ representation, we successfully reconcile the experimental specific heat and upper critical field anomalies. Crucially, we reveal that the apparent reversal of bulk gap hierarchies in directional tunneling experiments is a direct consequence of band-selective tunneling. This effect is governed by an elegant interplay between localized Fermi velocity 'hot spots' and specific Fermi surface topologies, rather than raw thermodynamic gap magnitudes alone. Our findings provide a clear microscopic picture of direction-dependent, band-selective tunneling in a highly uniaxial anisotropic superconductor, demonstrating how orientation-dependent transport constraints shape the observable signatures of multiband quantum condensates.

</details>

### [55] [Hierarchical Interdiffusion Kinetics in Nanoscale Ni/Al Multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12553)
*S. S. Riegler,I. Gallino,N. J. Peter,A. Tarasov,T. Meyer,J. Schmauch,C. Pauly,Y. H. Sauni Camposano,H. Bartsch,R. Busch,R. Schwaiger,P. Schaaf,J. Arlt*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过快速差示扫描量热法（FDSC）与关联扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）相结合，在五个数量级的升温速率范围内解析了Ni/Al反应性金属多层膜中的纳米尺度质量传输机制，揭示了晶界（grain boundary）作为控制金属间化合物形成起始的主导传输路径，其扩散过程呈现出从晶界扩散（~81 kJ/mol）到晶格扩散（~168 kJ/mol）的分级特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度质量传输（nanoscale mass transport）决定了反应性金属多层膜中金属间化合物（intermetallic）的形成起始，但其潜在机制仍不明确。因此，本研究旨在通过实验手段解析这一早期互扩散（interdiffusion）过程，并识别关键的微观结构控制参数。

Method: 采用快速差示扫描量热法（fast differential scanning calorimetry, FDSC）对自支撑Ni/Al多层膜（双层厚度20 nm）进行表征，结合关联扫描透射电子显微镜（correlative STEM）解析早期互扩散过程；通过跨越五个数量级（0.1–10,000 K/s）的变升温速率实验，实施等转化率Kissinger-Akahira-Sunose（KAS）分析，将热流信号与微观结构演化相关联。

Result: 沉积态多层膜为纳米晶结构（nanocrystalline），Al层中已存在显著的Ni富集（premixing）。退火过程中质量传输呈现分级特征：低温阶段Ni扩散局限于Al晶界（grain boundaries），激活能约为81 kJ/mol；高温阶段晶界向晶粒内部的晶格扩散（lattice diffusion）被激活，激活能约为168 kJ/mol，导致质量传输和热释放增加。

Conclusion: 晶界被确定为控制反应性多层膜中反应起始的主导传输路径（dominant transport pathways），并可作为关键微观结构设计参数（key microstructural design parameters）。FDSC与显微术联用的策略为研究缺陷介导的传输（defect-mediated transport）和非平衡相变（non-equilibrium phase transformations）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Nanoscale mass transport governs the onset of intermetallic formation in reactive metallic multilayers, yet the underlying mechanisms remain poorly understood. Here, we combine fast differential scanning calorimetry (FDSC) of free-standing Ni/Al multilayers (20 nm bilayer thickness) with correlative STEM to resolve the early interdiffusion regime. Varying the heating rate over five orders of magnitude (0.1 to 10,000 K/s) enables isoconversional Kissinger-Akahira-Sunose (KAS) analysis, linking heat-flow signatures to microstructural evolution. The as-deposited multilayers are nanocrystalline and exhibit pronounced premixing, with significant Ni enrichment throughout the Al layers. Upon annealing, mass transport proceeds hierarchically: at low temperatures, Ni diffusion is confined to Al grain boundaries (~81 kJ/mol), while at higher temperatures lattice diffusion from grain boundaries into the grain interiors becomes active (~168 kJ/mol), leading to increased mass transport and heat release. These findings identify grain boundaries as the dominant transport pathways controlling reaction onset and as key microstructural design parameters in reactive multilayers. By providing access to transient kinetic regimes and intermediate states, the combined FDSC-microscopy approach opens new opportunities for studying defect-mediated transport and non-equilibrium phase transformations.

### [56] [Compositional gradient engineering for enhanced ferroelectricity in ultrathin AlScN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12568)
*Zekun Hu,Haiwen Zhang,Rajeev Kumar Rai,Yuhong Cao,Xiaolei Tong,Pedram Yousefian,Hyunmin Cho,Bongjun Choi,Chao-Chuan Chen,Yunfei He,Kefei Bao,Chloe Leblanc,Eric A. Stach,Roy Olsson,Deep Jariwala*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出通过组分梯度化（compositional grading）策略，在连续纤锌矿AlN-AlScN晶格中构建成分梯度异质结构，从而缓解传统铁电（ferroelectric）AlScN薄膜在厚度缩小时因漏电、过早击穿和缺陷介导失效带来的限制。实验表明，20 nm梯度异质结构在保持铁电开关特性的同时，击穿场强提升21%，剩余极化增强10%，电阻率提高40倍；甚至在仅含2 nm铁电区的5 nm堆叠中仍可实现接近1 V的可测开关行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电AlScN在CMOS兼容非易失性存储器（non-volatile memory）方面具有应用前景，但其厚度缩小受限于漏电、过早击穿和缺陷介导的失效。这些限制阻碍了超薄铁电器件向可规模化方向的发展，亟需一种有效的缺陷与电场管理策略。

Method: 在连续纤锌矿AlN-AlScN晶格内引入组分梯度（compositional gradient），利用单调的Sc掺入和富AlN边界分布在薄膜厚度方向上的结构和极化不连续性，以减少缺陷形成和局部电场集中，从而制备20 nm及5 nm的梯度异质结构。

Result: 20 nm梯度异质结构实现了可逆铁电开关、固有的金属极化（metal-polar）初始态、击穿场强提升21%、剩余极化增强10%以及电阻率相比均质AlScN提高40倍。时域PUND（Positive Up Negative Down）测量显示后开关漏电显著抑制，表明缺陷辅助和极化耦合的导电被有效降低。在仅含2 nm Al₀.₆₄Sc₀.₃₆N铁电区的5 nm梯度堆叠中仍可观察到接近1 V的可测开关行为。

Conclusion: 组分梯度化可作为可扩展超薄纤锌矿铁电体的一种缺陷管理与电场管理策略（defect- and field-management strategy），有效提升铁电薄膜的介电鲁棒性（dielectric robustness），为在更小厚度尺度实现可靠铁电功能提供新途径。

Abstract: Ferroelectric AlScN is promising for CMOS-compatible non-volatile memory, but thickness scaling is limited by leakage, premature breakdown, and defect-mediated failure. Here we show that compositional grading within a continuous wurtzite AlN-AlScN lattice mitigates these limitations by distributing structural and polarization discontinuities across the film thickness, reducing defect formation and local field concentration. In a 20 nm graded heterostructure, monotonic Sc incorporation and AlN-rich boundaries produce reversible ferroelectric switching, an as-grown metal-polar state, a 21% higher breakdown field, 10% enhanced remanent polarization, and 40x higher resistivity relative to homogeneous AlScN. Time-domain PUND measurements reveal strongly suppressed post-switching leakage, consistent with reduced defect-assisted and polarization-coupled conduction. This improved dielectric robustness enables ferroelectric functionality in 5 nm graded stacks containing only a 2 nm $\mathrm{Al}_{0.64}\mathrm{Sc}_{0.36}\mathrm{N}$ region, with measurable switching near 1 V. These results establish compositional grading as a defect- and field-management strategy for scalable ultrathin wurtzite ferroelectrics.

</details>


### [57] [Computationally efficient method for determining limiting velocities of edge dislocations in anisotropic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12591)
*Daniel N. Blaschke*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 针对刃型位错（edge dislocation）在反射对称（reflection symmetry）但弹性常数 $c'_{16}$ 或 $c'_{26}$ 非零这一特殊情形下，原有计算极限速度（limiting velocity）的方法计算缓慢的问题，本文推导出了一种计算高效的求解方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体中位错的连续极限理论（continuum-limit theory）预测弹性能在晶体几何依赖的极限速度 $v_L$ 处出现发散，这些速度将位错滑移划分为亚音速、跨音速和超音速三个区间，对高应变率下的材料强度模型至关重要。然而，对于反射对称但弹性常数 $c'_{16}$ 或 $c'_{26}$ 非零的刃型位错这一特例，已有方法计算极限速度的速度极慢，需要加以改进。

Method: 本文推导了一种计算高效的解析方法，用于确定具有反射对称性的刃型位错的极限速度。

Result: 新方法显著提升了此前在该特殊情形下计算缓慢的问题的效率，使得能够快速确定相关极限速度 $v_L$。

Conclusion: 该工作弥补了位错连续极限理论中一个特定的计算缺陷，为高应变率下材料强度模型的构建提供了更高效的理论工具。

Abstract: The continuum-limit theory of dislocations in crystals predicts divergences in the elastic energy at crystal-geometry dependent limiting velocities $v_L$, which separate subsonic, transsonic, and supersonic dislocation glide regimes and are therefore import for material strength models at high strain rates. Although it is known how to calculate those limiting velocities, there is one special case - edge dislocations with reflection symmetry, but non-vanishing elastic constants $c'_{16}$ or $c'_{26}$ - where previous methods have been notoriously slow. In this letter, we address this deficiency by deriving a computationally efficient method for determining the limiting velocities of edge dislocations with reflection symmetry.

### [58] [Resolving Finite-Size Errors in EOM-CCSD Band Gaps of Solids with Interacting-Bath Dynamical Embedding Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12621)
*Jiachen Li,Christopher Hillenbrand,Christian Venturella,Enzhi Chen,Tianyu Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该工作采用可系统改进的格林函数嵌入框架ibDET，大幅提升周期性EOM-CCSD计算的布里渊区采样密度（最高至10×10×10），显著降低了有限尺寸误差，获得了比G₀W₀@PBE更准确（MAE=0.27 eV）的半导体和绝缘体带隙值，并展示了ibDET作为周期性高精度多体电子结构计算实用路径的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性EOM-CCSD理论在固体能带结构定量计算方面具有潜力，但因其计算标度（computational scaling）陡峭，只能使用较粗的k点网格（k-point mesh），导致有限尺寸误差（finite-size error）较大，不同基准测试对热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）带隙的估算存在明显分歧。因此，需要一种方法能够在可接受的计算成本下实现密集布里渊区采样（Brillouin-zone sampling），以减小有限尺寸效应并可靠地外推到热力学极限。

Method: 采用可系统改进的相互作用浴动力学嵌入理论（interacting-bath dynamical embedding theory, ibDET）作为格林函数嵌入框架（Green's function embedding framework），以适中的计算成本实现密集的布里渊区采样（最高至10×10×10的k点网格），对十种半导体和绝缘体的带隙进行EOM-CCSD计算，并与G₀W₀@PBE和G₀W₀@HF在同一数值设置下（PySCF）进行公平比较。

Result: 通过将k点采样提升至10×10×10（远超传统周期性EOM-CCSD可及的系统尺寸），显著降低了有限尺寸误差，获得了稳定的热力学极限外推（thermodynamic-limit extrapolation）。EOM-CCSD在十种半导体和绝缘体测试集上的平均绝对误差（mean absolute error, MAE）为0.27 eV，优于G₀W₀@PBE。对于ZnO，EOM-CCSD准确描述了Zn 3d带结合能（binding energy），尽管在带隙上存在高估。

Conclusion: ibDET为周期性系统中的高精度多体电子结构计算（many-body electronic structure calculations）提供了一条实用路径，能够在保持EOM-CCSD精度的同时有效克服其计算成本瓶颈。

Abstract: Periodic equation-of-motion coupled-cluster theory with single and double excitations (EOM-CCSD) has shown promise for quantitative calculations of band structures in solids. However, its steep computational scaling has limited calculations to relatively coarse $k$-point meshes, leading to sizable finite-size errors and discrepant estimates of thermodynamic-limit band gaps in recent benchmarks. In this work, we revisit EOM-CCSD band gaps for ten semiconductors and insulators using interacting-bath dynamical embedding theory (ibDET), a systematically improvable Green's function embedding framework that enables dense Brillouin-zone sampling at modest computational cost. By pushing the $k$-point sampling up to $10\times10\times10$, well beyond the system sizes accessible in canonical periodic EOM-CCSD calculations, we significantly reduce finite-size errors and obtain stable thermodynamic-limit extrapolations. We further compare $G_0W_0$@PBE, $G_0W_0$@HF, and EOM-CCSD on an equal footing using the same numerical settings in PySCF. We find that EOM-CCSD yields a mean absolute error of 0.27 eV relative to experimental band gaps for a test set of ten semiconductors and insulators, lower than that of $G_0W_0$@PBE. For ZnO, EOM-CCSD also accurately describes the Zn $3d$-band binding energy, despite overestimating the band gap. These results demonstrate that ibDET offers a practical route to high-accuracy many-body electronic structure calculations in periodic systems.

</details>


### [59] [Lock-In Infrared Thermography: Phase Analysis for Rapid, Wide-Range Thermal Conductivity Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12625)
*Ethan A. Scott,Jeffrey L. Braun,Jessica Reyes,Bruce Bolliger,Terrence Soares,John T. Gaskins,Marko J. Tadjer,Patrick E. Hopkins*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于相位锁定热成像（phase-based lock-in thermography）并结合多层热模型（multilayered thermal model）的非接触式方法，用于测量块体材料和层状结构的热导率（thermal conductivity）。该方法通过红外相机监测材料的热相位分布，并与热模型拟合以提取热导率参数，无需接触样品前表面且对表面粗糙度不敏感。通过测量热导率跨越三个数量级（约1 W/m/K 到 >2000 W/m/K）的材料，验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一种非接触、前表面可测、对表面粗糙度不敏感的热导率测量方法，且不严格依赖换能层（transducer layer）的应用，以满足不同材料体系（包括块体和层状结构）的热物性表征需求。

Method: 将相位锁定热成像（phase-based lock-in thermography）与常用于热反射分析（thermoreflectance analysis）的多层热模型相结合。利用红外相机锁定调制激光加热频率，监测材料热相位（thermal phase）的空间分布，然后通过热模型拟合该相位分布，以热导率等性质作为拟合参数进行提取。

Result: 成功测量了热导率跨度超过三个数量级（约1 W/m/K 到 >2000 W/m/K）的材料。同时指出，虽然该方法不严格需要使用换能层，但在实际应用中，施加可移除的粘附层（adhesive layer）作为近表面吸收层具有实用优势。

Conclusion: 该方法为非接触、前表面热导率测量提供了一种可行方案，具有对表面粗糙度不敏感且无需换能层的优点，能够适用于热导率范围极宽的材料。

Abstract: We report on a phase-based lock-in thermography approach, combined with a multilayered thermal model (often employed in thermoreflectance analysis), to measure the thermal conductivity of bulk materials and layered structures. The spatial distribution of the material's thermal phase is monitored with an infrared camera, which is locked into the frequency of a modulated laser used to heat the material. This phase distribution is then fit with a thermal model, in which properties such as thermal conductivity are extracted as fit parameters. This approach enables non-contact, front-side measurements, which are insensitive to surface roughness. The technique does not strictly require the application of a transducer layer, but we highlight the practical benefits of applying a removable adhesive layer to serve as a near-surface absorber. We demonstrate the efficacy of the method by measuring materials with thermal conductivities that span over three orders of magnitude (approximately 1 W/m/K to > 2000 W/m/K).

</details>


### [60] [Site Preferences and "Coloring Problem" in Cu-doped BiMn$_7$O$_{12}$ Quadruple Perovskite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12711)
*Cheng Peng,Mingyu Xu,Yang Zhang,Ismail El Baggari,Jie Li,Weiwei Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过高浓度Cu掺杂（x=0.05, 0.10, 0.15）研究了BiMn₇O₁₂四重钙钛矿（quadruple perovskite）体系。Cu取代抑制了单斜畸变，引入局域结构无序，并削弱了低温磁态。第一性原理计算与实验精修在Cu占位方面存在分歧，揭示了高度阻挫体系中的局域键合与亚稳性竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究轻量Cu掺杂对BiMn₇O₁₂四重钙钛矿体系中结构与磁性的影响，特别是在高度几何阻挫（geometric frustration）背景下Cu的择优占位及其引发的局域无序行为。

Method: 采用高压合成、单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal X-ray diffraction）、对分布函数（pair distribution function, PDF）分析、扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）、磁性测量和第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）等多种手段进行表征。

Result: 所有掺杂组分保持平均单斜I2/m结构，但Cu取代逐渐抑制单斜畸变，驱向赝立方对称；PDF分析显示局域结构无序增强、中程相干性降低；单晶精修表明Cu优先占据八面体Mn位（B位），而非Cu²⁺通常占据的平面正方形位点（square-planar site）；磁性测量显示两个特征异常（T₁~100-120 K，T₂~50-60 K）及显著磁不可逆性与场相关磁滞；Cu浓度升高抑制了低温磁态并削弱场致磁矩；第一性原理计算却偏好Cu占据平面正方形位点，与实验精修结果相悖。

Conclusion: Cu掺杂在四重钙钛矿体系中引发了局域键合、短程无序与亚稳性（metastability）之间的强烈竞争，导致实验占位与理论预测出现分歧；这一体系为研究高度阻挫氧化物中的无序效应与磁态调控提供了重要模型。

Abstract: Lightly Cu-doped BiMn$_7$O$_{12}$ (x = 0.05, 0.10, and 0.15) was investigated using high-pressure synthesis, single-crystal X-ray diffraction, pair distribution function (PDF) analysis, STEM, magnetic measurements, and first-principles calculations. All compositions retain an average monoclinic $I$2/$m$ structure, while Cu substitution progressively suppresses the monoclinic distortion and drives the lattice toward a pseudo-cubic metric symmetry. PDF analysis reveals increasing local structural disorder and reduced medium-range coherence with increasing Cu concentration, despite preservation of the overall quadruple-perovskite framework. Single-crystal refinements indicate enhanced electron density at the octahedral Mn B sites, suggesting preferential Cu occupation within the MnO$_6$ network rather than the conventional square-planar sites expected for Cu$^{2+}$. Magnetic measurements reveal two characteristic anomalies near $T_1$ ~ 100-120 K and $T_2$ ~ 50-60 K, together with pronounced magnetic irreversibility, field-dependent hysteresis, and unsaturated magnetization. Increasing Cu concentration progressively suppresses the low-temperature magnetic state and weakens the field-induced moment. First-principles calculations favor Cu occupation at the square-planar sites, contrasting with the experimental refinements and highlighting strong competitions among local bonding, short-range disorder, and metastability in this highly frustrated quadruple perovskite system.

</details>


### [61] [Extending the La Solubility Limit in Sr$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$ through High-Pressure High-Temperature Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12727)
*Cheng Peng,Weiwei Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究采用高压高温技术成功合成了La掺杂双层铱氧化物(Sr1-xLax)3Ir2O7，将La的实际掺入量大幅提升至x≈0.23。研究发现，在中等掺杂(x≈0.11)时体系表现为铁磁类似转变且保持强绝缘性，而在高掺杂(x≈0.23)时则呈现类金属电子行为但低温仍存在局域化效应，揭示了常压合成无法达到的新电子态和磁态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: La掺杂双层铱氧化物(Sr1-xLax)3Ir2O7是研究电子掺杂下自旋-轨道耦合辅助莫特态（spin-orbit-assisted Mott state）演化的重要平台，但常压合成中La的溶解度有限，限制了可研究的掺杂范围。

Method: 采用高压高温技术合成名义组分为(Sr1-xLax)3Ir2O7（x=0.05, 0.10, 0.15, 0.20）的多晶样品；利用单晶X射线衍射精修（single-crystal X-ray diffraction refinements）结合扫描电子显微镜-能量色散X射线能谱（SEM-EDX）确定实际组分；通过磁化率、电阻率等测量表征物理性质。

Result: 高压合成显著提升了La的实际掺入量：名义x=0.05和0.15对应实际组分为(Sr0.89La0.11)3Ir2O7和(Sr0.77La0.23)3Ir2O7；名义x=0.20时双层相失稳转变为立方钙钛矿Sr1-xLaxIrO3。(Sr0.89La0.11)3Ir2O7在186 K附近出现铁磁类似（ferromagnetic-like）转变，伴随磁滞回线和晶格异常，体系保持强绝缘性。(Sr0.77La0.23)3Ir2O7呈现类金属电子行为、磁有序减弱和载流子离域化增强，但低温下仍存在无序驱动局域化（disorder-driven localization）。

Conclusion: 高压合成技术可大幅扩展双层铱氧化物的有效掺杂范围，揭示出常压合成无法获得的电子态和磁态，为理解强自旋-轨道耦合体系中电子掺杂效应提供了新的实验平台。

Abstract: La-doped bilayer iridates provide an important platform for studying the evolution of the spin-orbit-assisted Mott state under electron doping, but the La solubility achieved by conventional ambient-pressure synthesis is limited. Here, we report the synthesis and physical properties of nominally La-doped (Sr$_{1-x}$La$_x$)$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$ (x = 0.05, 0.10, 0.15, and 0.20) prepared using high-pressure high-temperature techniques. Single-crystal X-ray diffraction refinements, supported by scanning electron microscopy-energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy (SEM-EDX), reveal significantly enhanced La incorporation, with nominal x = 0.05 and 0.15 corresponding to actual compositions of approximately (Sr$_{0.89}$La$_{0.11}$)$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$ and (Sr$_{0.77}$La$_{0.23}$)$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$, respectively. At nominal x = 0.20, the bilayer phase is no longer stabilized and instead transforms into cubic perovskite Sr$_{1-x}$La$_x$IrO$_3$. (Sr$_{0.89}$La$_{0.11}$)$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$ exhibits a ferromagnetic-like transition near 186 K accompanied by magnetic hysteresis and subtle lattice anomalies indicative of spin-lattice coupling. Despite its high electron-doping level, the compound remains strongly insulating, consistent with a heavily doped localized magnetic insulating state distinct from both parent Sr$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$ and ambient-pressure La-doped samples. In contrast, (Sr$_{0.77}$La$_{0.23}$)$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$ displays metal-like electronic behavior, weakened magnetic order, and enhanced carrier delocalization, although disorder-driven localization persists at low temperatures. These results demonstrate that high-pressure synthesis substantially extends the accessible doping range of bilayer iridates and reveals electronic and magnetic states inaccessible through conventional synthesis routes.

### [62] [Water Flow Through Polar and Non-Polar Nanopores: Insights from Multiscale Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12743)
*Elizane E. de Moraes,João Victor Lemos Valle,Bruno H. S. Mendonça,Ernane de Freitas Martins,Hélio Chacham,Pablo Ordejón*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过多尺度模拟（multiscale simulations）发现，六方氮化硼（hBN）纳米多孔膜的水通量显著高于石墨烯膜。这种增强的流动源于hBN孔的不对称结构诱导出电偶极矩（electric dipole moment），而石墨烯孔的对称性使其呈非极性特征。量子力学/分子力学（QM/MM）模拟进一步表明，水的存在会增强hBN孔的偶极矩，导致水分子在孔口出现强有序结构，而石墨烯孔附近水分子则呈随机分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球水资源压力日益严峻，亟需开发高效、选择性好的先进膜材料用于水过滤与输运。二维纳米多孔膜（two-dimensional nanoporous membranes）为研究极端限域条件下原子尺度结构与电子极化如何调控水流的机制提供了理想平台。

Method: 采用多尺度模拟（multiscale simulations），包括经典分子动力学模拟（classical molecular dynamics simulations）、量子力学计算（quantum-mechanical calculations）以及混合量子力学/分子力学模拟（hybrid QM/MM simulations），系统研究水流经石墨烯和六方氮化硼（hBN）纳米孔的行为。

Result: hBN膜的水通量显著高于石墨烯膜。量子力学计算证实hBN孔的不对称结构诱导出电偶极矩；经典分子动力学显示水分子在石墨烯孔附近呈随机无择优取向分布，而在hBN孔附近则形成强有序结构。QM/MM模拟进一步表明，水的存在使hBN孔的偶极矩增大；石墨烯孔则因对称性始终呈非极性特征。

Conclusion: hBN纳米孔的不对称极性与石墨烯孔的对称非极性导致二者截然不同的水输运特性，这些发现为设计先进纳滤膜（nanofiltration membranes）提供了重要的原子尺度设计依据。

Abstract: Global water stress has emerged as a critical challenge, driving the search for advanced membrane materials that enable efficient, selective water filtration and transport. In this context, two-dimensional nanoporous membranes provide an ideal platform to elucidate how atomic-scale structure and electronic polarization govern water flow under extreme confinement. In this study, we employ multiscale simulations to investigate the effect of water flow through nanopores in graphene and hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) membranes. Our results reveal significantly higher water flow in hBN membranes than in graphene. This enhanced flow is attributed to the asymmetry of the hBN pores, which induces an electric dipole moment, as confirmed by quantum-mechanical (QM) calculations. Classical molecular dynamics simulations further demonstrate that water molecules exhibit a random distribution with no preferential orientation near the graphene pores, whereas hBN induces strong structuring. Furthermore, hybrid quantum mechanics/molecular mechanics (QM/MM) simulations indicate that the dipole moment of the hBN pore increases in the presence of water, as evidenced by the average charge distribution. Conversely, the symmetric nature of graphene pores results in non-polar characteristics, as verified by both QM/MM and QM calculations. These findings provide valuable insights into the distinct water-transport properties when flowing through graphene and hBN nanopores, with potential implications for designing advanced nanofiltration membranes.

### [63] [Intrinsic Ductility from Shear Amorphization: From Pure Metals to Multi-Principal-Element Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12750)
*Morgan R. Jones,Duane D. Johnson,Nicolas Argibay*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将电子结构复杂性与本征延性直接关联的理论框架，利用非晶化激活能密度作为更低能量的断裂判据，统一解释了纯金属和固溶合金的延性流动，并通过Nb-Ta-V-Ti体系验证了该框架在多主元合金快速设计中的实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子结构与金属本征延性（intrinsic ductility）之间的直接联系长期以来难以建立，现有方法多依赖预存裂纹尖端的解理与位错形核，缺乏一个统一的、低能量断裂判据来描述延性行为。

Method: 通过将价电荷分布（valence charge distribution）、能带填充（band filling）和剪切应变效应简化为结构-性能关系，提出以非晶化激活能密度（activation energy density for amorphization）作为断裂判据，并结合解析表达式、从头算刚度常数、晶格参数和二元相互作用能构建统一理论。

Result: 该框架能够准确预测本征延性及韧脆转变温度（ductile-to-brittle transition temperature），并在Nb-Ta-V-Ti四元体系中生成了相图，同时解释了该体系的高强度与室温拉伸延性。

Conclusion: 该理论框架可作为结构多主元合金（multi-principal-element alloys）快速设计的实用工具，为金属延性预测提供了一种无需依赖传统裂纹尖端机制的新途径。

Abstract: Direct links between electronic structure and intrinsic ductility remain elusive for metals. A framework is proposed that reduces the complexities of valence charge distribution, band filling, and shear strain effects into structure-property relationships describing the intrinsic ductility of metals and alloys. Rather than relying on crystal cleavage and dislocation nucleation at preexisting crack tips, we show that a lower energy fracture criterion, i.e., the activation energy density for amorphization, enables accurate predictions of both intrinsic ductility and ductile-to-brittle transition temperatures. From analytical expressions and tabulated ab-initio stiffness constants, lattice parameters, and binary interaction energies, we present a unified theory that reconciles ductile flow in pure metals and solid-solution alloys. Phase diagrams generated for the Nb-Ta-V-Ti system simultaneously explain its high strength and room-temperature tensile ductility, validating this framework as a practical one for rapid design of structural multi-principal-element alloys.

### [64] [Molecular reference corrections for quantum Monte Carlo adsorption energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12779)
*Roman Fanta,Michal Bajdich*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了单行列式固定节点扩散蒙特卡洛（SD-FNDMC）在表面热化学计算中因分子参考态电子结构误差不可迁移导致的系统性偏差，并提出一种混合热化学循环，通过将分子形成贡献替换为耦合簇基准（coupled cluster reference）来修正该偏差，在Pt(111)和Cu(111)表面算例中验证了该方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确的表面热化学计算依赖于扩展板层（extended slabs）与分子参考态（molecular reference states）之间误差的平衡抵消；然而，当电子结构误差在热力学循环中涉及的化学物种间不可迁移时，这种平衡会失效。本文旨在诊断并修正单行列式固定节点扩散蒙特卡洛（SD-FNDMC）中因分子参考态不平衡引入的系统性偏差。

Method: 提出了一个混合热化学循环（hybrid cycle），将表面吸附结合能保留在SD-FNDMC级别，而将分子形成贡献替换为高精度的耦合簇（coupled cluster）基准参考。

Result: 对于Pt(111)表面的O和OH，修正较小；对OOH修正较大；几何匹配修正仅起次要作用。将其应用于Cu(111)表面的HCO和COH时，修正符号相反，表明偏差主要由分子参考态的电子结构控制，而非仅由吸附物几何结构决定。

Conclusion: 分子参考态不平衡是SD-FNDMC表面热化学中一个可分离的误差来源；所提出的混合循环在不修改SD-FNDMC板层吸附结合贡献的前提下，有效降低了该偏差。

Abstract: Accurate surface thermochemistry requires balanced error cancellation between extended slabs and molecular reference states. This balance can fail whenever the electronic-structure error is not transferable across the chemically distinct species entering a thermodynamic cycle. Here we examine this problem in single-determinant fixed-node diffusion Monte Carlo (SD-FNDMC) for oxygenated ORR intermediates on Pt(111). Gas-phase thermochemistry is used to diagnose the reference-state imbalance, and a hybrid cycle is introduced to separate slab-adsorbate binding from molecular formation. The hybrid cycle keeps the surface binding term at the SD-FNDMC level, where cancellation is expected to be most favorable, and replaces the molecular formation contribution with a benchmark coupled cluster reference. For Pt(111), the resulting correction is small for O and OH but larger for OOH, while the geometry-matched refinement gives only a secondary correction. Applying the same cycle to HCO and COH on Cu(111) gives corrections of opposite sign, showing that the bias is controlled primarily by the electronic structure of the molecular reference rather than by adsorbate geometry alone. This decomposition identifies molecular reference imbalance as a separable source of error in SD-FNDMC surface thermochemistry and reduces the corresponding bias without modifying the SD-FNDMC slab-binding contribution.

</details>


### [65] [A wrong ground-state structure of HfO$_2$ predicted by machine-learning interatomic potentials based on the PBE functional](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12811)
*Shuqi Tang,Jinchen Wei,Kang Wang,Junjie Zhou,Yihan Zhang,Menglin Huang,Shiyou Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现，基于PBE泛函密度泛函理论数据集训练的机器学习原子间势能（MLIP）错误地将HfO2的I41/amd结构预测为比已知基态单斜P21/c结构更稳定，该错误源于PBE泛函对含六配位Hf-O八面体单元的低密度结构的过度稳定化，而使用PBEsol或局部密度近似等泛函可有效抑制该误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势能（machine-learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）在材料模拟中广泛使用，但基于特定交换关联泛函（exchange-correlation functional）训练可能引入系统性误差，需评估其对晶体结构预测可靠性的影响。

Method: 使用基于Perdew-Burke-Ernzerhof (PBE) 泛函的MLIP对HfO2进行结构预测，并与实验已知基态及PBE基底层模型（如NequIP-OAM-L、MatterSim-v1-5M）进行对比，同时比较不同密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）泛函的计算结果。

Result: PBE泛函的MLIP预测了一个先前未被报道的I41/amd低能结构，其稳定性高于实验基态的P21/c结构，该错误同样出现在广泛使用的PBE基底层模型中。误差根源在于PBE泛函过度稳定了含六配位Hf-O八面体单元的低密度结构（如I41/amd和Pbcn相），并影响了沿铁电HfO2极化切换路径的能量景观和势垒高度。

Conclusion: 交换关联泛函近似中的误差会显著影响MLIP对晶体结构和相变模拟的可靠性，但这类误差可通过使用PBEsol或局部密度近似（local density approximation, LDA）等其他泛函在很大程度上得到抑制。

Abstract: Machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have become powerful tools for material simulations. Many MLIPs are trained based on density functional theory (DFT) datasets generated with the Perdew-Burke-Ernzerhof (PBE) exchange-correlation functional. Using a PBE-based MLIP for HfO2, we identify a previously unreported low-energy I41/amd structure, which is predicted to be more stable than the well-known ground-state structure, the monoclinic P21/c structure. Since experiments show clearly that HfO2 takes the P21/c structure as the ground state, this is obviously a wrong prediction. Unfortunately, the same prediction is also made by widely used PBE-based foundation models such as NequIP-OAM-L and MatterSim-v1-5M. Comparisons among different DFT functionals show that this error originates from the PBE functional, which overstabilizes low-density structures containing sixfold Hf-O octahedral units, such as the I41/amd and Pbcn phases. The error also affects the calculated energy landscapes and barrier heights along ferroelectric HfO2 polarization switching paths when there are large lattice relaxations. Fortunately, the error can be largely suppressed by other functionals such as PBEsol and local density approximation. Our study serves as a warning about the impact of errors in exchange-correlation functional approximations on the reliability of MLIP simulations of crystal structures and phase transitions.

### [66] [Leveraging rapid sintering to retain metastable zirconia in copper](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12860)
*Wangshu Zheng,Xi Chen,Xuyang Feng,Aiji Zou,Andrew Yun Ru Ng,Xiaoqing Wang,Zhili Dong,Qiang Guo,Chee Lip Gan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚稳陶瓷与延性金属复合的金属陶瓷有望兼具高韧性与高强度，但亚稳态的保留通常需要高温烧结，而这会导致微观结构粗化（microstructural coarsening）和基体约束松弛（matrix relaxation），形成trade-off。

Method: 采用超快高温烧结（UHS）策略，以约100°C/s的升温速率加热至900°C并仅保温20秒，利用焦耳加热（Joule heating）实现快速烧结。

Result: 在室温下成功获得含有高达50 wt%亚稳态奥氏体的氧化锆-铜金属陶瓷，微观结构呈现细晶且均匀的特征。

Conclusion: 超快烧结动力学有利于半热奥氏体（semi-thermal austenite）的形成，同时抑制铜晶粒生长和基体松弛，从而稳定高温相并保持微结构细化。该方法对基于铜的复合材料在相变增韧（transformation toughening）、自愈合（self-healing）和裂纹检测（crack detection）等应用中具有重要潜力。

Abstract: Cermets combining metastable ceramics and ductile metals promise superior toughness and strength. However, retaining metastability often requires high-temperature sintering that coarsens microstructures and relaxes matrix constraint. Here we introduce an ultrafast high-temperature sintering (UHS) strategy to overcome this trade-off in zirconia-copper cermets. By applying Joule heating at around 100 degrees C per second to 900 degrees C with only a 20 second hold, we obtained cermets containing up to 50 weight percent of metastable austenite in zirconia at room temperature within a fine-grained and homogeneous microstructure. The rapid sintering kinetically favors semi-thermal austenite formation while suppressing copper grain growth and matrix relaxation, thereby stabilizing the high-temperature phase and simultaneously preserving microstructural refinement. This approach offers significant potential for copper-based composites in applications such as transformation toughening, self-healing, and crack detection.

Abstract: The development of batteries with high energy density, short charging times and use of sustainable materials is critical for decarbonization. However, microstructural modifications induced by Li-alloying and their influence on battery operation remain elusive. Here, we unveil the previously unknown formation of an ordered B2 phase, which creates a conditional spinodal decomposition with the \b{eta}-body-centered cubic phase. ### [68] [Observation of orbital-angular-momentum-driven temperature modulation via the spin Peltier effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12992)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 角动量输运为超越传统电荷机制的能量流控制提供了新途径。尽管自旋电流（spin current）已知可介导自旋-量热电子学现象（如自旋佩尔捷效应），但轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）在热输运中的作用此前基本未被探索。

Method: 采用钇铁石榴石（yttrium iron garnet, YIG）/Pt/CuOx异质结构，制备楔形CuOx层并结合空间分辨主动热测量（spatially resolved active thermal measurement）技术，连续映射厚度依赖性，并在同一器件中定量分离自旋电流与轨道电流介导的贡献。

Result: 轨道介导的组分在中间厚度处呈现显著峰值，揭示了Cu/CuOx界面处轨道角动量产生与传播的特征长度尺度（characteristic length scale）。

Conclusion: 这些结果提供了直接实验证据，证明电荷流驱动的轨道角动量能够驱动自旋佩尔捷效应引起的温度调制，将界面轨道过程确立为热输运的额外通道，并为自旋-轨道量热电子学（spin-orbit caloritronics）提供了实现路径。

Abstract: Angular-momentum transport provides a pathway for controlling energy flow in solids beyond conventional charge-based mechanisms. While spin currents are known to mediate spin-caloritronic phenomena such as the spin Peltier effect (SPE), the role of orbital angular momentum in heat transport remains largely unexplored. Here we demonstrate orbital-angular-momentum-driven temperature modulation via the SPE in yttrium iron garnet/Pt/CuOx heterostructures. Using wedge-shaped CuOx layers combined with spatially resolved active thermal measurement techniques, we map the continuous thickness dependence and quantitatively disentangle the spin- and orbital-current-mediated contributions within a single device. The orbital-mediated component exhibits a pronounced maximum at an intermediate thickness, revealing a characteristic length scale for interfacial orbital-angular-momentum generation and propagation at the Cu/CuOx interface. These results provide direct experimental evidence that charge-current-driven orbital angular momentum can drive SPE-induced temperature modulation, establishing interfacial orbital processes as an additional channel for heat transport and providing a pathway toward spin-orbit caloritronics.

</details>


### [69] [A Geometric Design Principle for $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Topological Phases in Twisted Triangular-Lattice Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13015)
*Jiaheng Li,Jiaxuan Liu,Yan Zhang,Zhong Fang,Hongming Weng,Quansheng Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了扭转型三角晶格双层材料中，堆叠重构（stacking reconstruction）可自然产生蜂巢（honeycomb）莫尔超晶格，并通过几何调控实现时间反演不变的拓扑能带，以BiTeBr为例展示了具有非平庸Z₂指数的Γ谷莫尔价带，并通过外电场实现拓扑-平庸相变。该机制在多种三角晶格双层中均得到验证，提供了一条普适的、由几何控制的可电调莫尔量子自旋霍尔材料设计路径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 文章提出了一种基于几何驱动的设计原理：在三角晶格双层中，扭转与弛豫（relaxation）协同作用，将堆叠能（stacking-energy）景观中对称性相关的最小值提升为蜂巢莫尔晶格的两套子格。通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析BiTeBr的Γ谷莫尔价带，并构建四带瓦尼尔哈密顿量（four-band Wannier Hamiltonian）将其映射到扩展的Kane-Mele模型上。此外，还验证了其他代表性三角晶格双层材料。

Result: BiTeBr在多个转角范围内均展现出具有非平庸Z₂拓扑指数的Γ谷莫尔价带。外电场通过增强Rashba耦合（Rashba coupling）λ_R相对于内禀Kane-Mele耦合λ_SO的比值，驱动体系从拓扑相转变为平庸相。对于其他代表性三角晶格双层材料，相同的蜂巢重构和Kane-Mele机制均得到验证。

Conclusion: 堆叠重构（stacking reconstruction）是一种由几何控制、普适性强的材料设计路径，可用于制备电可调的莫尔量子自旋霍尔（moiré quantum spin Hall）材料。

Abstract: Twisted van der Waals bilayers provide a versatile platform for engineering moiré electronic states, yet a general design principle for time-reversal-invariant topological moiré bands remains elusive. Here, we establish a geometry-driven principle for triangular-lattice bilayers: symmetry-related minima of the stacking-energy landscape are promoted by twist and relaxation into the two sublattices of an emergent honeycomb moiré lattice. First-principles calculations for BiTeBr reveal robust $Γ$-valley moiré valence bands with a nontrivial $\mathbb{Z}_2$ index over a range of twist angles. A four-band Wannier Hamiltonian in the emergent honeycomb basis quantitatively maps these bands onto an extended Kane--Mele model. An out-of-plane electric field drives a transition to a trivial phase by enhancing the Rashba coupling $λ_R$ relative to the intrinsic Kane--Mele coupling $λ_{\rm SO}$. The same honeycomb reconstruction and Kane--Mele mechanism are verified in representative additional triangular-lattice bilayers, establishing stacking reconstruction as a general, geometry-controlled route to electrically tunable moiré quantum spin Hall materials.

### [70] [Holonomy Analysis of Optical-polarization Temperature Trajectories in Stress-induced Ferroelectric SrTiO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13074)
*Hirotaka Manaka,Kazuma Seike,Yoko Miura*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种数据驱动的几何框架（data-induced geometric framework），用于分析光学偏振（optical-polarization）数据中的温度轨迹（temperature trajectories），并将其应用于应力诱导铁电钛酸锶（SrTiO₃）的温致双折射成像（temperature-dependent birefringence imaging）。通过奇异值分解（singular value decomposition, SVD）分离出与偏振方向结构和温度演化模式相关的几何对象，并利用这些对象在实空间闭环上的输运定义和乐（holonomy）。和乐图揭示了与增强铁电转变温度及应力相关光学各向异性（optical anisotropy）对应的空间局域连接失配（connection mismatches），从而无需显式重构隐藏的应变或电极化场，即可诊断SrTiO₃中的力电不均匀性（electromechanical inhomogeneity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以直接通过光学测量明确诊断应力诱导铁电材料中的力电不均匀性，传统分析往往需要显式重构隐藏的应变或电极化场（strain or electric-polarization fields）。本文旨在发展一种基于测量数据本身诱导出的几何结构，从实验可测的光学偏振响应中提取关于铁电转变温度增强和应力相关各向异性的空间分布信息，而不依赖对隐藏场的直接反演。

Method: 将每个像素处的光学偏振响应沿温度轴视为一条轨迹（trajectory），并利用奇异值分解（SVD）将轨迹诱导的几何对象（geometry objects）分解为与光学偏振方向结构（optical-polarization-direction structure）相关的部分和与温度演化模式（temperature-evolution modes）相关的部分。随后通过将这些几何对象在实空间闭环上平行输运（transport）来定义和乐（holonomy），从而获得空间连接结构（connection structure）的映射。

Result: 和乐图显示出空间局域化的连接失配（connection mismatches），这些失配与增强的铁电转变温度（ferroelectric transition temperature）和应力相关光学各向异性在空间上相关。局域序参量（local order parameters）和角度梯度分析（angular-gradient analyses）确认，这些闭环尺度的信号区别于取向无序（orientational disorder）和简单空间变化。对温度演化模式的有符号和乐（signed holonomy）进一步在固定框架约定（fixed frame convention）下区分了正、负连接结构。

Conclusion: 数据诱导的温度轨迹连接几何（connection geometry of temperature trajectories）为诊断应力下SrTiO₃中的力电不均匀性提供了一种实验可及的分析工具，无需显式重构隐藏的应变或电极化场。该方法有望推广至其他具有类似温度依赖响应的材料体系。

Abstract: We develop a data-induced geometric framework for temperature trajectories in optical-polarization data and apply it to temperature-dependent birefringence imaging of stress-induced ferroelectric SrTiO$_3$. By treating the measured response as an observable projection of local material states, the optical-polarization response at each pixel is cast as a trajectory along the temperature axis. Singular value decomposition separates trajectory-induced geometric objects associated with optical-polarization-direction structure and temperature-evolution modes. Holonomies are then defined by transporting these objects around closed loops in real space. The resulting maps reveal spatially localized connection mismatches correlated with an enhanced ferroelectric transition temperature and stress-related optical anisotropy. Local order parameters and angular-gradient analyses confirm that these loop-level signals are distinct from orientational disorder and simple spatial variation. The signed holonomy of the temperature-evolution modes further resolves positive and negative connection structures under a fixed frame convention. These results demonstrate that the data-induced connection geometry of temperature trajectories provides an experimentally accessible diagnostic of electromechanical inhomogeneity in SrTiO$_3$ under stress, without explicitly reconstructing hidden strain or electric-polarization fields.

Abstract: Machine learning and computational inference, coupled with experimental data, promise to significantly accelerate our rate of learning in most scientific disciplines. In this study, we develop tools that connect microscopic observations to macroscopic device behaviour, a capability that is essential for accelerating the design of durable energy materials. To this end, we introduce a novel approach that integrates photoluminescence imaging with drift diffusion simulations to understand operation and degradation in fully fabricated perovskite solar cells. By employing Bayesian inference, we generate "inferred maps" of parameters that govern recombination processes present in devices. ### [73] [Decoding Crystallographic Surface Chirality with Machine Learning: From Atomic Geometry to Fermi Surface Projections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13144)
*Chetana Badala Viswanatha,Ka Man Yu,Benito Arnoldi,Anagha Aravind,Aaruni Kaushik,Jannis Lessmeister,Martin Aeschlimann,Benjamin Stadtmüller,S. Harshini Tekur*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一个双域机器学习框架（dual-domain machine learning framework），利用原子结构模型（实空间）和费米面投影的动量分辨光发射图（倒易空间）两类图像表示，直接对高米勒指数（high-Miller-index）金属表面的手性进行分类。ResNet18在原子模型上达到约73%的准确率，在费米面投影上达到约99%，并且后者仅需两张标注帧即可迁移到同步辐射实验图像。研究揭示了手性编码主要由倒易空间中费米面多边形与表面法向的相对取向决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 内禀手性金属表面（intrinsically chiral metal surfaces）在不对称催化、传感和自旋电子学中具有重要应用价值，但目前缺乏从实验观测量直接对其手性（handedness）进行一致分类的方法。

Method: 构建双域机器学习框架，在两个独立图像表示上进行分类：实空间的原子结构模型（atomic structure models）和倒易空间中费米面投影（Fermi surface projections）的模拟动量分辨光发射图。采用深度卷积神经网络ResNet18，在标注图像数据库上进行微调训练。

Result: ResNet18在原子模型上达到约73%的分类准确率，在费米面投影上达到约99%。后者经两张标注帧微调后可直接迁移到同步辐射实验图像。手性编码源于倒易空间中表面法向位置锚定费米面多边形取向的相对几何关系。

Conclusion: 手性更容易从动量空间电子模式（momentum-space electronic pattern）中恢复，而非局部原子几何构型，且费米面投影的高准确率对手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）在真实金属表面的无序鲁棒性具有直接意义。

Abstract: Intrinsically chiral metal surfaces, where handedness arises from the asymmetric step-kink-terrace topology of high-Miller-index planes, are model systems for enantiospecific catalysis, sensing, and spintronics. Yet, no consistent method exists to classify their handedness directly from experimental observables. We report a dual-domain machine learning framework that decodes crystallographic surface chirality from two independent image representations: atomic structure models in real space and simulated momentum-resolved photoemission maps of the Fermi surface projections in reciprocal space. ResNet18, a deep convolutional neural network, fine-tuned on a database of labeled images achieves ~73% classification accuracy on atomic models and ~99% on Fermi surface projections. We show that the latter transfers directly to synchrotron-acquired experimental images after fine-tuning on just two labeled frames. We identify a working correspondence between the two representations: just as the kink site geometry fixes the orientation of crystallographic planes in real space, the surface normal position in a momentum-resolved photoemission map anchors the orientation of the Fermi surface polygons in reciprocal space. It is precisely this relative orientation that encodes handedness into the map topology with high accuracy. The pronounced difference in accuracy shows that handedness is more readily recovered from the momentum-space electronic pattern than from the local atomic geometry of the kinked surface. This finding has direct implications for the disorder resilience of geometric chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS) at realistic metal surfaces.

### [74] [Thickness-Independent Quantum Geometric Responses Driven by Interlayer Antiferroic Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13237)

Method: 采用空间依赖的对称性分析（spatial-dependent symmetry analysis）揭示厚度无关行为的产生条件；结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对G型反铁磁构型的多层MnS进行反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）计算，并考察堆叠顺序的影响。

Abstract: Two-dimensional ferroic materials exhibit rich and intriguing physical phenomena, but their response properties generally depend sensitively on thickness, requiring precise layer-number control and thereby limiting practical applications. Here, we propose a general strategy for realizing thickness-independent quantum geometric responses through symmetry engineering induced by interlayer antiferroic coupling. Using spatial-dependent symmetry analysis, we show that thickness-independent behavior emerges when the symmetry breaking required for a given response is generated by interlayer antiferromagnetic (AFM) or antiferroelectric (AFE) coupling, without invoking topological mechanisms. Our first-principles calculations predict that multilayer MnS in the G-type AFM configuration exhibits a surface-dominated anomalous Hall effect, whose thickness-independent behavior can be significantly influenced by the stacking order. ### [75] [Polarizing ultrathin ferroelectric BaTiO3 films through interfacial layer polarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13396)

Result: SNO的带电原子面抑制了BaTiO₃（BTO）中退极化场（depolarizing field）诱导的临界厚度（critical thickness），从第一个沉积的单胞开始即观察到净极化（net polarization）。氧空位（oxygen vacancies）会抵消带负电的[NiO₂]⁻终止面SNO缓冲层的极化场。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了缺陷化学（defect chemistry）与极化界面（polarizing interfaces）之间的相互作用，为将铁电极化稳定至单胞极限提供了重要见解。

Abstract: An important requirement for the integration of ferroelectric thin films into devices is deterministic control of the polarization state in films of only a few unit cells in thickness. Here, we utilize the charged atomic planes of (001)-oriented SmNiO$_3$ (SNO) buffer layers as a polarizing template to stabilize the polarization in ferroelectric BaTiO$_3$ (BTO) model system thin films. We show that an upwards (downwards) oriented polarization is achieved by selection of the [SmO]$^+$ ([NiO$_2$]$^-$) buffer termination. Most importantly, the charged atomic planes of SNO suppress the depolarizing-field-induced critical thickness in BTO, and we record the emergence of a net polarization in our BTO films from the first unit cell deposited. Our experiments, guided by density-functional-theory (DFT) calculations, further highlight the impact of charged defects on the polarizing effectiveness of the SNO buffer. Specifically, oxygen vacancies counteract the polarizing field of the negatively charged, [NiO$_2$]$^-$-terminated surface of the SNO buffer. Our findings provide important insights into the interplay of defect chemistry and polarizing interfaces to stabilize ferroelectric polarization down to the single-unit-cell limit.

</details>

Abstract: Accelerated ageing using elevated temperatures and illumination is one of the most common methods to rapidly study the stability of novel semiconductor materials. Abstract: The structure and physical properties of the high-entropy multicomponent alloy FeCoNiB0.7Si0.3Be in the as-cast and melt-quenched states were studied. ### [80] [Symmetry-electronic fingerprints reveal competing magnetic phases in two-dimensional materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13548)
*Addis Fuhr,Zachary R. Fox,David Parker,Ayana Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对称电子指纹（symmetry-electronic fingerprint, SEF），这是一种物理可解释的表示方法，结合晶体对称性、Wyckoff位点几何与电子结构，结合随机森林集成学习（ensemble learning with random forests）实现对二维磁体磁基态、磁矩和磁各向异性的分类与回归，并将模型不确定性转化为诊断磁竞争机制的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维磁体为自旋电子学（spintronics）和量子技术提供了重要平台，但现有机器学习表示方法仅编码化学环境，未能捕捉控制磁性的对称性（symmetry）和交换物理（exchange physics），导致无法准确预测磁基态、磁矩和磁各向异性。

Method: 引入对称电子指纹（SEF），一种物理可解释的表示，编码晶体学对称操作（crystallographic symmetry operations）、Wyckoff位点几何（Wyckoff-site geometry）及位点分辨的电子结构（site-resolved electronic structure）；结合随机森林集成学习，同时实现磁有序分类、磁矩与磁各向异性能的回归。

Result: SEF训练的模型能够准确分类磁有序并回归磁矩和各向异性能，同时区分巡游Stoner铁磁性（itinerant Stoner ferromagnetism）与局域超交换（localized superexchange）的不同机制。高模型不确定性区域并非失败，而是诊断出铁磁（FM）与反铁磁（AFM）竞争、磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）、各向异性抑制及涌现非共线磁序（emergent non-collinear ordering）。Co-和Ni基卤化物与氧化物的第一性原理计算验证了这些预测。

Conclusion: 通过将对称性与交换物理直接编码到表示中（区别于传统描述符），SEF将模型不确定性转化为指南针，指向那些小扰动即可驱动共线、阻挫或非共线磁相之间转变的二维材料。

Abstract: Two-dimensional magnets offer compelling platforms for spintronics and quantum technologies, yet predicting their magnetic ground states, moments, and anisotropy remains challenging. This limitation primarily arises because existing machine-learning representations encode chemical environments without capturing the symmetry or exchange physics that govern magnetism. In this work, we introduce the symmetry-electronic fingerprint (SEF), a physically interpretable representation that encodes crystallographic symmetry operations, Wyckoff-site geometry, together with site-resolved electronic structure. Combined with ensemble learning with random forests, the SEF accurately classifies magnetic ordering while regressing moments alongside anisotropy energies while simultaneously resolving the distinct regimes of itinerant Stoner ferromagnetism from localized superexchange. What sets the SEF-trained models apart is that regions of elevated model uncertainty are not a failure but a diagnostic, identifying materials where these mechanisms compete. First-principles calculations on Co- and Ni-based halides and oxides confirm that these regions correspond to genuine near-degenerate FM and AFM phases with magnetic frustration, suppressed anisotropy, and emergent non-collinear ordering. By encoding symmetry together with exchange physics directly into the representation unlike conventional descriptors, the SEF transforms model uncertainty into a compass pointing toward two-dimensional materials where small perturbations drive transitions between collinear, frustrated, or non-collinear magnetic phases.

### [81] [Lone-Pair-Induced Lattice Softness Enables Ultralow Thermal Conductivity in Hybrid Organic-Inorganic Perovskite GuaPbI$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13561)
