<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统无机热电材料在纳米结构工程下已接近性能瓶颈，而有机热电材料虽具有本征低热导率，但电荷传输能力有限且对形貌高度敏感，亟需一种能够同时实现低热导与可接受电导的新型材料设计策略。

Method: 首先提出基于孤对电子驱动的化学诱导晶格软化策略；利用基于物理引导的符号回归机器学习框架（physics-guided symbolic-regression-based machine learning）识别孤对电子主导且热导率被抑制的成分区间，筛选出候选材料GuaPbI₃；通过机械化学合成得到结晶性GuaPbI₃；采用电学测量和阻抗谱（impedance spectroscopy）表征电输运；利用密度泛函理论（DFT）计算电子结构；通过洛伦兹数（Lorenz number）分析评估Wiedemann-Franz定律的偏离行为。

Result: 合成得到的GuaPbI₃在室温下热导率低至κ = 0.088 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹；电学测量显示存在电子活性且偏压依赖的体传导通道，阻抗谱证实为体相主导的输运；DFT计算揭示弱色散价带、价带-导带不对称性以及晶格内电荷重排导致的局域静电场微环境；计算输运系数显示载流子输运对化学势高度敏感；洛伦兹数分析表明在带边附近偏离传统Wiedemann-Franz行为。

Conclusion: 富孤对电子的杂化框架可产生软且电子异质性的晶格环境，从而在抑制声子输运的同时保留电子可及态，确立了化学诱导晶格软化作为超低热导杂化材料的设计原则（design principle）。

Abstract: Thermoelectric cooling efficiency is fundamentally constrained by lattice thermal conductivity, yet conventional inorganic thermoelectrics have approached a performance plateau despite extensive nanostructural engineering. Organic thermoelectrics possess intrinsically low thermal conductivity but often suffer from limited and morphology-sensitive charge transport. Here, we introduce a lone-pair-driven materials design strategy based on chemically induced lattice softness in hybrid organic-inorganic perovskites. A physics-guided symbolic-regression-based machine-learning framework identifies a lone-pair-dominated compositional regime associated with suppressed lattice thermal conductivity and selects GuaPbI3 as a candidate material. Mechanochemical synthesis yields crystalline GuaPbI3 with an ultralow room-temperature thermal conductivity of kappa = 0.088 W m^-1 K^-1. Electrical measurements reveal electronically active, bias-dependent bulk conduction pathways despite strong phonon suppression, while impedance spectroscopy confirms bulk-dominated transport. Density functional theory calculations indicate weakly dispersive valence bands, valence-conduction asymmetry, and localized electrostatic microenvironments from charge redistribution within the lattice. Calculated transport coefficients suggest strong sensitivity of carrier transport to chemical potential, while Lorenz-number analysis indicates deviations from conventional Wiedemann-Franz behavior near the band edges. These results support a picture in which lone-pair-rich hybrid frameworks generate soft and electronically heterogeneous lattice environments that suppress phonon transport while preserving electronically accessible states. This work establishes chemically induced lattice softness as a design principle for ultralow-thermal-conductivity hybrid materials.

Method: 以亚铁磁尖晶石Li₀.₅AlₓFe₂.₅₋ₓO₄（LAFO）薄膜作为模型体系，通过改变化学组分和衬底类型调控外延应变（epitaxial strain），并系统研究Al浓度对饱和磁化强度、磁各向异性、吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）参数及SOT效率的影响。

Result: PMA可通过外延应变（化学组分和衬底选择）进行调控，低SOT开关电流密度与较小但有限的PMA相关。超低阻尼主要源于仅Fe³⁺为磁性活性阳离子，Al替代分布引起的无序起次要作用。SOT效率由界面质量决定，与化学组分无关。通过调节Al浓度，可在保持超低吉尔伯特阻尼参数（低至2×10⁻⁴）和组分无关的阻尼类SOT效率的同时，系统调控饱和磁化强度和磁各向异性。

Conclusion: 确定了最优组分LAFO x=0.7（Li₀.₅Al₀.₇Fe₁.₈O₄），该材料兼具超低阻尼、具有小各向异性场的稳定PMA以及低SOT开关临界电流密度，是用于节能自旋波和自旋电子学器件的有前景的材料平台。

Abstract: Ultra-thin magnetic insulator films that simultaneously exhibit ultra-low magnon damping, perpendicular magnetic anisotropy (PMA), and low spin-orbit torque (SOT) switching current densities are highly desirable, albeit challenging, for next-generation spintronic technologies that exploit spin waves to transport information without dissipative charge currents. Here, we demonstrate this combination of properties in ferrimagnetic spinel Li$_{0.5}$Al$_{x}$Fe$_{(2.5-x)}$O$_4$ (LAFO) thin films. Through this model system, we find that PMA can be tuned by epitaxial strain in the form of chemical composition and substrate choice and that low SOT switching current densities correlate with small but finite PMA. Ultra-low damping is stabilized primarily by having only Fe$^{3+}$ as magnetically active cations with secondary effects due to increased disorder from Al substitution distribution. SOT efficiency is governed by interface quality and independent of chemical composition. By varying the Al concentration, we systematically tune the saturation magnetization and magnetic anisotropy while maintaining ultra-low Gilbert damping parameters as low as $2\times10^{-4}$ and composition-independent damping-like SOT efficiencies. We identify an optimal composition LAFO x=0.7 (Li$_{0.5}$Al$_{0.7}$Fe$_{1.8}$O$_4$), which combines ultra-low damping, stable PMA with small anisotropy fields, and low critical current densities for SOT switching, establishing it as a promising material platform for energy-efficient spin-wave and spintronic devices.

</details>


### [83] [Cepstral Analysis to accelerate Green-Kubo thermal conductivity calculations of Metal-Organic Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13588)
*Florian P. Lindner,Egbert Zojer,Sandro Wieser*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出将倒谱分析（cepstral analysis）与基于平衡分子动力学的Green-Kubo（GK）模拟相结合，用于预测金属有机框架（MOFs）的热导率。该方法在MOF-5、HKUST-1和ZIF-8三种原型框架上验证，结合机器学习矩张量势（moment tensor potentials），显著降低了统计噪声，减少了对用户自定义参数的敏感性，并在约1-2 ns总采样时间内实现收敛，为MOFs及其他低热导率材料提供了高效、可重复且可自动化的近从头算精度热输运预测框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属有机框架（MOFs）在气体存储与分离等应用中具有前景，但其热输运性能的可靠计算预测仍面临挑战。传统的基于平衡分子动力学的Green-Kubo（GK）模拟受统计噪声严重影响，且依赖多个模糊的用户自定义参数，阻碍了方法的可迁移性和自动化。

Method: 将倒谱分析（cepstral analysis）与平衡分子动力学Green-Kubo（GK）模拟相结合。采用基于DFT参考数据训练的机器学习矩张量势（moment tensor potentials），在MOF-5、HKUST-1和ZIF-8三种原型框架上进行验证。

Result: 倒谱方法在较宽的相关长度范围内均能给出稳定结果，并在约1-2 ns总采样时间内实现收敛。相比之下，传统的直接GK分析表现出不规则的收敛行为和对手动参数选择的强烈敏感性。

Conclusion: 倒谱分析驱动的Green-Kubo模拟结合机器学习势，为MOFs及其他复杂低热导率材料的热输运预测提供了一种高效、可重复且可自动化的框架，达到近从头算（ab initio）精度。

Abstract: Metal-organic frameworks (MOFs) are promising porous materials for applications such as gas storage and separation, where heat transport can critically affect device performance. However, reliable computational prediction of their thermal conductivities remains challenging. In particular, equilibrium molecular-dynamics-based Green-Kubo (GK) simulations, as the most widely used approach, are severely affected by statistical noise. Moreover, they rely on multiple ambiguous, user-defined parameters, which hinder transferability and automation. Here, we demonstrate for metal-organic frameworks that cepstral analysis in combination with GK simulations provides a robust route to massively mitigate these problems, while simultaneously reducing the required sampling times. This is shown for three prototypical frameworks, MOF-5, HKUST-1, and ZIF-8, employing machine-learned moment tensor potentials trained on DFT reference data. In contrast to conventional, direct GK analysis, which shows erratic convergence and strong sensitivity to ad hoc choices of parameters, the cepstral approach yields stable results across a wide range of correlation lengths and achieves convergence within about 1-2 ns of total sampling time. This establishes cepstral analysis base Green-Kubo simulations combined with machine-learned potentials as an efficient, reproducible and automation-ready framework for near ab initio accuracy prediction of thermal transport in MOFs and other complex low-thermal-conductivity materials.

### [84] [Morphology control and low-temperature magnetotransport in chiral 2D perovskite R-(MBA)$_2$PbI$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13664)
*Shehreen Aslam,Sam Saiter,Bradley Lloyd,Paul Kliewer,Matthew P. Hautzinger,Matthew C. Beard,Meenakshi Singh*

TL;DR: 本文通过工程化调控二维手性杂化钙钛矿（如R-(MBA)₂PbI₄）的薄膜形貌，克服了其面内电阻过高的瓶颈，首次实现了稳健的横向器件集成。在霍尔棒（Hall-bar）几何结构中，该研究在暗场条件下成功进行了霍尔测量（Hall measurement），明确了p型导电行为，并获得了此前无法获取的关键电学参数：霍尔迁移率约0.2 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹，载流子密度约3×10¹⁴ cm⁻²。此外，在穿过晶界（grain boundary）的输运路径上观察到了增强的磁电阻（magnetoresistance）效应，表明形貌对面内输运具有强烈影响。该工作实现了面内磁输运（magnetotransport）表征，为后续研究手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity, CISS）的基本机制以及加速手性材料在自旋电子学（spintronics）器件中的集成奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过工程化调控R-(MBA)₂PbI₄薄膜的形貌，实现稳健的横向器件集成；采用霍尔棒（Hall-bar）几何结构，在暗场条件下进行霍尔测量（Hall measurement），同时分析穿越晶界（grain boundary）的磁电阻（magnetoresistance）行为。

Result: 暗场下成功完成霍尔测量，明确识别出其p型导电特性，霍尔迁移率约为0.2 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹，载流子密度约为3×10¹⁴ cm⁻²；在穿越晶界的输运路径上观察到增强的磁电阻效应。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了面内磁输运（magnetotransport）的可行性，为探究手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity, CISS）的基本机制铺平了道路，并加速了手性材料向功能化自旋电子学（spintronic）器件的集成。

Abstract: Two-dimensional chiral hybrid perovskites, such as R/S-(MBA)\textsubscript{2}PbI\textsubscript{4}, are leading candidates for realizing and studying chirality-dependent charge and spin transport. However, their prohibitive in-plane resistance has precluded the electrical characterization. Here, we overcome this bottleneck by engineering the thin-film morphology of the chiral perovskite $R\text{-(MBA)}_2\text{PbI}_4$, enabling the first robust lateral device integration. In Hall-bar geometries, we demonstrate Hall measurements under dark conditions, unambiguously identifying p-type conduction with a Hall mobility of $\sim 0.2 \text{cm}^2 \text{V}^{-1} \text{s}^{-1}$ and a carrier density of $\sim 3\times10^{14} \text{ cm}^{-2}$, parameters previously inaccessible in this class of materials. Furthermore, we observe enhanced magnetoresistance along transport paths crossing grain boundaries, highlighting the strong influence of morphology on in-plane transport. This work demonstrates in-plane magnetotransport, enabling future investigations of the fundamental mechanisms of chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) and accelerating the integration of chiral materials into functional spintronic devices.

### [85] [Flux-explicit Cheeger bounds for magnetic Laplacians on compact metric graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12453)
*Björn Dahlke*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在有限紧连通度量图上引入磁Cheeger常数（magnetic Cheeger constant），通过在通常边界项上叠加子图势的受挫指数（frustration index），证明该指数等价于由周期（periods）决定的有限维ℓ¹通量距离（flux distance），进而建立谱下界的Cheeger型不等式、磁热半群（magnetic heat semigroup）与磁能量的L²衰减界，强调通量依赖性与度量图自包含表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Cheeger不等式（Cheeger inequality）推广到带实磁势（real magnetic potential）的度量图（metric graph）上的磁Laplacian（magnetic Laplacian），建立谱下界与Aharonov-Bohm通量（Aharonov-Bohm fluxes）之间的直接联系。

Method: 引入一个包含子图受挫指数（frustration index）的磁Cheeger常数，证明该指数等价于由势在环路上的周期决定的ℓ¹通量距离，从而将Cheeger常数直接表达为Aharonov-Bohm通量的函数，并由此推导Cheeger型下界（Cheeger type lower bound）。

Result: 获得了谱底部（bottom of the spectrum）的Cheeger型下界，并导出以全局环流通量向量（global cycle flux vector）与积分通量格点（integral flux lattice）之距离表示的显式下界，同时得到磁热半群与磁能量的L²衰减界（L² decay bounds）。

Conclusion: 所获常数并非最优，但重点在于揭示了通量依赖性（flux dependence），并提供了一个自包含的度量图表述（self contained metric graph formulation）。

Abstract: Let (Γ) be a finite compact connected metric graph and let (A\in L^\infty(Γ)) be a real magnetic potential. The magnetic Laplacian (H_A) with standard vertex conditions is defined by the closed quadratic form [
q_A[u]=\sum_e\int_e |(-i\partial_x-A_e)u_e|^2,dx. ]
A magnetic Cheeger constant is introduced by adding to the usual boundary term the frustration index of the potential on subgraphs. The first point of the paper is that, on a metric graph, this frustration index is exactly a finite dimensional (\ell^1) flux distance determined by the periods of (A) on cycles. Consequently the Cheeger constant can be written directly in terms of Aharonov Bohm fluxes. We prove a Cheeger type lower bound for the bottom of the spectrum and derive the corresponding explicit lower estimate in terms of the distance of the global cycle flux vector from the integral flux lattice. The estimate also gives (L^2) decay bounds for the magnetic heat semigroup and for the magnetic energy. The constants are not asserted to be sharp; the emphasis is on the flux dependence and on the self contained metric graph formulation.

### [86] [King Function for Shifted Gaussian: Laguerre Structure, Spectral Theory and Density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12455)
*Yanpeng Wang,Zhe Gao*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了移位高斯分布（shifted Gaussian distributions）球谐展开中作为径向核出现的King函数（King function）。通过建立King–Laguerre展开，推导了King微分方程及其自伴算子的酉等价性，证明了King函数在径向速度空间（radial velocity space）中的稠密非正交性（dense non-orthogonal system），并给出了加权可积性准则和闭合矩公式（closed-form moment formulas）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移位高斯分布在球谐展开（spherical harmonic expansion）中产生的径向核——King函数，其数学性质尚不清晰，特别是与已有Laguerre层次（co-moving Laguerre hierarchy）的关系、谱表示以及逼近理论基础有待建立。

Method: 通过King–Laguerre展开建立了King函数与协动Laguerre层次的关系；推导了King微分方程并证明其对应的自伴算子在Gauss加权Hilbert空间（Gaussian-weighted Hilbert space）中酉等价于半直线上的自由径向Schrödinger算符（free radial Schrödinger operator）；利用谱表示获得了广义本征函数。

Result: 证明了实参数King函数位于预解集（resolvent set）中，并在自然径向速度空间中构成一个稠密非正交系统；推导了加权L¹可积性准则（weighted L¹-integrability criteria）和闭合矩公式，论证了King函数归一化（normalization）的合理性。

Conclusion: King函数不仅与Laguerre层次有清晰的解析联系，其算子结构等价于径向Schrödinger问题，且在逼近论（approximation theory）层面为King混合表示（King mixture representations）提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study King function arising as radial kernels in the laboratory-frame spherical harmonic expansion of shifted Gaussian distributions. We first clarify their relation with the co-moving Laguerre hierarchy by means of a King--Laguerre expansion. We then derive the King differential equation and show that the associated self-adjoint operator in a Gaussian-weighted Hilbert space is unitarily equivalent to the free radial Schrödinger operator on the half-line. This yields the spectral representation and generalized eigenfunction. Finally, we prove that real-parameter King function, lies in the resolvent set, form a dense non-orthogonal system in a natural radial velocity space, providing an approximation-theoretic basis for King mixture representations. Weighted \(L^1\)-integrability criteria and closed-form moment formulas are also derived, justifying the normalization of King function.

### [87] [Quasi-Product States and Factor Types for the One-Dimensional Hard-Core Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12458)
*Farrukh Mukhamedov,Yuri Suhov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过拓扑马尔可夫链编码一维硬芯吉布斯测度，构造了路径AF-代数并证明了平稳马尔可夫测度诱导出忠实对角态。其GNS表示生成的冯·诺依曼代数为超有限因子，类型由参数κ=q/p²唯一决定：κ=1时为II₁型，κ≠1时为III_λ型（λ=min{κ,κ⁻¹}），并给出了中心化子与权重流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维硬芯吉布斯测度（hard-core Gibbs measure）对应的拟乘积态（quasi-product state），旨在通过算子代数方法刻画其统计力学性质，并完整分类所生成的冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra）的类型。

Method: 先将模型编码为拓扑马尔可夫链（topological Markov chain），构造容许硬芯词的路径AF-代数（path AF-algebra）。利用平稳马尔可夫测度在该代数上建立Evans意义下的忠实对角态（faithful diagonal state），进而通过GNS表示（GNS representation）生成冯·诺依曼代数，并基于转移矩阵参数κ=q/p²进行类型分类。

Result: 所生成的冯·诺依曼代数是超有限因子（hyperfinite factor）。当κ=1时因子为II₁型；当κ≠1时因子为III_λ型，其中λ=min{κ,κ⁻¹}。同时给出了该因子的中心化子（centralizer）与权重流（weight flow）的具体刻画。

Conclusion: 一维硬芯吉布斯测度对应的算子代数结构可通过单一参数κ完整分类，揭示了经典统计力学系统与冯·诺依曼因子类型之间的精确对应关系。

Abstract: We study a quasi-product state associated with the one-dimensional hard-core Gibbs measure. After coding the model by the topological Markov chain, we construct the standard path $AF$-algebra of admissible hard-core words and show that the stationary Markov measure induces on it a faithful diagonal state in the sense of Evans. We then analyze the von Neumann algebra generated by the corresponding GNS representation. The resulting algebra is a hyperfinite factor, and its type is determined by the single parameter \(κ=q/p^2,\) where \(\begin{pmatrix}p&q\\ 1&0\end{pmatrix}\) is the transition matrix of the Markov chain. More precisely, the factor is of type $\mathrm{II}_1$ when $κ=1$, and of type $\mathrm{III}_ł$ with \( ł=\min\{κ,κ^{-1}\}\) for $\k\neq 1$. We also specify the centralizer and the weight flow for the resulting factor.

### [88] [Thermodynamic coefficients in third-order relativistic fluid dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12463)
*Teboho Abram Moloi,Azwinndini Muronga*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于相对论扩展热力学（relativistic extended thermodynamics）的14个独立场，推导了第三阶流体动力学方程。方程遵循相对性原理、熵原理及双曲性要求，并给出了超相对论气体和简并相对论气体的平衡性质中新增系数的显式表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流体动力学模型在相对论框架下对高阶耗散效应（如剪切应力张量、热流等）的描述尚不完善，需要发展基于物理原理（熵原理、相对性原理）且满足双曲性（hyperbolic）的第三阶流体方程，以确保扰动传播具有有限速度。

Method: 采用包含14个独立场的相对论扩展热力学方法，构建了第三阶流体动力学方程。方法自动嵌入相对性原理、熵原理和双曲性要求；将熵、四流（four-current）、剪切应力张量（shear-stress tensor）、动态压力（dynamic pressure）和热流（heat flux）等量展开至三阶（立方阶），并计算相应的平衡系数。

Result: 给出了超相对论气体（ultra-relativistic gas regime）和非简并相对论气体（non-degenerate relativistic gas）中新计算的平衡系数。非简并条件下系数消去了逸度（fugacity），便于归一化；超相对论情形则提供了这些系数的上界。部分系数与早期动理学理论（kinetic theory）计算结果吻合良好，另一些系数存在轻微差异。

Conclusion: 所提出的第三阶相对论流体动力学方程在理论上自洽，且数值上部分系数与已有动理学结果一致，验证了方法的有效性；同时为高阶相对论流体建模提供了新的系数参考和边界约束。

Abstract: We developed the third-order hydrodynamic equations using relativistic extended thermodynamics of gases with 14 independent fields. The resulting fluid equations are based on the relativity principle, the entropy principle, and the requirement of hyperbolic, and hence finite, propagation of disturbances, which is automatically incorporated. The expressions of entropy, four-current, shear-stress tensor, dynamic pressure, and heat flux are expanded up to third order (cubic). We explicitly present the newly calculated coefficients in the equilibrium properties of an ultra-relativistic gas regime and the non-degenerate relativistic gas. Contrary to the general cases, the non-degenerate regime eliminates fugacity from the coefficients, allowing for the easy normalization of these coefficients, and the ultra-relativistic regime provides us with the upper bounds of these coefficients. We found good agreement on some of the coefficients as compared to calculations from earlier models, specifically in kinetic theory, and other coefficients had slightly different values to those obtained in kinetic theory.

### [89] [Chiral Long-Range Order in three Euclidean Lattice Gross-Neveu Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13075)
*Simone Fabbri,Leonardo Goller*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过Hubbard-Stratonovich变换、反射正性（Reflection Positivity）、棋盘估计（Chessboard Estimates）和Peierls型轮廓论证，严格证明了二维欧几里得格点Gross-Neveu模型在费米子味数为偶数、耦合足够小且味数足够大时，存在手征荷费米子质量双线性项的长程序（Long-Range Order），并建立了与平均场（large-N）预测的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在统计力学与量子场论中，证明格点费米子模型的长程序存在性是一个重要而困难的非微扰问题。以往结果多依赖于大N展开或数值模拟，缺乏严格的数学证明，且对于不同格点离散化方案（如naive费米子和staggered费米子）的普适性验证尚不充分。

Method: 首先对两类格点Gross-Neveu模型执行Hubbard-Stratonovich变换，将费米子系统映射为玻色子系统，并建立所得测度的反射正性。随后结合棋盘估计与Peierls型轮廓论证，在足够小的耦合常数和足够大的费米子味数条件下证明长程序的存在性，并得到玻色两点函数（即费米子质量-质量关联函数）的一致逐点界。

Result: 在三种标准格点离散化（包括naive和staggered费米子）下，均证明二维欧几里得格点Gross-Neveu模型中存在长程序；获得了玻色两点函数的统一逐点界，表明其受有效势极小值定量控制；结果不依赖于具体离散化方案，具有跨实现的一致性。

Conclusion: 该工作为格点Gross-Neveu模型中的长程序提供了完全严格且非微扰的证明，并将严格理论与大N（平均场）预言建立了直接联系。该分析对格点离散化方案具有鲁棒性，适用于同一连续模型的不同实现。

Abstract: We prove the existence of Long-Range Order in a class of two-dimensional Euclidean lattice Gross-Neveu models with an even number of fermion flavors, covering three standard lattice discretizations, including naive and staggered fermions widely used in numerical studies. By performing a Hubbard-Stratonovich transformation, we map the fermionic systems to bosonic ones and establish Reflection Positivity for the resulting measures. Exploiting this structure, we combine Chessboard Estimates with a Peierls-type contour argument to prove Long-Range Order for the chirally charged fermion-mass bilinear $\overlineψψ$ at sufficiently small coupling and sufficiently large flavor number. Our analysis is robust with respect to the choice of lattice discretization and applies uniformly across different realizations of the same underlying continuum model. Moreover, we obtain uniform pointwise bounds on the bosonic two-point function, equivalently on the fermionic mass-mass correlator, showing that it is quantitatively controlled by the minimizers of the effective potential. This provides a fully rigorous and non-perturbative demonstration of Long-Range Order in lattice Gross-Neveu models and establishes a direct connection between the rigorous theory and its large-$N$ (mean-field) predictions.

</details>


### [90] [Rapid mixing for Gibbs measures in Riemannian manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13453)
*Ángela Capel,Marco Castrillón-López,Sofyan Iblisdir,Angelo Lucia,Pablo Páez-Velasco,David Pérez-García*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了黎曼流形上的Langevin动力学，识别了确保对数Sobolev不等式存在（即快速混合到吉布斯测度）的条件，并证明了在这些条件下可实现维度多项式级的混合时间。该结果通过定义域和黎曼浸没像域中Langevin过程之间的关系获得，该关系本身可能具有独立价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维复杂流形上，Langevin动力学的混合速率（mixing rate）与对数Sobolev不等式（logarithmic Sobolev inequality）的成立条件尚不明确。作者希望找到能够保证快速混合到吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure）的几何与热力学条件，并排除贫瘠高原（barren plateaus）和虚假局部极小值（spurious local minima）等不良现象。

Method: 作者分析了黎曼流形（Riemannian manifold）上的Langevin动力学，通过建立定义域与黎曼浸没（Riemannian submersion）像域中Langevin过程之间的关系，推导出混合时间的上界。该关系将流形的曲率（curvature）、逆温度（inverse temperature）以及从鞍点逃离的方向（escaping directions from saddle points）等几何与物理因素统一纳入分析框架。

Result: 确定了确保对数Sobolev不等式存在（即快速混合到吉布斯测度）的条件，具体涉及流形曲率、逆温度、鞍点逃离方向，并排除了贫瘠高原与虚假局部极小值。在这些条件满足时，混合时间（mixing time）可实现维度多项式级（polynomial in the dimension）。

Conclusion: 黎曼流形上Langevin动力学的快速混合可通过一组明确的几何与热力学条件来保证，所得多项式混合时间为高维采样提供了理论依据。此外，所发现的Langevin过程在黎曼浸没下的关系可能对更广泛的随机过程分析具有独立意义。

Abstract: Langevin dynamics on Riemannian manifolds is analyzed. Conditions ensuring the existence of a suitable logarithmic Sobolev inequality (rapid mixing to the Gibbs measure) are identified. These conditions involve the curvature of the manifold, the inverse temperature, escaping directions from saddle points, and exclude barren plateaus and spurious local minima. We show that when these conditions are met, mixing times polynomial in the dimension of the manifold are achievable. This result is obtained through a relation between Langevin processes in the domain and in the image of a Riemannian submersion. Such a relation can be of independent interest.

### [91] [Birkhoff conjecture and finite energy foliations in Hill's lunar problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12912)
*Lei Liu,Pedro A. S. Salomão*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文证明希尔月球问题中 Birkhoff 逆行轨道猜想，通过构造全局辛坐标变换使有界正则化分量达到严格凸性，从而获得临界能量以下盘状全局截面和临界能量以上的 2-3-2 有限能叶状结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明希尔月球问题（Hill's lunar problem）中 Birkhoff 逆行轨道猜想（retrograde orbit conjecture），并系统描述临界能量附近及以上的全局动力学结构。

Method: 结合伪全纯曲线方法（pseudo-holomorphic curve techniques）与一个新的凸性定理（convexity theorem）。具体构造一个显式全局辛坐标变换（global symplectic change of coordinates），使有界正则化分量在临界能量以下严格凸，进而应用 Hofer-Wysocki-Zehnder 有限能叶状结构理论（finite energy foliations theory）。

Result: 对于临界值以下每个能量，逆行轨道界定一个盘状全局截面（disk-like global surface of section）；对于略高于临界值的能量，构建 2-3-2 有限能叶状结构，其结合由逆行轨道和临界点附近的 Lyapunov 轨道（Lyapunov orbits）组成。由此推出存在无穷多条周期轨道和无穷多条渐近于 Lyapunov 轨道的轨迹。

Conclusion: 严格凸性导出强动力学后果，包括周期轨道的 Conley-Zehnder 指标下界（lower bounds for Conley-Zehnder indices），从而完整验证了 Birkhoff 逆行轨道猜想，并建立了临界能量附近的全局动力学图景。

Abstract: We prove Birkhoff's retrograde orbit conjecture in Hill's lunar problem by showing that the retrograde orbit bounds a disk-like global surface of section for every energy below the critical value. We also obtain a global description of the dynamics through the critical energy level by constructing finite energy foliations for energies slightly above it. The binding of these foliations consists of the retrograde orbit together with the Lyapunov orbits near the critical points. As a consequence, there exist infinitely many periodic orbits and infinitely many trajectories asymptotic to the Lyapunov orbits. The proof combines pseudo-holomorphic curve techniques with a new convexity theorem for Hill's lunar problem. More precisely, we construct an explicit global symplectic change of coordinates under which the bounded regularized component becomes strictly convex up to the critical energy level. This convexity implies strong dynamical consequences, including lower bounds for the Conley-Zehnder indices of periodic orbits, and allows the application of the Hofer-Wysocki-Zehnder theory of finite energy foliations. As a result, we obtain disk-like global surfaces of section below the critical level and $2-3-2$ foliations for energies slightly above it.

### [92] [The censored stochastic six-vertex model and parabolic Kazhdan--Lusztig $R$-polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12670)
*Hindy Drillick,Levi Haunschmid-Sibitz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机六顶点模型的删节版本，旨在建立其与阻塞测度之间的随机占优关系，从而为控制第二类粒子的行为提供分析工具。

Method: 通过引入删节版随机六顶点模型，利用抛物型 Kazhdan--Lusztig $R$-多项式作为核心工具，并借助随机六顶点模型与对称群 Iwahori--Hecke 代数之间的关联来解释这些多项式的出现。进一步将归一化抛物型 Kazhdan--Lusztig $R$-多项式构建为过程的交织核。

Result: 对于参数 $b_1 < b_2$，从初始条件 ${1}_{x>0}$ 出发的删节版模型在任意时刻随机受控于阻塞测度。该结果可作为单调自旋系统删节不等式的部分类比。

Conclusion: 这一随机占优结果使得对第二类粒子行为的控制成为可能；同时，交织关系的发现揭示了该过程与 Kazhdan--Lusztig 理论之间的深层结构联系。

Abstract: We introduce a censored version of the stochastic six-vertex model. We show that for parameters $b_1 < b_2$, this model started from the initial condition ${1}_{x>0}$ is stochastically dominated at any time by the blocking measure. This is a partial analog of the censoring inequality for monotone spin systems. In particular, this result allows us to control the behavior of second-class particles. The proof uses parabolic Kazhdan--Lusztig $R$-polynomials, whose appearance is explained using a connection between the stochastic six-vertex model and the Iwahori--Hecke algebras of symmetric groups. Furthermore, we find an intertwining relation for this process using normalized parabolic Kazhdan--Lusztig $R$-polynomials as an intertwining kernel.

### [93] [Scaling limits of the single-curve interface and outermost loops in the planar random field Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13147)
*Fenglin Huang,Léonie Papon,Aoteng Xia*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了近临界平面随机场伊辛模型（random field Ising model, RFIM）在 Dobrushin 边界条件下，分离正负自旋的界面具有标度极限（scaling limit），其律是共形协变的（conformally covariant），且几乎必然关于 SLE₃ 绝对连续；同时，该模型在正边界条件下的最外自旋环（outermost spin loops）存在子列极限，且任何此类极限几乎必然关于 CLE₃ 奇异。这一绝对连续与奇异的二分性（dichotomy）说明，单界面不足以探测近临界 RFIM 磁化场相对于临界伊辛磁化场的奇异性，而最外自旋环可以。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解近临界随机场伊辛模型中界面与环的标度极限行为，并刻画其与临界伊辛模型（critical Ising model）中 SLE₃/CLE₃ 之间的测度论关系（绝对连续 vs. 奇异），是随机几何与统计力学交叉领域的重要问题。

Method: 采用概率论与共形场论（conformal field theory）方法，研究具有 Dobrushin 边界条件的近临界平面 RFIM 的界面标度极限（scaling limit），以及具有+1 边界条件的模型的最外自旋环的子列极限。

Result: 近临界 RFIM 中的单一界面的标度极限服从一个共形协变的随机曲线，其律几乎必然关于 SLE₃ 绝对连续；而最外自旋环的任何子列极限则几乎必然关于 CLE₃ 奇异。

Conclusion: 单一界面与最外自旋环在测度论性质上的二分性源于两者对磁化场（magnetization field）探索深度的差异：单界面未能充分探测近临界 RFIM 磁化场的奇异性，而最外自旋环能探测到该奇异性。

Abstract: We prove that the interface separating $+1$ and $-1$ spins in the near-critical planar random field Ising model (RFIM) with Dobrushin boundary conditions has a scaling limit, whose law is conformally covariant and almost surely absolutely continuous with respect to SLE$_3$. The limiting curve can be seen as a massive version of SLE$_3$ in the sense of Makarov and Smirnov, but in a random environment. We then show that the outermost spin loops of the near-critical planar RFIM with $+1$ boundary conditions have subsequential limits and that any of these limits is almost surely singular with respect to CLE$_3$. This dichotomy between absolute continuity of the single interface and singularity of the outermost loops reflects the fact that a single interface does not explore enough of the magnetization field of the near-critical RFIM to detect the singularity of this field with respect to the critical Ising magnetization field, whereas the outermost spin loops do.

### [94] [Interference Queueing Networks: A Replica Mean-Field Approach in the Symmetric Setting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13264)
*Philippe Sarotte,Nahuel Soprano-Loto,François Baccelli*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出一个超越全缓冲（full-buffer）假设的无线通信网络性能评估模型：将网络建模为环形拓扑（torus）上的N个相互作用队列，每个队列对应一个发射-接收对，其服务速率由香农容量（Shannon capacity）决定并受邻居活动状态影响。通过副本平均场极限（replica mean-field limit），推导了系统的稳定区域（stability region）、稳态分布近似以及指数收敛速率，并建立了混沌传播（propagation of chaos）和长时间行为结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统无线网络性能评估普遍采用全缓冲（full-buffer）假设，即每个发射器始终处于活动状态，这忽略了实际网络中发射器仅在有数据发送时才占用信道的动态特性。为更真实地刻画网络行为，需要建立一个能反映队列状态与干扰之间相互依赖关系的分析模型。

Method: 将无线网络建模为环形（torus）上N个相互作用的队列系统。每个队列具有齐次到达率（homogeneous arrival rate），服务速率由香农容量（Shannon capacity）给出，该容量依赖于对应的信干噪比（Signal-to-Interference-plus-Noise Ratio, SINR）。由于干扰发射器仅在其队列非空时发射，SINR及服务速率在邻居队列为空时得到改善。通过副本平均场极限（replica mean-field limit）方法获得稳态分布近似和指数收敛速率，并证明混沌传播（propagation of chaos）和长时间行为。

Result: 推导了该相互作用队列系统的稳定区域（stability region），获得了系统稳态分布（stationary distribution）的近似表达式以及系统收敛到稳态的指数速率（exponential rate of convergence）。

Conclusion: 所提出的模型突破了全缓冲假设的限制，为分析实际无线通信网络中发射器活动与干扰之间的动态耦合关系提供了一个理论框架。副本平均场极限方法有效简化了复杂相互作用系统的分析，并给出了稳定性和收敛性的定量刻画。

Abstract: We propose a model for evaluating the performance of wireless communication networks beyond the ubiquitous full-buffer assumption, under which every transmitter is always active. The network is represented by N interacting queues arranged on a torus, with homogeneous arrival rate and service rates depending on the activity of neighboring interferers. More precisely, each queue is associated with a transmitter-receiver pair, and its service rate is given by the Shannon capacity, which depends on the corresponding Signal-to-Interference-plus-Noise Ratio (SINR). Since interfering transmitters only emit when their queue is non-empty, the SINR and hence the service rate improves when neighboring queues are empty. We derive the stability region of the system, together with approximations of its stationary distribution and its exponential rate of convergence to stationarity. These approximations are obtained via a replica mean-field limit, for which we establish propagation of chaos and long-time behavior results.

</details>

### [95] [Scaffolds for Higher Tropical Grassmannians: Foundations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25211)
*Nick Early,Thomas Lam*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文引入"脚手架（scaffolds）"作为高维旗单纯复形的一维骨架，推广了Trop G(2,n)的系统发育树，并证明其可通过k点距离函数模拟所有热带格拉斯曼流形中的点。主要结果是用正规CAT(0)平面图唯一表示任意整数正热带普吕克向量，并揭示了其与SL(3)-webs、热带线性空间及仿射建筑中的膜的嵌入关系，同时建立了Early基展开与对偶编织物链组合的直接联系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入"脚手架（scaffolds）"概念，作为高维非正曲率旗单纯复形的一维骨架；通过k点距离函数（k-point distance function）刻画热带格拉斯曼流形中的点；对CAT(0)平面图（CAT(0) planar graphs）进行详细研究，证明其可作为三平面热带格拉斯曼流形的正脚手架。

Result: 构造了任意整数正热带普吕克向量（positive tropical Plücker vector）由正规CAT(0)平面图（normal CAT(0) planar graph）的唯一表示；证明正规CAT(0)平面图可嵌入热带线性空间作为Lam-Postnikov膜，嵌入仿射建筑作为Keel-Tevelev膜；Early的基展开（Early's planar basis expansion）可直接从对偶网（dual web）的链组合计算。

Abstract: Scaffolds are the one-dimensional skeleta of high-dimensional flag simplicial complexes of nonpositive curvature. They generalize the phylogenetic trees of Trop G(2,n) to arbitrary $k$, drawing together SL(k)-web bases, affine buildings, the combinatorics of the positive tropical Grassmannian and low-dimensional topology. We prove that scaffolds model points in all tropical Grassmannians via a $k$-point distance function.
  In this paper, we study in detail CAT(0) planar graphs, which are positive scaffolds for the tropical Grassmannian of three-planes. CAT(0) planar graphs are directed versions of the diskoids of Fontaine-Kamnitzer-Kuperberg, planar dual to SL(3)-webs. Our main result is the construction of a unique representation of any given integer positive tropical Plucker vector by a normal CAT(0) planar graph. We show that any normal CAT(0) planar graph embeds into the tropical linear space as a Lam-Postnikov membrane, and embeds into the Keel-Tevelev membrane within the affine building. We show that Early's planar basis expansion can be computed directly from the strand combinatorics of the dual web, and connect this expansion to Petersen-Pylyavskyy-Speyer's noncrossing tableaux, explored further in our companion paper.

### [96] [Noncrossing Duality and the Geometry of Positive Tropical Linear Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25212)
*Nick Early,Thomas Lam*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文为正热带格拉斯曼流形（positive tropical Grassmannian）建立了系统的代数与多面体理论基础，通过引入热带对偶性（tropical duality）将其扇结构与非交叉扇（noncrossing fan）相联系，并揭示了整数正热带线性空间（positive tropical linear space）的度量几何由非交叉表（noncrossing tableau）的列数控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管正格拉斯曼流形（positive Grassmannian）已通过plabic图和正合胞（positroid cell）的组合学被深入理解，但其热带版本——正热带格拉斯曼流形（positive tropical Grassmannian）Trop$_{>0}G(k,n)$——在一般$k$下缺乏类似的结构性框架。该流形的全局面结构以及其所参数化的热带线性空间的内部度量几何仍然基本上是未知的。

Method: 提出一种基本的“热带对偶性”（tropical duality），类比于簇变量（cluster variable）的$u$-坐标与$\mathbf{g}$-向量之间的对偶，将第一作者引入的两类对象——热带普吕克向量（tropical Plücker vector）的平面基（planar basis）与正配置空间（positive configuration space）上的平面交比（planar cross-ratio）——配对起来。进而将正热带格拉斯曼流形的扇结构与Santos、Stump和Welker的非交叉扇（noncrossing fan）相联系，并在整数正热带线性空间的有界复形（bounded complex）与超单纯形（hypersimplex）上的中心屋顶函数（central roof function）的次微分之间建立实现关系。

Result: 建立了Trop$_{>0}G(k,n)$的整数点与非交叉表（noncrossing tableau）之间的全局双射。将有界复形嵌入到基本尖顶单形（fundamental alcoved simplex）的扩张中，并证明扩张因子——即该复形的几何直径——由单一不变量“平面运动学权重”（planar kinematics weight, $K$权重）控制，该权重等于关联非交叉表的列数。

Conclusion: 本文为一般$k$下的正热带格拉斯曼流形提供了系统的代数与多面体基础，填补了该领域在结构框架上的空白。研究成果被应用于作者在更高维热带格拉斯曼流形支架（scaffolds）方面的平行工作中。

Abstract: While the positive Grassmannian is deeply understood through the rich combinatorics of plabic graphs and positroid cells, its tropical counterpart, the positive tropical Grassmannian Trop$_{>0}G(k,n)$, has lacked a comparable structural framework for general $k$. Both the global face structure of Trop$_{>0}G(k,n)$ and the internal metric geometry of the tropical linear spaces it parametrizes have remained largely uncharted. This paper develops a systematic algebraic and polyhedral foundation that resolves this gap.
  The engine of our framework is a fundamental tropical duality, analogous to the duality between cluster variables (or more precisely, their $u$-coordinates) and $\mathbf{g}$-vectors, pairing two families of objects introduced by the first author: the planar basis of tropical Plücker vectors and the planar cross-ratios on the positive configuration space. We prove that this duality links the fan structure of the positive tropical Grassmannian to the noncrossing fan of Santos, Stump, and Welker, yielding a global bijection between integer points of $Trop_{>0}G(k,n)$ and noncrossing tableaux.
  We then study how this discrete combinatorial data controls the continuous metric geometry of positive tropical linear spaces. We realize the bounded complex of an integer positive tropical linear space as the subdifferential of a central roof function on the hypersimplex, and use this realization to embed it into a dilate of the fundamental alcoved simplex. The dilation factor, and hence the geometric diameter of the complex, is governed by a single invariant, the planar kinematics ($K) weight, which we show equals the number of columns in the associated noncrossing tableau.
  The results of this work are applied in our parallel work on scaffolds for higher tropical Grassmannians.

</details>


### [97] [A local bijection between alternating sign matrices and descending plane partitions and a Striker--Fulmek-type $q$-statistic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13653)
*Michael J. Schlosser*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明了一种在交错符号矩阵（alternating sign matrices, ASMs）与下降平面分拆（descending plane partitions, DPPs）之间的局部双射，并基于此构建了一个保留统计量的 refined q-计数框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为 Behrend–Di Francesco–Zinn-Justin 的 refined 纤维中 ASM 与 DPP 之间的对应关系提供一个构造性的局部双射证明，并在此基础上建立统计量保持的计数结构。

Method: 通过移动 ASM 与 DPP 图像中的边界线构造局部映射，每一步仅改变边界的有限邻域；在生长图（growth-diagram）语言中，边界状态表示为普通 ASM 行前沿与移位 DPP 路径前沿，基本移动为可逆的 Fomin 型方规则（Fomin-type square rules）。检验局部移动的合流性（confluence）、每个方块的可逆性以及完成后的边界再次满足坐标不等式；唯一的终端选择通过半径二扇规则（radius-two fan rule）在可见高度轮廓上解决。

Result: 同一局部框架为 refined ASM 提供了一个统计量，其生成函数为 DPP 度数枚举子（degree enumerator）。该统计量包含一个 Striker–Fulmek 二次核（quadratic core）\(Q_{\rm SF}(A)\)，加上一个有界扇边界修正项，以及在正常边界规范（normal gauge）外的显式紧致势端点项。

Conclusion: 该论文同时给出了一个局部 ASM–DPP 双射和一个统计量保持的 refined q-计数；附录文件重现了选定的局部检验与算术示例。

Abstract: We prove a local bijection between alternating sign matrices (ASMs) and descending plane partitions (DPPs) in the refined fibres of Behrend--Di Francesco--Zinn-Justin. The map is constructed by moving a boundary line through the ASM and DPP pictures. At each step only a bounded neighbourhood of that boundary is changed. In growth-diagram language, the boundary states are ordinary ASM row frontiers and shifted DPP path frontiers, and the elementary moves are reversible Fomin-type square rules. The proof checks that overlapping local moves are confluent, that every square is invertible, and that the completed boundary again satisfies the ordinary ASM and DPP coordinate inequalities. The only terminal choice is resolved by a radius-two fan rule on the visible height contour.
  The same local framework gives a statistic on refined ASMs whose generating function is the DPP degree enumerator. The statistic has a Striker--Fulmek quadratic core \[
  Q_{\rm SF}(A)=
  \sum_{1\le r<s\le n}\ \sum_{1\le b<a\le n}
  (n-r+1)A_{r,a}A_{s,b}, \] plus a bounded fan-boundary correction and, outside the normal boundary gauge, an explicit compact-potential endpoint term. In the normal gauge this is \[
  W_{\rm ASM}^{\rm SF}(A)=Q_{\rm SF}(A)+B_{\rm fan}(A). \] Thus the paper gives both a local ASM--DPP bijection and a statistic-preserving refined \(q\)-enumeration. The supplementary files reproduce selected local checks and the displayed arithmetic examples.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mes-hall'></div>

### [98] [Composite Quantum Geometry and Semiclassical Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12525)
*Henry Davenport,Yoonseok Hwang,Johannes Knolle,Frank Schindler*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文推导了绝缘体与半导体中复合束缚态（如激子、三激子）的半经典运动方程，发现中性复合物中存在量子几何偶极子而非贝里曲率项，带电复合物则需谨慎选择无穷多等效贝里曲率中的物理正确版本。以魔角扭曲双层石墨烯中的三激子为例，展示了量子几何偶极子与贝里曲率共同驱动横向漂移及内禀偶极振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解复合束缚态（如激子（exciton）和三激子（trion））在电场下的动力学行为，特别是探索超出单电子图像（single-electron picture）的量子几何（quantum geometric）效应。

Method: 采用半经典运动方程（semiclassical equations of motion）方法，从理论上推导一般复合束缚态在绝缘体（insulator）与半导体（semiconductor）中的动力学，并区分中性复合物与带电复合物的几何贡献。

Result: 中性复合物中，均匀外电场不耦合至贝里曲率（Berry curvature）项，而是出现量子几何偶极子（quantum geometric dipole）；带电复合物如三激子存在额外的贝里曲率贡献，但存在无穷多等效的复合贝里曲率（composite Berry curvature），需依据复合物空间中心（spatial centre）的定义做出正确选择。在魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene）中的三激子中，量子几何偶极子与贝里曲率共同诱导横向漂移（transverse drift），且偶极矩（dipole moment）随时间振荡。

Conclusion: 复合物动力学中存在单电子所不具有的量子几何效应，且中性复合物与带电复合物的几何贡献形式不同，需谨慎定义复合物的空间中心以选择正确的贝里曲率版本。

Abstract: We derive semiclassical equations of motion for general composite bound states in insulators and semiconductors, covering excitations such as excitons and trions. For neutral composites we find that a uniform external electric field does not couple to a Berry curvature term, contrary to the naive expectation from single-electron dynamics. Instead, a distinct quantum geometric quantity appears generically in the equations of motion. This quantity is the difference between inequivalent Berry connections that can be defined for the composite, generalising the concept of the quantum geometric dipole previously studied for excitons. In the case of charged composites such as trions, we find an additional Berry curvature contribution to the equations of motion. As we demonstrate, however, there is an infinite family of inequivalent composite Berry curvatures, and so care must be taken to make the correct choice that describes the physical dynamics. We explain how this choice should be made dependent on the definition of a spatial centre for the composite. We end by discussing composite dynamics that have no single-electron counterpart. We find that trions in magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene undergo a transverse drift under an applied electric field and that this is driven not only by the Berry curvature contribution but also by the quantum geometric dipole. The interplay of these two geometric contributions further imprints itself on the trion's internal dynamics, causing its dipole moment to oscillate in time.

</details>


### [99] [Optical pulse-induced quantum geometric waves in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12696)
*Luis Fernando Cardenas Castillo,Wei Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文证明在短光脉冲作用下，石墨烯（graphene）中布洛赫态（Bloch states）的量子度量（quantum metric）在动量-时间空间（kx, ky, t）中变得动态，并表现出波状行为。这种量子度量波反映了脉冲引起的Floquet能带结构，同时还生成了静态石墨烯中不存在的贝里曲率波（Berry curvature wave）。可观测的Fisher信息波（Fisher information wave）构成了量子度量波的一部分，可通过泵浦-探测实验测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索短光脉冲作用下石墨烯中量子度量（quantum metric）的动态行为及其与Floquet能带结构之间的关系，并揭示脉冲诱导的贝里曲率（Berry curvature）波和Fisher信息波等新现象。

Method: 通过求解含时薛定谔方程（time-dependent Schrödinger equation）进行分析，假设可以忽略关联（correlations）和非平衡效应（out-of-equilibrium effects），以揭示脉冲引起的量子度量波与Floquet能带结构的对应关系。

Result: 量子度量在动量-时间空间表现出类似波的行为，其动量和时间分量具有非常不同的时间依赖性，且在脉冲通过后仍持续存在。短光脉冲还在原本无此特性的静态石墨烯中诱导出贝里曲率波（Berry curvature wave）。导带和价带中的时间依赖电子密度产生了Fisher信息波（Fisher information wave），它构成量子度量波的一部分。

Conclusion: 量子度量波和Fisher信息波是脉冲诱导的可观测动态现象，其中Fisher信息波可通过泵浦-探测实验（pump-probe experiments）直接测量，为实验验证提供了可行的途径。

Abstract: We show that, under a short optical pulse, the quantum metric of Bloch states in the momentum-time (kx, ky , t) of graphene becomes dynamic and exhibits a wave-like behavior near Dirac points. This quantum metric wave reflects the Floquet-band structure caused by the pulse, as revealed by solving the time-dependent Schrödinger equation assuming that correlations and out-of-equilibrium effects can be ignored. The momentum and temporal components of the metric have very distinct time dependence that persists even after the pulse has passed. In addition, the pulse also generates a Berry curvature wave that is otherwise absent in static graphene. The time-dependent electron densities in conduction and valence bands also give arise to a Fisher information wave that constitutes part of the quantum metric wave, and is readily measurable by pump-probe experiments.

</details>


### [100] [Role of quantum confinement in semiconductor-superconductor core-shell nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12715)
*Tudor Gabriel Dumitru,Anna Sitek,Gunnar Thorgilsson,Sigurdur I. Erlingsson,Tudor Dan Stanescu,Andrei Manolescu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过微观模型计算，研究了半壳金属超导体覆盖的半导体纳米线中观测到的超流相干性，发现高能横向模可形成环绕纳米线的电子-空穴混合本征态，从而解释Little-Parks效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验观察到半壳金属超导体覆盖的半导体纳米线中存在通量依赖的超流振荡，其周期为h/2e，类似于管状超导体（tubular superconductor）中的Little-Parks振荡（Little-Parks oscillations）。该工作旨在从微观理论角度解释这一现象的物理机制。

Method: 采用微观模型计算，对比全壳与半壳金属层的结果。利用从近邻化半导体纳米线（proximitized semiconductor nanowire）的格林函数（Green's function）导出的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），其中超导体的存在通过自能（self energy）表示。进一步将金属-半导体界面处的静电能带弯曲（electrostatic band-bending）建模为半导体侧的一个矩形窄量子阱（rectangular narrow quantum well）。

Result: 有效哈密顿量的本征态性质由正常态下对应横向模（transverse modes）的空间轮廓决定。对于半壳纳米线，能量足够高的横向模会扩展出界面量子阱区域，产生具有混合电子-空穴特征（mixed electron-hole character）的本征态，这些态环绕纳米线的整个圆周，与全壳系统（full-shell system）的本征态类似。

Conclusion: 识别出这些高能横向模形成的环绕本征态是导致实验中观测到的Little-Parks效应的物理根源。

Abstract: This work is motivated by the experimentally observed coherence of the supercurrent in semiconductor nanowires covered by a half-shell metallic superconductor, which leads to flux dependent supercurrent oscillations with period h/2e, as expected for a tubular superconductor, i.e. Little-Parks oscillations. We perform microscopic model calculations and compare the results for full and half metallic shells. We use an effective Hamiltonian derived from the Green's function of the proximitized semiconductor nanowire, where the presence of the superconductor is represented by a self energy. Furthermore, we incorporate the electrostatic band-bending at the metal-semiconductor interface as a rectangular narrow quantum well on the semiconductor side. The properties of the eigenstates of the effective Hamiltonian are determined by the spatial profile of the corresponding transverse modes in the normal state. For half-shell wires, transverse modes with high-enough energy expand outside the interface quantum well and generate eigenstates with mixed electron-hole character that surround the entire circumference of the nanowire, similar to eigenstates of the full-shell system. We identify these states as being responsible for the observed Little-Parks effect.

</details>


### [101] [Nonmonotonic temperature dependence of the thermopower of atomic-size gold contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12734)
*Thomas B. Möller,Marcel Strohmeier,Johannes Boneberg,Paul Leiderer,Wolfgang Belzig,Elke Scheer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过机械可控断裂结（MCBJ）技术测量了原子尺寸金接触的热电势（thermopower），发现其在18 K至295 K范围内呈现非单调温度依赖关系，在约150 K处出现最小值-2 μV/K，该行为与Landauer公式预期的线性依赖不符，论文将其归因于超越Landauer模型且与经典声子拖曳（phonon drag）符号相反的声子贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子尺寸接触的热电性质研究尚不充分，经典Landauer公式对量子相干导体预测的热电势呈线性温度依赖，但实验证据有限，需要更系统的测量来检验这一理论预期并探索潜在的声子贡献。

Method: 采用MCBJ技术制备原子尺寸金接触，在18 K至295 K温度范围内测量热电势；利用集成在光刻结构中的温度计直接测量聚焦激光加热一侧接触引起的温升；同时构建了基于能量依赖透射函数的理论模型。

Result: 电导直方图确认了输运的量子特性；系综平均热电势呈现非单调温度依赖，在约150 K处达到最小值-2 μV/K；低温和高温下的热电势值与文献报道一致，但中间温区的非单调行为与Landauer公式预测的线性依赖不符；理论模型仅能定性而非定量复现非单调行为。

Conclusion: 实验数据表明存在超越Landauer模型的声子贡献，其符号与块体材料中经典声子拖曳效应相反；热电势为原子尺寸结构的输运性质提供了重要洞见，且对于自由电子金属的原子接触，Landauer模型的线性近似在研究更复杂输运性质时必须谨慎使用。

Abstract: We report measurements of the thermopower of atomic-size gold contacts realized by the mechanically controllable break junction (MCBJ) technique over a temperature range from 18 K to 295 K. A thermometer included in the lithographic structure close to the constriction provides a direct measurement of the temperature increase generated by heating one side of the contact with a focused laser beam. While the conductance histograms confirm the quantum nature of the transport, we observe a nonmonotonic temperature dependence of the ensemble-averaged thermopower with a minimum of $-2\,μ$VK$^{-1}$ at about 150 K. The values for the thermopower obtained at the lowest and the high temperature are compatible with values reported in the literature, but the nonmonotonic behavior in between disagrees with the expected linear dependence for quantum coherent conductors described by the Landauer formula. We develop a theoretical model based on an energy dependent transmission function that qualitatively reproduces the nonmonotonic behavior, but fails quantitatively. We therefore interpret our data as a result of phonon contributions to the thermopower beyond the Landauer model and with opposite sign than the classical phonon drag known from bulk systems. Our findings show that, firstly, the thermopower gives important insight into the transport properties of atomic-size structures and second that the linear approximation of the Landauer model has to be used with caution when studying more complex transport properties even for atomic contacts from free-electron metals.

</details>


### [102] [Quantum charge pumping in helical systems: A comparative study of short- and long-range hopping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12914)
*Leila Eslami,Santanu K. Maiti,Fatemeh Bourbour*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用Keldysh非平衡格林函数方法，研究了通过紧束缚模型描述的螺旋结构（包含短程跳跃SRH或长程跳跃LRH）的电荷泵浦现象，揭示了螺旋性与扩展跳跃范围对能量分辨电流和直流泵浦电流的联合调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然量子泵浦已在多种低维系统中被研究，但高阶电子跳跃（超越最近邻）下螺旋几何结构中的谱电流和泵浦直流电流的详细行为尚未被系统探索。

Method: 采用Keldysh非平衡格林函数（Keldysh non-equilibrium Green's function）方法，对由紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）描述的单股螺旋结构进行电荷泵浦分析，模型中分别包含短程跳跃（short-range hopping, SRH）和长程跳跃（long-range hopping, LRH），并在时间周期性端电势下考察其响应。

Result: 对于LRH，当能级稀疏分布时，泵浦直流电流随化学势出现明显的类平台（plateau-like）区域，符合绝热输运（adiabatic transport）预期；而SRH产生参数敏感的电流，无清晰平台。平台稳定性由驱动频率控制：高频下Floquet边带混合（Floquet side-band mixing）破坏平台，产生振荡电流。相位依赖近似正弦，零相位滞后时电流为零。螺旋系统中，衰减指数（decay exponent）ℓ_c作为有效结构参数可调控泵浦电流的幅度和符号。

Conclusion: 这些发现填补了具有扩展跳跃的螺旋系统中谱电流和泵浦电流理解的空白，并为分析其他手性或准一维系统中的类似现象提供了可用工具。

Abstract: Using the Keldysh non-equilibrium Green's function approach, we investigate charge pumping through a single-stranded helical structure described by a tight-binding model that includes either short-range hopping (SRH) or long-range hopping (LRH). While quantum pumping has been studied in various low-dimensional systems, the detailed behavior of the spectral current and the pumped dc current in helical geometries in the presence of higher-order electron hopping (beyond nearest neighbors) has not yet been systematically explored. Here, we focus on the interplay between helicity and extended hopping ranges, analyzing how they jointly control the energy-resolved and dc pumped currents under time-periodic end potentials. For LRH, the pumped dc current exhibits pronounced plateau-like regions as a function of chemical potential when energy levels are sparsely spaced -- consistent with adiabatic transport -- whereas SRH yields more parameter-sensitive currents without clear plateaus. The plateau stability is controlled by the drive frequency: at higher frequencies, Floquet side-band mixing destroys the plateaus, leading to oscillatory currents. The phase dependence remains nearly sinusoidal, and the current vanishes at zero phase lag, confirming the necessity of out-of-phase potentials. Crucially, in helical systems, the decay exponent $(\ell_c)$ acts as an effective structural parameter that can tune both the magnitude and sign of the pumped current, offering a geometric knob for controlling quantum pumping. Our findings not only fill a gap in the understanding of spectral and pumped currents in helical systems with extended hopping but also provide tools that can be applied to analyze similar phenomena in other chiral or quasi-one-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [103] [A micromagnetic model with bidirectional magneto-thermal coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12933)
*Peiru Yi,Zian Xia,Weichao Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过将随机Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert（sLLG）方程与广义热传导方程耦合，建立了一个严格自洽的双向磁-热耦合模型，克服了传统自旋热电子学（spin caloritronics）中单向耦合近似的局限性。该模型严格满足热力学第一定律并恢复平衡玻尔兹曼统计，为研究非平衡磁-热动力学（如单向自旋波热输运效应）提供了微观基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自旋热电子学中的微磁框架采用单向耦合近似，忽略了磁耗散对热库的反馈效应，无法精确描述磁与热之间的双向能量交换过程。

Method: 将随机Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert（sLLG）方程与广义热传导方程进行双向耦合，将局部温度作为动力学变量（dynamical variable），使阻尼诱导的耗散和随机功以局域热源形式反馈到热浴中；并利用Ito随机微积分（Ito stochastic calculus）进行解析证明。

Result: 解析证明该耦合系统严格服从热力学第一定律（first law of thermodynamics）并自发恢复平衡态的玻尔兹曼统计（Boltzmann statistics）。空间分辨微磁模拟验证了能量交换机制，捕捉到由磁矩空间变化导致的有限热浴温度降低，以及交换相互作用下态密度的修正。

Conclusion: 该双向耦合框架为研究复杂非平衡磁-热动力学（如单向自旋波热输运效应）提供了稳健的微观基础，有助于推动先进自旋热电子学（spin-caloritronic）应用的发展。

Abstract: Most conventional micromagnetic frameworks in spin caloritronics rely on a unidirectional coupling approximation, wherein thermal fluctuations drive magnetization dynamics while the feedback of magnetic dissipation onto the thermal reservoir is neglected. Here, we establish a rigorously self-consistent bidirectional magneto-thermal coupling model by integrating the stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert (sLLG) equation with a generalized heat transfer equation. In this closed-loop framework, the local temperature acts as a dynamical variable, and the damping-induced dissipation alongside stochastic work dynamically feeds back into the thermal bath as localized heat sources. Utilizing Ito stochastic calculus, we analytically prove that this coupled system strictly obeys the first law of thermodynamics and spontaneously recovers the correct Boltzmann statistics at equilibrium. Spatially resolved micromagnetic simulations further validate the energy exchange mechanism, capturing the finite-bath temperature reduction induced by spatial variation of magnetic moments and the modified density of states under exchange interactions. This bidirectional framework provides a robust microscopic foundation for investigating complex nonequilibrium magneto-thermal dynamics, such as the unidirectional spin-wave heat conveyer effect, paving the way for advanced spin-caloritronic applications.

</details>


### [104] [Understanding quantum behaviors of an electron in a uniform magnetic field alternatively](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13290)
*Jin-Ming Wang,Yuan-Zao Gao,Dai-Lin Cun,Jian Jing*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过分析均匀磁场中电子的概率流密度，发现一个临界半径将平面自然划分为内部顺时针流动区和外部逆时针流动区，总概率流为零源于这两个区域的精确抵消。该双向流动图景为负角动量量子数的存在以及朗道能级的无限简并性提供了动力学解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子力学中，均匀磁场中电子的负角动量量子数态的总概率流为零，这与经典回旋运动图像相矛盾。虽然存在基于经典轨道的几何解释，但仍有必要探索其他替代性解释。

Method: 论文分析了概率流密度（probability current density），识别出一个临界半径（critical radius），该半径自然地将平面划分为内顺时针流动区和外逆时针流动区。通过定义相对于临界半径的分区动能角动量（partitioned kinetic angular momentum），揭示了电子同时携带两个相反旋转分量的内在竞争结构。

Result: 总概率流为零源自内部顺时针流与外部逆时针流的精确抵消。负量子数体现为内部反向旋转的强度，而净动能角动量（net kinetic angular momentum）保持为正。

Conclusion: 双向流动图景不仅为负角动量量子数的存在提供了动力学解释，也为朗道能级（Landau levels）的无限简并性（infinite degeneracy）提供了动力学诠释。

Abstract: Quantum mechanically, an electron moving in a uniform magnetic field forms Landau levels. A curious feature is that for states with a negative angular quantum number, the total probability current vanishes, which appears to contradict the classical picture of cyclotron motion. While a geometric interpretation based on classical orbits exists, alternative interpretations remain of interest. In this paper, we examine the probability current density and identify a critical radius that naturally partitions the plane into an inner clockwise-flow region and an outer counterclockwise-flow region. We show that the vanishing total current results from an exact cancellation between these two regions. Furthermore, by defining a partitioned kinetic angular momentum with respect to the critical radius, we reveal an intrinsic competitive structure: the electron simultaneously carries two opposing rotational components. The negative quantum number manifests in the strength of the inner counter-rotation, while the net kinetic angular momentum remains positive. This bidirectional flow picture also provides a dynamical interpretation of the infinite degeneracy of Landau levels.

</details>


### [105] [Phonon polariton confinement in isotopically pure MOVPE-grown BN triangles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13483)
*Maximilian Scharpey,Oskar Schröer,Daniel Wigger,Lena Miler,Jakub Iwański,Andrzej Wysmołek,Johannes Binder,Iris Niehues*

TL;DR: 本文研究了大面积外延氮化硼（BN）中声子极化激元（phonon polariton）的传播与限制特性，利用MOVPE生长的BN材料通过s-SNOM和nano-FTIR技术实现了长传播距离和可调谐的模式限制，为全外延微纳极化激元谐振器在纳米光子学和量子光学中的应用奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子极化激元具有双曲色散（hyperbolic dispersion）等独特性质，剥离型六方氮化硼（hBN）已被证明是相关研究的 promising 材料。然而，要实现实际应用，必须在大面积外延BN中实现高效声子极化激元传播与限制，这是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 采用金属有机气相外延（MOVPE）生长的BN材料，利用散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（s-SNOM）和纳米傅里叶变换红外光谱（nano-FTIR）研究声子极化激元特性。

Result: 观察到异常长的声子极化激元传播长度，表明BN层具有高晶体质量。通过外延生长的同位素纯三角形岛，进一步实现了高效的声子极化激元限制，且模式图案可通过入射光波长进行调谐。

Conclusion: 本研究为在纳米光子学（nanophotonics）和量子光学（quantum optics）中实现全外延、微米级、高质量的极化激元谐振器铺平了道路。

Abstract: Phonon polaritons, quasiparticles formed by the resonant hybridization of light and lattice vibrations, exhibit unique properties like the possibility of hyperbolic dispersions. In this context, exfoliated hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) has emerged as a promising material for phonon polariton-based research. However, to advance toward practical applications, it is essential to demonstrate efficient phonon-polariton propagation and confinement in large-area epitaxial BN. To address this topic, we use metalorganic vapor phase epitaxy (MOVPE)-grown BN and investigate the phonon polariton properties using scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscopy (s-SNOM) and nanoscale Fourier transform infrared spectroscopy (nano-FTIR). We report remarkably long phonon polariton propagation lengths, indicating the high crystalline quality of the BN layer. By using epitaxially grown isotopically pure triangular islands, we further demonstrate efficient phonon-polariton confinement with mode patterns tunable by the incident light wavelength. Our results pave the way for implementing all-epitaxial, microscale, high-quality polariton resonators for nanophotonics and quantum optics.

### [106] [Thermoelectric information engine driven by an autonomous Maxwell demon across quantum-to-classical transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13500)
*Maximiliano Bernal Santibañez,Felipe Barra,Jose Mondaca*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过Redfield主方程研究了一个三端热电引擎（thermoelectric engine），分析量子相干性（quantum coherence）与信息流（information flow）的作用。系统由双量子点与一个监控量子点构成，可解释为自主麦克斯韦妖（autonomous Maxwell demon）。研究发现两种由量子-经典转变（quantum-to-classical transition）界定的动力学 regime，并识别出声子浴（phonon bath）诱导的退相干（decoherence）如何抑制相干输运与信息流，从而揭示相干性对“妖”机制的增强作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在三端热电引擎中，研究量子相干性与信息流的作用，并澄清该装置在何种参数范围内可被解释为自主麦克斯韦妖。

Method: 采用Redfield主方程（Redfield master equation）描述系统动力学，辅以合适的Lindblad近似（Lindblad approximation）捕捉稳态行为；引入声子浴以研究退相干与非相干输运效应。

Result: 识别出两个由量子点间隧穿强度（interdot tunneling strength）控制的动力学 regime，分别对应第一类量子-经典转变；声子浴在弱隧穿 regime 诱导第二类转变，抑制相干输运与信息流向监控点；在特定参数区域，退相干削弱相干贡献的同时也削弱信息流，表明相干性可增强“妖”机制。

Conclusion: 模型展示了相干隧穿、退相干与非相干声子辅助输运在自主信息引擎中的竞争关系，并明确了各动力学 regime 下适用的热力学 Lindblad 描述。

Abstract: We study a three-terminal thermoelectric engine, focusing on the role of quantum coherence and information flow. A double-dot connects two reservoirs at different chemical potentials, while a third dot monitors their occupation via Coulomb interaction and can be interpreted as an autonomous Maxwell demon. Within the parameter range where the device operates as an engine, we identify conditions under which this interpretation holds. The system dynamics is described within a Redfield master equation that allows us to identify two distinct dynamical regimes with steady states well captured by suitable Lindblad approximations. These two regimes define a first quantum-to-classical transition controlled by the interdot tunneling strength. We further consider the effect of a phonon bath coupled to the double-dot, which induces a second quantum-to-classical transition by generating incoherent transport and decoherence in the small interdot tunneling regime. We identify a parameter region where phonon-induced decoherence suppresses both the coherent transport contribution and the information flow toward the monitoring dot, suggesting that coherence can enhance the demon mechanism in this regime. By tracking information and transport properties across these crossovers, our model shows how coherent tunneling, decoherence, and incoherent phonon-assisted transport compete in an autonomous information engine, while clarifying which thermodynamic Lindblad description is appropriate in each regime.

### [107] [Micron-sized magnonic 3-port rectilinear circulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13540)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用纳米线光栅实现自旋波的手性激发，设计了一个包含三个直线单向自旋波束通道的循环器，并采用全三端口自旋波谱学进行实验表征。

Result: 首次实验证实了微米级磁子循环器中三端口之间的自旋波循环；工作频带虽窄，但可通过调节外磁场（最高 100 mT）和光栅尺寸在 2–8 GHz 范围内实现宽范围调谐。

Abstract: The development of miniaturized non-reciprocal microwave technologies compatible with integrated circuit architectures remains a critical challenge for modern information technology. Here, we present the first experimental characterization of a micron-sized prototypical magnon circulator. Taking advantage of the chiral excitation of spin-waves via nanowire gratings, we propose an original design of a circulator involving three channels of rectilinear and unidirectional spin-wave beams. We demonstrate via a full 3-port spin-wave spectroscopy a genuine spin-wave circulation between the three ports. The narrow frequency band of operation can be tuned over a broad range of frequencies ($2$-$8$ GHz) with both an external field of up to $100$ mT, and the dimensions of the grating specifying the wavevectors. This proposed scheme opens up possibilities for new architectures of integrated and miniaturized non-reciprocal microwave devices.

### [108] [Engineering electrically-switchable quantum anomalous Hall states by spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13651)
*Maosen Qin,Ziwei Wang,Gyeongmin Kim,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Steven H. Simon,Siddharth A. Parameswaran,Hryhoriy Polshyn*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过在扭曲单层-双层石墨烯（tMBG）中引入WSe₂的邻近（proximity）耦合，实现对量子反常霍尔（QAH）态非易失性栅极开关行为的磁性能工程调控，并揭示了邻近诱导自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）在锁定自旋与谷自由度、调控磁化反转中的核心作用，进一步展示了无需重置磁态即可在QAH与金属态之间以及不同陈数（Chern number）QAH态之间进行栅极切换的功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯莫尔体系中基于QAH态的非易失性栅极开关为实现基于手性边缘态（chiral edge states）的拓扑电子学提供了有前景的路线，但该开关机制的有意利用需要同时控制QAH态的磁性质（magnetic properties）和亚稳定性（metastability）。此前演示主要依赖莫尔器件内禀的磁性能量景观（magnetic energy landscape），亟需一种可工程化调控该景观的新方法。

Method: 通过在扭曲单层-双层石墨烯（twisted monolayer-bilayer graphene, tMBG）上引入WSe₂的邻近耦合（proximity coupling），利用邻近诱导的自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）来重塑磁化反转（magnetization reversals），从而实现对QAH态非易失性电学开关行为中竞争态磁性质的调控。

Result: WSe₂邻近耦合可以重塑tMBG中负责QAH态非易失性电学开关的磁化反转过程，该效应归因于邻近诱导的SOC对自旋和谷自由度（spin and valley）的锁定作用，以及相较于非邻近体系对竞争态磁化特性的修改。此外，tMBG中强烈的磁亚稳定性（magnetic metastability）使得磁态可以在不重置的情况下，在QAH态与金属态之间、以及陈数|C|=2和1的QAH态之间进行栅极调控。

Conclusion: 邻近诱导的自旋-轨道耦合提供了一种在石墨烯基体系中工程化调控磁性能和可开关磁态的新途径，所展示的栅极可调QAH态切换功能为基于QAH手性边缘态的新型器件架构指明了方向。

Abstract: Nonvolatile gate-driven switching of quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) states in graphene moiré systems provides a promising route toward topological electronics based on chiral edge states. However, deliberate use of this switching mechanism requires control over both the magnetic properties and metastability of QAH states. While previous demonstrations mostly relied on the intrinsic magnetic energy landscape of moiré devices, here we show that this landscape can be engineered through proximity coupling to WSe2. We find that proximitizing twisted monolayer-bilayer graphene by WSe2 reshapes the magnetization reversals responsible for nonvolatile electrical switching of QAH states. We attribute this effect to the proximity-induced spin-orbit coupling (SOC), which can lock spin and valley and modify the magnetization of the competing states involved in switching compared with non-proximitized graphene systems. Our findings establish proximity-induced SOC as a new way to engineer magnetic properties and switchable magnetic states in graphene-based systems. We further demonstrate that strong magnetic metastability in tMBG allows the magnetic states to be gate-tuned between QAH and metallic regimes, and between QAH states with Chern numbers |C| = 2 and 1 without resetting the magnetic state. This functionality points toward new device architectures based on QAH chiral edge states.

### [109] [Dynamical large deviations and long-range correlations for local weak wave turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12624)
*Brice Douet,Freddy Bouchet*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文针对波湍流（wave turbulence）中的谱涨落问题，发展了一套基于大偏差理论（large deviation theory）的概率框架，导出局部波相互作用下的新大偏差原理，并分析了非平衡谱周围的高斯涨落结构，发现了三种长程关联贡献。该理论可推广至非均匀波湍流，为Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱的不稳定性及间歇性（intermittency）现象提供新解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典波湍流的动理学方程仅能描述波谱的平均演化，无法刻画有限尺寸效应和间歇性（intermittency）导致的涨落行为。为此，需要建立一个概率框架来研究波谱动力学时空轨迹的涨落特性，从而系统描述典型和稀有涨落。

Method: 基于先前波湍流的大偏差理论（large deviation theory）进行简化处理，推导了局部波相互作用（local wave interactions）条件下的新大偏差原理。在一篇联合文章中，该方法被推广为具有两个守恒量（质量和能量）的宏观涨落理论（Macroscopic Fluctuation Theory）的广义形式。本文利用该框架，分析了非平衡谱周围高斯涨落（Gaussian fluctuations）的方程结构，并采用一种适用于仅固定通量（fluxes）的边界条件的新方法进行计算。

Result: 在非平衡谱的高斯涨落中，除了通常的平衡贡献外，发现了三种长程关联（long-range correlations）贡献：一种由体相中的通量（flux in the bulk）驱动，一种由强迫（forcing）驱动，另一种由强迫的可能涨落驱动。这些贡献首次在仅固定通量的边界条件下被计算出来。该方法为更复杂场景下的波湍流分析提供了通用且可复现的方法。

Conclusion: 该理论可推广至非均匀波湍流（inhomogeneous wave turbulence），为某些一维非均匀四波相互作用模型（如Majda-McLaughlin-Tabak模型）中Kolmogorov-Zakharov谱的不稳定性（instability）提供了可能的解释。工作开启了对两点关联函数中普适与非普适性质的讨论，并为间歇性（intermittency）现象的研究开辟了新方向，部分间歇性现象已在文中得到初步发展。

Abstract: Wave turbulence describes the statistical dynamics of dispersive waves with weakly nonlinear interactions. While the classical kinetic equation captures the mean evolution of the wave spectrum, the study of its fluctuations due to finite-size effects and intermittency requires a probabilistic framework for space-time trajectories of the spectrum dynamics. Following the previous large deviation theories for wave turbulence, we develop a simplification meant for qualitative and numerical predictions of measurable quantities. We derive a new large deviation principle in the case of local wave interactions. It fully characterizes typical and rare fluctuations of the spectrum. In a joint article, we obtain a theory which is a generalised form of Macroscopic Fluctuation Theory, but with 2 conserved quantities (mass and energy). In this paper, we use it to analyse the structure of the equation for Gaussian fluctuations around out-of-equilibrium spectra. In addition to the usual equilibrium contribution, we obtain long-range correlations, which can be decomposed into 3 contributions: one is driven by the flux in the bulk and another is driven by the forcing and its possible fluctuations. In addition, these contributions are computed for the first time with a method adapted to boundary conditions where only the fluxes are fixed. The results provide a general, replicable method for analyzing wave turbulence in more complex settings. Finally, the generalization of this theory to the inhomogeneous wave turbulence provides a possible explanation to the instability of the Kolmogorov-Zakharov spectra in some 1D inhomogeneous models with 4-wave interactions such as the Majda-McLaughlin-Tabak. This work opens the discussion regarding universal and non universal properties in two-point correlation functions. This opens new range of study on the phenomena of intermittency which is partially developed here.

### [110] [Self-similar imploding solutions of the 1D compressible Euler equations with a far field cutoff](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12758)
*Jack Luong,Scott Ramsey,Andrea L. Bertozzi,Roy Baty*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对Kidder一维等熵压缩欧拉方程（Euler equations）的汇聚解（imploding solution），提出用恒定密度截断（constant density cutoff）替代无界远场条件，发现截断处出现非中心稀疏波（non-centered rarefaction）抑制了汇聚，并给出了精确解析解和数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的光滑汇聚解（如Guderley解）虽然理论完备，但在数值计算中不稳定且难以实现；而Kidder解虽有闭式解且可数值计算，但在远场无界。因此，需要一种既能保持可计算性又能消除远场无界性的替代方法。

Method: 采用一维Kidder公式，将原来的无界远场条件替换为初始数据的恒定密度截断（constant density cutoff），从而构造了一个有界域上的解析可解问题。

Result: 截断处产生了一个非中心稀疏波（non-centered rarefaction），该波有效抑制了汇聚过程。给出了该截断问题的精确解析解（exact analytic solution），并通过数值模拟验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 该截断模型克服了Kidder解远场无界的缺陷，提供了精确解析解并揭示了非中心稀疏波对汇聚的抑制机制，为可压缩欧拉方程汇聚问题的数值计算提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Imploding solutions to the radially symmetric, isentropic, compressible Euler equations have been well-studied, inspired by the work of Guderley. However, these smooth imploding solutions are shown to be numerically unstable and difficult to compute in practice. On the other hand, the imploding solution of Kidder has a closed form solution and is numerically computable. But, it is unbounded in the far field. We consider Kidder's formulation in one dimension in which the unbounded far field condition is replaced with a constant density cutoff of the initial data. Strikingly, a non-centered rarefaction emerges from the cutoff and suppresses the implosion. We present an exact analytic solution to the problem with the cutoff and support our theoretical predictions with numerical simulations.

</details>


### [111] [Optimal minimax formula for bounds on ensemble averages of statistically stationary three-dimensional Navier-Stokes flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12825)
*Anne Bronzi,Cecília F. Mondaini,Ricardo M. S. Rosa*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程（Navier-Stokes equations）的系综平均（ensemble averages）流动量，建立了一个最优上界公式，该公式呈现为极小极大问题（minimax problem）形式。作者通过利用Foias-Prodi平稳统计解（Foias-Prodi stationary statistical solutions）空间克服了三维情形下全局适定性（global well-posedness）缺失的挑战，并发现最优上界在至多两个Dirac delta测度（Dirac delta measures）的特定凸组合（convex combinations）上达到，而非单个测度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Tobasco、Goluskin和Doering（2018）提出的有限维系统极小极大框架以及Rosa和Temam（2022）建立的二维Navier-Stokes方程结果推广至三维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程，并解决三维情形因缺乏全局适定性所带来的根本性困难。

Method: 在Foias-Prodi平稳统计解空间中开展工作，利用概率测度（probability measures）特定子空间在相空间弱拓扑（weak topology of the phase space）下的紧致性（compactness）与连续性（continuity）性质，推导出极小极大形式的能量耗散率（energy dissipation rate）上界公式，并通过分析均值能量耗散不等式（mean energy dissipation inequalities）的约束来刻画达到最优界的极值测度（extreme points）结构。

Result: 得到了三维Navier-Stokes方程系综平均流动量的最优上界公式，该公式形式为极小极大问题。区别于以往情形，三维最优上界并非由单个Dirac delta测度达到，而是在至多两个Dirac delta测度的特定凸组合上达到。

Conclusion: 本文建立的三维最优上界公式扩展了此前有限维与二维情形的理论框架，揭示了三维Navier-Stokes方程中达到最优上界的测度具有独特的极值结构——即凸组合而非单一测度，这反映了三维湍流问题中均值能量耗散不等式所带来的约束特性。

Abstract: We establish an optimal upper bound formula for ensemble averages of flow quantities associated with the three-dimensional incompressible Navier-Stokes equations. The formula takes the form of a minimax problem, extending the framework developed by Tobasco, Goluskin, and Doering (2018) for finite-dimensional systems and by Rosa and Temam (2022) for the two-dimensional Navier-Stokes equations. The lack of global well-posedness for the 3D case presents a significant challenge, which we overcome by working within the space of Foias-Prodi stationary statistical solutions. The minimax formula is derived by exploiting suitable compactness and continuity properties of specific subspaces of probability measures under the weak topology of the phase space. A distinguishing feature of our result is the characterization of the maximizing measures: unlike the previous cases, the optimal bounds in 3D are achieved on extreme points that are specific convex combinations of at most two Dirac delta measures, instead of exactly one, a structure that naturally appears from the constraints given by the mean energy dissipation inequalities in the characterization of the Foias-Prodi stationary statistical solutions.

</details>


### [112] [A symmetry theorem for localizable steady solutions of the 3D Euler equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13462)
*Daniel Peralta-Salas,Radu Slobodeanu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明，在有界区域Ω内，任何解析的可局部化（localizable）三维稳态欧拉流（steady Euler flow）必然是轴对称的，且Ω是旋转对称区域，其横截面为凸边界曲线围成的圆盘或圆环。这是三维稳态欧拉流的首个对称性定理，并表明在磁流体动力学（MHD）平衡中，满足等动力条件（isodynamic condition）的磁场满足Grad猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gavrilov利用可局部化性质构造了首个光滑紧支撑的三维欧拉稳态解。本文旨在探索可局部化三维稳态欧拉流在解析条件下是否必然具有对称性，并揭示该性质在磁约束聚变等离子体平衡理论（如Grad猜想）中的关联。

Method: 基于可局部化（localizable）的定义——压力函数沿流线为常数——作为核心分析前提，结合解析性（analyticity）假设，对三维欧拉流在有限区域内的几何与对称性进行数学证明。

Result: 任何解析的可局部化三维稳态欧拉流在有界区域Ω内必然是轴对称的（axisymmetric），且Ω为旋转对称区域，其横截面为圆盘（disk）或圆环（annulus），边界曲线为凸（convex）。这是三维稳态欧拉流的首个对称性定理。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，在磁流体动力学（MHD）平衡框架下，Grad猜想对于满足等动力条件（isodynamic condition）的磁场成立。等动力条件由Palumbo在1960年代提出，旨在最小化等离子体约束装置中的粒子漂移效应。

Abstract: A steady Euler flow is localizable if the pressure function is constant along its stream lines. This property was used by Gavrilov to construct the first smooth compactly supported steady states of 3D Euler. We prove that any analytic localizable 3D Euler flow in a bounded domain $Ω$ is axisymmetric and $Ω$ is a rotationally symmetric domain whose transverse section is a disk or an annulus with convex boundary curves. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first symmetry theorem for 3D steady Euler flows. In the context of MHD equilibria, this result shows that Grad's conjecture holds true for magnetic fields satisfying the isodynamic condition, a property introduced by Palumbo in the 1960's to minimize the effect of particle drifts in plasma confinement devices.

</details>

### [113] [Self-similar asymptotics in the decay problem for the Volterra lattice with zero boundary condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13137)
*V. E. Adler,B. I. Suleimanov*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文研究零边界条件下Volterra格点（Volterra lattice）初始稳态的衰变问题，证明该过程渐近自相似，并计算了衰变波的传播速度、渐近主导项与修正项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解零边界条件下Volterra格点初始稳态的衰变动力学，揭示其渐近行为与波传播特性。

Method: 通过解析分析，证明衰变过程具有渐近自相似性（asymptotically self-similar），并在主扇区（main sector）和过渡扇区（transition sector）中分别推导了传播速度、渐近主导项及修正项。

Result: 确定了衰变波的传播速度、渐近展开的主导项及修正项，涵盖波的主扇区和过渡扇区。

Conclusion: 零边界条件下Volterra格点的初始稳态衰变是一个渐近自相似过程，波前传播速度与扇区结构可由解析形式描述。

Abstract: The article is devoted to the problem of decay of initial stationary state for the Volterra lattice with zero boundary condition. We show that this process is asymptotically self-similar and calculate the propagation velocity of the decay wave, the leading terms of the asymptotics and corrections, in the main and transition sectors of the wave.

</details>

### [114] [Manipulation of the gyrotropic mode frequency and band structure in an FM / AFM disk via vortex imprinting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13181)
*E. V. Skorokhodov,E. A. Karashtin,I. A. Fedotov,I. Yu. Pashen'kin,M. V. Sapozhnikov*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在铁磁/反铁磁（FM/AFM）异质结系统中，交换耦合效应对涡旋动力学的影响尚未得到充分的实验研究，尤其是旋回模式的频率变化和非线性行为。

Method: 制备了Ni80Fe20(12 nm)/Ir80Mn20(5 nm) FM/AFM异质结微米级圆盘，将涡旋磁态（vortex magnetic state）印刻到AFM层中，并采用磁共振力显微镜（magnetic resonance force microscopy, MRFM）对单个FM/AFM圆盘中的磁振荡进行局部研究。

Conclusion: 涡旋动力学在非中心对称系统（noncentrosymmetric system）中表现出强非线性行为，该非线性是双倍频率峰出现的根本原因。

Abstract: We experimentally investigate the magnetic gyrotropic mode in a system of vortex ferromagnetic (FM) nanooscillator exchange coupled to an antiferromagnetic (AFM) layer. The micron-sized disks formed from the Ni80Fe20(12 nm) / Ir80Mn20 (5 nm) FM/AFM heterostructure are prepared so that the vortex magnetic state is imprinted into the AFM layer. We apply a magnetic resonance force microscopy (MRFM) method to locally study magnetic oscillations in single FM/AFM disks. We show that the gyrotropic mode frequency is significantly (approximately 4 times) shifted to the high frequency compared to similar structure consisting of a single ferromagnetic disk. Upon applying an in-plane magnetic field, we observe a strong peak at a double frequency which was previously predicted in theory. This is governed by the fact that vortex dynamics is strongly nonlinear in a noncentrosymmetric system under investigation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Following our earlier work on studying 3-dimensional nuclear recoil response to Galactic Weakly Interacting Massive Particles (WIMPs) in directional direct Dark Matter detectors, in this paper, we simulate 3-D coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CEvNS) events induced by Solar B-8 neutrinos. Our numerical results show that, in contrast to the approximately fixed patterns of the WIMP-induced signals, the characteristic ring-like angular distributions of the nuclear recoil flux/energy of CEvNS events show clearly annual variations along the trajectories of the moving direction of incident Solar neutrinos in different celestial coordinate systems without experimentally distinguishable target dependence.

### [116] [Black Hole Polarimetry III: Universal Polarization of Synchrotron Radiation at the Horizon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12518)
*Andrew Chael,Alexandru Lupsasca,George N. Wong,Zachary Gelles,Eliot Quataert*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文发现黑洞事件视界附近同步辐射的线偏振模式具有普适行为，完全由黑洞自旋和观测者倾角决定，与磁场几何无关，并推导出解析公式。该模式在广义相对论磁流体模拟和M87*的观测中均可验证，可用于测量黑洞自旋及检验Blandford–Znajek过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量黑洞事件视界附近偏振编码的电磁能量流方向，可以判断能量是否由吸积等离子体或黑洞自旋提供；但此前缺乏对偏振模式是否依赖于磁场构型的理解，因此需要检验该模式的普适性。

Method: 在稳态、轴对称且退化的克尔磁层中，考虑从贯穿越过视界的磁力线（horizon-threading field lines）底部发射的同步辐射（synchrotron radiation）的线偏振（linear polarization），推导其观测偏振模式的解析表达式，并与广义相对论磁流体力学（General Relativistic Magnetohydrodynamics, GRMHD）模拟的时均图像进行对比。

Result: 发现观测到的偏振模式具有普适性：完全由黑洞自旋（black hole spin）和观测者倾角决定，与磁场几何无关；并推导出依赖于自旋的视界偏振模式（spin-dependent horizon polarization pattern）的简单解析公式。该模式在GRMHD模拟的时均图像中也趋近于理论预测值。

Conclusion: 未来利用微角秒分辨率的甚长基线干涉测量（Very-Long-Baseline Interferometry, VLBI）观测M87*，可检测偏振向视界唯一值的趋势，从而实现对黑洞自旋的新测量，并为磁场线穿越视界并通过Blandford–Znajek过程提取旋转能提供证据。

Abstract: Polarized images of a black hole encode the direction of electromagnetic energy flow near its event horizon. Measuring polarization from near-horizon emission can determine whether this energy flow is powered by the accreting plasma or the black hole spin. Here we consider the linear polarization of synchrotron radiation emitted from the base of horizon-threading field lines in a time-stationary, axisymmetric, and degenerate Kerr magnetosphere. We show that the observed polarization pattern displays universal behavior: it is completely determined by the black hole spin and observer inclination and is independent of the magnetic field geometry. We derive a simple analytic formula for this spin-dependent horizon polarization pattern. We find that this predicted pattern is also approached in time-averaged images from General Relativistic Magnetohydrodynamic simulations. Future observations with Very-Long-Baseline Interferometry at microarcsecond resolution could detect the trend of polarization toward the unique horizon value in M87*. Such observations may enable new measurements of black hole spin and provide evidence that magnetic field lines thread the horizon and extract spin energy via the Blandford--Znajek process.

</details>


### [117] [Implementation of multi-grid Poisson solver in numerical relativity and its application to gravitational collapse of massive star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12542)
*Kenta Kiuchi,Hirotada Okawa*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种数值相对论（numerical relativity）中基于网格的新多重网格泊松求解器（multi-grid Poisson solver），并在双黑洞、静态与旋转中子星、引力坍缩大质量恒星等初始值问题中验证了其性能。通过约束保持重网格方案（constraint-preserving regrid prescription）与多重网格求解器结合，实现了对9倍太阳质量恒星引力坍缩至核反弹（core bounce）的高分辨率模拟，重子质量、ADM质量与类ADM角动量分别达到约10^{-3}%和10^{-2}–10^{-1}%的守恒精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数值相对论中的引力坍缩与双致密天体模拟需要高效精确的泊松求解器（Poisson solver），但现有方案在精度与计算效率上存在平衡问题，尤其在高分辨率多尺度问题中表现不足。

Method: 提出基于网格的多重网格泊松求解器（grid-based multi-grid Poisson solver），在约束保持重网格方案下动态调整分辨率，并应用于数值相对论中微子辐射输运流体动力学模拟（neutrino-radiation-transfer hydrodynamics simulation）。

Result: 在双黑洞、静态/旋转中子星及9倍太阳质量恒星引力坍缩至核反弹的模拟中，重子质量、ADM质量（ADM mass）及类ADM角动量（ADM-like angular momentum）的守恒误差分别约为10^{-3}%和10^{-2}–10^{-1}%。

Conclusion: 新开发的多重网格泊松求解器结合约束保持重网格方案，能够在大质量恒星引力坍缩模拟中实现高精度守恒，为数值相对论中多尺度问题的计算提供可靠工具。

Abstract: We develop a new grid-based multi-grid Poisson solver in numerical relativity. We report the performance of the multi-grid Poisson solver in the initial value problems for two-puncture black holes, a static spherical neutron star, a uniformly rotating neutron star in equilibrium, and a gravitationally collapsing massive star. As a demonstration, we conduct a numerical-relativity neutrino-radiation-transfer hydrodynamics simulation of the gravitational collapse of the $9M_\odot$ massive star in Ref.~\cite{Aguilera-Dena:2020mfh} up to the core bounce. During the simulation, we employ the constraint-preserving regird prescription with the newly developed multi-grid Poisson solver to improve the resolution. It shows that the baryonic mass, the Arnowit-Deser-Misner (ADM) mass, and the ADM-like angular momentum are, respectively, preserved with $O(10^{-3})\%$ and $O(10^{-2})$--$O(10^{-1})$\% accuracy.
