### [118] [Classification of Compact Stars via Machine Learning and Neural Network Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13369)
*D. Neraki,G. Koufetidis,I. Stergakis,Th. Diakonidis,Ch. C. Moustakidis*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用机器学习（machine learning）和深度学习（deep learning）技术，基于大规模物态方程（equation of state, EoS）数据集，训练分类模型以从可观测宏观性质（质量、半径、潮汐形变能力）推断致密星（中子星与夸克星）的内部组成，结果显示高精度区分是可行的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多信使天文学（multimessenger astronomy）的进展虽提升了对致密物质的理解，但致密星（compact star）的内部组成（中子星、夸克星、混合星或含奇异组分的星体）仍然不确定。本文旨在探究是否能从质量、半径和潮汐形变能力等可观测物理量推断致密星的内部组成。

Method: 采用机器学习（machine learning）和深度学习（deep learning）技术，在描述中子星（neutron star）和夸克星（quark star）的大量物态方程（equation of state, EoS）数据集上进行训练。从这些EoS生成对应的质量-半径关系（mass-radius relation），涵盖广泛的恒星构型，随后训练分类模型以根据宏观性质识别致密天体的类型。

Result: 合适的可观测量组合能够以非常高的准确率区分中子星与夸克星，表明机器学习方法在探测致密物质组成方面具有潜力。

Conclusion: 机器学习方法可有效从宏观观测推断致密星内部组分，但需进一步研究纳入混合星（hybrid star）及其他奇异物质（exotic matter）场景，以验证该方法论的鲁棒性和普适性。

Abstract: Recent advances in multimessenger astronomy, particularly through gravitational-wave observations of compact-object mergers, have significantly improved our understanding of dense matter. Nevertheless, the internal composition of compact stars remains uncertain. Depending on the underlying equation of state (EoS), these objects may be neutron stars composed primarily of nucleons, quark stars made of deconfined quark matter, or hybrid stars containing both hadronic and quark phases. More exotic constituents, such as hyperons, meson condensates, or dark matter, have also been proposed. In this work, we investigate whether the internal composition of compact stars can be inferred from observable quantities, including mass, radius, and tidal deformability. To address this problem, we employ machine-learning and deep-learning techniques trained on a larg dataset of EoSs describing both neutron stars and quark stars. From these EoSs, we generate the corresponding mass radius relations spanning a wide range of stellar configurations. The resulting dataset is used to train and evaluate classification models aimed at identifying the nature of compact objects from their macroscopic properties. Our results indicate that suitable combinations of observables can distinguish neutron stars from quark stars with very high accuracy. These findings demonstrate the potential of machine-learning approaches as tools for probing the composition of dense matter. However, further studies incorporating additional scenarios, including hybrid stars and other exotic forms of matter, are required to establish the robustness and general applicability of this methodology.

</details>

### [119] [Basis sets and Coulomb resolutions in rotational coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13324)
*Edward Lilley*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用广义拉普拉斯对称算子（generalised Laplacian symmetry operators），在多个可分离坐标系（包括两个R-可分离系统）中构造基组或库仑分解（Coulomb resolutions），并给出了三个可用单个雅可比多项式（Jacobi polynomial）封闭表达的基组，同时展示了球极坐标或长球面坐标基组向双球面或环面坐标基组的变换方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展基组构造的可行几何构型，以服务于星系动力学（galactic dynamics）和计算化学（computational chemistry）领域的实际需求。

Method: 采用广义拉普拉斯对称算子，在多种可分离坐标系（包括两个R-可分离系统）中构造基组或库仑分解；通过单个雅可比多项式实现三个基组的封闭形式（closed-form）表达，并建立球极坐标或长球面坐标基组向双球面或环面坐标基组的变换关系。

Result: 推导出三个可用单个雅可比多项式封闭表达的基组，其中两个在长球面坐标（prolate spheroidal coordinates）中，一个在柱坐标（cylindrical coordinates）中；任何球极坐标（spherical polar coordinates）或长球面坐标基组均可变换为双球面（bispherical）或环面（toroidal）坐标基组。

Conclusion: 本文成功拓展了可构造基组的坐标系种类，特别是引入R-可分离系统，为相关领域的基组选择提供了更多几何可能性。

Abstract: Using generalised Laplacian symmetry operators, we construct basis sets or Coulomb resolutions in several separable coordinate systems, including two R-separable systems. This expands the possible geometries in which basis set construction is feasible, a problem which is relevant to both galactic dynamics and computational chemistry. In particular we derive three basis sets (two in prolate spheroidal and one in cylindrical coordinates) which are expressible in closed-form using a single Jacobi polynomial. We also show how any spherical polar or prolate spheroidal basis set may be transformed into a bispherical or toroidal basis set.

</details>

### [120] [Constraining the real scalar singlet extension of the SM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12533)
*Moritz Bosse,Gudrun Hiller,Daniel Litim,Fabio Maltoni,Michael J. Ramsey-Musolf,Simone Tentori,Guotao Xia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在标准模型实标量单态扩展（real scalar singlet extension）框架下，结合电弱相变（electroweak phase transition）、高标度真空稳定性与对撞机探针，发现当单态标量质量接近1 TeV时仍存在与强一阶电弱相变兼容的参数空间，并指出HL-LHC和FCC将分别提供大范围检验和最终发现能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的电弱相变是平滑交叉（crossover），无法解释重子不对称性（baryogenesis）所需的强一阶相变，且其真空稳定性在高能标下存在问题。本文旨在通过实标量单态扩展，同时探索强一阶电弱相变、真空稳定性与对撞机实验之间的关联。

Method: 将电弱相变分析和真空稳定性分析与当前及未来的对撞机探针联合研究，探针包括：精确希格斯测量（precision Higgs measurements）、希格斯三线性耦合（Higgs trilinear coupling）、电弱精密可观测量（Electroweak Precision Observables, EWPO）以及重单态类标量在ZZ和双希格斯（di-Higgs）末态中的共振搜索。

Result: 存在与强一阶电弱相变兼容的参数空间，单态类标量质量最高可达约1 TeV。希格斯自耦合（Higgs self-coupling）的偏差大于希格斯-Z耦合的偏差，使希格斯势测量成为关键探针。HL-LHC可检验大部分参数空间，FCC将提供终极发现和模型区分能力。

Conclusion: 实标量单态扩展模型能够同时实现强一阶电弱相变和真空稳定性，且未来对撞机（特别是FCC）对该参数空间具有强大的检验与区分能力，为超出标准模型的新物理提供了可检验的理论框架。

Abstract: The real scalar singlet extension of the standard model provides a minimal framework in which the Higgs sector can realise a strong first-order electroweak phase transition and improve the stability of the electroweak vacuum. We combine the electroweak phase transition and high-scale vacuum stability with current and projected collider probes, including precision Higgs measurements, the Higgs trilinear coupling, EWPO and resonant searches for a heavy singlet-like scalar in $ZZ$ and di-Higgs final states. Focusing on a singlet heavier than the standard model Higgs, we find that there is parameter space compatible with a strong first-order electroweak phase transition for singlet-like scalar masses up to nearly 1 TeV. Deviations in the Higgs self-coupling can be larger than those in the Higgs--$Z$ coupling, making Higgs-potential measurements a key probe. We find that the HL-LHC will test a large fraction of the parameter space, while the FCC will provide ultimate discovery and model-discrimination capabilities.

</details>


### [121] [Mass spectra and electromagnetic characteristics of the $K^{(*)}\bar D^{(*)}$ and $K^{(*)}{D}^{(*)}$ molecular tetraquarks from the coupled-channel dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13088)

### [122] [Electroweak precision physics via angular distributions in hadronic $τ$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13139)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 推导了任意双赝标量末态（包括τ极化）的全微分角分布；将结果线性扩展到弱有效场论（Weak Effective Field Theory, WEFT）的新物理耦合框架；构造了极化和非极化τ的基准可观测量，使主导强子形状因子在标准模型预言中自然抵消。

Result: 获得了无需对主导强子形状因子建模即可计算的标准模型基准观测量；这些可观测量对超出标准模型（Beyond-the-Standard-Model, BSM）的修正，特别是来自张量流（tensor currents）的修正，具有特征性响应。

Conclusion: 该工作为Belle II、Chiral Belle等极化τ实验、超级τ-粲工厂及FCC-ee等未来高统计量设施提供了具体的检验目标，用以测试强子τ衰变的电弱结构（electroweak structure）。

Abstract: Hadronic tau decays provide a unique low-energy laboratory for the charged-current interaction between quarks and leptons. Their use as an electroweak precision sector is, however, limited by nonperturbative QCD dynamics in the resonance region, encoded in hadronic form factors. In this work we show that angular information in two-hadron tau decays can be used to construct observables in which these form factors cancel, leading to first-principles Standard Model predictions up to light-quark-mass and radiative corrections. We derive the fully differential distributions for arbitrary two-pseudoscalar final states, including tau polarization, and extend them to the Weak Effective Field Theory at linear order in new-physics couplings. We then illustrate our strategy with several benchmark observables, for both unpolarized and polarized taus, whose Standard Model predictions can be obtained without modelling the dominant hadronic form factors and which receive characteristic beyond-the-Standard-Model corrections, in particular from tensor currents. Abstract: We consider different scenarios which lead to a damping of the neutrino oscillation probability and investigate their impact on the first JUNO results. Finally, we study the effect of invisible neutrino decay. In all cases with the first data JUNO can already place competitive bounds on the parameter space of the scenarios under consideration, while also maintaining a robust measurement of the standard neutrino oscillation parameters.

### [124] [Are Primordial Black Holes a Natural Dark Matter Candidate?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12775)
*Stefano Profumo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过三种互补的微调测度（fine-tuning measures），系统比较了多种原初黑洞（PBH）暗物质产生机制和粒子暗物质基准的自然性（naturalness），发现了三种自然性普遍性类别（universality classes），并指出“PBH暗物质普遍精细调谐”的说法混淆了最差情形与完整景观。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）在行星质量窗口（asteroid-mass window, $10^{17}$-$10^{22}$ g）内可构成全部暗物质，但常被认定为精细调谐（fine-tuned）。本文旨在系统性检验这一论断是否成立。

Method: 作者将三种互补的微调测度（fine-tuning measures）统一应用于广泛的理论景观（landscape）：三种非暴胀PBH产生机制、六类暴胀PBH模型以及七个粒子暗物质基准，所有模型均针对同一观测目标进行评估。由此识别出三种由丰度映射（abundance map）的解析结构完全决定的自然性普遍性类别（naturalness universality classes）。

Result: 发现三类自然性普遍性类别：偏畴壁（biased-domain-wall）PBH与离共振弱相互作用大质量粒子（off-resonance WIMP）及冻入粒子（freeze-in particles）同属最自然层级；早期物质主导（early-matter-domination）和一阶相变（first-order phase transition）PBH机制与共湮灭WIMP处于中间层级，其微调测度等于形成标度与物质-辐射平衡标度之比的对数；单场超慢滚暴胀（single-field ultra-slow-roll inflationary collapse）因双指数敏感性而严重调谐。

Conclusion: “PBH暗物质普遍是精细调谐的”这一说法混淆了最差情形与涵盖所有自然性层级的完整景观。此外，三测度协议解决了文献中Barbieri-Giudice与Iovino-Riotto两种微调测度之间的张力，两者在本文发展的两层分解框架下得到调和。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) in the asteroid-mass window ($10^{17}$-$10^{22}$ g) can account for all of the dark matter without violating any observational constraint, yet are routinely dismissed as fine-tuned. I put that dismissal to the test by applying three complementary fine-tuning measures uniformly across a broad landscape: three non-inflationary PBH production mechanisms, six classes of inflationary PBH models, and seven particle dark matter benchmarks, all evaluated against the same observable target. Three distinct naturalness universality classes emerge, determined entirely by the analytic structure of the abundance map rather than by the nature of the dark matter candidate. Biased-domain-wall PBHs are as natural as off-resonance weakly interacting massive particles and freeze-in particles; early-matter-domination and first-order phase transition PBH mechanisms occupy an intermediate tier alongside coannihilating WIMPs, unified by a structural identity in which the fine-tuning measure equals the logarithm of the ratio of the formation scale to the matter-radiation equality scale; and single-field ultra-slow-roll inflationary collapse is severely tuned for a distinct reason: a double exponential in which the power spectrum amplitude is itself exponentially sensitive to the inflaton potential coefficients, on top of the exponential collapse sensitivity of the abundance map. My main conclusion is that {\em the claim that PBH dark matter is generically fine-tuned conflates the worst case with a landscape spanning every naturalness tier}. The three-measure protocol also resolves a tension in the recent literature: the Barbieri-Giudice and Iovino-Riotto fine-tuning measures answer complementary questions and are reconciled within the two-layer decomposition developed here.

Method: 首先构建标量场与扭率耦合的理论，使中微子质量随局部密度变化（mass varying neutrino mass）。随后分析该机制如何修改标准MSW共振条件（MSW resonance condition），并计算对应的味转换概率（flavor conversion probability）。最后利用Super-Kamiokande、Borexino、SNO等太阳中微子实验数据进行参数约束。

Result: 该机制以一种独特方式修改了标准MSW共振条件，导致味转换概率出现可探测的偏移。基于太阳中微子实验数据，研究给出了对扭率-标量耦合参数（torsion-scalar coupling parameters）的约束限制。

Conclusion: 该工作通过质量可变中微子振荡（mass varying neutrino oscillations）为teleparallel引力提供了具体的实验检验途径。所得到的耦合参数约束为进一步区分不同引力理论提供了观测依据。

Abstract: In the Cartan teleparallel formulation of gravity, a scalar field coupled to the torsion tensor can acquire an environment dependent effective mass. This gives rise to a screening effect: Inside dense bodies such as the Sun, the scalar field is suppressed, causing the mass varying neutrino mass to vary with local density. We investigate the impact of this torsion-induced screening on solar neutrino oscillations. The mechanism modifies the standard MSW resonance condition in a distinct way, leading to detectable shift in the flavor conversion probability. Using data from solar neutrino experiments (Super-Kamiokande, Borexino, SNO), we place constraints on the torsion-scalar coupling parameters. ### [126] [Electroweak First-Order Phase Transition Triggered by Non-Gaussian Fluctuations of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-Symmetric Spectator Scalar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13514)
*Bo-Qiang Lu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种利用Z₂对称旁观者标量场（spectator scalar field）的非高斯原始涨落（non-Gaussian primordial fluctuations）触发宇宙一阶电弱相变（first-order electroweak phase transition）的新机制。该旁观者场的大幅度涨落可改变希格斯粒子热质量（Higgs thermal mass）并增强热势垒（thermal barrier），从而推动强一阶相变的发生。非高斯性显著提高了大幅度涨落的出现概率，使宇宙中相当大比例的区域能够经历该相变。该旁观者场同时可通过相干振荡（coherent oscillations）充当冷暗物质（cold dark matter）候选者，再现观测到的遗迹丰度（relic abundance）。所产生的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）峰值位于10⁻³–10⁻¹ Hz频段，有望被未来空间干涉仪（space-based interferometers）探测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入一个具有Z₂对称性的旁观者标量场，利用其原始非高斯涨落来局域性地修改希格斯粒子的有效热势能（effective thermal potential）。非高斯性（non-Gaussianities）被纳入涨落谱，以增强大幅度涨落的发生概率。随后通过旁观者场的相干振荡动力学自然地与冷暗物质遗迹丰度（cold dark matter relic abundance）建立联系。

Result: 非高斯涨落能够有效提升热势垒高度，使得宇宙中相当大比例的区域经历强一阶电弱相变。该旁观者场通过相干振荡可复现观测到的暗物质遗迹丰度。对应相变过程产生的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）峰值出现在10⁻³–10⁻¹ Hz频率范围内，处于未来空间引力波探测器的灵敏度窗口内。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了一个将电弱一阶相变触发、暗物质产生与随机引力波信号三者统一联系的新机制。非高斯原始涨落在其中发挥了核心作用。这一机制不仅避免了引入过多新粒子自由度，还给出了未来空间干涉仪（如LISA、TianQin、DECIGO等）可检验的引力波特征信号。

Abstract: We propose a novel mechanism to trigger a first-order cosmological electroweak phase transition using non-Gaussian primordial fluctuations of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric spectator scalar field. We show that the large fluctuations of the spectator field can modify the Higgs thermal mass and enhance the thermal barrier, thereby enabling a strong first-order phase transition. Non-Gaussianities in the primordial fluctuation spectrum significantly increase the probability of large-amplitude fluctuations, allowing a substantial fraction of the Universe to undergo the transition. The spectator field also naturally serves as a cold dark matter candidate through its coherent oscillations, reproducing the observed relic abundance. The resulting stochastic gravitational wave background peaks in the $10^{-3}$-$10^{-1}$ Hz band, making it detectable by future space-based interferometers.

### [127] [The Residual $288$ of the $E_8\timesωE_8$ Program as Adjoint-Lineage Scaffolding Labels: an Ontology, and the Status of the Bifermionic Lagrangian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12477)
*Tejinder P. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在 $E_8\times\omega E_8$ 八元数统一方案中论证，$E_8$ 的维数（496）并非粒子计数，而是一个标签账簿（label ledger）；通过将手征费米子实现为 Cl(6) 极小理想旋量（minimal-ideal spinors）而非 $E_8$ 表示分量，规避了 Distler-Garibaldi 无-go 定理；框架超出标准模型的内容仅为惰性中微子和一个复合标量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在八元数统一方案中，$E_8$ 的大维数（496）是否对应真实粒子谱一直存在争议，尤其是 Distler-Garibaldi 无-go 定理对手征费米子的限制。本文旨在澄清 $E_8\times\omega E_8$ 框架中 496 这个数字的物理含义，并论证其不构成对粒子谱的过大约束。

Method: 将每个 $E_8$ 分支为 $SU(3)_{st}\times E_6$，并用分裂复数单位 $\omega$ 标记可见分支与前引力分支（pre-gravitational branch）；手征费米子由 Cl(6) 极小理想旋量承载而非 $E_8$ 表示分量；通过分析 496 标签的双分支伴随表示（adjoint reservoir）与广义迹动力学拉格朗日量（Generalized Trace Dynamics Lagrangian）中 208 个结构之间的差异，得到残余的 288，并将其解释为伴随谱系表示标签账簿（adjoint-lineage representation-label ledger）。

Result: 双费米子种子是厄米的，$E_6$-协变通道由 $\bar{27}\otimes 27 = 1\oplus 78\oplus 650$ 分类：每个分支的 78 提供规范流和一个复合电弱二重态，而 $E_6$ 单态电弱惰性；电荷和区 A 在裸种子中缺失；252 个 $SU(3)_{st}$-带标签在旋量本体论条件下不能是任何储备中的物质双线性。因此 $E_8\times\omega E_8$ 的规模是标签账簿的维数，而非粒子计数。

Conclusion: $E_8\times\omega E_8$ 框架不预测超出标准模型的大量新粒子；其额外内容仅限于惰性中微子（sterile neutrinos）和一个复合标量（composite scalar）。大维数 496 是支撑结构的账簿性标签，而非真实粒子谱。

Abstract: In the $E_8\timesωE_8$ octonionic unification program, each $E_8$ branches as $SU(3)_{st}\times E_6$, supplying one geometric $SU(3)_{st}$ per branch, while the split-complex unit $ω$ grades the visible and pre-gravitational branches; matter and gauge content is carried by $E_6\times E_6$, with chiral fermions realized as Cl(6) minimal-ideal spinors rather than $E_8$ representation components -- which places the chiral sector outside the Distler-Garibaldi no-go theorem. Comparing the 496-label two-branch adjoint reservoir with the 208 structures matched in the Generalized Trace Dynamics Lagrangian leaves a residual 288. We argue that this 288 is an adjoint-lineage representation-label ledger -- bookkeeping for the scaffolding -- and not a particle spectrum. The bifermionic seed is Hermitian, with $E_6$-covariant channels classified by $\bar{27}\otimes 27 = 1\oplus 78\oplus 650$: each branch's 78 supplies the gauge currents and a composite electroweak doublet, while the $E_6$ singlet is electroweak-inert. The charge-sum sector A is absent from the bare seed, and the 252 $SU(3)_{st}$-charged labels cannot be matter bilinears in any reservoir, conditional on the spinor ontology. The size of $E_8\timesωE_8$ is thus the dimension of a label ledger, not a count of particles; beyond the Standard Model, the framework's content is sterile neutrinos and a second composite scalar.

### [128] [Polarization Formalism for Photon-Gravitational Wave Mixing Around Magnetars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12546)
*Jean-Simon Côté,Jean-François Fortin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了磁星磁层中的格森斯坦效应（Gertsenshtein effect），通过求解斯托克斯参数（Stokes parameters）的演化方程，指出文献中常用的绝热近似（adiabatic approximation）通常并不成立。在两种特定几何构型下得到解析结果，并由此导出随机引力波背景的下界与上界，最终表明磁星电磁辐射转化产生的引力波对随机背景的贡献可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用格森斯坦效应探测高频随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background），该频段远高于标准宇宙学源的范围，但此前文献中的绝热近似缺乏严格论证。

Method: 通过求解电磁波与引力波在磁星磁层中耦合时的斯托克斯参数演化方程，重新审视格森斯坦效应；在绝热近似有效的两种特定几何构型下推导解析结果。

Result: 导出了来自磁星电磁辐射转化为引力波的随机背景下界，以及由背景引力波转化为电磁辐射不超出观测到的磁星X射线波段流量所给出的上界。结果表明磁星电磁发射经格森斯坦转化产生的引力波贡献可忽略。

Conclusion: 格森斯坦效应中常见的绝热近似在一般情形下并不成立；磁星电磁辐射转化产生的引力波对随机引力波背景的贡献极小，但该效应仍可用于对高频引力波背景施加观测约束。

Abstract: The Gertsenshtein effect can be used to probe the stochastic gravitational wave background at high frequencies, well above the range of standard cosmological sources. In this paper, we revisit the conversion between electromagnetic and gravitational waves in the magnetosphere of magnetars by solving the evolution equations of the associated Stokes parameters. In the process, we point out that the adiabatic approximation usually taken in the literature is not generally justified in the context of the Gertsenshtein effect. To derive analytical results, we focus our attention on two specific geometries where the adiabatic approximation is valid. From these, we derive a lower bound on the stochastic gravitational wave background from the conversion of magnetar electromagnetic emission into gravitational waves, and an upper bound by requiring that the conversion of background gravitational waves into electromagnetic radiation does not exceed the observed magnetar flux in the X-ray band. Our results demonstrate that gravitational waves generated through the Gertsenshtein conversion of magnetar electromagnetic emission produce a negligible stochastic background, as anticipated.

</details>


### [129] [Subtraction of infrared divergences in light-quark QCD sum rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13409)
*Ding-Kun Lian,Jin-Peng Zhang,Zi-Xi Ou-Yang,Qi-Nan Wang,Hua-Xing Chen,Wei Chen,Jia-Jun Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对QCD求和规则中轻夸克系统在Wilson系数里出现的红外发散问题，提出了一种在传播子层面消除IR发散的改进方法，并给出了相应的减除公式。该方法相比依赖夸克与胶子凝聚混合的传统方法更直观且易于应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在QCD求和规则（QCD sum rules）中，轻夸克（light-quark）系统的Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）在计算某些凝聚（condensates）时会出现红外发散（infrared divergences, IR divergences）。这些发散显式地体现在坐标空间（coordinate-space）轻夸克传播子（propagators）表达式中，需要加以消除。

Method: 提出一种改进方法，在传播子层面直接消除红外发散；同时给出一个实现该过程的减除公式（subtraction formula）。该方法不依赖现有的基于同维度夸克与胶子凝聚（quark and gluon condensates）之间混合（mixing）来消除IR发散的途径。

Result: 提出的方法能够有效消除QCD求和规则中轻夸克系统Wilson系数里的红外发散，且相比现有方法更直观、更易于在实际QCD求和规则计算中应用。

Conclusion: 本文提出的传播子层面减除方案为QCD求和规则计算中红外发散的消除提供了一种更简洁、更具操作性的替代工具。

Abstract: In QCD sum rules for light-quark systems, infrared (IR) divergences can appear in the Wilson coefficients of certain condensates. These divergences manifest explicitly in the coordinate-space expressions of the light-quark propagators. We propose an improved method to eliminate these IR divergences at the propagator level and present a subtraction formula that implements this procedure. Compared to the existing methods that rely on the mixing between quark and gluon condensates of the same dimension to eliminate IR divergences, this method is more intuitive and easier to apply in practical QCD sum rule calculations.

</details>

Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器在3000.00到3119.88 MeV能量范围内采集的e⁺e⁻湮灭数据，研究了e⁺e⁻→Kₛ⁰K⁺π⁻+c.c.过程的截面线形，测量了J/ψ强衰变与电磁衰变振幅之间的相对相位和大小，并通过分波分析获得了子过程的截面与分支比，未观测到直接CP破缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确测量J/ψ粒子通过强相互作用和电磁相互作用的衰变振幅之间的相对相位与大小关系，检验量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）对强子衰变的预言，并探索可能存在的直接CP破缺（direct CP violation）信号。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在26个质心能量点（3000.00至3119.88 MeV）采集的e⁺e⁻湮灭数据，总积分亮度约440.7 pb⁻¹；对e⁺e⁻→Kₛ⁰K⁺π⁻+c.c.过程的截面线形（cross section lineshape）进行研究，并采用分波分析（partial wave analysis）提取子过程的信息。

Result: J/ψ强衰变与电磁衰变振幅的相对相位和大小测量为(123.7±5.3)°、4.31±0.22或(-123.1±5.2)°、4.38±0.22；对应分支比为(5.17±0.20)或(5.36±0.20)×10⁻³。子过程e⁺e⁻→K̅⁰K*(892)⁰+c.c.和e⁺e⁻→K⁺K*(892)⁻+c.c.的相位和大小也分别给出，大相对相位偏离正交关系（orthogonality relation）超过3σ。分支比测量与世界平均值一致，精度提升两倍以上。分支比之比及强振幅比值偏离1达2.1-2.3σ。未观测到直接CP破缺。

Conclusion: J/ψ衰变中强相互作用与电磁相互作用振幅之间的相位偏离正交假设，暗示了超出简单预期的强作用动力学效应；所有分支比测量结果与世界平均值一致且精度显著提升；未发现直接CP破缺证据。

Abstract: Using $e^+e^-$ annihilation data collected at 26 center-of-mass energy points between 3000.00 and $3119.88~\text{MeV}$ with the BESIII detector, corresponding to a total integrated luminosity of about $440.7~\text{pb}^{-1}$, we study the cross section lineshape of $e^+e^-\to K_S^0 K^+π^-+c.c.$. The relative phases and magnitudes between $J/ψ$ strong and electromagnetic decay amplitudes are measured to be $(123.7\pm5.3)^\circ;4.31\pm0.22$ or $(-123.1\pm5.2)^\circ;4.38\pm0.22$, with corresponding branching fractions $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\to K_S^0 K^+π^-+c.c.)=(5.17\pm0.20)$ or $(5.36\pm0.20)\times10^{-3}$. Based on a partial wave analysis, the cross sections of $e^+e^-\to\bar K^0 K^*(892)^0+c.c.$ and $e^+e^-\to K^+ K^*(892)^-+c.c.$ are obtained. For these subprocesses, the relative phases and magnitudes are determined as $(155.2\pm15.5)^{\circ};3.67\pm0.27$ or $(-154.1\pm15.5)^{\circ};3.71\pm0.25$ and $(180.1\pm31.8)^{\circ};25.06\pm2.51$, respectively. The large relative phases deviate from the orthogonality relation expected from experiment and from the assumption of purely real amplitudes by more than $3σ$. The measured branching fractions $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\to\bar K^0 K^*(892)^0)+c.c.=(4.18\pm0.18)$ or $(4.31\pm0.19)\times10^{-3}$, $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\to K^+ K^*(892)^-+c.c.)=(7.09\pm0.28)\times10^{-3}$ are all consistent with the world average values, but achieve better than a twofold improvement in precision. The ratios between the branching fractions of $J/ψ\to\bar K^0 K^*(892)^0+c.c.$ and $J/ψ\to\bar K^+ K^*(892)^-+c.c.$ are $\mathcal{R}_{K^*\bar{K}}=0.589\pm0.012$ or $0.612\pm0.013$. After subtracting the electromagnetic contribution, the corresponding strong amplitude ratios are $\mathcal{R}^{3g}_{K^*\bar{K}}=0.884\pm0.050$ or $0.909\pm0.044$, which deviate $2.3$ or $2.1σ$ from the unity. No evidence for direct $CP$ violation is observed.

</details>


### [131] [Observation of the decays $B^{+} \to Σ_{c}(2455)^{++} \barΞ_{c}^{\prime-}$ and $B^{0} \to Σ_{c}(2455)^{0} \barΞ_{c}^{\prime0}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12905)
*Belle,Belle II Collaborations,:,M. Abumusabh,A. Aggarwal,H. Ahmed,J. K. Ahn,Y. Ahn,M. Akdag,N. Akopov,S. Alghamdi,M. Alhakami,N. Althubiti,K. Amos,M. Angelsmark,N. Anh Ky,C. Antonioli,K. Arai,H. Vismaya,L. Vitale,V. Vobbilisetti,R. Volpe,M. Wakai,S. Wallner,M. -Z. Wang,A. Warburton,M. Watanabe,S. Watanuki,C. Wessel,X. P. Xu,B. D. Yabsley,S. Yamada,W. Yan,W. P. Yan,J. Yelton,K. Yi,J. H. Yin,K. Yoshihara,C. Z. Yuan,J. Yuan,L. Yuan,Y. Yusa,L. Zani,F. Zeng,M. Zeyrek,B. Zhang,X. Zhao,V. Zhilich,J. S. Zhou,Q. D. Zhou,L. Zhu,R. Žlebčík*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次观测到了B+介子衰变为Σc(2455)++与反Ξc′-以及B0介子衰变为Σc(2455)0与反Ξc′0的过程，显著性分别为6.4σ和5.3σ（含系统误差），并测量了相应的分支比。该结果基于Belle与Belle II探测器收集的大数据样本，是首次发现B介子衰变为属于同一SU(3)味六重态（flavor sextet）的一对粲重子-反重子态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在粒子物理中，B介子衰变至粲重子对的研究有助于理解强相互作用的非微扰动力学（non-perturbative dynamics）以及SU(3)味对称性（flavor symmetry）的破缺效应。此前尚未观测到B介子衰变为属于同一SU(3)味六重态的一对粲重子-反重子态的过程。

Method: 该分析采用了在KEKB对撞机（KEKB collider）上Belle探测器收集的771.6×10^6个Υ(4S)衰变数据样本，以及在SuperKEKB对撞机（SuperKEKB collider）上Belle II探测器收集的520.6×10^6个Υ(4S)衰变数据样本，通过重建末态粒子进行信号提取与显著性分析。

Result: B+ → Σc(2455)++ 反Ξc′-和B0 → Σc(2455)0 反Ξc′0两个衰变过程首次被观测到，统计显著性分别为6.4σ和5.3σ。分支比测量结果为:B+通道(1.68 ± 0.31 ± 0.12 +1.49/−0.54)×10^−3,B0通道(1.28 ± 0.32 ± 0.10 +0.30/−0.21)×10^−3，其中第一项为统计不确定度，第二项为系统不确定度，第三项来自反Ξc−和反Ξc0衰变绝对分支比的不确定度。

Conclusion: 该结果是首次观测到B介子衰变为属于同一SU(3)味六重态（flavor sextet）的一对粲重子-反重子态（charmed baryon-antibaryon pairs），为粲重子对产生机制和SU(3)味对称性研究提供了新的实验依据。

Abstract: We report the first observation of the decays $B^{+} \to Σ_{c}(2455)^{++} \barΞ_{c}^{\prime-}$ and $B^{0} \to Σ_{c}(2455)^{0} \barΞ_{c}^{\prime0}$, with significances of $6.4\,σ$ and $5.3\, σ$, respectively, including systematic uncertainties. This analysis is based on data samples containing $771.6 \times 10^{6}$ $Υ(4S)$ decays collected with the Belle detector at the KEKB collider and $520.6 \times 10^{6}$ $Υ(4S)$ decays collected with the Belle~II detector at the SuperKEKB collider. The branching fractions are measured to be $\mathcal{B}(B^+ \to Σ_c(2455)^{++} \barΞ_c^{\prime -}) = (1.68 \pm 0.31 \pm 0.12^{+1.49}_{-0.54}) \times 10^{-3}$ and $\mathcal{B}(B^0 \to Σ_c(2455)^{0} \barΞ_c^{\prime 0}) = (1.28 \pm 0.32 \pm 0.10^{+0.30}_{-0.21}) \times 10^{-3}$, where the first and second uncertainties are statistical and systematic, respectively, and the third arises from the uncertainties in the absolute branching fractions of $\barΞ_{c}^{-}$ and $\barΞ_{c}^{0}$ decays. This result represents the first observation of $B$-meson decays into a pair of charmed baryon-antibaryon states belonging to the same $SU(3)$ flavor sextet.

</details>


### [132] [Optimization of muon suppression using sweeper magnets for the Forward Physics Facility at the HL-LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13062)
*Akitaka Ariga,Tomoko Ariga,Jeremy Atkinson,Jamie Boyd,Kohei Chinone,Radu Dobre,Elena Firu,Haruhi Fujimori,Stephen Gibson,Daiki Hayakawa,Enrique Kajomovitz,Alex Keyken,Umut Kose,Laurie Nevay,Ken Ohashi,Simon Thor*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文研究如何利用扫场磁铁（sweeper magnet）系统抑制高亮度LHC（HL-LHC）上前向物理设施（FPF）中中微子探测器面临的前向缪子本底。通过结合SIBYLL、BDSIM、Geant4及真实磁场图的模拟框架，优化后的多级扫场磁铁配置可将缪子通量从无磁铁时的$3.8\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$每$\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$降低至$1.5\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$每$\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$，验证了该方案的有效性并强调了真实传输模拟与几何约束的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高亮度LHC（HL-LHC）上的前向物理设施（Forward Physics Facility, FPF）计划对TeV量级中微子进行高统计量测量，但前向缪子通量极高，构成了中微子探测器的主要本底挑战。因此，亟需有效的本底抑制方案。

Method: 采用包含SIBYLL事件生成、BDSIM束流传输、Geant4粒子追踪及真实磁场图（magnetic field maps）的模拟框架，评估扫场磁铁（sweeper magnet）在多级配置下对前向缪子本底的抑制效果。

Result: 无磁铁时缪子通量为$3.8\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$每$\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$。仅LHC隧道内放置单个磁铁可达目标水平$2\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$每$\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$；在TI18隧道和FPF入口增加额外磁铁后，优化配置下通量进一步降至$1.5\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$每$\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$。

Conclusion: 优化后的多级扫场磁铁系统能显著降低前向缪子本底，同时突显了真实传输模拟与几何约束（geometrical constraints）在实现进一步抑制中的重要性。

Abstract: The Forward Physics Facility (FPF) at the High-Luminosity LHC (HL-LHC) will enable high-statistics measurements of TeV-scale neutrinos, but the intense flux of forward muons poses a major challenge for neutrino detectors in the far-forward region.
  We investigate the suppression of background muons using sweeper magnets with a simulation framework combining SIBYLL event generation, BDSIM beam transport, Geant4 particle tracking, and realistic magnetic field maps.
  Starting from a muon flux of $3.8\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$ per $\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$ without magnets, a magnet in the LHC tunnel alone achieves the target level of $2\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$ per $\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$. Additional magnets at the TI18 tunnel and FPF entrance further reduce the flux to $1.5\times10^3~\mathrm{cm^{-2}}$ per $\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$ in the optimized configuration.
  These results demonstrate that a properly optimized multi-stage sweeper magnet system can significantly reduce the forward muon background, while also highlighting the importance of realistic transport simulations and geometrical constraints in achieving further suppression.

</details>


### [133] [AgentRivet: an automated system for producing Rivet routines from journal publications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13535)
*Antonio J. Costa,Caterina Doglioni,Christian Gütschow,Andrew D. Pilkington,Sukanya Sinha*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出并实现了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的自动化工作流AgentRivet，旨在自动生成粒子物理对撞机实验中缺失的Rivet分析例程。实验表明，AgentRivet能产出语法错误少、物理保真度合理的例程，但物理实现问题仍存在，主要源于论文中的模糊定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子物理对撞机实验将Rivet例程作为模型无关测量的分析保存策略的一部分；然而当前分析覆盖率不完整，仅有39%的测量具有公开可用的Rivet例程。因此，需要自动化方法补全缺失例程。

Method: 设计并实现了一个基于大语言模型（Large Language Model, LLM）的多步自动化工作流AgentRivet，从已发表论文中提取物理分析信息并编写缺失的Rivet例程，中间包含代码审查和物理审查环节作为自主质量控制的一部分。

Result: 使用OpenAI、Anthropic和Google提供的商业大语言模型，针对ATLAS和CMS实验的两项近期测量进行了测试。AgentRivet生成的例程语法错误少，物理保真度合理且与相关出版物解释一致；但物理实现问题仍然存在，主要源于论文中细微但模糊的定义，部分模型在清晰定义下仍难以实现复杂观测量。

Conclusion: AgentRivet能够有效生成具备合理质量的Rivet例程，但物理实现中的问题提示需要更精确的论文定义和进一步的方法改进。

Abstract: Particle physics collider experiments provide Rivet routines as part of the analysis preservation strategy for model-independent measurements. Rivet is a C++ toolkit that allow new theoretical models to be compared to the measurements, thus aiding the development and tuning of Monte Carlo event generators as well as searches for physics beyond the Standard Model. However, analysis coverage is known to be incomplete, with only 39% of measurements having documented and publicly available Rivet routines. In this article, we design and implement an automated workflow based on Large Language Models with the goal of providing the missing routines. This multi-step workflow, referred to as AgentRivet, extracts the physics analysis information from published papers and writes the missing Rivet routines, with intermediate code- and physics- reviews as part of an autonomous quality control. We report the results obtained using commercial Large Language Models, provided by OpenAI, Anthropic, and Google, for two recent measurements from the ATLAS and CMS experiments. We find that AgentRivet produces competent Rivet routines with few syntax errors. The physics fidelity of the routines is reasonable and follows the explanations given in the relevant publications. Nevertheless, physics-implementation issues do arise and are investigated using the artefacts produced by AgentRivet. The majority of physics implementation issues arise from subtle-but-ambiguous definitions in the given publication, although some models struggle to implement complex observables even when clear definitions are given.

</details>


### [134] [First Measurement of Sub-GeV $ν_μ$ Charged-Current Coherent Pion Production on Argon in MicroBooNE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13613)
*MicroBooNE collaboration,P. Abratenko,D. Andrade Aldana,J. Asaadi,A. Ashkenazi,S. Balasubramanian,B. Baller,A. Barnard,G. Barr,D. Barrow,J. Barrow,V. Basque,J. Bateman,B. Behera,O. Fang,B. T. Fleming,W. Foreman,D. Franco,A. P. Furmanski,F. Gao,D. Garcia-Gamez,S. Gardiner,G. Ge,S. Gollapinni,E. Gramellini,P. Green,H. Greenlee,L. Gu,W. Gu,R. Guenette,L. Hagaman,M. D. Handley,O. Martinez Lopez,M. G. Manuel Alves,S. Martynenko,A. Mastbaum,I. Mawby,N. McConkey,B. McConnell,L. Mellet,J. Mendez,J. Micallef,T. Mohayai,A. Mogan,M. Mooney,A. F. Moor,C. D. Moore,L. Mora Lepin,M. A. Hernandez Morquecho,M. M. Moudgalya,S. Mulleria Babu,D. Naples,A. Navrer-Agasson,N. Nayak,M. Nebot-Guinot,C. Nguyen,L. Nguyen,J. Nowak,N. Oza,O. Palamara,N. Pallat,V. Paolone,A. Papadopoulou,V. Papavassiliou,H. Parkinson,S. F. Pate,N. Patel,Z. Pavlovic,E. Piasetzky,K. Pletcher,I. Pophale,X. Qian,J. L. Raaf,V. Radeka,A. Rafique,M. Reggiani-Guzzo,J. Rodriguez Rondon,M. Rosenberg,M. Ross-Lonergan,I. Safa,C. Sauer,D. W. Schmitz,A. Schukraft,W. Seligman,M. H. Shaevitz,R. Sharankova,J. Shi,L. Silva,E. L. Snider,S. Soldner-Rembold,J. Spitz,M. Stancari,J. St. John,T. Strauss,A. M. Szelc,N. Taniuchi,K. Terao,C. Thorpe,D. Torbunov,D. Totani,M. Toups,A. Trettin,Y. -T. Tsai,J. Tyler,M. A. Uchida,T. Usher,B. Viren,J. Wang,L. Wang,M. Weber,H. Wei,A. J. White,S. Wolbers,T. Wongjirad,K. Wresilo,W. Wu,E. Yandel,T. Yang,L. E. Yates,H. W. Yu,G. P. Zeller,J. Zennamo,C. Zhang,Y. Zhang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用MicroBooNE液氩时间投影室（liquid argon time projection chamber）在费米实验室Booster中微子束上完成了氩核上带电电流相干π产生（charged-current coherent pion production）截面的首次测量，通量平均截面为 (9.1 ± 1.2_stat ± 1.2_syst) × 10^{-40} cm²/Ar，该过程因其清晰的两体运动学特征可用于约束中微子流强不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电电流相干π产生过程具有清晰的两体运动学特征——中微子与整个原子核发生相干相互作用，产生前向μ子和π介子且不发生核碎裂——使其成为约束当前及未来振荡实验（如DUNE）中微子流强不确定性的有效工具。该测量填补了亚GeV中微子能量下氩核上相干π产生截面的数据空白。

Method: 实验利用MicroBooNE液氩时间投影室采集的数据集（对应1.26×10^{21}个质子打靶），平均中微子能量为0.8 GeV。通过分析带电电流相干π产生事件，测量通量平均截面（flux-averaged cross section）。

Result: 测得通量平均截面为 (9.1 ± 1.2_stat ± 1.2_syst) × 10^{-40} cm²/Ar，其中统计不确定度和系统不确定度均为 1.2 × 10^{-40} cm²/Ar。这是亚GeV中微子能量下氩核上带电电流相干π产生截面的首次测量结果。

Conclusion: 该测量结果为亚GeV能区氩核上带电电流相干π产生过程提供了首个实验数据。该过程的两体干净运动学特性可用于约束中微子流强不确定性，对当前及未来的中微子振荡实验（如DUNE）具有重要价值。

Abstract: We report a measurement of the charged-current coherent pion production cross section on argon using the MicroBooNE liquid argon time projection chamber exposed to the Booster Neutrino Beam at Fermilab. The measurement uses the MicroBooNE data set corresponding to $1.26 \times 10^{21}$ protons on target with a mean neutrino energy of $0.8$~GeV. The flux-averaged cross section is measured to be $(9.1 \pm 1.2_{\text{stat}} \pm 1.2_\text{syst}) \times 10^{-40}\,\text{cm}^2/\text{Ar}$. This result represents the first measurement of charged-current coherent pion production on argon at sub-GeV neutrino energies. Due to its clean two-body kinematics, where the neutrino interacts coherently with the entire nucleus producing a forward muon and pion with no nuclear breakup, this process provides a useful tool for constraining neutrino flux uncertainties in current and future oscillation experiments such as DUNE.

</details>

# math.NA [[Back]](#toc)

### [135] [Momentum Space Algorithm for Electronic Structure of Double-Incommensurate Trilayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13434)
*Ken Beard,Daniel Massatt*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 针对双层非公度二维材料（incommensurate 2D materials）的电子结构计算，现有动量空间与连续模型（continuum model）存在精度或收敛性问题。本文针对双非公度三层石墨烯（double incommensurate trilayer graphene）引入动量空间框架，并提出一种高效的截断方案（truncation scheme），显著改善态密度（density of states）及动量局域态密度（momentum local density of states）的收敛性。算法在扭曲三层石墨烯（twisted trilayer graphene）的第一性原理（ab initio）模型中实现并验证了收敛性，数值结果表明该动量空间算法本质上比连续模型更高阶，能够捕捉魔角（magic angles）附近平带（flat bands）的带行为变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用第一性原理（ab initio）模型计算非公度二维材料（incommensurate 2D materials）的电子结构，对预测材料性质和指导实验至关重要。然而，现有针对双层非公度体系的动量空间与连续模型（continuum model）在推广到三层的双非公度（double-incommensurate）情形时，会引入四维格点空间（four-dimensional lattice space），导致态密度（density of states）的数值收敛性极差。

Method: 本文为双非公度三层石墨烯（double incommensurate trilayer graphene）构建了一个动量空间框架（momentum space framework），并提出了一种针对四维格点空间的高效截断方案（truncation scheme）。该算法是紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）的精确变换，本质上比连续模型（continuum model）阶数更高，并在扭曲三层石墨烯（twisted trilayer graphene）的第一性原理模型上实现并验证了收敛性估计。

Result: 所提出的截断方案显著改善了态密度（density of states）和动量局域态密度（momentum local density of states）的收敛性。数值验证表明，该动量空间算法能够捕捉魔角（magic angles）附近平带（flat bands）的能带行为变化，且精度高于连续模型。

Conclusion: 提出的动量空间框架与高效截断方案有效解决了双非公度三层石墨烯体系电子结构计算中的收敛难题，为更复杂的非公度二维材料体系的第一性原理计算提供了新的高效数值工具。

Abstract: Numerical algorithms for computing electronic structure of incommensurate 2D materials using ab initio models is critical for predicting material properties and guiding experiment. For bilayers, momentum space and continuum models have been introduced to approximate observables of ab initio tight-binding models using a momenta description despite the lack of periodicity in the tight-binding model required for Bloch theory. A similar structure has been introduced for double-incommensurate trilayers using a continuum model, where the three lattices are all mutually incommensurate. However, this description leads to a four-dimensional lattice space, and numerical convergence of the density of states was observed to have poor convergence.
  In this work, we introduce a momentum space framework for double incommensurate trilayer graphene, and introduce an efficient truncation scheme of the four-dimensional lattice to drastically improve convergence of the density of states and momentum local density of states (a parallel object to classical band structure). We implement this algorithm on an ab initio model of twisted trilayer graphene and validate convergence estimates. We further verify numerically that the momentum space algorithm, inherently higher order than the continuum model as it is an exact transformation of the tight-binding model, captures altered band behavior near the flat bands at magic angles.

</details>

### [136] [From Loss Diagnosis to Rational Design: A Unified Analytical Model for Photoelectrochemical Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12641)
*Ziyan Pan,Giulia Tagliabue*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一的光电化学（PEC）电池损耗分析框架，该框架适用于内建结（BIJ）和半导体-电解液结（SEJ）光电极，能够通过拟合实验电流-电压数据实现热力学、光学、复合和界面贡献的定量能量损耗分解，并借助效率图、桑基图等工具指导材料选择与优化策略，最终推动PEC体系从经验优化向机理驱动的理性设计范式转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光电化学（photoelectrochemical, PEC）电池在太阳能驱动的化学储能与原料合成中具有潜力，但实际部署受限于光吸收、载流子输运、界面电荷转移以及半导体-电解液匹配等多重耦合损耗。现有模型仅针对特定架构处理这些损耗，无法进行定量实验诊断也无法提供可操作的优化设计指导，因而亟需一个统一的、具备实验可拟合性的损耗分析框架。

Method: 该框架基于一套物理意义一致的参数，统一适用于内建结（built-in junction, BIJ）和半导体-电解液结（semiconductor-electrolyte junction, SEJ）两种光电极架构。通过生成理想与真实条件下的电流-电压曲线与效率指标（efficiency metrics），构建效率图（efficiency maps）以界定理论极限与材料选择窗口；进一步通过拟合实验电流-电压数据，将能量损耗分解为热力学（thermodynamic）、光学（optical）、复合（recombination）和界面（interfacial）四类贡献，并借助桑基图（Sankey diagrams）直观展示太阳能入射后的吸收、耗散与化学转化的能量流。

Result: 该框架已通过涵盖太阳能水分解、CO₂还原、NH₃合成及太阳能氧化还原液流电池等领域的先进文献结果进行验证。它能够实现对光伏级吸收材料（如Si、钙钛矿）与中间带隙半导体（如赤铁矿hematite、BiVO₄）的系统比较，识别出限制每类材料的关键因素，并将性能瓶颈直接映射到助催化剂集成（co-catalyst integration）或纳米结构调控（nanostructuring）等优化策略上。

Conclusion: 该统一损耗分析框架支持从经验优化到基于机理的理性设计（mechanism-informed rational design）的范式转变，为高效PEC能量转换系统提供了定量诊断工具和系统性的材料-架构优化指导。

Abstract: Photoelectrochemical (PEC) cells are a compelling route to solar-driven chemical energy storage and feedstock synthesis, yet their deployment is hindered by coupled losses spanning light absorption, carrier transport, interfacial charge transfer, and semiconductor-electrolyte matching. Existing models address these losses in an architecture-specific manner and fall short of quantitative experimental diagnosis or actionable design guidance. Here, we introduce a unified loss-analysis framework applicable to both built-in junction (BIJ) and semiconductor-electrolyte junction (SEJ) photoelectrodes within a consistent set of physically meaningful parameters. The framework delivers current-voltage curves and efficiency metrics under ideal and real conditions, constructing efficiency maps to delineate theoretical limits and material-selection windows. Critically, by fitting experimental current-voltage data, it enables quantitative energy-loss decomposition into thermodynamic, optical, recombination, and interfacial contributions, pinpointing performance bottlenecks in real devices and mapping them directly onto optimization strategies such as co-catalyst integration or nanostructuring. Energy flows are visualized through Sankey diagrams, providing an intuitive picture of how incident solar energy is absorbed, dissipated, or converted into chemical output. Validated against state-of-the-art literature results spanning solar water splitting, CO2 reduction, NH3 synthesis, and solar redox flow batteries, the framework further enables systematic comparison of photovoltaic-grade absorbers (e.g., Si, perovskites) with intermediate-bandgap semiconductors (e.g., hematite, BiVO4), identifying key factors limiting each material class. Together, these capabilities support a paradigm shift from empirical optimization to mechanism-informed rational design of high-efficiency PEC energy-conversion systems.

### [137] [Fine-tuning MLIP foundation models: strategies for accuracy and transferability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12704)
*Tamás Lajos Tompa,Eszter Varga-Umbrich,Ilyes Batatia,Alin M. Elena,Noam Bernstein,Gábor Csányi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了七种微调策略在五种化学基准、三代基础模型及跨五个数量级训练集上的表现，发现基础模型质量、正确初始化原子参考能量（E0）和超参数选择是比微调策略本身更关键的前提条件；在满足前提后，朴素全参数微调适用于单系统任务，而多头回放（multihead replay）是唯一能保持分布外鲁棒性（out-of-distribution robustness）的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管微调（fine-tuning）机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potential, MLIP）基础模型以适配特定任务日益重要，但目前缺乏关于何时以及如何微调的系统性指导。

Method: 评估了七种微调策略：朴素全参数更新（naive full-parameter updates）、两种冻结层变体、低秩适配（Low-Rank Adaptation, LoRA）、多头回放（multihead replay）、伪标签回放（pseudolabelled replay）以及回放结合LoRA。在MACE代码库中实现了三项新功能：适用于等变消息传递架构（equivariant message-passing architecture）的LoRA、解耦回放数据来源的伪标签回放，以及用于微调流程的模型感知原子参考能量（model-aware atomic reference energy, E0）重估计。

Result: 基础模型质量、正确的E0初始化和精选超参数是前提条件，其影响通常超过微调策略本身；满足前提后，大多数策略均能达到强目标任务精度，一致优于从头训练的模型。朴素微调在单系统应用中收敛最优，而多头回放是唯一能一致保持分布外鲁棒性（out-of-distribution robustness）的方法。

Conclusion: 微调实践应优先关注基础模型质量、E0初始化和超参数选择；具体策略的选择取决于部署范围：单系统任务选用朴素微调，需保持分布外鲁棒性的更广部署则选用多头回放。

Abstract: Adapting machine-learned interatomic potential (MLIP) foundation models to specialised tasks through fine-tuning is an increasingly important practice, yet systematic guidance on when and how to fine-tune is currently limited. We evaluate seven fine-tuning strategies -- naive full-parameter updates, two layer-freezing variants, Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), multihead replay, pseudolabelled replay, and replay combined with LoRA -- across five chemically diverse benchmarks (aqueous NaCl, ice polymorphs, S$_\mathrm{N}$2 reactions, SPICE biomolecules, and lithium electrolytes), three generations of foundation models, and training sets spanning five orders of magnitude. To support this evaluation we implement three capabilities in the MACE codebase: LoRA adapted for equivariant message-passing architectures, including both scalar and equivariant linear layers; pseudolabelled replay, which decouples the replay data source from the original pretraining corpus; and model-aware atomic reference energy (E0) reestimation for fine-tuning workflows. We find that foundation model quality, correct E0 initialisation, and well-chosen hyperparameters are prerequisites whose impact routinely exceeds that of the fine-tuning strategy itself. Once these prerequisites are met, most strategies achieve strong target-task accuracy, consistently surpassing models trained from scratch. The practical distinction depends on deployment scope: naive fine-tuning offers the best convergence for single-system applications, while multihead replay -- with either original or pseudolabelled data -- is the only approach tested that consistently preserves out-of-distribution robustness, maintaining both pretraining-distribution accuracy for broader deployment and many-body short-range repulsion.

### [138] [An approximate application of quantum gravity to the rotation problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12461)
*R. Michael Jones*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证了量子引力（quantum gravity）可以通过路径积分（path integral）中的相位干涉（phase interference）自然地解决广义相对论中的“旋转问题”（Rotation Problem），即在初始奇点（initial singularity）后约四分之一秒，量子宇宙学（quantum cosmology）会将有效贡献的宇宙的相对均方根旋转率限制在极小的量级（如约10^{-51} rad/year），且该结论对量子引力的具体细节不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论的爱因斯坦场方程允许物质与惯性系之间存在任意大的相对旋转，但观测显示其相对旋转率极小，这一理论与观测之间的巨大反差构成了“旋转问题”。该文旨在解释为何测得的相对旋转率如此之小。

Method: 采用量子引力中的路径积分方法，每条“路径”对应一个具有不同均方根（rms）相对旋转率的宇宙学模型，并基于爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action）进行计算，考虑惯性系与物质分布的大尺度相对旋转。计算依赖可见宇宙的尺度、普朗克时间（Planck time）、真空光速、哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）以及暴胀（inflation）期间的e-foldings数。

Result: 在暴胀持续50个e-foldings的条件下，对路径积分有显著贡献的宇宙在初始奇点后约0.25秒时的相对均方根旋转率低于约10^{-51} rad/year；暴胀持续55或60个e-foldings时该上限进一步降低。即使不考虑暴胀，显著贡献的宇宙的相对旋转率也低于约10^{-32} rad/year。计算显示作用量在零相对均方根旋转率处取极值（extremum）。

Conclusion: 几乎任何合理的量子引力理论都可以通过相位干涉解决旋转问题，且该结论对量子引力理论的细节不敏感，因为主要因子仅依赖于少数基本物理参数和暴胀参数。

Abstract: Arbitrary initial conditions allow solutions of Einstein's field equations for General Relativity to have arbitrarily large relative rotation of matter and inertial frames. The ``Rotation Problem'' is to explain why the measured relative rotation rate is so small. Nearly any reasonable theory of quantum gravity can solve the rotation problem by phase interference. Even as early as about a quarter of a second after the initial singularity, quantum cosmology would limit the cosmologies that contribute significantly to a path integral calculation to have relative rms rotation rates less than about $10^{-51}$ rad/year. Those calculations are based on using 50 e-foldings during inflation. For 55 or 60 e-foldings, the cosmologies contributing significantly to the path integral would have even smaller relative rotation rates. In addition, although inflation dominates the calculation, even if there had been no inflation, the cosmologies contributing significantly to the path integral would have relative rotation rates less than about $10^{-32}$ rad/year at about a quarter of a second after the initial singularity. These calculations are insensitive to the details of the theory of quantum gravity because the main factor depends only on the size of the visible universe, the Planck time, the free-space speed of light, the Hubble parameter, and the number of e-foldings during inflation. These calculations use the Einstein-Hilbert action in quantum gravity, including large-scale relative rotation of inertial frames and the matter distribution, in which each ``path'' is a cosmology with a different rms relative rotation rate. The calculation shows that the action is an extremum at zero rms relative rotation rate.

</details>


### [139] [Black Hole Radiation Sparsity and Bekenstein Entropy Loss in Non-Commutative Schwarzschild Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12470)
*Abdellah Touati*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在非对易规范引力理论框架下，研究了Schwarzschild黑洞的辐射稀疏性、Bekenstein熵损失和总粒子发射。结果表明温度发散行为被消除，熵出现对数修正，总发射粒子数与熵行为成比例，且黑洞在蒸发末期表现出极端稀疏的辐射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将非对易（non-commutative, NC）规范引力理论应用于Schwarzschild黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole, SBH），以修正传统黑洞热力学中存在的温度发散行为，并进一步探索NC效应对黑洞辐射稀疏性、熵损失及粒子发射过程的影响。

Method: 基于非对易规范引力理论构建修正的Schwarzschild黑洞几何；计算畸变Hawking温度（deformed Hawking temperature）和修正熵，并在此基础上推导Bekenstein熵损失（Bekenstein entropy loss）与总发射粒子数；通过稀疏性参数η分析Hawking辐射的稀疏程度。

Result: 温度的发散行为被消除，熵出现对数修正（logarithmic correction）；总发射粒子数与NC SBH的熵行为成比例，符合非热辐射（non-thermal radiation）特征；NC SBH表现出极端稀疏的辐射（η ≫ 1），且在蒸发末期辐射稀疏性发散，黑洞停止辐射。

Conclusion: 非对易几何有效消除了Schwarzschild黑洞的温度奇点，并给出了熵的对数修正；辐射的极端稀疏性表明NC效应显著改变了黑洞蒸发末期的行为，最终导致黑洞停止辐射。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the sparsity of black hole radiation, the Bekenstein entropy loss, and the total particle emission of a Schwarzschild black hole (SBH) within the framework of non-commutative (NC) gauge theory of gravity. First, we provide a brief review of black hole (BH) thermodynamics, computing both the deformed Hawking temperature and entropy. In this geometry, the divergent behavior of the temperature is removed, and a logarithmic correction to the entropy emerges. We then present the NC corrections to the Bekenstein entropy loss of the SBH alongside the total number of emitted particles. Our results show that the total number of emitted particles is proportional to the entropy behavior of the NC SBH, which is consistent with non-thermal radiation. Finally, we analyze the sparsity of Hawking radiation in this geometry, finding that the NC SBH exhibits extremely sparse radiation ($\hatη \gg 1$), which diverges at the final stage of evaporation as the black hole ceases to radiate.

### [140] [Gotta light? Illuminating AGN disks with LISA EMRIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12531)
*Federico Fantocolli,Francisco Duque,Jonathan Gair*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了未来激光干涉空间天线（LISA）对嵌入吸积盘的极端质量比旋进（EMRI）所受气体扭矩的约束能力，采用基于贝叶斯框架的分析表明，即使在无电磁对应体的情况下，LISA也能同时估算盘面密度和吸积率（即总光度），且扭矩振幅约束精度可达约10%，从而推动在强场引力区（sub）微秒差距尺度上的吸积物理探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于牛顿力学的预测低估了LISA对EMRI-吸积盘系统的约束能力，且线性信号近似（Fisher矩阵）是否适用于此类非线性系统尚不明确。作者旨在利用最新相对论双星-盘相互作用模型，评估LISA在无电磁对应体条件下能否同时约束气体扭矩参数，并检验Fisher矩阵近似的有效性。

Method: 采用全贝叶斯（fully Bayesian）推断框架，结合最近发展的相对论双星-吸积盘相互作用模型，对LISA观测EMRI嵌入吸积盘时的气体扭矩参数进行约束。同时与基于线性信号（Fisher矩阵）近似的简化测量约束进行对比。

Result: 与基于牛顿结果的先前预测相反，LISA可在无电磁对应体情况下同时估算盘面密度和吸积率（总光度）。Fisher矩阵近似在此类系统中不成立。对于典型EMRI观测，扭矩振幅约束精度可达约10%，能够探测（sub）微秒差距尺度上的吸积物理。

Conclusion: 该结果增强了LISA探测强场引力区（sub）微秒差距尺度吸积物理的能力，可补充电磁观测；同时提升LISA回答大质量黑洞增长与星系共演化问题的能力，并通过与活动星系核（AGN）星表交叉关联识别EMRI宿主星系，改善这些源作为（暗）标准汽笛（siren）的宇宙学应用。

Abstract: We study the ability of the upcoming Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) to constrain gas torques acting on extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) when these are embedded in accretion disks, using recently developed relativistic models for the binary-disk interaction. Using a fully Bayesian setup, we find that, contrary to previous forecasts based on Newtonian results, these observations can provide simultaneous estimates of the disk surface density and the accretion rate (or, equivalently, its total luminosity) without the need for an electromagnetic counterpart. Our analysis also indicates that simpler measurement constraints based on the linear-signal (Fisher matrix) approximation are not valid for these systems. For typical EMRI observations, the torque amplitude can be constrained to within ~10%, strengthening the prospect of probing accretion physics at (sub)microparsec scales, deep in the strong-field gravity regime and complementing electromagnetic observations. This also strengthens LISA's ability to help answering questions such as how massive black holes grow and coevolve with their host galaxies and, by helping to identify the EMRI's host galaxy through cross-correlation with AGN catalogues, to improve the use of these sources as (dark) sirens for cosmology.

</details>


### [141] [Maxwell equations in Schwarzschild spacetime for static and freely falling observers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12630)
*F. L. Carneiro,L. V. A. Cunha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在弯曲时空（curved spacetime）中构建了基于四脚场（tetrad）的经典电动力学（classical electrodynamics）形式体系，并将其应用于史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中的静态观测者和径向自由下落观测者。研究发现：引力场通过度规函数在静态观测者视角下引入几何修正；径向自由下落观测者因局域径向加速产生运动学贡献，导致电荷密度与径向电流混合、电磁场耦合；最后通过有效介质类比（effective-medium analogy）解释了上述结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有弯曲时空电动力学形式体系难以直接保持观测者所测电磁场的物理直观性，因此需要一种基于四脚场（tetrad）的框架，使得电磁场能够直接对应于实际观测者的测量结果，并清晰揭示引力场对不同观测者电磁规律的影响。

Method: 采用四脚场框架将经典电动力学推广至弯曲时空，并将该形式体系具体应用于史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中两个不同观测者家族——静态观测者（static observers）和径向自由下落观测者（radially free-falling observers），在同一坐标系下推导其麦克斯韦方程组（Maxwell equations）。还进一步考虑了弱场近似（weak-field regime）和近水平（near-horizon regime）极限情况。

Result: 对于静态观测者，麦克斯韦方程保持通常的球对称结构，但引力通过度规函数在径向和时间方向引入几何修正，这些修正可用固有径向距离（proper radial distance）、固有时间（proper time）以及时移函数（lapse function）的径向变化来解释。对于径向自由下落观测者，局域径向推流（radial boost）带来额外的运动学贡献，导致电荷密度与径向电流混合，电磁场在时间-径向投影中耦合，而角向安培-麦克斯韦方程和法拉第方程保持与静态观测者相同的形式。弱场及近水平区域的结果可通过有效介质类比来描述：史瓦西几何对静态观测者表现为静止的非均匀介质，对自由下落观测者则在时间-径向区段表现为径向运动的有效介质。

Conclusion: 所提出的四脚场框架能够自然地区分不同观测者的电磁测量结果，并揭示引力场对不同观测者视角下电磁规律的具体修正形式；有效介质类比为理解弯曲时空中的电磁行为提供了直观的物理图像。

Abstract: Classical electrodynamics in curved spacetime is formulated within a tetrad-based framework that preserves the direct physical interpretation of the electromagnetic fields measured by an observer. The formalism is applied to Schwarzschild spacetime for two distinct families of observers described in the same coordinate system: static observers and radially free-falling observers. For static observers, Maxwell equations retain their usual spherical structure, while the gravitational field introduces geometrical corrections in the radial and temporal sectors through the metric function. These corrections are interpreted in terms of proper radial distance, proper time, and the radial variation of the lapse function. For radially free-falling observers, additional kinematical contributions arise from the local radial boost relating the free-falling frame to the static one. As a consequence, charge density mixes with radial current, and the electric and magnetic sectors become intertwined in the temporal-radial projections of Maxwell equations, whereas the angular Ampère-Maxwell and Faraday equations retain the same structure found for the static observer. The weak-field and near-horizon regimes are also examined, and the results are discussed through an effective-medium analogy, in which the Schwarzschild geometry behaves as an inhomogeneous geometrical medium at rest for static observers and as a radially moving effective medium in the temporal-radial sector for free-falling observers.

</details>


### [142] [Higher Dimensional Loop Quantum Black hole in de Sitter Spacetime: Quasinormal Modes and Shadow Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12698)
*Kourosh Nozari,Sara Saghafi,Ali Mohammadpour*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了德西特背景下高维圈量子修正黑洞的动力学与光学性质，通过三种方法计算无质量标量扰动的准正则模（quasinormal modes），分析圈量子修正与时空维度对谱的影响，并结合黑洞阴影与M87*事件视界望远镜观测数据约束模型参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）效应与高维时空结构在强引力区域的可观测后果，为量子引力理论提供现象学检验途径。

Method: 采用时域演化配合Prony提取法（Prony extraction）、矩阵法（matrix method）以及WKB近似（WKB approximation）三种独立方法计算无质量标量扰动的准正则模；通过零测地线（null geodesics）分析构建黑洞阴影（black hole shadow），并与Event Horizon Telescope对M87*的观测约束进行比较。

Result: 三种方法计算的准正则模结果高度一致；圈量子修正对谱产生中等程度的偏移，而时空维度的影响更为显著，导致振荡频率（oscillation frequency）和衰减率（damping rate）均升高；所有模式的负虚部表明在探测参数范围内系统是动力学稳定的；阴影半径对圈量子参数、宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）和时空维度均敏感，额外维度通常减小阴影尺寸。

Conclusion: 准正则模与黑洞阴影可作为互补的探针，用于在强引力框架下检验圈量子引力效应和高维时空结构。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical and optical properties of a higher-dimensional loop-quantum-corrected black hole in a de Sitter background. The quasinormal modes of massless scalar perturbations are computed using time-domain evolution with Prony extraction, the matrix method, and the WKB approximation, showing good agreement among the three approaches. We find that loop quantum corrections induce moderate shifts in the quasinormal spectrum, whereas the spacetime dimensionality has a much stronger impact, leading to higher oscillation frequencies and damping rates. The negative imaginary parts of all modes indicate dynamical stability against massless scalar perturbations within the explored parameter range. We also analyze null geodesics and construct the corresponding black hole shadow. The shadow radius depends sensitively on the loop quantum parameter, the cosmological constant, and the number of spacetime dimensions, with extra dimensions generally reducing the shadow size. By comparing the theoretical shadow radius with the Event Horizon Telescope constraints for M87$^{\ast}$, we obtain bounds on the parameter space of the model. These results suggest that quasinormal modes and black hole shadow observables can provide complementary probes of loop quantum gravity effects and higher-dimensional spacetime structure in the strong-gravity regime.

### [143] [Asymmetric quantum steering harvested near a Lorentz-violating BTZ black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12766)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 考虑两个Unruh-DeWitt探测器分别放置在洛伦兹破缺BTZ黑洞外部不同径向位置，利用黑洞时空诱导的局域环境差异（如有效热噪声）来研究量子导引的获取与方向性。

Result: 发现反直觉现象：处于更高有效温度的探测器反而展现出更强的可导引性，与日常热力学直觉相反；量子导引仅存在于有限的探测器能隙（energy gap）窗口内，并在最优区间达到最大值；洛伦兹破缺在最优能隙附近对导引的抑制最强，表明最大关联提取对对称性破缺效应具有增强的敏感性。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹破缺充当了对时空量子信息容量的几何约束，同时限制了量子关联的强度与方向性。

Abstract: We investigate the harvesting of quantum steering and its directional asymmetry between two Unruh-DeWitt detectors in a Lorentz-violating BTZ black hole spacetime. Since the detectors are located at different radial positions outside the black hole, they experience inequivalent local environments induced by gravitational redshift, causing Alice to undergo stronger effective thermal noise than Bob. Remarkably, we uncover a counterintuitive phenomenon in which the detector subjected to a higher effective temperature exhibits stronger steerability than the other one, revealing a nontrivial inversion of thermal intuition in curved spacetime. Furthermore, quantum steering survives only within a finite window of detector energy gaps and reaches its maximum within an optimal regime. We find that Lorentz violation suppresses steering most strongly near this optimal energy gap, indicating an enhanced sensitivity of maximal correlation extraction to symmetry breaking effects. Our results demonstrate that Lorentz violation acts as a geometric constraint on the quantum information capacity of spacetime, simultaneously restricting both the strength and the directionality of quantum correlations.

### [144] [Constraining Kerr supermassive black hole properties using gravitational waves from inspiraling stellar-mass binary black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12784)
*Jie Wu,Jin-Tao Yao,Mengfei Sun,Jin Li,Zhoujian Cao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了未来空间引力波探测器通过观测环绕超大质量黑洞（SMBH）运动的恒星质量双黑洞（BBH）来约束SMBH性质的能力，基于稳定层级三重系统模型和LISA配置，发现SMBH质量和轨道参数在高信噪比下可达到约10^{-5}的相对测量精度，自旋大小及方向可约束在百分之几以内，且对于M87*类系统，引力波观测能提供比当前电磁观测更精确的SMBH参数测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于稳定的层级三重系统（hierarchical triple systems）模型，在Kerr时空中描述BBH运动，结合后牛顿波形（post Newtonian waveform）与运动源变换（moving-source transformation）计算调制的引力波信号。采用LISA配置与第二代时间延迟干涉测量技术（time delay interferometry），利用Fisher信息矩阵（Fisher information matrix）估计参数不确定度。

Result: 外半长轴（outer semimajor axis）对参数精度影响最大，而SMBH自旋和轨道偏心率主要影响各自的不确定度。高信噪比信号下，SMBH质量与轨道参数的相对不确定度可达10^{-5}量级，自旋大小及其取向可约束在百分之几以内。对M87*类系统的应用表明，引力波观测能提供比当前电磁观测更精确的SMBH质量和自旋测量。

Conclusion: 空间引力波天文学在精确探测SMBH性质方面具有巨大潜力，能够以高精度实现SMBH质量和自旋等关键参数的测量，超越现有电磁观测手段的精度水平。

Abstract: We study the capability of future space-based gravitational-wave (GW) detectors to constrain supermassive black hole (SMBH) properties through observations of inspiraling stellar-mass binary black holes (BBHs) orbiting them. Focusing on stable hierarchical triple systems, we model the BBH motion in Kerr spacetime and compute the modulated GW signals using the post Newtonian waveform combined with moving-source transformation. Based on the LISA configuration and second-generation time delay interferometry technology, we estimate parameter uncertainties with the Fisher information matrix. Our results show that the outer semimajor axis has the strongest influence on parameter precision, while the SMBH spin and eccentricity mainly affect their own uncertainties. For high-SNR signals, the SMBH mass and orbital parameters can be measured with relative uncertainties on the order of $10^{-5}$, while the spin magnitude and its orientation can be constrained to within a few percentages. Applying the method to an M87*-like system, GW observations provide more precise measurements of the SMBH mass and spin compared with current electromagnetic observations, highlighting the potential of space-based GW astronomy to probe SMBH properties with high accuracy.

### [145] [Strong deflection limit-analysis using Picard-Fuchs equation in Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12819)
*Tadashi Sasaki*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-狄拉顿（Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton）理论中，针对特定狄拉顿耦合常数下的带电球对称黑洞，将光线偏转角表示为椭圆积分，建立其满足的皮卡-傅克斯（Picard-Fuchs）偏微分方程组，并利用与潘勒韦VI型方程（Painlevé VI）相关的哈密顿系统，通过零电荷极限确定强偏转极限下对数公式中的常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-狄拉顿理论中，带电黑洞的光线偏转问题涉及复杂的数学结构，现有方法难以精确解析求解偏转角，尤其是强偏转极限下的对数行为。

Method: 将偏转角表示为关于两个无量纲变量(s, z)的椭圆积分，导出其满足的二阶线性偏微分方程组（皮卡-傅克斯方程）。针对每种狄拉顿耦合情形，将该方程组简化为关于变量s的一阶常微分方程，并利用皮卡-傅克斯方程的可积性所引出的潘勒韦VI型方程哈密顿系统，求解强偏转极限对数公式中的常数。

Result: 强偏转极限下对数公式中的常数\bar{a}和\bar{b}满足由皮卡-傅克斯方程导出的一阶常微分方程，通过潘勒韦VI型方程的哈密顿系统得以求解；在零电荷极限下与史瓦西（Schwarzschild）情形一致时，非零电荷下的\bar{a}和\bar{b}被唯一确定。

Conclusion: 本文建立的方法为求解特定耦合常数下狄拉顿黑洞的强偏转极限提供了精确解析框架，并可推广至其他可积模型。

Abstract: We consider the deflection of light by a spherically symmetric and electrically charged black hole solution in the Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton theory with specific values of the dilaton coupling constant where the deflection angle can be represented as elliptic integrals. We show that the deflection angle as a function of two dimensionless variables $(s,z)$, which are related to the background charge and the impact parameter, respectively, satisfies a system of 2nd-order linear partial differential equations called the Picard-Fuchs (PF) equations. For each case of the dilaton coupling, the PF equations lead to 1st-order ordinary differential equations with respect to the variable $s$ for the constants $\bar{a}$ and $\bar{b}$ in the log-formula for the strong deflection limit. Using the Hamiltonian system associated with Painlevé VI equations, which holds as a result of the integrability of the PF equations, we solve the equations for $\bar{a}$ and $\bar{b}$. By requiring consistency with the Schwarzschild case in the zero-charge limit, $\bar{a}$ and $\bar{b}$ for nonzero charge are uniquely determined.

### [146] [Tests of general relativity at the fourth post-Newtonian order with GW230627 and GW250114](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12931)
*Xi-Min Liang,Yuan-Zhu Wang,Tao Zhu,Wen Zhao,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）网络探测到的两个极高信噪比引力波事件，首次对广义相对论在4后牛顿（PN）和4.5PN阶的旋近相位效应进行了观测约束。贝叶斯推断结果表明，所有偏离参数均与广义相对论预测一致，确立了高阶后牛顿旋近检验的首个经验基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波观测为检验强场、高动态及相对论性区域中的广义相对论（general relativity, GR）提供了前所未有的实验平台。传统的参数化后牛顿（parameterized post-Newtonian, PN）波形检验仅局限于对3.5PN阶以内的旋近系数施加约束，而更高阶（4PN和4.5PN）效应此前从未被观测检验过。

Method: 利用近期将解析致密双星相位（analytical compact binary phasing）拓展至4.5PN阶的理论突破，选取LVK网络记录的两个特殊事件——具有最高信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）的GW250114\_082203，以及具有最长旋近相位与最高旋近阶段SNR的GW230627\_015337——对与4PN和4.5PN系数相关的无量纲偏离参数（dimensionless deviation parameters）$δφ_i$进行贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）。

Result: 所有分析结果与广义相对论预测完全一致。四个偏离参数的当前90%置信区间（credible intervals）的量级为$\mathcal{O}(1) \text{-} \mathcal{O}(10)$，广义相对论零值（null values，$δ\hatφ_a= 0$）完全包含在这些置信区间之内。

Conclusion: 本研究首次建立了4PN和4.5PN旋近阶广义相对论检验的经验基线，为利用当前及下一代引力波探测器开展高精度广义相对论零检验（null tests）铺平了道路。

Abstract: Gravitational wave (GW) observations provide an unprecedented laboratory for testing general relativity (GR) in the strong-field, highly dynamic, and relativistic regimes. Within the parameterized post-Newtonian (PN) formalisms, waveform generation tests have conventionally been limited to constraining inspiral coefficients up to the 3.5PN order. Leveraging the recent theoretical breakthrough that extended the analytical compact binary phasing to the 4.5PN order, we present the first observational constraints on these higher-order effects. Our analysis utilizes two exceptional events detected by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) network: GW250114\_082203, which boasts the highest signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) recorded to date, and GW230627\_015337, which features a uniquely prolonged inspiral phase and the highest inspiral phase SNR to date. By performing Bayesian inference on the dimensionless deviation parameters ($δφ_i$) associated with the 4PN and 4.5PN coefficients, we find that our results are fully consistent with the predictions of GR. While the current 90\% credible intervals for the four deviation parameters are of order $\mathcal{O}(1) \text{-} \mathcal{O}(10)$, the general relativistic null values ($δ\hatφ_a= 0$) are entirely encapsulated within the bounds. This investigation establishes the first empirical baseline for 4PN and 4.5PN inspiral tests of GR, paving the way for high-precision null tests of GR with current and next-generation GW detectors.

### [147] [Tidal Love numbers and the dynamical instability of AdS bubbles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13014)
*Gerui Chen,Yu Tian,Hongbao Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本工作研究了AdS气泡（AdS bubbles）的非径向扰动及其潮汐Love数（tidal Love numbers, TLNs），计算了高角量子数下的奇偶宇称TLNs，发现奇宇称TLNs为负、偶宇称TLNs在特定条件下为正，且随着l增大TLNs趋于零；在p/σ>0的区域，高l下偶宇称TLNs变为负值，与eikonal极限下自引力膜的不稳定性判据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究AdS气泡的非径向扰动及其潮汐Love数，以深入理解这类引力系统的稳定性与响应特性，并检验与eikonal极限下自引力膜（self-gravitating membranes）不稳定判据的关联。

Method: 计算了奇宇称（odd-parity）和偶宇称（even-parity）TLNs至l=6，在k→∞极限下进行；并在整个k参数空间（0到∞）中计算了偶宇称TLNs至高阶l=41。

Result: 奇宇称TLNs为负值，偶宇称TLNs在υ²_s=-1条件下为正值；随着l增大，TLNs趋近于零。在p/σ>0的区域，随着l增大，越来越多的偶宇称TLNs变为负值；在l=41时，除p/σ接近零的狭窄区域外，TLNs全部为负值。

Conclusion: 高l下偶宇称TLNs的符号变化与Yang等人提出的eikonal极限下自引力膜的不稳定性判据吻合良好，表明该方法可为AdS气泡的稳定性分析提供有效工具。

Abstract: In this work, we study non-radial perturbations of AdS bubbles and their tidal Love numbers (TLNs). The odd- and even-parity TLNs are computed up to $l=6$ in the limit $k \to \infty$. The odd-parity TLNs are found to be negative, while the even-parity TLNs are positive for $\upsilon^2_s=-1$. As $l$ increases, the tidal Love numbers approach zero. The TLNs of the even-parity sector up to order $l=41$ are also calculated over the entire parameter space of $k$, from $0$ to $\infty$. We find that in the region where $p/σ>0$, an increasing number of TLNs become negative as $l$ increases. For $l = 41$, the highest order we have examined, the TLNs are negative everywhere except in a narrow region very close to the zero of $p/σ$, which agrees well with the instability criterion in the eikonal limit for self-gravitating membranes proposed by Yang {\it et al.}\ [P. R. L. {\bf 130}, 011402 (2023)].

### [148] [Thermodynamics of polymerized vacuum regular black holes in anti-de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13167)
*Sepideh Bakhoda,Ioannis Soranidis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从有效圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity, LQG）动力学出发，导出了一类真空规则黑洞（regular black hole），并将其推广至渐近反德西特（anti-de Sitter, AdS）时空。基于去参数化的Lemaître–Tolman–Bondi (LTB) 表述，在球对称性下构造了具有德西特（de Sitter, dS）核与反德西特核的规则黑洞模型，并系统研究了其扩展相空间中的热力学，特别是Hawking–Page相变。结果表明，正则化主要通过变形外视界分支影响相变温度，而核心类型（dS或AdS）对热力学行为的差异具有独立于规则化本身的重要作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从量子引力理论（圈量子引力）的有效动力学出发，系统构建一类自洽的规则黑洞解，避免经典广义相对论中的奇点问题，并将构造推广至具有负宇宙学常数的AdS时空，为后续热力学研究提供统一的解析框架。

Method: 采用去参数化的Lemaître–Tolman–Bondi (LTB) 表述，引入辅助尘埃场（dust field）仅用于定义内禀时间（internal time），不作为物质源。在球对称性下，动力学简化为独立径向壳层，得到因子化壳层哈密顿量（factorized shell Hamiltonian）和Birkhoff型性质。以此为基础构造不同核心类型的规则黑洞，并在扩展相空间中分析其热力学。

Result: 成功构造了具有德西特核与反德西特核的规则黑洞模型；发现主导相变为Hawking–Page型，由黑洞自由能与热AdS背景的交叉决定；正则化通过变形物理外视界分支及端点结构定量改变Hawking–Page温度；在大的AdS半径下，dS核解的Hawking–Page温度高于AdS核解，但在AdS尺度接近下限时顺序可能反转。

Conclusion: 两类规则黑洞（dS核与AdS核）之间的热力学差异并非仅由正则化本身引起，而是取决于核心变形如何相对于热AdS参考背景修改视界分支结构。不同核心类型在有限参数区间内可导致相变温度的定性差异。

Abstract: We derive a class of vacuum regular black holes inspired by effective loop quantum gravity dynamics and extend the construction to asymptotically anti-de Sitter spacetimes. The derivation is based on a deparameterized Lemaître--Tolman--Bondi formulation, where an auxiliary dust field is introduced only to define an internal time and does not act as a matter source. In spherical symmetry, the dynamics reduces to a set of independent radial shells, giving rise to a factorized shell Hamiltonian and to a Birkhoff-type property: for a fixed reconstruction function and cosmological constant, the static geometry is uniquely determined by the mass. Within this framework, we construct several regular black hole models with de Sitter cores and corresponding models with anti-de Sitter cores. We then study their thermodynamics in the extended phase space, with particular emphasis on the Hawking--Page transition. For the class of models considered, the dominant transition is of Hawking--Page type, determined by the crossing of the black hole free energy with the corresponding thermal-AdS background. The regularization affects the quantitative transition temperature by deforming the physical outer-horizon branch, including its endpoint structure. In the large anti-de Sitter radius regime, the de Sitter core solutions exhibit a higher Hawking--Page temperature than their anti-de Sitter-core counterparts, while the ordering can be modified close to the lower admissible range of the AdS scale. Thus, the thermodynamic differences between the two classes are not a consequence of regularity alone, but arise from how the core deformation modifies the horizon branch relative to the thermal-AdS reference background.

</details>


### [149] [Absorption cross section of a Schwarzschild black hole for a massive vector field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13217)
*Kaustubh Mukund Vispute,Rajesh Karmakar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Frolov-Krtouš-Kubizňák-Santos (FKKS)基下，研究了Schwarzschild黑洞对任意频率的有质量矢量场（massive vector field）的吸收截面，数值计算了透射与反射系数，揭示了质量项导致的纵向自由度（longitudinal degree of freedom）和标量型分支（scalar-type branch）等新特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鉴于近年来超轻玻色场（ultralight bosonic fields）在黑洞时空中的研究进展，理解有质量矢量玻色子（massive vector bosons）的透射特性具有重要物理意义。

Method: 在FKKS基下，通过归一化Proca场的守恒流（conserved flux）自然地导出吸收截面与反射系数和透射系数的标准关系，并在任意频率下对这些量进行数值计算。

Result: 与无质量（光子）情形相比，有质量矢量场因质量项引入了纵向自由度以及偶宇称横模（even parity transverse modes）中的标量型分支，打破了无质量情形下偶奇宇称扇区的简并性（degeneracy）。这些特征在透射谱和吸收谱中均有体现。

Conclusion: 有质量矢量玻色子的透射特性对于当前超轻玻色场在黑洞时空中的研究具有特殊意义。

Abstract: In the present work, we study the absorption cross section of a Schwarzschild black hole for a massive vector field over arbitrary frequencies. Working in the Frolov-Krtouš-Kubizňák-Santos (FKKS) basis, we show how the conserved flux of the normalized Proca field naturally leads to the usual definitions of the absorption cross section in terms of the reflection and transmission coefficients. We then numerically compute these quantities over arbitrary frequencies. In contrast to the massless (photon) case, massive vector bosons exhibit new features arising from the field mass. In particular, the mass term introduces a longitudinal degree of freedom in addition to the transverse modes. Furthermore, it leads to a scalar-type branch in the even parity transverse modes, thereby breaking the usual degeneracy with the odd parity sector found in the massless case. We illustrate how these characteristics manifest themselves in the transmission and absorption spectrum. Given the recent developments in the study of ultralight bosonic fields in black hole spacetimes, the present analysis of the transmission properties of massive vector bosons bears particular significance.

</details>

Method: 采用幂律形式的 $f(T)=α(-T)^{n}$ 函数修正遥平行引力；利用对数和对数周期两种参数化形式描述解耦参数，进而通过红移（redshift）依赖关系推导哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）；基于宇宙计时器数据集和联合（CC+Pantheon）数据集，运用 $\chi^{2}$ 极小化的贝叶斯分析方法约束模型参数。

Result: 解耦参数、能量密度（energy density）、压强（pressure）、状态方程参数（equation of state parameter）及能量条件（energy conditions）的详细演化被呈现；几何诊断（geometrical diagnostics）显示模型明显偏离标准宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）行为，指向一个动态演化的暗能量场景；模型在热力学上保持自洽，并且估算的宇宙年龄与观测约束相符。

Conclusion: 所提出的修正遥平行引力模型能够提供一种动态暗能量的可行描述，其与观测数据的兼容性以及热力学一致性共同验证了该理论框架的稳健性和有效性。

Abstract: In this study, we probe the cosmological evolution of the universe within the framework of modified teleparallel gravity by considering a power-law form of the function $f(T)=α(-T)^{n}$. To characterize the expansion dynamics, we employ logarithmic and log-periodic parametrizations of the deceleration parameter. These specific parametrizations provide a flexible and well-structured description of the cosmic expansion history across different cosmological epochs. The corresponding Hubble parameter is obtained as a function of redshift, facilitating a systematic investigation of the background dynamics. The model parameters are constrained using cosmic chronometer (CC) and joint (CC+Pantheon) datasets through a Bayesian analysis based on the $χ^{2}$-minimization approach. The evolution of key cosmological quantities, including the deceleration parameter, energy density, pressure, equation of state parameter and energy conditions, is examined in detail. The geometrical diagnostics indicate a clear departure from the standard cosmological constant behavior, pointing toward a dynamically evolving dark energy scenario. Further, the proposed models remain thermodynamically consistent and the estimated age of the universe is found to be compatible with observational constraints, thereby reinforcing the robustness and viability of the framework.

### [151] [Solar-System Bounds on Ricci-flat Spindle Deformations of Schwarzschild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13325)
*Zhong-Xi Yu,Hong-Da Lyu,Shoulong Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从唯象学角度约束了一类新型四维广义相对论（general relativity）中变形黑洞解的几何变形参数$B$。利用行星近日点进动（perihelion precession）和Cassini光行时延迟（Shapiro time delay）两个经典太阳系检验，得出$|B|\lesssim 10^{-24}{-}10^{-23}\ {\rm cm}^{-1}$（近日点进动）及$|B|\lesssim 10^{-21}\ {\rm cm}^{-1}$（光行时延迟）的强上限，表明若纺锤形（spindle）变形延伸到太阳系弱场区域，其效应必须被极度压制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一类新型变形黑洞精确解被提出后，其变形由参数$B$控制，且几何结构变为非渐近平坦（non-asymptotically flat）的纺锤形时空。目前没有已知的天体物理机制能产生这种变形，但可从唯象学角度追问：如果该变形延伸到太阳系外部弱场区域，其大小上限是多少。

Method: 利用两个经典太阳系检验——行星近日点进动修正和Shapiro型光行时延迟的Cassini估计——导出$B$诱导的前导阶（leading-order）修正。将修正量与观测不确定度比较，从而约束$B$的上限。

Result: 行星近日点额外进动的观测不确定度给出最强约束$|B|\lesssim 10^{-24}{-}10^{-23}\ {\rm cm}^{-1}$；Cassini光行时延迟估计给出互补的零测地线灵敏度约束$|B|\lesssim 10^{-21}\ {\rm cm}^{-1}$。

Conclusion: 若此类纺锤形几何变形延伸到太阳系外部区域，其变形在太阳系尺度上必须被极度压制。

Abstract: Recently, a new class of deformed black-hole exact solutions was constructed in four-dimensional general relativity. The deformation is controlled by a parameter $B$, which survives after demagnetizing a black hole immersed in an external Bertotti-Robinson magnetic field and changes the global structure of the spacetime into a non-asymptotically flat spindle geometry. Although no astrophysical mechanism for generating such a deformation is currently known, it is natural to ask phenomenologically how large such a geometric deformation could be if it extended over the weak-field solar exterior. Using two classical Solar-System tests, we derive the leading corrections to planetary perihelion precession and to the light travel time in a Shapiro-type configuration. Requiring the \(B\)-induced perihelion advance to be smaller than the observational uncertainties in the supplementary perihelion precessions of planets gives the strongest bounds, \( |B|\lesssim 10^{-24}\text{--}10^{-23}\ {\rm cm}^{-1}\), while a Cassini time delay estimate gives a complementary null-geodesic sensitivity at the level \( |B|\lesssim 10^{-21}\ {\rm cm}^{-1}\). These results show that any such spindle deformation, if extended to the solar exterior geometry, must be extremely suppressed on Solar-System scales.

### [152] [Bounds on $Λ$ at the Galactic Center](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13356)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用围绕银河系中心（Galactic Center）Sgr A* 公转的 S2、S1、S14 三颗恒星的天体测量与光谱观测数据，通过数值积分 Schwarzschild-de Sitter 时空中的类时测地线并辅以贝叶斯马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）推断，对宇宙学常数 Λ 给出了上限约束：68% 置信度下 Λ ≲ 6.9×10⁻⁴⁸ m⁻²，95% 置信度下 Λ ≲ 1.0×10⁻³⁸ m⁻²。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学常数 Λ 是描述宇宙加速膨胀的关键参数，但其在局域引力系统中的直接探测和约束仍较欠缺。利用银河系中心（Galactic Center）附近恒星的高精度轨道观测，可为 Λ 在百秒差距（parsec）尺度上的大小提供独立的检验约束。

Method: 采用 Schwarzschild-de Sitter 时空中的类时测地线（timelike geodesic）数值积分来建模恒星运动，同时包含相对论红移（relativistic redshift）和时间延迟（time-delay）修正。轨道参数与时空参数通过贝叶斯 MCMC 分析（Bayesian MCMC analysis）进行推断。

Result: 联合 S2、S1 和 S14 三颗恒星的轨道约束后，得到 Λ 的上限：在 68% 可信度下 Λ ≲ 6.9×10⁻⁴⁸ m⁻²，在 95% 可信度下 Λ ≲ 1.0×10⁻³⁸ m⁻²。

Conclusion: 银河系中心恒星的高精度轨道观测能够对宇宙学常数 Λ 施加有意义的局域上限，且联合多颗恒星轨道可有效提升约束能力。

Abstract: We constrain the cosmological constant $Λ$ using astrometric and spectroscopic observations of the S2, S1, and S14 stars orbiting Sgr A$^*$. The stellar motion is modelled by numerically integrating timelike geodesics in Schwarzschild-de Sitter spacetime, including relativistic redshift and time-delay corrections. Orbital and spacetime parameters are inferred using a Bayesian MCMC analysis. The resulting posterior distributions place upper bounds on the magnitude of $Λ$ at the Galactic Center (GC). Combining the independent constraints from the S2, S1, and S14 orbits yields upper bounds of $Λ\lesssim 6.9\times10^{-48} \mathrm{m}^{-2}$ at 68\% credibility and $Λ\lesssim 1.0\times10^{-38} \mathrm{m}^{-2}$ at 95\% credibility.

### [153] [Beyond the Metric: Geometrical Measurability as a Constraint on Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13522)
*Matteo Tuveri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于广义相对论（general relativity）经验意义的量子引力（quantum gravity）认识论约束条件：任何可行的量子引力理论必须在恢复几何本身的同时，恢复客观几何测量的物理可能性。该主张通过四个典型案例（Rindler视界与Unruh效应、黑洞热力学与Jacobson方程、引力波探测、Weyl共形引力）加以论证，并讨论了其对量子引力的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力中时空几何可能是涌现的（emergent）、有效的（effective）、热力学的（thermodynamic）、关系性的（relational）或依赖于参考系的（frame-dependent），这使得在经典广义相对论中隐含的客观几何测量条件变得非平凡。因此，需要明确一个认识论约束，以确保量子引力理论能够恢复广义相对论的经验内容。

Method: 本文从广义相对论的经验意义出发，提炼出恢复广义相对论所需的物理条件：有效度规（effective metric）、连续极限（continuum limit）或类爱因斯坦动力学（Einstein-like dynamics），以及关系几何量可被客观确定的物理条件（包括测量装置和参考系的动力学稳定性、物理系统间的因果可及性、记录形成（record formation）、以及允许描述下的不变性）。通过四个案例——Rindler视界与Unruh效应、黑洞热力学与Jacobson方程、引力波探测、Weyl与共形引力——展开分析，并以涌现引力和量子参考系为例讨论对量子引力的启示。

Result: 提出了一个普适的认识论约束条件：任何可行的量子引力方法必须恢复客观几何测量的物理可能性。Weyl与共形引力作为临界案例（limiting case）被讨论，其中共形不变性（conformal invariance）提出了一个尖锐问题：空间和时间的尺度依赖测量能否在物理上被固定。

Conclusion: 量子引力不仅需要恢复几何本身，还必须同时恢复客观几何测量的物理条件。这构成一个一般性的认识论约束，对评估和发展量子引力理论具有指导意义。

Abstract: This paper develops an epistemological constraint on quantum gravity grounded in the empirical meaning of general relativity. The central claim is that a complete recovery of general relativity requires an effective metric, a continuum limit, or Einstein-like dynamics together with the physical conditions under which relational geometrical quantities can be objectively determined. These conditions concern the dynamical stability of measuring devices and reference systems, causal accessibility among physical systems, record formation, and invariance under admissible descriptions. In classical general relativity, they are usually implicit in the use of clocks, rods, light signals, freely falling bodies, detectors, and gauge-invariant observables. In quantum gravity, however, they become non-trivial because spacetime geometry may be emergent, effective, thermodynamic, relational, or frame-dependent. This claim is developed through four cases: Rindler horizons and the Unruh effect, black-hole thermodynamics and Jacobson's equation-of-state derivation, gravitational-wave detection, and Weyl and conformal gravity. The latter is discussed as a critical limiting case in which conformal invariance raises a sharp question about whether scale-dependent measurements of space and time can be physically fixed. Implications for quantum gravity are also discussed using emergent gravity and quantum reference frames as examples. The perspective developed in the study suggests a general epistemological constraint on quantum gravity: any viable approach must recover the physical possibility of objective geometrical measurement together with geometry itself.
