### [154] [Trapped Surface as a Cosmic Censor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13592)
*Hideo Furugori,Daisuke Yoshida,Kaho Yoshimura*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于局域几何的捕获面判据（trapped surface criterion），用于判断黑洞过充电或过自旋思想实验中弱宇宙监督假设（weak cosmic censorship）是否成立。在零收敛条件（null convergence condition）和一般性条件下，物质注入会使视界截面变为闭合捕获面，任何无法容纳该捕获面的终态时空都将被排除。该判据排除了超极端Reissner-Nordström、Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter、Kerr-Newman终态以及Weyl类裸奇点，且不依赖于渐近电荷或表征裸奇点的极端条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检验弱宇宙监督假设（weak cosmic censorship hypothesis）的方法通常依赖渐近电荷（asymptotic charges）或极端条件（extremal condition）来判定裸奇点（naked singularity），但这些判据并非完全局域或普适。本文旨在构建一个完全基于局域几何的判据，以更可靠地排除导致裸奇点形成的终态时空。

Method: 作者提出了一个局域几何判据：在零收敛条件和一般性条件下，物质注入会使黑洞视界截面（horizon cross section）转变为闭合捕获面（closed trapped surface）。若终态时空无法容纳该捕获面，则该终态被判定为不可实现，从而违反弱宇宙监督。

Result: 该捕获面判据成功排除了超极端（superextremal）的Reissner-Nordström、Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter和Kerr-Newman终态，以及Weyl类裸奇点（Weyl-class naked singularities）。该判据不依赖于渐近电荷或表征裸奇点的极端条件。

Conclusion: 捕获面判据为检验弱宇宙监督假设提供了全新的局域几何视角，相较于传统方法更具普适性，可涵盖更广泛的时空类型，并可能推广到其他引力理论或非渐近平坦时空。

Abstract: We formulate a local geometric criterion for weak cosmic censorship in black hole overcharging and overspinning thought experiments. Under the null convergence and generic conditions, matter injection turns a horizon cross section into a closed trapped surface. Any final spacetime unable to accommodate this surface is ruled out. This trapped surface criterion excludes superextremal Reissner-Nordström, Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter, and Kerr-Newman final states, as well as Weyl-class naked singularities. Our criterion does not rely on asymptotic charges or on an extremal condition characterizing naked singularities.

### [155] [Geometrically Regular Black Object Solutions in Lower-Dimensional Gauss-Bonnet Gravity and Its Unimodular Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13635)
*G. Alencar,T. M. Crispim,C. R. Muniz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在低维爱因斯坦-高斯-邦内特（EGB）引力框架下，通过构建非线性电动力学支持的规则黑洞、Simpson-Visser黑洞弹跳几何以及单模引力扩展，解决了由高曲率修正导致的曲率奇点问题，并分析了这些规则致密天体的热力学性质，包括蒸发过程修正、残余物形成和相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准BTZ黑洞对应的真空EGB解在原点处产生真实的曲率奇点（curvature singularity），表明高曲率修正反而恶化了时空的紫外行为。因此，本文旨在通过重建物质部分来恢复时空的正则性，同时保持BTZ型的渐近结构。

Method: 首先，推导由非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics）支持的规则黑洞解，直接从场方程确定相应的电磁拉格朗日量（electromagnetic Lagrangian）。其次，将分析扩展到Simpson-Visser黑洞弹跳（black-bounce）几何，获得整个时空曲率不变量（curvature invariants）有限的光滑喉部构型。最后，构建低维EGB引力的单模扩展（unimodular extension），通过时空依赖的宇宙学函数（cosmological function）实现真空与物质部分之间的动力学交换，使标准麦克斯韦场（Maxwell field）支持规则几何。

Result: 规则黑洞和黑洞弹跳解的热力学性质表明，物质部分修改了蒸发过程，允许残余物（remnant）形成，并产生非平凡的相变。在黑洞弹跳情形中，热力学量在适当极限下平滑地恢复为EGB-BTZ行为。

Conclusion: 低维EGB引力为探索高曲率修正、规则致密天体、非线性电动力学和单模引力之间的相互作用提供了一个有用的理论实验室。

Abstract: We investigate the construction of regular compact objects in the recently proposed lower-dimensional Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet (EGB) gravity obtained through regularized dimensional reduction. Unlike the standard BTZ black hole, the corresponding vacuum EGB solution develops a genuine curvature singularity at the origin, providing an interesting setting in which higher-curvature corrections deteriorate the ultraviolet behavior of spacetime. To address this issue, we reconstruct matter sectors capable of restoring regularity while preserving the BTZ-like asymptotic structure. First, we derive regular black-hole solutions supported by nonlinear electrodynamics and determine the corresponding electromagnetic Lagrangians directly from the field equations. We then extend the analysis to Simpson--Visser black-bounce geometries, obtaining smooth throat configurations with finite curvature invariants throughout the spacetime. As an alternative regularization mechanism, we formulate a unimodular extension of lower-dimensional EGB gravity and show that standard Maxwell fields can support regular geometries through a dynamical exchange between the vacuum and matter sectors mediated by a spacetime-dependent cosmological function. We further investigate the thermodynamic properties of the regular black-hole and black-bounce solutions, showing that the matter sector modifies the evaporation process, allows for remnant formation, and produces nontrivial phase transitions. In the black-bounce case, the thermodynamic quantities smoothly recover the EGB-BTZ behavior in the appropriate limit. These results demonstrate that lower-dimensional EGB gravity provides a useful laboratory for exploring the interplay between higher-curvature corrections, regular compact objects, nonlinear electrodynamics, and unimodular gravity.

</details>

*Laura Bridera,Emanuel Gallo,Thomas Mädler*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用仿射-零特征 formulation（affine-null characteristic formulation），引入合适的辅助变量（auxiliary variables），将主场方程转化为一组径向超曲面方程（radial hypersurface equations）的层级系统，并补充标量场的输运方程（transport equation）。

Result: 获得了渐近量（asymptotic quantities）与平衡律（balance laws）；作为一致性检验，直接从层级系统中恢复了无标量场的Reissner-Nordström-Tangherlini族（包括非极端与极端分支）。

Conclusion: 该框架为在高维仿射-零坐标（affine-null coordinates）中研究带电标量动力学和精确黑洞解提供了系统化的工具。

Abstract: We develop an affine-null characteristic formulation of the Einstein-Maxwell system coupled to a charged complex scalar field in $n$-dimensional spherical symmetry. By introducing suitable auxiliary variables, the main field equations are cast into a hierarchical system of radial hypersurface equations, supplemented by a transport equation for the scalar field. We discuss the associated characteristic initial-boundary value problem for asymptotic, vertex and null-boundary configurations, and derive the corresponding asymptotic quantities and balance laws. As a consistency check, we recover the scalar-free Reissner-Nordström-Tangherlini family, including both the non-extremal and extremal branches, directly from the hierarchy. The resulting framework provides a systematic setting for the study of charged scalar dynamics and exact black-hole solutions in higher-dimensional affine-null coordinates.

<details>

Method: 利用逆格森斯坦效应（inverse Gertsenshtein effect），通过地球磁场将高频引力波转换为电磁辐射，并借助甚大阵列（VLA）和阿塔卡马大型毫米波/亚毫米波阵列（ALMA）等射电望远镜进行观测搜索。

Result: 未观测到统计显著信号，在1 GHz–1 THz频段上给出了新的特征应变（characteristic strain）上限，最强约束为 $h_c \lesssim 10^{-18}$，较现有界限提升了三个数量级。

Conclusion: 该结果为奇异引力波源（exotic gravitational-wave sources）的探索开辟了新的参数空间，并为未来使用平方千米阵列（SKA）等下一代设施发现高频引力波奠定了基础。

Abstract: The detection of high-frequency gravitational waves (HFGWs) above 10 kHz provides a crucial probe of exotic astrophysical phenomena and new physics. We report the first search for HFGWs via their conversion to electromagnetic radiation through the inverse Gertsenshtein effect in Earth's magnetic field, utilizing radio telescopes including the Very Large Array (VLA) and the Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA). Since no statistically significant signal is observed, we obtain new upper limits on the characteristic strain across the 1 GHz -- 1 THz band, with the most stringent constraint reaching $h_c \lesssim 10^{-18}$, improving upon existing bounds by up to three orders of magnitude. These results significantly advance the exploration of uncharted parameter space for exotic gravitational-wave sources, paving the way for future discoveries with next-generation facilities such as the Square Kilometre Array (SKA).

An oceanic site above the Pacific LLSVP is considered a particularly favorable detector location. The Ocean Bottom Detector (OBD) project aims to leverage this spatial resolving advantage by deploying a kiloton-scale liquid scintillator detector directly on the ocean floor, enabling unprecedented sensitivity for mantle geoneutrino detection. These findings demonstrate the critical role of combining geophysical and geochemical data to guide detector site selection, ultimately improving constraints on Earth's internal heat and the HPE distribution.

### [159] [How alignment controls heat transport in polymer chains with kinks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12738)
*Igor V. Parshin,Igor V. Rubtsov,Alexander L. Burin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文揭示聚合物分子链中的扭结（kinks）会破坏平移对称性，导致对长波声子（包括纵波和横波）产生强散射，从而使热导率随分子链长度增加而快速下降，解释了为何高度取向聚合物具有高热导率而随机取向聚合物热导率极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释聚合物热导率对分子取向高度敏感（高度取向聚合物热导率高，随机取向聚合物热导率低几个数量级）的物理机制。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究分子链中扭结（kinks）对长波声子（phonons）的散射行为，考察扭结如何破坏纵波和横波的平移对称性（translational symmetry）。

Result: 即使在长波极限下，扭结仍会对纵波和横波声子产生强散射，导致随机取向扭结使热导率随分子链长度增加而快速下降。

Conclusion: 分子取向控制（即扭结工程，kink engineering）可作为调控聚合物热传输性能的有效途径。

Abstract: Thermal transport in long polymer molecules is commonly attributed to ballistic propagation of long-wavelength acoustic phonons, which act as Goldstone modes arising from translational symmetry, while the transport of other phonons is suppressed by Anderson localization. This mechanism leads to thermal conductivity that increases with molecular length. Consistent with this picture, strongly aligned polymers exhibit exceptionally high thermal conductivity, whereas poorly aligned polymers are orders of magnitude less conductive and function as thermal insulators. Here we show that this strong sensitivity to molecular alignment originates from phonon scattering by molecular kinks. Even in the long-wavelength limit, the kink scattering remains strong because kinks break translational symmetry both for longitudinal and transverse phonons. As a result, randomly oriented kinks cause a rapid decrease in thermal conductivity with increasing molecular length. These findings identify alignment control by means of kink engineering as a route for tuning thermal transport in polymers.

### [160] [Collective alignment controls rotation frustration in granular flows of elongated particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13070)
*Antonio Pol,Riccardo Artoni,Patrick Richard*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过三维离散元模拟，揭示了细长颗粒在密集约束剪切流中转动抑制的根本机制是颗粒集体取向排列（由向列序参数量化），而非以往认为的颗粒形状、摩擦或固相分数等单一因素，并提出了一个仅依赖向列序参量的标度律来统一描述平均角速度与局部剪切率的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细长颗粒的密集颗粒流（dense granular flows）相较于球形颗粒表现出显著的转动抑制现象，但其背后的物理机制尚不清晰。摘要旨在厘清颗粒形状、摩擦及边界条件等因素在其中的具体作用。

Method: 采用三维离散元模拟（three-dimensional discrete element simulations），系统变化颗粒长径比（aspect ratio）、颗粒间摩擦（interparticle friction）以及边界条件，分析细长颗粒在密集、约束剪切流中的角动力学（angular dynamics）。

Result: 发现平均角速度的降低不能归因于颗粒形状、摩擦或固相分数（solid fraction）中的任何一个单独因素，而是受剪切作用下集体取向排列（collective alignment）程度的控制，该程度由向列序参量（nematic order parameter）量化。基于此，提出了一个通过阻碍参数（hampering parameter）联系平均角速度与局部剪切率的标度律（scaling law），该参数仅依赖于向列序参量。

Conclusion: 该标度律成功地将不同颗粒属性（形状、摩擦）、不同流动模式的数据统一起来，并且额外验证了两种不同的流动构型，表明该机制具有跨构型的普适性。

Abstract: Dense granular flows made of elongated particles exhibit a strong inhibition of particle rotation compared to spherical grains, but the mechanisms responsible for this effect remain unclear. Using three-dimensional discrete element simulations, we investigate the angular dynamics of elongated particles in dense, confined shear flows. We systematically vary particle aspect ratio, interparticle friction, and boundary conditions to elucidate their respective roles. We show that the reduction of the average angular velocity cannot be attributed to particle shape, friction, or solid fraction alone. Instead, it is controlled by the degree of collective alignment developed under shear, quantified by a nematic order parameter. Based on this observation, we propose a simple scaling law linking the average angular velocity to the local shear rate through a hampering parameter that depends solely on the orientational order via the nematic order parameter. This scaling successfully collapses data obtained for different particle properties (shape, friction), different flow patterns, and, remarkably, remains valid for two additional flow configurations.

### [161] [Real-time quantification of fluid flows around bubbles during directional solidification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13228)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气泡液体的定向凝固（directional solidification）对许多材料的微观结构（microstructure）和性能至关重要，但控制气泡行为的流体动力学（fluid dynamics）机制尚不清楚。现有理论假设马兰戈尼流起关键作用，但缺乏直接实验验证。

Method: 采用低温共聚焦显微镜和粒子图像测速技术，在含有表面活性剂（surfactants）和示踪粒子（tracers）的水凝固过程中，定量测量气泡周围的流体流动。

Result: 体积膨胀主导流体运动，速度与凝固速率（1–20 μm/s）呈线性关系；马兰戈尼流速度小于5 μm/s，贡献可忽略；扩散泳和热泳贡献同样极小。

Conclusion: 实验结果挑战了现有理论模型中对马兰戈尼流主导作用的假设，为控制凝固材料中气泡的分布提供了新的物理框架。

Abstract: Directional solidification of bubbly liquids plays a critical role in shaping the microstructure and properties of many materials, yet the fluid dynamics governing bubble behavior during solidification remain poorly understood. Using cryo-confocal microscopy and particle image velocimetry, we quantify fluid flows around bubbles during solidification of water containing surfactants and tracers. Our results reveal that volumetric expansion dominates fluid motion, with velocities scaling linearly with the solidification rate (1-20$~μm/s$), while Marangoni flows-hypothesized to play a key role-are negligible ($< 5~μm/s$) under our experimental conditions. Diffusiophoresis and thermophoresis also contribute minimally. These findings challenge existing theoretical models and provide a framework for controlling bubble distribution in solidified materials

### [162] [Tracking microscopic irreversibility during yielding of a colloidal fractal gel with Rheo-Echo-XPCS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13484)
*William Chèvremont,Julien Bauland,Emmeline Brassac,Gonzalo Sanchez Vera,Stefano Aime,Frédéric Pignon,Thomas Gibaud*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过引入流变回波X射线光子相关光谱（rheo-echo-XPCS）技术，在振荡剪切同步非线性采集条件下直接测量了碳黑胶体分形凝胶在屈服过程中的不可逆纳米尺度动力学，发现去相关速度与损耗正切呈线性标度关系，并观察到从压缩指数到拉伸指数的连续演化，揭示了网络碎裂过程中应力传递从体相到准一维丝状骨架的维度约化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解软物质屈服过程中微观结构动力学与宏观力学响应之间的关联是软物质物理（soft matter physics）的一个核心挑战。

Method: 作者引入流变回波X射线光子相关光谱（rheo-echo-XPCS）技术，采用与振荡剪切同步的非线性采集方式，在应变幅度控制下直接测量不可逆纳米尺度动力学；并将其应用于碳黑胶体分形凝胶（carbon black colloidal fractal gel）体系，通过分析涡度方向强度自关联函数中的时间周期回波来解析非仿射结构重排。

Result: 实验发现两个关键结果：(i) 在所有应变下均存在弹道式的去相关行为，满足τ∝q⁻¹标度关系，其中去相关速度v_τ=1/⟨qτ⟩与损耗正切（loss tangent）tanδ=G''/G'呈线性标度，确立了tanδ作为不可逆结构去相关速率的直接宏观表征；(ii) 函数形式从低应变下的压缩指数（compressed exponential, α≃1.5）连续演化为高应变下的拉伸指数（stretched exponential, α≃0.5），对应网络碎裂过程中应力传递从三维体相到准一维丝状骨架的维度约化（d_f从3降至1）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了宏观损耗正切与微观不可逆结构重排速率之间的直接定量联系，并揭示了屈服过程中应力传导路径的维度约化机制，为理解软物质屈服行为的微观起源提供了新的实验视角。

Abstract: Understanding how microscopic structural dynamics relate to macroscopic mechanical response during yielding remains a central challenge in soft matter physics. Here, we introduce rheo-echo X-ray photon correlation spectroscopy (rheo-echo-XPCS) with nonlinear acquisition synchronized to oscillatory shear, enabling direct measurement of irreversible nanoscale dynamics under strain amplitude control. Applying this to a carbon black colloidal fractal gel, we resolve time-periodic echoes in the vorticity-direction intensity autocorrelation function whose decay encodes non-affine structural rearrangements. We find: (i)~ballistic-like decorrelation with $τ\propto q^{-1}$ at all strains, where the decorrelation velocity $v_τ= 1/\langle qτ\rangle$ scales linearly with the loss tangent $\tanδ= G''/G'$, establishing $\tanδ$ as a direct macroscopic signature of the rate of irreversible structural decorrelation; (ii)~functional form continuous evolution from compressed exponential ($α\simeq 1.5$) at low strain, consistent with three-dimensional dipolar strain fields in the intact network-to stretched exponential ($α\simeq 0.5$) at high strain, reflecting a dimensional reduction from $d_f = 3$ to $d_f = 1$ as stress transmission shifts from bulk to quasi-one-dimensional filamentary backbones during network fragmentation.

### [163] [Limits of constant-parameter constitutive models for hydrogels under inertial cavitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13584)
*Tianyi Chu,Joseph Beckett,Zhiren Zhu,Jonathan B. Estrada,Spencer H. Bryngelson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于时间分辨参数估计的惯性微空化流变学（IMR）改进方法，通过移动重叠窗口上的迭代集合平滑器（MIEnKS-MDA）来识别恒定参数本构模型在空化过程中的失效时刻，并揭示聚丙烯酰胺水凝胶和明胶在不同温度和交联剂浓度下的剪切模量与粘度的时间演化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软材料在高应变率下的力学表征因高柔顺性、非线性黏弹性（nonlinear viscoelastic behavior）及历史依赖性响应而极具挑战。现有的惯性微空化流变学（inertial microcavitation rheometry, IMR）及其变体依赖于拟合窗口的选择，暗示恒定参数的本构模型不足以描述完整的空化（cavitation）事件，因此需要更精细的时间分辨方法。

Method: 利用改进的迭代集合平滑器与多重数据同化（modified iterative ensemble Kalman smoother with multiple data assimilation, MIEnKS-MDA），在移动重叠窗口上对neo-Hookean Kelvin–Voigt (NHKV) 本构模型中的参数进行时间分辨估计，分析窗口依赖性以识别恒定参数假设失效的时刻。

Result: 在聚丙烯酰胺（polyacrylamide, PAAm）水凝胶中，推断的剪切模量（shear modulus）和黏度（viscosity）随时间先下降后趋于平稳，且温度敏感性较弱。在明胶（gelatin）凝胶中，参数演化表现出显著的温度依赖性，低温和高温下呈现不同趋势；前两次气泡塌缩过程中，表观剪切模量和黏度均出现显著变化。

Conclusion: 在预设的NHKV本构结构内进行时间分辨参数估计，能够诊断恒定参数模型在空化过程中的不足，从而为发展更优的基于物理学的复杂气泡-材料相互作用模型提供指导。

Abstract: Mechanical characterization of soft materials at high strain rates is challenging due to their high compliance, nonlinear viscoelastic behavior, and potentially history-dependent responses. Inertial microcavitation rheometry (IMR) addresses this challenge by coupling laser-induced cavitation (LIC) experiments with numerical simulations of bubble dynamics models to infer constitutive models and material parameters. Both IMR and its variants infer parameters that depend on the chosen fitting window, which suggests that a constant-parameter constitutive model is insufficient to describe the full cavitation event. We use this window dependence to identify when the constant-parameter assumption fails, rather than to report a single effective parameter set. The constitutive parameters are estimated over moving, overlapping windows using a modified iterative ensemble Kalman smoother with multiple data assimilation (MIEnKS-MDA). Within the neo-Hookean Kelvin--Voigt (NHKV) constitutive model, we obtain time-resolved estimates of the constitutive response in polyacrylamide (PAAm) hydrogels with different crosslinker concentrations. The inferred shear modulus and viscosity generally decrease and then plateau during cavitation, while exhibiting relatively weak temperature sensitivity. For gelatin gels, by contrast, the inferred property evolution shows a pronounced temperature dependence, with distinct trends at low and high temperatures. Moreover, both the apparent shear modulus and viscosity exhibit significant variations during the first two bubble collapses. These results show that time-resolved parameter estimation within the prescribed NHKV constitutive structure can diagnose where the constant-parameter model assumption falls short during cavitation, thereby guiding the development of improved physics-based models of complex bubble--material interactions.

</details>


### [164] [Exploratory digital alchemy for colloidal crystal discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13586)
*Shih-Kuang,Lee,Sun-Ting Tsai,Sharon C. Glotzer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出探索性数字炼金术（Exploratory Digital Alchemy, EDA），一种基于统计力学（statistical mechanics）的正向设计（forward design）方法，通过融合数字炼金术（Digital Alchemy, DA）与元动力学（metadynamics, MetaD），释放对目标晶体的先验约束，实现对新型胶体粒子设计的自由能景观探索。在二维Lennard-Jones Gauss势（LJGP）和三维振荡对势（oscillating pair potential, OPP）体系中的实验表明，EDA能够成功识别稳定亚稳态Frank-Kasper相的势参数范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数字炼金术（DA）作为一种逆向设计（inverse design）方法，要求目标结构已知（a priori），其最优设计无法保证目标结构是最稳定或唯一稳定的结构，这限制了其在探索未知新型胶体设计中的适用性。因此，需要一种正向设计（forward design）方法来克服这一局限。

Method: 本文提出了探索性数字炼金术（EDA），其核心思路是：首先释放DA中对目标晶体的先验约束，然后引入基于元动力学（metadynamics, MetaD）的探索导向偏差（exploration-oriented bias），从而在广义系综（generalized ensemble）中对自由能景观进行探索。

Result: 在二维LJGP体系中，EDA能够分析不同温度下不同势参数对应的自由能景观。在三维OPP体系中，EDA成功识别出一系列能够稳定亚稳态Frank-Kasper相（metastable Frank-Kasper phases）的势参数范围。

Conclusion: EDA融合了标准DA框架与元动力学，为研究广义系综中的炼金术反应（alchemical reactions）提供了潜在工具，并为优化新型胶体设计提供了更加适用的正向探索方案。

Abstract: Digital Alchemy (DA), introduced by Van Anders et al., is a statistical mechanics-based generalized thermodynamic ensemble method that employs computer simulations to optimize colloidal particle design. This approach applies the principles of statistical mechanics to predict and tailor particle attributes that lead to desired self-assembled structures or material properties. However, as an inverse design method, its main limitation is that the target structure must be known \textit{a priori}. Therefore, the optimal design from DA does not guarantee the targeted structure is the most or the only stable one. This highlights the importance of forward design with an exploratory scheme for optimizing novel colloid designs, which becomes more suitable in such cases. In this paper, we introduce Exploratory Digital Alchemy (EDA), an enhanced forward design scheme that begins by releasing the constraint of the target crystal from DA, followed by an exploration-oriented bias that has been extensively used in enhanced sampling methods such as metadynamics (MetaD). We demonstrate the utility of EDA through examples involving particles interacting via a two-dimensional Lennard-Jones Gauss potential (LJGP) and a three-dimensional oscillating pair potential (OPP). We applied EDA to study the free energy landscapes given different potential parameters of LJGP at different temperatures. With the exploratory scheme, we've also successfully identified a wide range of OPP potential parameters that stabilize metastable Frank-Kasper phases. Our approach fuses the standard DA framework with metadynamics, which could potentially be useful for studying alchemical reactions in a generalized ensemble.

</details>


### [165] [Geometric formulation of state-dependent Langevin dynamics using scalar free energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13617)
*Kento Yasuda,Zhongqiang Xiong,Zhanglin Hou,Kenta Ishimoto,Xinpeng Xu,Shigeyuki Komura*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过引入标量自由能并将扩散张量作为位形空间的度量，构建了一种几何一致的朗之万方程，显式地处理了状态依赖扩散中的坐标协变性，并将虚假漂移表达为扩散度量的克里斯托费尔贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统朗之万方程（Langevin equation）在状态依赖扩散中存在虚假漂移（spurious drift），其自由能通常不按标量变换，导致协方差（covariance）不显式，需要一种几何上自洽的公式化表述。

Method: 引入标量自由能（scalar free energy），将扩散张量（diffusion tensor）作为位形空间（configuration space）的度量（metric），从而构建几何一致的朗之万方程；虚假漂移被表达为扩散度量的克里斯托费尔贡献（Christoffel contribution）。

Result: 该几何公式化与通过非标量与标量自由能之间关系得到的传统公式等价，但显式地体现了坐标协变性（coordinate covariance）；在坐标变换、几何约束以及从曲面向平坦空间投影等代表性例子中验证了一致性。

Conclusion: 所提出的几何方法为状态依赖扩散提供了一种协变显式的朗之万方程表述，在约束布朗运动和各向异性系统等场景中具有理论一致性与应用价值。

Abstract: Stochastic dynamics with state-dependent diffusion are widely used for Brownian motion in confined, anisotropic, and hydrodynamically coupled systems. The conventional Langevin formulation includes a spurious drift associated with multiplicative noise, but its free energy generally does not transform as a scalar, meaning that the covariance is not explicit. Here, we formulate a geometrically consistent Langevin equation by introducing a scalar free energy and using the diffusion tensor as a metric on configuration space. The spurious drift is then expressed as a Christoffel contribution of the diffusion metric. While our formulation is equivalent to the conventional one through the relation between the non-scalar and scalar free energies, it makes the coordinate covariance explicit. We demonstrate its consistency in representative examples of state-dependent diffusion arising from coordinate transformations, geometrical confinement, and projection from curved to flat spaces.

</details>

### [166] [Infinite-Order Lattice Chiral Anomalies and CPT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12510)
*Elijah Lew-Smith,Salvatore D. Pace,Shu-Heng Shao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在1+1维无质量狄拉克费米子的晶格实现中，Onsager对称性具有二阶反常；但引入晶格CPT对称性后，该反常增强为无限阶，从而更忠实地匹配了连续统中的手征反常（chiral anomaly）。论文还讨论了对应的2+1维对称性保护拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全局对称性反常（anomaly）的一个关键属性是其"阶"（order），即$n$个副本系统的对角对称性无反常所需的最小整数$n$。许多晶格反常具有有限阶，而连续统中的微扰反常（perturbative anomaly）——由费曼图（Feynman diagrams）捕获——具有无限阶。本文旨在研究晶格上手征对称性（chiral symmetry）的反常阶结构，并探讨如何通过晶格CPT对称性使其更接近连续统手征反常。

Method: 论文以1+1维无质量狄拉克费米子（massless Dirac fermion）的晶格实现为背景，分析Onsager对称性（手征对称性的晶格版本）的反常阶。通过引入晶格CPT对称性，观察其对反常阶的增强效应，并与连续统手征反常进行对比。此外，论文还讨论了2+1维对称性保护拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases, SPT phases）与这些无限阶晶格反常之间的对应关系。

Result: Onsager对称性在晶格上具有二阶反常（order-two anomaly）。当施加晶格CPT对称性时，反常从二阶增强为无限阶，从而在晶格上重现了与连续统手征反常一致的反常结构。

Conclusion: 晶格CPT对称性能够将Onsager对称性的反常从有限阶提升为无限阶，使晶格手征对称性更忠实地模拟连续统中的手征反常。这一发现揭示了晶格反常与连续统反常之间的深层联系，并通过2+1维SPT相为无限阶晶格反常提供了拓扑物理实现。

Abstract: A key property of a global symmetry's anomaly is its order: the smallest integer $n$ for which the diagonal symmetry of the $n$-copy system is anomaly-free. While many familiar lattice anomalies have finite order, perturbative anomalies in the continuum$-$those captured by Feynman diagrams$-$have infinite order. In this paper, we show that the Onsager symmetry, a lattice realization of the chiral symmetry of a 1+1d massless Dirac fermion, has an order-two anomaly. However, imposing lattice CPT symmetry enhances this anomaly from order two to infinite order, yielding a lattice chiral symmetry structure that more faithfully matches the continuum chiral anomaly. We also discuss the corresponding 2+1d symmetry-protected topological phases for these infinite-order lattice anomalies.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将轴子畴壁耦合的麦克斯韦理论建模为谱边界值问题；通过分析手性依赖的耦合机制——轴子梯度（axion gradient）引发不同极化（polarization）的光子感受不同的有效势（effective potential），从而形成束缚态或受到排斥。

Result: 有限宽度的轴子畴壁普遍支持一种局域化、可归一化、具有线性无隙色散的手征电磁模式。该模式源于轴子梯度引起的手性依赖耦合：一种极化感受吸引势并形成束缚态，另一种极化受到排斥。该模式在广泛的畴壁结构和轴子质量范围内均鲁棒存在。

Conclusion: 轴子畴壁普遍支撑一种此前被忽视的局域手征表面光子模式。这一发现可能对相关凝聚态或宇宙学系统中的手征现象（chiral phenomena）产生重要影响。

Abstract: We analyze Maxwell theory coupled to an axion domain wall as a spectral boundary value problem. We find that a finite-width axion domain wall generically supports a localized normalizable chiral electromagnetic mode with linear, gapless dispersion. This mode arises from helicity-dependent coupling sourced by the axion gradient: one polarization experiences an effective attractive potential and forms a bound state, while the opposite polarization is repelled. The existence of this chiral surface photon is robust over a wide regime of wall structures and axion masses. Our result shows that axion domain walls generically support a localized chiral photon that has been missed in previous analyses.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立局域零超曲面截断的相空间与渐近平坦引力红外相空间之间的精确对应关系，从而将红外软引力子模与零曲面几何量联系起来。

Method: 通过对闵可夫斯基时空中零超曲面的任意截断构造相空间，并利用辛几何（symplectic geometry）方法证明其与渐近平坦引力红外相空间的辛同构关系；具体通过将截断涨落映射为领头软引力子模，将超平移戈德斯通模映射为截断尺寸与其辛伴侣（零时间偏移）的乘积来实现对应。

Result: 成功建立了零曲面截断相空间与渐近平坦引力红外相空间之间的辛同构；截断涨落与领头软引力子模精确对应；超平移戈德斯通模等于截断尺寸与其辛伴侣（零时间偏移）的乘积。

Conclusion: 零超曲面截断的几何自由度编码了渐近平坦引力的红外结构，为理解软引力子与局部几何量之间的深层联系提供了严格框架。

Abstract: We construct the phase space for an arbitrary cut of a null hypersurface in Minkowski spacetime and demonstrate that it is symplectomorphic to the infrared phase space of asymptotically flat gravity. Fluctuations of the cut are mapped to the leading soft graviton mode. Furthermore, the supertranslation Goldstone mode is mapped to the product of the size of the cut with its symplectic partner, the null time offset.

### [169] [Multi-entropy in heavy local quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12526)
*Kosei Fujiki,Kenya Tasuki*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究二维全息共形场论（holographic CFT）中重局域淬火（heavy local quench）后三体纠缠的时间演化。采用真多熵（genuine multi-entropy）作为诊断量，通过微扰和完全反冲几何两种方法分析发现：真多熵受全局鞍点选择（global saddle selection）控制，而非局域能量响应或准粒子传播；其时间依赖由时间和有理函数的对数确定，与重算符维度无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子多体系统中纠缠结构在非平衡动力学中的演化机制，特别是三体及以上纠缠（tripartite entanglement）在局域淬火后的行为，以弥补以往多集中于两体纠缠研究的不足。

Method: 从体（bulk）和边界（boundary）两种视角计算相邻区间的真多熵。体一侧采用微扰分析和完全反冲几何（fully back-reacted geometry）两种方法；边界一侧采用重光真空块近似（heavy-light vacuum block approximation）。

Result: 微扰分析表明，真空测地线网络（geodesic network）上的一阶小质量扰动在淬火后任意时刻恒为零。在完全反冲几何中，真多熵源于三重测地线网络选择的缠绕数与成对测地线独立选择的缠绕数之间的失配。在尖锐淬火极限下，真多熵的时间依赖由时间和有理函数的对数动力学固定，且与重算符维度无关。

Conclusion: 在该设定下，真多熵由全局鞍点选择（global saddle selection）主导，而非局域能量响应或准粒子传播机制。CFT计算在重光真空块近似下重现了相同的公式，其中重背景均匀化映射（uniformization map）中的分支选择对应体中的缠绕数选择。

Abstract: We study the time evolution of tripartite entanglement in heavy local quenches in two-dimensional holographic conformal field theories. Our diagnostic is the genuine multi-entropy of adjacent intervals, computed from both bulk and boundary perspectives. A perturbative bulk analysis shows that the first-order small-mass perturbation around the vacuum geodesic network cancels identically at any time after the quench. In the fully back-reacted geometry, a vacuum-subtracted genuine multi-entropy arises from a mismatch between the winding selected by the trivalent geodesic network and the windings selected independently by the pairwise geodesics. In the sharp quench limit, the time dependence of genuine multi-entropy is kinematically fixed to logarithms of rational functions of time and is independent of the heavy operator dimension. The CFT calculation reproduces the same formula within the heavy-light vacuum block approximation, where the branch choice in the heavy-background uniformization map corresponds to the winding selection in the bulk. These results indicate that, in this setup, the genuine multi-entropy is controlled by global saddle selection, rather than by a local energy response or quasiparticle propagation.

### [170] [How traversable is a traversable wormhole?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12528)
*Ben Freivogel,Alessandro Fumagalli,Marija Tomašević*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了Maldacena-Milekhin-Popov四维可穿越虫洞中的低频散射，发现标量探针在低频下传输被抑制，但存在共振完全透射；而带电无质量费米子在低能量下以接近单位概率穿越虫洞，揭示了与Callan-Rubakov效应的意外联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）在不同类型探针（probe）下的传输特性，以期理解虫洞穿越性的决定因素及其与黑洞物理之间的深层联系。

Method: 基于Maldacena-Milekhin-Popov提出的四维可穿越虫洞模型，对低频散射过程进行解析计算，得到标量探针（中性及带电）和带电无质量费米子的传输概率（transmission probability）。

Result: 标量探针的穿越强烈依赖于时间尺度：在信号发出后约光穿越时间尺度上传输被参数抑制，大部分信号被反射或暂时困于虫洞喉部；随后被困信号逐步泄漏，最终累积传输截面（transmission cross-section）趋近对应黑洞吸收截面（absorption cross-section）的一半。尽管低频传输普遍被抑制，传输谱中存在共振频率（resonant frequencies）实现完美透射。带电无质量费米子在低能量下以接近单位概率穿越虫洞，其高效吸收机制与Callan-Rubakov效应高度相似。

Conclusion: 标量探针最适合揭示这类磁虫洞（magnetic wormholes）的独特特征，而带电无质量费米子是穿越虫洞传递信息的理想载体。

Abstract: To answer the above question, we study low-frequency scattering in the four-dimensional traversable wormhole of Maldacena, Milekhin, and Popov. The resulting transmission probabilities reveal that wormhole traversability depends strongly on the nature of the probe. For scalar probes, both neutral and charged, traversability depends on the time scale. On time scales of order the light-crossing time after sending in a signal, the transmission is parametrically suppressed, with most of the incoming signal reflected or temporarily trapped inside the wormhole throat. As time progresses, the trapped signal gradually leaks out, so that at late times the accumulated transmission cross-section approaches one half of the corresponding black hole absorption cross-section. Despite this generic suppression at low frequencies, the transmission spectrum also exhibits resonant frequencies at which transmission becomes perfect. Charged massless fermions tell a very different story. Unlike scalars, they traverse the wormhole with essentially unit probability at low energies. The same mechanism underlies their efficient absorption by magnetic black holes and realizes a channel closely analogous to the Callan-Rubakov effect, revealing unexpected connections with monopole-fermion scattering. Putting everything together, we conclude that scalar probes are best suited for uncovering distinct features of these magnetic wormholes, while charged massless fermions are the ideal carriers of information through them.

</details>


### [171] [Analytic approaches to perturbations of strongly coupled Yang-Mills plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12529)
*Inês Aniceto,Paolo Arnaudo,Alex Ratcliffe,Michał Spaliński*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过量子塞伯格-威滕（Seiberg–Witten）周期与精确WKB分析，系统研究了AdS黑洞膜标量拟正规模（quasinormal modes）在全波数范围内的行为，克服了传统截断方法在大波数或高阶模下的收敛性局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在杨-米尔斯等离子体（Yang-Mills plasma）的扰动研究中，标量拟正规模作为波数的函数需要在从零到无穷的全范围内被理解。传统的经典谱方法（classical spectral methods）基于边界值问题的截断，在高波数或高模式数下会面临收敛性限制，因此需要更系统的分析工具来评估和控制这一截断的有效性。

Method: 本文首先指出，截断边界值问题在Nekrasov–Shatashvili极限下可自然地用量子塞伯格-威滕周期（quantum Seiberg–Witten periods）进行解析解释，谱条件被组织为计数参数小值的瞬子展开（instanton expansion）。随后，通过精确WKB分析（exact WKB analysis），以波数的倒数作为展开参数，导出以周期积分（period integrals）和斯托克斯几何（Stokes geometry）表达的精确量子化条件。

Result: 研究表明，当波数或模式数增大时，物理点会趋近于瞬子展开收敛域的边界，从而限制了截断方法的有效性。通过精确WKB分析获得的量子化条件同时包含了微扰和非微扰修正。重求和后的拟正规模在远超严格大波数区域仍保持精确，并可解析延拓至波数为零。

Conclusion: 精确WKB分析与塞伯格-威滕方法的结合，为全波数范围的拟正规模提供了自洽的描述框架，克服了传统截断方法的局限性，并建立了黑洞物理与可积系统（integrable systems）之间的深层联系。

Abstract: We study perturbations of Yang-Mills plasma, represented by scalar quasinormal modes of AdS black branes, as functions of the wave number $q$ in the entire range from zero to infinity. At finite $q$, these modes can be computed by classical spectral methods based on truncating the boundary value problem. We show that this truncation admits a natural analytic interpretation in terms of quantum Seiberg--Witten periods in the Nekrasov--Shatashvili limit, with the spectral condition organised as an instanton expansion around small values of the counting parameter. The physical black-brane problem corresponds to evaluating this series at a finite value of the counting parameter, and the Seiberg--Witten formulation provides a systematic way to analyse when the truncation is under control. In particular, it reveals that, as $q$ or the mode number $N$ increases, the physical point approaches the boundary of the domain of convergence of the instanton expansion, limiting the validity of the truncation approach. We overcome this limitation through an exact WKB analysis in which $q^{-1}$ acts as the expansion parameter. The resulting exact quantisation conditions, expressed in terms of period integrals and the associated Stokes geometry, incorporate both perturbative and non-perturbative corrections. The resummed quasinormal modes remain accurate far beyond the strict large-$q$ regime and can be analytically continued all the way to $q=0$, notably by using the Seiberg--Witten approach, providing a consistent description of the QNM spectrum.

</details>


### [172] [Fermion Families and Pontryagin Class: Topological Field Theory via Colour Symmetry Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26202)
*Zheyan Wan,Juven Wang,Shing-Tung Yau*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用拓扑约束下的反常（anomaly）分类与对称性扩张（symmetry extension）方法，论证了标准模型（SM）中恰好存在3族夸克与轻子（以及3种色自由度）的必然性。通过5d自旋配边群（spin bordism group）分类4d分立$Z_n$对称性下的费米子反常，证明仅群上调（group-cohomology）子类可被拓扑量子场论（TQFT）抵消，并构造了可替代3个右手中微子$\nu_R$的反常边界TQFT。进一步对广义SM的分析表明，$N_c=N_f=3$是唯一满足所有约束（包括重子为费米子）的最小正整数解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释标准模型中恰好存在3族夸克与轻子这一“家族谜题”（family puzzle），试图从拓扑约束与反常抵消的角度给出第一性原理的推导，而非唯象假设。

Method: 利用5d自旋配边群（5d spin bordism group）对4d离散$Z_n$对称性下的费米子反常（fermionic anomalies）进行分类，区分可被4d拓扑量子场论（TQFT）抵消的群上调（group-cohomology）子类$H^5(Z_n,U(1))\cong Z_n$与不可抵消的超越群上调（beyond-group-cohomology）部分$A_{Z_n} p_1$（除$n=2,3$外）。通过对称性扩张（symmetry extension）构造$Z_n\to Z_{n^2}\to Z_n$序列，证明奇数维上循环（cocycle）在该扩张下平凡化，并构建相应的反常边界TQFT。

Result: 构造了一个Spin$\times Z_3$-对称的4d $Z_3$-规范TQFT，在缺失3个右手中微子$\nu_R$的条件下抵消SM的$(\mathbf{B+L})$-规范-引力混合反常。对于广义SM($N_c$色, $N_f$族)，缺失的$N_f$个$\nu_R$可由该反异常TQFT替代。最小整数解为：$N_c=3, N_f\ge3$；$N_c=4, N_f\ge2$；$N_c=12, N_f\ge6$。当要求重子为费米子（$N_c$为奇数）时，$N_c=N_f=3$是唯一解。此外证明在mod 3上同调类中$A_{Z_3}p_1\equiv 0\mod3$。

Conclusion: 标准模型中3族夸克与轻子以及3种色自由度的出现并非偶然，而是由拓扑反常抵消与对称性扩张条件共同决定的必然结果。该工作为“家族谜题”提供了一个基于拓扑量子场论和反常分析的严格理论解释。

Abstract: Family puzzle asks why the Standard Model (SM) features exactly 3 families of quarks and leptons. Motivated by topological constraints, we study 4-dimensional fermionic anomalies with discrete $Z_n$ symmetry, classified by the 5d spin bordism group. We show that only the group-cohomology subclass H$^5(Z_n,U(1))\cong Z_n$ can be canceled by an anomalous $Z_n$-symmetric 4d $Z_n$-gauge topological quantum field theory (TQFT), while beyond-group-cohomology $A_{Z_n} p_1$ involving the Pontryagin class $p_1$ cannot (except $n=2,3$). More generally, we prove that any cocycle $α_d\in$H$^d(Z_n,U(1))$ in odd spacetime dimension $d\ge3$ is trivialised by the symmetry extension $1\to Z_n\to Z_{n^2}\to Z_n\to 1,$ and we construct the corresponding symmetric anomalous boundary TQFT. For $d=5$ and $n=3$, this yields a Spin$\times Z_3$-symmetric 4d $Z_3$-gauge TQFT that cancels the mixed discrete $(\bf B+L)$-gauge-gravitational anomaly of the SM in the absence of 3 "sterile" right-handed neutrinos $ν_R$. We further analyze a generalized SM with $N_c$ colors and $N_f$ families and argue that missing $N_f$ copies of the $ν_R$ can be naturally replaced by that 4d anomalous $Spin\times_{Z_2^F} Z_{2 N_f,{{\bf B} + {\bf L}}}$ symmetric $Z_{N_c}$-gauge TQFT under the anomaly cancellation, via an appropriate $Z_{N_c}$-color symmetry extension construction $1\to Z_{N_c}\to Spin\times Z_{N_cN_f}\to Spin\times_{Z_2^F} Z_{2N_f}\to1$ of anomalous topological order. For minimal nonzero positive integers $N_c$ and $N_f$, we find the minimal color extensions: $N_c=3, N_f \ge 3$; $N_c=4, N_f \ge 2$; and $N_c=12, N_f \ge 6$. If we further require that an SM baryon is a fermion so $N_c$ is odd, then $Z_{N_c}=Z($SU$(N_c))$ color center, we prove 3 families and 3 colors, $N_c=N_f=3$, is the unique case that stands out. We also prove that $A_{Z_3}p_1= 0\mod3$ for the mod 3 cohomology class in an appropriate context.

### [174] [Wigner continuous-spin equations in $\mathbf{AdS_D}$: bosonic and fermionic cases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12537)
*Lev N. Astrakhantsev,Anastasia A. Golubtsova,Mikhail A. Podoinitsyn*

TL;DR: 该论文在任意维反德西特空间（anti-de Sitter space, AdS）中，为玻色和费米连续自旋场（continuous-spin fields）构造了类Wigner运动方程（Wigner-like equations of motion）。通过协变化普通导数并变形约束以形成闭合代数，在度规-类形式论（metric-like formalism）中得到了定义so(2,D-1)等距代数表示的一类一阶约束系统。利用这些约束计算了二次和四次卡西米尔算符（Casimir operators）的本征值，并与Metsaev的分类进行了对比。关键代数角色由洛伦兹子代数so(1,D-1)的Howe对偶（super）代数的特殊算符——玻色情况下的sl(2)卡西米尔算符和费米情况下的osp(1|2)超代数卡西米尔鬼算符（Casimir's ghost）——所扮演。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典平直空间中的连续自旋场Wigner约束推广到弯曲的AdS背景，并同时处理玻色和费米两种情况，以统一描述连续自旋场的动力学。

Method: 采用度规-类形式论（metric-like formalism），通过协变化普通导数和变形约束条件使约束构成闭合代数，构造定义so(2,D-1)等距代数表示的类Wigner运动方程；利用李-洛伦兹导数（Lie-Lorentz derivative）实现约束，并运用Howe对偶（Howe duality）代数（玻色：sl(2)，费米：osp(1|2)）的算符来组织约束代数。

Result: 成功构造了AdS空间中玻色和费米连续自旋场的类Wigner运动方程及相应的一阶约束系统；计算了二次和四次卡西米尔算符的本征值，并与Metsaev的连续自旋表示分类进行了比较。

Conclusion: Howe对偶代数（sl(2)和osp(1|2)）的特殊算符在组织约束代数及其一致性中起着关键作用，所构造的约束系统为AdS空间连续自旋场提供了规范理论基础。

Abstract: We construct Wigner-like equations of motion for symmetric continuous-spin fields in anti-de Sitter space of arbitrary dimension, treating both the bosonic and fermionic cases. We generalise the classical flat-space Wigner constraints for bosonic continuous-spin fields, and for the fermionic case we adopt the equations proposed by Bekaert and Mourad as our starting point. This is achieved by covariantising the ordinary derivatives and deforming the resulting constraints so that they form a closed algebra. The construction is carried out in a metric-like formalism and yields a system of first-class constraints that define a representation of the $\mathfrak{so}(2,D-1)$ isometry algebra, realised via the Lie-Lorentz derivative. Using these constraints, we compute the eigenvalues of the quadratic and quartic Casimir operators and compare the obtained values with Metsaev's classification of continuous-spin representations for both the bosonic and fermionic cases. A crucial algebraic role is played by special operators of the (super)algebra Howe-dual to the Lorentz subalgebra $\mathfrak{so}(1,D-1)$: the $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$ Casimir operator in the bosonic case, and the Casimir's ghost of the $\mathfrak{osp}(1|2)$ superalgebra in the fermionic case. Both objects naturally organise the constraint algebra and ensure its consistency.

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种在固定希尔伯特空间（fixed Hilbert space）中自动改善有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）的途径。

Abstract: Given a quantum critical wavefunction in any dimension, we propose a reconstructed Hamiltonian, analogous to the ones previously found for 1+1d CFT and for 2+1d bosonic liquid topologically-ordered states. We test numerically that, for known regularized approximate CFT groundstates (on the icosahedron and the fuzzy sphere), (1) they are close to the groundstate of their reconstructed Hamiltonian, and (2) the spectrum of their reconstructed Hamiltonian on the unit sphere has CFT properties (integer spacing of descendants) and matches known low-lying energies. ### [176] [Vacuum photon emission and mean electromagnetic field in pair-creating external backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12547)
*I. A. Aleksandrov,E. V. Perelygin,D. V. Chubukov*

Method: 采用Keldysh-Schwinger-Fradkin非平衡技术（nonequilibrium technique）进行实时微扰描述；同时基于in-Fock空间中单位算符的谱分解（spectral decomposition of the identity operator）给出独立推导，其中真空不连通项通过广义光学定理（optical theorem）消去。

Result: 导出了通过精细结构常数（fine-structure constant）第二非零阶的光子平均数密度：领头阶（order α）复现了已知的顶点（vertex）和蝌蚪（tadpole）机制，完整的α²阶修正包含干涉（interference）、圈（loop）和感应电流（induced-current）贡献；还计算了通过e³阶的平均电磁场（mean electromagnetic field），包括感应真空电流（induced vacuum current）的电磁 dressing，并通过Schwinger-Dyson方程验证。

Abstract: We develop a perturbative description of vacuum radiative processes in quantum electrodynamics with a prescribed external electromagnetic background capable of producing electron-positron pairs. Since the initial vacuum is then unstable and the in- and out-vacua are inequivalent, radiative observables require a real-time formulation beyond the ordinary in-out approach of vacuum-stable QED. Using the Keldysh-Schwinger-Fradkin nonequilibrium technique, we derive the mean number density of emitted photons through the second nonvanishing order in the fine-structure constant. In addition, we compute the mean electromagnetic field through order $e^3$, including the electromagnetic dressing of the induced vacuum current, and verify it using the corresponding Schwinger-Dyson equations. The final formulas are expressed in terms of exact solutions and propagators of the Dirac equation in the external background and apply to general spacetime-dependent field configurations.

### [177] [Tachyonic Encore: A universal shift of inflationary observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12549)
*Diogo S. Gorgulho,Margherita Putti,Rodrigo Gonzalez Quaglia,Ema Dimastrogiovanni,Matteo Fasiello,Diederik Roest*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种与暴胀子势能形式（inflaton-potential）基本无关的普适机制：一个轻轴子（axion）伴子，初始位于势能山顶（hilltop）附近，通过纯引力的多场动力学（multi-field dynamics）重塑暴胀可观测量。暴胀结束后轴子开始滚动，诱发等曲率模（isocurvature mode）的瞬时效应（tachyonic phases），在超视界尺度上产生近乎尺度不变的曲率功率谱（curvature power spectrum）增强，从而压低张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）并改变标量谱倾斜（scalar tilt）。这些效应能使原本被CMB观测排除的暴胀子势能与数据相符，并预言可被未来巡天检验的局域非高斯性（local non-Gaussianity）$f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc.}\sim \mathcal{O}(1)$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CMB观测对暴胀模型施加了严格约束，许多原本合理的暴胀子势能（inflaton potential）因预言过高的张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）或错误的标量谱倾斜（scalar tilt）而被排除。作者试图寻找一种不依赖暴胀子势能具体形式的普适机制，通过引入额外的轻自由度（axion spectator），在不修改暴胀子势能本身的情况下，使被排除的势能重新与观测一致。

Method: 作者考虑一个轻轴子（axion）作为伴子场（spectator），初始位于其势能的山顶（hilltop）。暴胀期间轴子被冻结，系统表现为有效单场（effectively single-field）背景轨迹。暴胀结束后轴子开始滚动，引发场空间（field space）中的转向（turn），导致等曲率模（isocurvature mode）出现瞬时的快速振荡（tachyonic phases）。这一“加速再奏”（tachyonic encore）完全发生在超视界（super-horizon）尺度上，通过纯引力多场动力学（purely gravitational multi-field dynamics）影响可观测量。

Result: 该机制产生近乎尺度不变的曲率功率谱（curvature power spectrum）增强，压低张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio），并将标量谱倾斜（scalar tilt）偏移为暴胀子与轴子各自的绝热与熵倾斜（adiabatic and entropic tilts）在视界穿越（horizon crossing）时的加权组合。这些效应能使原本被CMB数据排除的暴胀子势能重新与观测相符。同时该机制预言局域非高斯性（local non-Gaussianity）$f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc.}\sim \mathcal{O}(1)$，处于未来巡天的可探测范围内。

Conclusion: 作者提出了一种与暴胀子势能（inflaton-potential）形式无关的轻轴子伴子机制，通过暴胀后的超视界动力学（super-horizon dynamics）调控CMB可观测量，能够有效调和部分暴胀子势能与CMB观测之间的矛盾。该机制还给出了可被未来巡天检验的非高斯性信号（non-Gaussianity）预言，为探测多场暴胀（multi-field inflation）提供了观测途径。

Abstract: We propose a generic, largely inflaton-potential-independent mechanism in which a light axion spectator, initialized near the hilltop of its potential, reshapes inflationary observables through purely gravitational multi-field dynamics. During inflation the axion is frozen and the background follows an effectively single-field trajectory. After inflation ends, the axion rolls, inducing a turn in field space and transient tachyonic phases of the isocurvature mode. The resulting ``tachyonic encore'' occurs entirely on super-horizon scales. These phases generate a nearly scale-invariant enhancement of the curvature power spectrum, suppressing the tensor-to-scalar ratio and shifting the scalar tilt to a weighted combination of adiabatic and entropic tilts at horizon crossing. We show that these effects can reconcile otherwise disfavored inflaton potentials with current CMB constraints. The same dynamics predict local non-Gaussianity, $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc.}\sim \mathcal{O}(1)$, within reach of upcoming surveys.

### [178] [The state/defect correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12560)
*Adrien Arbalestrier,Elise Paznokas,Stathis Vitouladitis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了任意维度高阶规范理论（higher-form gauge theories）中态与缺陷之间的一一对应关系。该对应不依赖于共形不变性（conformal invariance），而是基于电性与磁性高阶对称性（higher-form symmetries）的混合反常（mixed anomaly）所关联的无穷多守恒荷。在p-形式麦克斯韦理论（p-form Maxwell theory）中，这些荷生成一个扩展的Kac-Moody代数，同时作用在态和扩展算符上，从而将S^p × S^{d-p-1}上的希尔伯特空间组织成最高权表示（highest-weight representations），实现态与p维缺陷的直接等同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高阶规范理论中态与缺陷之间的内在联系，并建立不依赖共形对称性（conformal symmetry）的普适性对应框架。

Method: 基于电性和磁性高阶对称性之间的混合反常推导出无穷多守恒荷，这些荷生成扩展的Kac-Moody代数，利用该代数将S^p × S^{d-p-1}上的希尔伯特空间组织成最高权表示，从而实现态与p维缺陷的直接对应。

Result: 在p-形式麦克斯韦理论中，态与p维缺陷（例如由局域规范不变算符修饰的Wilson-'t Hooft缺陷）存在一一对应关系，其中缺陷被映射为挤压能量本征态（squeezed energy eigenstates）。该构造在非线性电动力学（non-linear electrodynamics）的一类相互作用理论中仍然成立，并进一步关联到高自旋流（higher-spin currents）。

Conclusion: 高阶规范理论中存在一种普适的态-缺陷对应关系，其根源在于高阶对称性之间的混合反常所生成的无穷维对称代数，且该对应超越共形场论范畴，可推广至一类相互作用理论。

Abstract: We formulate a one-to-one correspondence between states and defects for higher-form gauge theories in arbitrary dimensions. The correspondence is not predicated on conformal invariance, as these theories are in general not conformal. Instead, it relies on the existence of infinitely many conserved charges associated with the mixed anomaly of electric and magnetic higher-form symmetries. In $p$-form Maxwell theory, these charges generate an extended Kac-Moody algebra that acts simultaneously on states and on extended operators. We show that this algebra organizes the Hilbert space on $S^p \times S^{d-p-1}$ into highest-weight representations allowing for a direct identification between states and $p$-dimensional defects. In particular, Wilson-'t Hooft defects dressed with local gauge-invariant operators are mapped to squeezed energy eigenstates. We further relate these novel symmetries to higher-spin currents and demonstrate that their construction persists in a class of interacting non-linear electrodynamics theories.

</details>

### [180] [The $μ$-extension of iterated integrals and nested sums](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12584)
*J. Blümlein,A. M. Gavrilik,U. Y. Lunga,O. Mykhailiv*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了量子场论微扰计算中单尺度费曼图积分解析积分的μ-扩展方法，分析了不同字母表（polylogarithms、Nielsen integrals、cyclotomic letters等）对应的迭代积分与嵌套和的结构，指出除平方根字母表外，μ-扩展保持在同一函数空间的多项式形式及Hopf代数结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论（quantum field theory）微扰计算中的单尺度费曼积分（single-scale Feynman integrals）需要系统化的解析积分方法，而现有的特殊函数类（如polylogarithm推广族）的μ-扩展性质尚未被完整刻画。

Method: 通过分析Kummer-Poincaré迭代积分（iterated integrals）在多种字母表（cyclotomic letters、二次型字母、平方根字母等）上的结构，构造其μ-扩展及关联嵌套和；对于较复杂情形给出封闭解或算法，并研究μ-扩展函数空间的代数性质。

Result: 除平方根字母表（square-root valued alphabets）外，μ-扩展映射到同一函数空间且为μ的多项式形式；对于含中心二项式系数（central binomials）的嵌套和或平方根字母表，μ-扩展导致更高阶超越函数（higher transcendental functions）。在所有其他情形下，μ-扩展通过将μ补充到基域（ground field），保持了由（拟）shuffle积（(quasi)shuffle product）蕴含的Hopf代数结构（Hopf algebra structure）。

Conclusion: 论文建立了费曼积分μ-扩展的系统框架，揭示了不同字母表下函数空间行为的分类：大部分情形保持多项式扩展和代数结构，仅平方根字母表等特殊情形需要更高阶超越函数。

Abstract: The analytic integration of single-scale Feynman integrals emerging in perturbative calculations in quantum field theories can be performed within special classes of functions, which appear as consecutive generalizations of the polylogarithm in form of Kummer-Poincaré iterative integrals over special alphabets and extensions thereof. These are the polylogarithms, Nielsen integrals, the iterated integrals over linear denominator terms, cyclotomic letters, letters induced by quadratic forms, and square-root valued letters. These integrals are solutions of first-order factorizing differential equations. They are related to specific nested sums via the Mellin transform and their expansions around $x=0$. We construct the $μ$-extensions of these iterated integrals and the associated nested sums. We present closed form solutions or provide algorithms in the case of more involved cases to derive the respective $μ$-extensions and study the algebras of the $μ$-extended function spaces. Except for the case of square-root valued alphabets, the $μ$-extension maps into the same function space polynomially in $μ$. This is also the case for the associated nested sums. For square-root valued alphabets or sums containing central binomials, the $μ$-extension leads to higher transcendental functions. In all other cases the $μ$-extension preserves the Hopf algebra structure implied by the (quasi)shuffle product, by supplementing $μ$ to the ground field.

</details>


### [181] [Analytic structure of the QCD phase diagram in the complex-temperature plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12622)
*Gokce Basar,Vladimir V. Skokov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将温度视为复变量，研究了QCD相图的解析结构。结合普适临界标度、第一性原理格点QCD提取和有效模型三个视角，分析了复温度平面中的杨-李边奇点（Yang-Lee edge singularities），并论证了复温度与复化学势奇点轨迹受相同标度变量控制，可用于检验临界点搜索和约束临界标度区域。最后通过迭代共形Padé方法从格点QCD数据中提取了连续极限下的复温度奇点位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子色动力学（QCD）相图的解析结构是理解强相互作用物质在高温、高密度下行为的核心问题。以往研究主要关注复化学势平面中的奇点，对复温度平面中奇点的角色认识不足。本文旨在系统研究QCD相图在复温度平面中的解析结构，特别是杨-李边奇点如何界定热力学可观测量温度依赖性的解析区域，并与复化学势方法互补。

Method: 本文采用三种互补视角：第一，基于普适临界标度理论（universal critical scaling）分析奇点行为；第二，从格点QCD（lattice QCD）数据出发进行第一性原理提取；第三，在随机矩阵模型（random-matrix model）和夸克-介子模型（quark-meson model）等有效模型中显式演示奇点轨迹。在格点QCD数据分析中，采用迭代共形Padé方法（iterated conformal-Padé approach）提取连续极限下的复温度奇点位置。

Result: 在小实化学势区域，主导复温度奇点允许在μ²下进行解析展开；在临界点附近，则交叉为伊辛临界标度（Ising critical scaling）所决定的普适Puiseux形式。复温度与复化学势的奇点轨迹由相同的标度变量和映射系数控制，二者比较可对临界点搜索提供严格的相容性检验并约束临界标度区域的范围。基于格点QCD数据的分析表明，在物理夸克质量下，主导奇点的实部位于手征极限转变温度与物理质量手征磁化率峰值温度之间，其虚部非零。

Conclusion: 复温度平面中的杨-李边奇点是研究QCD相图解析结构的重要工具，与复化学势方法互补且受相同临界标度控制，可有效检验临界点搜索方案的可靠性。格点QCD数据分析结果与理论预期一致，为后续系统研究有限密度下QCD相图提供了新的分析框架和约束条件。

Abstract: We study the analytic structure of the QCD phase diagram by treating temperature as a complex variable. The nearest Yang-Lee edge singularities in the complex $T$ plane bound the domain of analyticity of temperature-dependent thermodynamic observables and complement the more commonly studied singularities in the complex chemical-potential plane. Our analysis combines three complementary perspectives: universal critical scaling, a first-principles extraction from lattice-QCD data, and explicit illustrations in effective models. We illustrate the resulting structure in a random-matrix model and in a quark-meson model, where the singularity trajectories can be followed explicitly. At small real chemical potential, the leading complex-temperature singularity admits an analytic expansion in $μ^2$, while near a critical point it crosses over to the universal Puiseux form dictated by Ising critical scaling. We show that the complex-$T$ and complex-$μ$ trajectories are controlled by the same scaling variables and mapping coefficients, so their comparison provides a stringent consistency test of critical-point searches and constrains the extent of the critical scaling regime. Finally, we analyze lattice-QCD data at $μ=0$ using an iterated conformal-Pade approach and extract the continuum location of the nearest complex-temperature singularity. The result is consistent with the expectation that, at physical quark masses, the real part of the leading singularity lies between the chiral-limit transition temperature and the physical-mass chiral-susceptibility peak temperature, while its imaginary part remains nonzero.

### [182] [Quantum Stochastic Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12636)
*Robson Christie,Jaewoo Joo,Greg Kaplanek,Vincent Vennin,David Wands*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在开放量子系统框架下系统表述了随机暴胀（stochastic inflation），证明德西特时空中的自由测试场满足GKLS型非幺正动力学，并通过Wigner-Weyl变换将其与经典福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）联系起来，同时探讨了轻场与重场区域的不同量子—经典过渡行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机暴胀的传统处理主要基于经典随机方法，其量子起源尚待更严格的推导。本文旨在将随机暴胀形式化为一个开放量子系统（open quantum system）问题，从而为场粗粒化过程中的信息损失与非幺正演化提供第一性原理的量子描述。

Method: 将固定物理尺寸小斑块中的粗粒化场（coarse-grained field）及其总动量视为一对正则变量，作用于单模福克空间（one-mode Fock space）作为“体”（bulk）。随时间步进对体进行重新定义，将新加入的共动模（comoving mode）作为纠缠模求迹，得到体密度矩阵的非幺正演化方程。在德西特时空的自由测试场情形下，推导出GKLS方程，并对其做Wigner-Weyl变换得到福克-普朗克方程；进而通过连续测量方案将GKLS动力学解开为随机薛定谔方程（stochastic Schrödinger equations）。

Result: 自由测试场在德西特时空中严格导出了GKLS型动力学，其由一个有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）和一个非厄米林德布拉德算符（non-Hermitian Lindblad operator）生成，表明扩散与哈勃摩擦来自同一量子通道。Wigner-Weyl变换后的福克-普朗克方程与经典随机暴胀的相空间分布方程一致。轻场区域中，通过过阻尼约化得到Starobinsky慢滚福克-普朗克方程，斑块纯度被强烈抑制；重场区域中场扩散被抑制，斑块保持近纯欠阻尼振子态，无法进行经典随机处理。

Conclusion: 随机暴胀可以等价地视为一个开放量子系统中的非马尔可夫退相干过程，其经典随机方程来源于量子动力学在特定条件下的约化。轻场允许经典随机描述而重场不能，这为暴胀量子涨落何时可作经典随机处理提供了明确的判据。

Abstract: We formulate stochastic inflation in an open quantum system framework. The field coarse-grained in a patch of fixed physical size, and the total momentum of that patch, form a canonical pair and act on a one-mode Fock space which we identify as the "bulk". At each time step, new comoving modes join the coarse-grained patch and the bulk has to be redefined. This redefinition produces an entangled mode that is traced over, yielding a non-unitary evolution equation for the bulk's density matrix. For a free test field in de Sitter, one obtains GKLS dynamics, generated by an effective Hamiltonian and a single non-Hermitian Lindblad operator, hence diffusion and Hubble friction originate from the same quantum channel. The Wigner-Weyl transform of the GKLS equation leads to a Fokker-Planck equation for the Wigner function, which matches the one that applies to the classical phase-space distribution of stochastic inflation. We also provide several schemes under which one can unravel the GKLS dynamics into stochastic Schrodinger equations when continuous measurements of the decoupled mode are performed, making contact with Langevin formulations of stochastic inflation. In the light-field regime, an additional overdamped reduction can be performed by integrating out the momentum variable in the Wigner distribution, leading to Starobinsky's slow-roll Fokker-Planck equation. In that regime, the purity of the patch is strongly suppressed. In contrast, for heavy fields, field diffusion is suppressed and the coarse-grained patch remains close to a pure underdamped oscillator, which prevents a classical stochastic treatment.

### [183] [Quantum Gravity Induced Entanglement from Propagating Gravitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12901)
*Anom Trenggana,Freddy P. Zen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过Feynman-Vernon影响泛函框架下的算符方法，展示了量子化引力场（quantized gravitational field）的传播模式与谐振子势中两个大质量粒子之间的相互作用如何导致粒子纠缠。研究发现，纠缠产生源于引力场的量子贡献，且并非瞬时形成，而是存在与粒子间距成正比的时延，体现了引力相互作用的因果传播特性。尽管产生的纠缠量极小，但若初始态选择为压缩态（squeezed state），纠缠量可被增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子化引力场是否以及如何通过其传播模式诱导两个大质量粒子之间产生纠缠，以加深对引力量子性质及其因果传播特性的理解。

Method: 采用算符方法（operator-based approach），基于Feynman-Vernon影响泛函（Feynman-Vernon influence functional）框架进行分析。

Result: 引力场对纠缠的影响编码在其对易关系（commutation relations）中，纠缠源于引力场的量子贡献；纠缠并非瞬时建立，而是存在与粒子间距成正比的时延；纠缠量整体极小，但选择压缩态作为初始态可增强纠缠量。

Conclusion: 在该模型框架下，引力场通过其量子贡献诱导纠缠，且纠缠建立过程符合因果传播规律；尽管效应极小，初始态选择为压缩态可部分增强效果。

Abstract: In this work, we show how the interaction between propagating modes of the quantized gravitational field and two massive particles trapped in a harmonic oscillator potential can cause the two particles to become entangled. To demonstrate this, we employ an operator-based approach within the framework of the Feynman-Vernon influence functional. Through this method, we find that the effect of the gravitational field on the generated entanglement is encoded in the commutation relations of the gravitational field. This result indicates that, within the framework of the model considered, entanglement arises through the quantum contributions of the gravitational field. Furthermore, this work also shows that entanglement is not formed instantaneously after the two particles interact with the gravitational field. Instead, there exists a time delay, proportional to the distance between the particles, before entanglement is established. This result reflects the causal propagation nature of gravitational interactions. In general, the entanglement generated through this mechanism is extremely small. Nevertheless, if the initial quantum states of the two massive particles are chosen to be squeezed states, the amount of generated entanglement can be enhanced, although the resulting effect remains very small.

### [184] [Double copy of form factors with multiple operator insertions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12929)
*Xinyue Li,Gang Yang,Guorui Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种“染色”（dyeing）程序，将色单态算符提升为伴随色态，从而解决了多算符插入下形状因子（form factors）双拷贝（double copy）中虚假极点（spurious poles）的结构复杂性问题；该框架揭示了新的标量排序结构，并可通过逆“漂白”（bleaching）操作恢复原始形状因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将散射振幅的双拷贝推广到涉及局域规范不变算符（local gauge-invariant operators）的更一般物理量是当前的核心开放问题。尽管单算符插入的形状因子双拷贝已取得进展，但其产生的虚假极点结构和隐藏因式分解关系难以推广到多算符插入的情形。

Method: 提出了一种“染色”程序，将色单态（color-singlet）算符提升为伴随色态（adjoint colored state）；原始形状因子通过逆“漂白”操作（即U(1)退耦）恢复。在该框架下，虚假极点被重新解释为染色态的传播子（propagators），隐藏因式分解关系则源自染色振幅的BCJ关系。

Result: 该框架成功解决了多算符插入下形状因子双拷贝中虚假极点结构复杂的问题，并揭示了一种新的标量排序（scalar-ordering）结构，该结构在双拷贝到引力时得以保留。

Conclusion: 所提出的染色-漂白框架为多算符插入的形状因子双拷贝提供了统一的图像，并揭示了引力理论中新的排序结构，为双拷贝方法的进一步推广奠定了基础。

Abstract: Extending the double copy of scattering amplitudes to more general physical quantities involving local gauge-invariant operators is a central open question. While progress has been made in the double copy of form factors (FFs) with a single-operator insertion, it has led to two intriguing features: poles that are spurious from the FF viewpoint become physical propagators in gravity, and FFs obey hidden factorization relations on these poles. This picture is difficult to generalize to FFs with multiple operator insertions due to even more complicated spurious pole structures. We resolve this problem by introducing a "dyeing" procedure that promotes color-singlet operators to adjoint colored states, while the original FF is recovered by the inverse "bleaching" (U(1) decoupling) operation. In this new picture, the spurious poles are propagators of the dyed state, and the hidden factorization relations follow from BCJ relations of the dyed amplitudes. For multiple operator insertions, this framework uncovers a new scalar-ordering structure that survives the double copy to gravity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 在保持电磁对偶性的非线性电动力学形变中，因果性与无焦散性之间存在严格的二择一关系（trade-off），且未形变的麦克斯韦理论在相关区域中具有独特的因果地位。

Abstract: Can a classically relevant stress-tensor deformation be exactly solvable, duality preserving, and physically causal? We construct an exact power-law family of nonlinear electrodynamics preserving electromagnetic duality, together with a parallel two-dimensional Lax-integrable realization. Its auxiliary geometry yields the full characteristic-cone phase diagram and a universal finite-energy fold. For the Maxwell seed, every nonzero relevant branch is acausal, whereas every causal branch is caustic-free; undeformed Maxwell theory is the only causal point in the relevant regime.

### [186] [The Graviton Propagator in Asymptotically Safe Gravity with Non-Local Form Factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13098)
*Emiliano Maria Glaviano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文分析了四维量子引力中，由渐近安全形状因子（asymptotically safe form factors）驱动下的背景引力子传播子（background graviton propagator）的流动。在曲率展开到二次项近似下，构造了$k=0$极限下的传播子并研究了其动量依赖。通过解析延拓至闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime），得到相应的闵可夫斯基传播子，发现仅在$q^2=0$处有一个正留数的单极点，且在该近似下无额外的鬼极点（ghost poles）。对应的牛顿势（Newtonian potential）在$r=0$处是正则的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 渐近安全（asymptotic safety）是构建紫外完备量子引力理论的重要候选方案，但背景引力子传播子的具体行为及其在动量空间中的解析性质尚需明确检验。本文旨在通过曲率展开至二次项近似，考察渐近安全形状因子驱动下传播子的流动结构，并检验是否存在非物理的鬼态（ghost states）以及牛顿势在原点处的奇异性问题。

Method: 在四维量子引力中，基于曲率展开至二次项（quadratic order in the curvature expansion）的近似框架，分析由渐近安全形状因子（asymptotically safe form factors）驱动下的背景引力子传播子（background graviton propagator）的重整化群（renormalization group）流动。构造了$k=0$极限下的传播子，研究其动量依赖，继而将非局域形状因子（non-local form factors）解析延拓（analytic continuation）至闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime），得到对应的闵可夫斯基传播子。

Result: 在该近似下，传播子仅在$q^2=0$处出现一个正留数的单极点（single pole with positive residue），未发现额外的鬼极点（ghost poles）。对应的牛顿势（Newtonian potential）在$r=0$处表现正则（regular），不存在传统爱因斯坦引力中通常出现的奇异性。

Conclusion: 渐近安全量子引力在曲率二次展开近似下，背景引力子传播子不含非物理的鬼态，且牛顿势在原点处无奇异性。该结果支持渐近安全框架在红外区域具有良好解析性质的可行性。

Abstract: We analyze the flow of the background graviton propagator driven by the running of asymptotically safe form factors in four-dimensional quantum gravity at quadratic order in the curvature expansion. We construct the propagator in the $k=0$ limit and investigate its momentum dependence. The non-local form factors are then analytically continued to Minkowski spacetime, from which the corresponding Minkowskian propagator is obtained. We find a single pole at $q^2=0$ with positive residue and no additional ghost poles at this level of approximation. The corresponding Newtonian potential is found to be regular at $r=0$.

</details>


### [187] [From 2D Yang-Mills to Calogero-Sutherland via a colored particle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13388)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过规范不变性（gauge invariance）和拓扑紧致性（compactness）将柱面上的杨-米尔斯理论约化为有限维量子系统；对阿贝尔情形识别出与环面朗道问题（Landau problem on a torus）的等价性；对非阿贝尔SU(N)情形进行广义构造，导出约化后的一维量子多体哈密顿量。

Result: 阿贝尔情形下，系统等价于环面上的朗道问题，展现出简并基态结构（degenerate ground state structure）。非阿贝尔SU(N)情形下，系统约化为带奇异卡洛杰罗-萨瑟兰型相互作用（singular Calogero-Sutherland-type interaction）的一维量子多体问题。

Conclusion: 柱面上的杨-米尔斯-粒子耦合系统在规范约束下可约化为有限维量子系统，其非阿贝尔推广自然导出一类具有可积模型特征的奇异相互作用，为理解规范理论中的多体量子效应提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study Yang-Mills theory coupled to a particle on a cylinder, where gauge invariance and compactness reduce the dynamics to a finite dimensional quantum system. In the Abelian case, this yields a model equivalent to the Landau problem on a torus, with a degenerate ground state structure. We generalize this construction to non-Abelian gauge groups and show that, for SU(N), the system reduces to a one dimensional quantum many body problem with a singular Calogero-Sutherland-type interaction.

Method: 利用大N近似整合出物质场（matter fields），保留由共形反常诱导的有效作用量中的Fefferman-Graham共形不变项。在静态时空近似下，计算Schwarzschild黑洞周围的诱导应力张量，并引入边界条件进行渐近分析。

Result: 边界条件选择了类似Unruh的渐近扇区，但应力张量并非唯一确定；出现了一个新的单参数族量子毛发，该量子毛发在近视界区域显著改变了应力张量的形式。

Conclusion: 这种新出现的量子毛发暗示一种新的半经典机制，使得黑洞形成的信息能够被编码在视界（horizon）之外，为黑洞信息问题提供了可能的解决方案。

Abstract: When matter fields are integrated out in a large N approximation, the conformal anomaly induces an effective action up to conformally invariant correction terms. In the present work, we consider the implications on black hole evaporation of such a term involving a conformal invariant found by Fefferman and Graham. Working in an approximation where the spacetime is static, we compute the induced stress tensor around a Schwarzschild black hole. The boundary conditions select an Unruh-like asymptotic sector, but not a unique stress tensor. A new one-parameter family of quantum hair emerges which changes the stress tensor in the near-horizon region. This suggests a new semiclassical mechanism by which information about black hole formation could be encoded outside the horizon.

Abstract: We study the one-loop correction to the entropy of near-extremal black holes in three-dimensional massive gravity at the special point where the theory exhibits a unique maximally symmetric vacuum and non-constant curvature hairy black holes can achieve extremality even in the static case. Focusing on the near-horizon AdS$_2\times S^1$ geometry, we evaluate the contribution of boundary graviton modes that become exact zero modes in the extremal limit. Abstract: ZX calculus provides a graphical formalism for reasoning about quantum processes, built from two interacting Frobenius algebras associated with the Z and X bases of a qubit. While it has found widespread application in quantum information and computing, its relationship to quantum field theory has only recently begun to be explored. In this work, we further develop this connection by providing a generalization of ZX calculus to two-dimensional Yang Mills theory with a compact gauge group. The key observation is that both frameworks can be organized around the Hopf Frobenius algebraic structure associated with a group algebra, which can in turn be described by the diagrammatics of two dimensional topological quantum field theory. ### [191] [Black Hole Thermodynamics Meets On-Shell Amplitudes: Local Detailed Balance and Thermal Spectrum from Spin Universality and Unitarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13599)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宏观物体内部状态高度简并，其热耗散与辐射过程的微观描述尚缺乏一个统一的在壳理论框架。现有方法难以简洁地同时处理平衡与非平衡热过程，且自旋自由度在宏观非旋转物体中的作用未被充分认识。

Method: 将平衡渐进态表示为在壳粒子，非平衡过程描述为在壳跃迁振幅；利用宏观对称性导出自旋普适性，使所有自旋态受单一普适耦合支配。

Result: 吸收与发射概率由同一耦合控制，局域细致平衡可直接从在壳数据导出。应用于黑洞时，框架再现了热辐射谱，并将霍金温度关联到与幺正时间演化（unitary time evolution）相容的最大吸收条件。

Conclusion: 该在壳框架为理解宏观物体热辐射提供了一个统一的理论基础，并揭示了宏观对称性与自旋普适性在热动力学中的核心作用。

Abstract: We develop an on-shell framework for thermal dissipation and radiation by macroscopic objects, whose large degeneracy of internal states is encoded in their entropy. In this framework, equilibrium asymptotic states are represented as on-shell particles, while non-equilibrium processes are described by on-shell transition amplitudes between them. A central observation is that spinning states remain essential even for macroscopically non-rotating objects. Consistency with macroscopic symmetries then implies spin universality, whereby all spinning states are governed by a single universal coupling. A key consequence is that absorption and emission probabilities are controlled by the same coupling, yielding local detailed balance directly from on-shell data. Applied to black holes, our framework reproduces the thermal emission spectrum and relates the Hawking temperature to the condition of maximal absorption consistent with unitary time evolution.

### [192] [Cosmological Dynamics of the Thermal Scalar Near the Hagedorn Temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13611)
*Arnab Pradhan,Luis Rufino,Scott Watson*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将热标量（thermal scalar）耦合到弦框架引力-膨胀子有效作用量（string-frame gravi-dilaton effective action），研究了Hagedorn转变附近缠绕模（winding mode）的宇宙学动力学。结果表明：低于Hagedorn温度时存在边界态（boundary states）而非吸引子（attractors），缠绕模的反作用可逆转宇宙膨胀；高于Hagedorn温度时快子热标量（tachyonic thermal scalar）产生负有效能密度但满足零能量条件（null energy condition），可实现Brustein-Veneziano型分支变换，但无法提供优雅退出（graceful exit）；在Hagedorn温度本身二次理论失效，需高阶相互作用。该框架表明Hagedorn退出问题无法在二次有效理论内解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究热标量（thermal scalar）在Hagedorn转变附近的宇宙学动力学，以及缠绕模（winding mode）在弦宇宙学（string cosmology）中的作用。

Method: 将热标量耦合到弦框架引力-膨胀子有效作用量（string-frame gravi-dilaton effective action），构建场论框架分析Hagedorn温度附近的缠绕模动力学。

Result: 低于Hagedorn温度时存在边界态而非吸引子，缠绕模反作用可逆转膨胀；高于Hagedorn温度时快子热标量产生负有效能密度但满足零能量条件（null energy condition），可实现Brustein-Veneziano型分支变换但无法提供优雅退出（graceful exit）；Hagedorn温度下二次理论失效。

Conclusion: 热标量阐明了Hagedorn转变周围的动力学结构，并表明Hagedorn退出问题（Hagedorn exit problem）无法在二次有效理论（quadratic effective theory）框架内解决。

Abstract: We study the cosmological dynamics of the thermal scalar the winding string mode that becomes massless at the Hagedorn transition by coupling it to the string-frame gravi dilaton effective action. This provides a field-theoretic framework for investigating winding mode dynamics near the Hagedorn temperature and their role in string cosmology.
  Below the Hagedorn temperature, the phase space contains static configurations in which the thermal scalar balances the shifted dilaton evolution. These configurations are boundary states rather than attractors, and when the thermal scalar mass depends on the scale factor, winding mode back reaction opposes expansion and can reverse it. Above the Hagedorn temperature, the tachyonic thermal scalar generates negative effective energy density while preserving the null energy condition, enabling branch changes of the Brustein Veneziano type. These transitions do not provide the graceful exit required to connect the Hagedorn phase to standard cosmological evolution. At the Hagedorn temperature itself, the quadratic effective theory breaks down and higher order interactions become essential.
  Because the thermal scalar originates as a Euclidean order parameter, our Lorentzian treatment should be viewed as an effective dynamical model of the Hagedorn transition. Within this framework, the thermal scalar clarifies the dynamical structure surrounding the Hagedorn transition and shows how the Hagedorn exit problem cannot be resolved within the quadratic effective theory alone.

### [193] [A Graphical Coaction for FRW Integrals from Partial/Relative Twisted (Co)homology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13627)
*Andrew J. McLeod,Andrzej Pokraka,Lecheng Ren*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文为共形耦合标量理论中所有圈阶的弗里德曼-罗伯逊-沃克（Friedmann-Robertson-Walker, FRW）积分构造了一个图形协作（graphical coaction），利用相交理论（intersection theory）与（部分/相对）扭结（上）同调（(partial/relative) twisted (co)homology）将FRW积分及其不连续性和导数分解为原始费曼图（Feynman diagram）的装饰构建块，从而实现了对宇宙学可观测量解析性质的组合学分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇宙学微扰计算中，FRW积分在圈层次上的解析结构缺乏统一的组合学框架，特别是其不连续性（discontinuities）和导数与原始费曼图之间的代数关系尚不明确。作者希望借助代数几何中的相交理论和扭结上同调来系统化这一分解过程，从而揭示控制FRW积分的微分方程（即运动学流（kinematic flow））的组合学起源。

Method: 采用相交理论与（部分/相对）扭结（上）同调的工具，将FRW积分（及其不连续性和导数）分解为可表示为原费曼图装饰的基本构建块。由此构造出一个纯图形化的协作（coaction）描述，其中仅需从图中直接读取的有理预因子（rational prefactors）作为代数系数。

Result: 成功构建了适用于所有圈阶FRW积分的图形协作框架，并证明该协作自然导致了控制FRW积分的微分方程（运动学流）的组合学结构。此外，开发了配套网页应用（https://frwcoaction.ca）和Mathematica笔记本，可计算任意图形的图形协作、微分和不连续性。

Conclusion: 该工作为剖析宇宙学可观测量的解析性质提供了一个全面的组合学框架；运动学流的组合学规则是所构造协作的自然推论。配套的网页应用和Mathematica工具降低了该方法的使用门槛，便于推广至更广泛的宇宙学微扰计算场景。

Abstract: We construct a graphical coaction for Friedmann-Robertson-Walker (FRW) integrals at all loop orders in conformally-coupled scalar theories with non-conformal polynomial interactions. Our construction makes use of intersection theory in the context of (partial/relative) twisted (co)homology, which we use to decompose FRW integrals (and their discontinuities and derivatives) into building blocks that can be represented as decorations of the original Feynman diagram. This facilitates a purely graphical description of the coaction, up to rational prefactors that can be read off from the graph. Our construction provides a comprehensive combinatorial framework for dissecting the analytic properties of cosmological observables; in particular, we demonstrate that the combinatorics of the differential equations that govern FRW integrals -- their so-called kinematic flow -- is a natural consequence of our coaction.
  We have also developed a user-friendly web application that computes the graphical coaction of any graph: https://frwcoaction.ca. Whenever possible, the web application also computes the differentials and discontinuities. A Mathematica notebook with the same functionality is also hosted at on a public GitHub repository.

</details>


### [194] [One-loop five-point gluing analytically](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13665)
*B. Eden,M. Gottwald*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文首次完全解析计算了四维 N=4 超杨-米尔斯理论（N=4 super Yang-Mills theory）中应力张量多重态（stress tensor multiplet）的单圈五点函数（one-loop five-point function），通过将留数序列重求和为欧拉积分（Euler integrals），并利用广义超几何函数（generalised hypergeometric functions）的交集理论（intersection theory）进行积分计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法分为两个步骤：首先将留数序列（series of residues）重求和为欧拉积分；然后对可能的积分直接进行积分，无法直接积分的情形则利用广义超几何函数的交集理论进行恢复和计算。

Result: 成功实现了对所有过程（all processes）的完整解析求值，这是首次完成此项工作。

Conclusion: 本文通过解析方法完全计算了 N=4 超杨-米尔斯理论中应力张量多重态的单圈五点函数，验证并补全了此前基于可积性方法的部分结果，为相关形式体系提供了完整的解析基础。

Abstract: The one-loop five-point function of stress tensor multiplets in N=4 super Yang-Mills theory in four dimensions has previously been studied by integrability methods. The finite-size viz gluing corrections defining it were originally matched on the known field theory result - establishing many features of the formalism on the way - and later to a good extent also analytically evaluated. For the first time, we present a full analytic evaluation of all processes. The starting point is the re-summation of series of residues into Euler integrals. These are directly integrated where possible or otherwise recovered from intersection theory for generalised hypergeometric functions.

</details>
